Chapter i. Du ri tor fai-tor pa' me rik' du ma telv-tor wuh dunap k' wuh ahm t' wuh adventures t' tom sawyer; tonk'peh ik ain't rai tukh. Ik dunap vesh' tor k' mr. Ulidar twain, heh au var-tor wuh yeht'es, mainly. Tra' vesh' vel if au sakadau, tonk'peh mainly au var-tor wuh yeht'es. Ik nam-tor nothing. I worla gla-tor anybody tonk'peh ti veh wak il wuh'ashiv, rik' ish-veh vesh' ezyet polly, il wuh kir'an, il sos'eh mary. Ezyet pollytom's ezyet polly, she isand mary, heh wuh kir'an douglas nam-tor ek' var-tor pa' svi' ik dunap, if nam-tor mostly wuh yeht dunap, k' ein stretchers, u' i leralmin-tor fa'. I' wuh yut ik wuh dunap salan abru nam-tor nash: tom heh me afer-tor wuh donku ik wuh robbers ip-sut svi' wuh tauk, heh ish-veh tor etek don-ka. Etek prah shehkuh thousand dollars apieceall pi-maat-tukh. Ish-veh vesh' wuh awful glan t' donku lu ish-veh vesh' piled abru. Muhl, judge thatcher au nem-tor ish-veh heh shitau ish-veh si' na' eku'ko, heh ish-veh zaprah etek wuh dollar wuh gad apiece ek' wuh tevun roundmore do wuh ak'shem kupi var-tor ra tor tor k'. Wuh kir'an douglas she nem-tor me na' ish-veh sa-fu, heh kal-tor she would sivilize me; tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' rough living svi' wuh kelek ek' wuh wak, panahik uf dismal regular heh tevan wuh kir'an vesh' svi' ek' ish-veh yut; heh ni lu i couldn't lamok ish-veh rai longer i lit si'. I prah vi' t'nash-veh hinek a'cit heh t'nash-veh slor-tukh-hogshead va'ashiv, heh vesh' elik heh satisfied. Tonk'peh tom sawyer au shi'kar me abru heh leralmin-tor au vesh' going tor palikaya wuh zhel t' robbers, heh i lau hau kuv i would hal-tor pla' tor wuh kir'an heh nam-tor respectable. Ni i went pla'. Wuh kir'an she maf-tor abru' me, heh puvutau me wuh ri donku-tor pakik lamb, heh she puvutau me wuh lot t' vath ahm, nuh', tonk'peh she worla tvai rai klau k' ish-veh. She shitau me svi' au uzh sai-vel va'ashiv, heh i couldn't tor nothing tonk'peh wadashaya heh wadashaya, heh olau ek' runelau abru. Muhl, yi, wuh hinek vel palikau va'ashiv. Wuh kir'an rung wuh kus-vakh na' mu'yor-yem, heh du had tor sarlah tor wak. Lu du prah tor wuh pasu du couldn't hal-tor gas'rak tor eating, tonk'peh du had tor bek-tor na' wuh kir'an tor k'hy ne' ish-veh patam heh grumble wuh pi' abru' wuh victuals, hi tra' vikau't really sovek-vel wuh tukh k' au, ik nam-tor, nothing goh kanok-vei vesh' pufas-tor k' itself. Svi' wuh subok t' odds heh shahtau ish-veh nam-tor natya; vel prah rish-tor abru, heh wuh juice ves t' swaps pa', heh wuh vel hal-tor weh-rom. Po' mu'yor-yem she prah si' ish-veh dunap heh oren-tor me pa' moses heh wuh bulrushers, heh i vesh' svi' wuh wadashaya tor talal si' ek' pa' ish-veh; tonk'peh k'-heh-k' she kal-tor ish-veh si' ik moses had vesh' tevik wuh considerable wu wak; ni yi i didn't tun rai weht pa' ish-veh, fai'ei i ri tor nem-tor rai fek svi' tevik sutra. Takov ak i aitlu tor vuzh, heh ya'akash wuh kir'an tor kal-tor me. Tonk'peh she wouldn't. She leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh tvai practice heh wasn't sok'i, heh i bolau ar'kadan tor ri tor ish-veh sovek weht. Ik nam-tor aishan wuh yut k' ein sutra. Au prah ne' fi' wuh vel lu au ri tor fai-tor nothing pa' ish-veh. La' she vesh' wuh-bothering pa' moses, if vesh' rai pi-maat tor ish-veh, heh rai nam-tor-tor tor anybody, hasu hal-tor, gla-tor du, wi finding wuh tepul t' lafot k' me na' doing wuh vel ik had ein rom svi' ish-veh. Heh she nem-tor snuff, nuh'; t' rivak ik vesh' ek' gas'rak, fai'ei she ovsoh ish-veh herself. Ish-veh ko-kai, din-tor watson, wuh tolerable slim hinek maid, k' goggles fi', had aishan sarlah tor ha-tor k' ish-veh, heh nem-tor wuh eku na' me i' k' wuh spelling-dunap. She ar'kada me middling lerash na' pa' wuh wadan, heh yi wuh kir'an tor ish-veh ease abru. I couldn't lam-tor ish-veh mau longer. Yi na' wuh wadan ish-veh vesh' tevalik pasik, heh i vesh' fidgety. Din-tor watson would leralmin, "ri tor shitau ish-veh ash'ya abru tra', huckleberry; " heh "ri tor scrunch abru spo' ik, huckleberryset abru zehik; " heh takov ak she would leralmin, "ri tor haf heh sakadaya spo' ik, huckleberrywhy ri tor du ar'kadan tor kloshah?" yi she var-tor me ek' pa' wuh rasahkos shi, heh i leralmin-tor i istau i vesh' tra'. She prah mad yi, tonk'peh i didn't tvai rai klau. Ek' i aitlu vesh' tor hal-tor somewheres; ek' i aitlu vesh' wuh rubah, i vikau't particular. She leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' wicked tor leralmin ra i leralmin-tor; leralmin-tor she wouldn't leralmin ish-veh na' wuh bosh panu; she vesh' going tor ha-tor ni u' tor hal-tor tor wuh rom shi. Muhl, i couldn't gla-tor rai advantage svi' going wilat she vesh' going, ni i tor abru t'nash-veh kashek i wouldn't ar'kadan na' ish-veh. Tonk'peh i worla leralmin-tor ni, fai'ei ish-veh would goh tor trouble, heh wouldn't tor rai rom. I' she had prah wuh palikaya, heh she went fi' heh var-tor me ek' pa' wuh rom shi. She leralmin-tor ek' wuh ak'shem would ma tor tor tra' vesh' tor hal-tor pa' ek' gad wu k' wuh harp heh uralau, ek'wak heh ek'wak. Ni i didn't nah-tor mau t' ish-veh. Tonk'peh i worla leralmin-tor ni. I ya'akash ish-veh kuv she reckoned tom sawyer would hal-tor tra', heh she leralmin-tor ri k' wuh considerable glan. I vesh' glad pa' ik, fai'ei i aitlu ish-veh heh me tor nam-tor teretuhr. Din-tor watson she potau pecking na' me, heh ish-veh prah tiresome heh lonesome. K'-heh-k' au zaprah wuh niggers svi' heh had prayers, heh yi kanok-veh vesh' ska' tor sar-tak. I went abru tor t'nash-veh tvi-shal k' wuh krus t' ha'fek, heh shitau ish-veh fi' wuh pasu. Yi i eku ne' svi' wuh ku-san k' wuh krani heh ar'kada tor nah-tor t' vel cheerful, tonk'peh ish-veh vikau't rai nam-tor-tor. I olau ni lonesome i danik istau i vesh' tevik. Wuh yel vesh' shining, heh wuh mor rustled svi' wuh lapan ek'wak ni mournful; heh i puzhu-tor wuh owl, maf ska', vi-whooing pa' somebody ik vesh' tevik, heh wuh whippowill heh wuh dog maf-tor pa' somebody ik vesh' going tor tev-tor; heh wuh salan vesh' trying tor zhal vel tor me, heh i couldn't tor si' ra ish-veh vesh', heh ni ish-veh tor wuh samu shivers sahr-tor abru' me. Yi maf si' svi' wuh lapan i puzhu-tor ik ves t' wuh ralash ik wuh tam'a tor lu ish-veh aitlu tor var-tor pa' vel ik's fi' its kashek heh mokuhlek't tor itself ken-tor, heh ni mokuhlek't shom hagik svi' its shi'vukhut, heh has tor hal-tor pa' ik yut kanok mu-yor grieving. I prah ni ne'-hearted heh pahth-tor i did istaya i had ein apc'koik. Takov ak wuh a'lazb went crawling abru t'nash-veh tipan, heh i vathlau ish-veh ska' heh ish-veh lit svi' wuh ha'fek; heh fa' i kupi budge ish-veh vesh' ek' shriveled abru. I didn't bolaya anybody tor var-tor me ik ik vesh' wuh awful rasahkos glat heh would zaprah me ein rasahkos kunli, ni i vesh' pahth-tor heh danik hutau wuh sai-vel ska' t' me. I prah abru heh da-tor pa' svi' t'nash-veh ash'yaidar rehkuh wak heh tuhsau t'nash-veh thasek kanok wak; heh yi i tied abru wuh pi' klachek t' t'nash-veh isachya k' wuh og-elakh tor potau witches maf. Tonk'peh i hadn't rai guhl'es. Du tor ik lu du've pakik wuh horseshoe ik du've afer-tor, instead t' nailing ish-veh abru abru' wuh svep, tonk'peh i hadn't ek'wak puzhu-tor anybody leralmin ish-veh vesh' sovek yut tor potau ska' rasahkos kunli lu du'd pustau wuh a'lazb. I eku ne' va'ashiv, wuh-shaking ek' abru', heh prah si' t'nash-veh mev na' wuh vuzh; na' wuh kelek vesh' ek' u' fam dvun u' tevakh i', heh ni wuh kir'an wouldn't fai-tor. Muhl, po' wuh akarshif i puzhu-tor wuh wak-vel maf ska' svi' wuh kahr hal-tor boomboomboomtwelve licks; heh ek' fam dvun againstiller do ek'wak. Takov ak i puzhu-tor wuh pi'gel snap ne' svi' wuh gu'gelik svi' wuh treessomething vesh' wuh stirring. I eku fam dvun heh shroi. Directly i kupi aishan barely zhu-tor wuh "me-yow! Me-yow!" ne' tra'. Ik vesh' rom! Leralmin-tor i, "me-yow! Me-yow!" u' mos u' i kupi, heh yi i shitau si' wuh ta'hal heh parish-tor s' wuh krani fi' tor wuh foshuhl. Yi i trel-tor ne' tor wuh solektra heh ukrau svi' among wuh lap, heh, sure hiyet, tra' vesh' tom sawyer waiting na' me. Chapter ii. Etek went tiptoeing bi' wuh yut svi' wuh lap pla' na' wuh shaht t' wuh kir'an's bah-ker, stooping ne' ni u' wuh khlup wouldn't theshau etwel patam. Lu etek vesh' be' dvun-tor k' wuh af'tum i tevan-tor abru' wuh gir heh tor wuh ralash. Etek scrouched ne' heh laid fam dvun. Din-tor watson's suk' nigger, ahmau jim, vesh' setting svi' wuh af'tum svep; etek kupi gla-tor ish-veh takov pa'shik, fai'ei tra' vesh' wuh ta'hal za' ish-veh. Au prah abru heh sakadau ish-veh talu si' pa' wuh minute, listening. Yi au leralmin-tor: "vi dah?" au shroi ein weht; yi au sarlah tiptoeing ne' heh lam-tor gas'rak svi' etek; etek kupi wuh estuhl ish-veh, nearly. Muhl, kesik ish-veh vesh' minutes heh minutes ik tra' vikau't wuh ralash, heh etek ek' tra' ni ikap-tor teretuhr. Tra' vesh' wuh shi fi' t'nash-veh mal-nik ik prah tor drizhan, tonk'peh i dasn't scratch ish-veh; heh yi t'nash-veh kaluk palikau tor drizh; heh thurai t'nash-veh pla', gas'rak svi' t'nash-veh tipan. Seemed spo' i'd tev-tor kuv i couldn't scratch. Muhl, i've pubeglanau ik vel plenty wak opi'. Kuv du nam-tor k' wuh quality, il na' wuh mem-lu til-kum, il trying tor hal-tor tor yuk lu du ain't sleepyif du nam-tor anywheres wilat ish-veh skil-tor't tor na' du tor scratch, po du dungi drizh ek' abru' svi' abru'le t' wuh thousand shitau. Takov ak jim leralmin-tor: "leralmin, vi nam-tor du? Whar nam-tor du? Dog t'nash-veh aushfa ef i didn' zhu-tor sumf'n. Muhl, i fai-tor ra i's gwyne tor tor: i's gwyne tor eku ne' la' heh shroi var-tor i zhu-tor ish-veh agin." ni au eku ne' fi' wuh solektra betwixt me heh tom. Au gal-tor ish-veh pla-tor tehnat wuh lap, heh sakadau ish-veh mal si' till veh t' au danik estuhl veh t' t'nash-veh. T'nash-veh han palikau tor drizh. Ish-veh drizh-tor till wuh bezhun-masu sarlah vi' t'nash-veh bezhun. Tonk'peh i dasn't scratch. Yi ish-veh palikau tor drizh fi' wuh svi'udish. Thurai i prah tor drizhan ne'rak. I didn't fai-tor uf i vesh' going tor eku fam dvun. Nash miserableness went fi' u' mau u' shehkuh il stehkuh minutes; tonk'peh ish-veh seemed wuh glan longer do ik. I vesh' drizhan svi' leh-wun natya shitau i'. I reckoned i couldn't lamok ish-veh weht'n wuh minute longer, tonk'peh i eku t'nash-veh zud lerash heh prah pok tor ar'kadan. Aishan yi jim palikau tor esh-tor ras; thurai au palikau tor snoreand yi i vesh' takov ak kel'o va'ashiv. Tom au tor wuh glat tor mekind t' wuh pi' ralash k' ish-veh mouthand etek went creeping maf fi' etwel el'ru heh mal-nef. Lu etek vesh' lehkuh ash'ya ska' tom zhal-tor tor me, heh aitlu tor tie jim tor wuh lap na' mihrsh. Tonk'peh i leralmin-tor rai; au lau wake heh tor wuh ertaya, heh yi au'd talal si' i vikau't svi'. Yi tom leralmin-tor au hadn't prah ha'fek hiyet, heh au would trel svi' wuh af'tum heh prah ein weht. I didn't aitlun ish-veh tor ar'kadan. I leralmin-tor jim lau wake abru heh sarlah. Tonk'peh tom aitlu tor resk ish-veh; ni etek slid svi' tra' heh prah rehkuh ha'fek, heh tom laid kaukuh cents fi' wuh pasu na' vlitau. Yi etek prah si', heh i vesh' svi' wuh wadashaya tor prah maf; tonk'peh nothing would tor tom tonk'peh au bolau ukrau tor wilat jim vesh', fi' ish-veh el'ru heh mal-nef, heh mavau vel fi' ish-veh. I bek-tor, heh ish-veh seemed wuh rom du', kanok-vei vesh' ni fam dvun heh lonesome. U' ak u' tom vesh' pla' etek tresahk bi' wuh yut, pa' wuh bah-ker foshek, heh k'-heh-k' zaprah abru fi' wuh menal fik t' wuh kunel wuh vath vla t' wuh kelek. Tom leralmin-tor au trel-tor jim's taik ska' t' ish-veh patam heh geldau ish-veh fi' wuh sikrus gas'rak abru' ish-veh, heh jim stirred wuh pi', tonk'peh au didn't wake. Afterwards jim leralmin-tor wuh witches bewitched ish-veh heh shitau ish-veh svi' wuh trance, heh fau-tor ish-veh ek' abru' wuh fupa s', heh yi eku ish-veh ne' wuh lap va'ashiv, heh geldau ish-veh taik fi' wuh sikrus tor gluvaya vi ovsoh ish-veh. Heh thurai wak jim var-tor ish-veh au leralmin-tor au fau-tor ish-veh ne' tor uzh orleans; heh, po' ik, kanok wak au var-tor ish-veh au sak-tor ish-veh weht heh weht, till k'-heh-k' au leralmin-tor au fau-tor ish-veh ek' abru' wuh panu, heh zungor ish-veh danik tor tevakh, heh ish-veh pla' vesh' ek' abru' saddle-kan-tor. Jim vesh' monstrous yaut pa' ish-veh, heh au prah ni au wouldn't hardly beglanau wuh vath niggers. Niggers would sarlah miles tor zhu-tor jim var-tor pa' ish-veh, heh au vesh' weht glazhau abru tor do sovek nigger svi' ik shasol. Flekh niggers would lamok k' ish-veh ru'lut tu'ash heh glazhau ish-veh ek' abru', ka u' kuv au vesh' wuh wonder. Niggers nam-tor kwon-hau-ov talking pa' witches svi' wuh gu'gelik k' wuh af'tum yon; tonk'peh whenever veh vesh' talking heh letting fi' tor fai-tor ek' pa' such vel, jim would pavesh-tor svi' heh leralmin, "hm! Ra du fai-tor 'bout witches?" heh ik nigger vesh' corked abru heh had tor nem-tor wuh pla' ku-san. Jim kwon-hau-ov potau ik kaukuh-svitan krus pauk ish-veh talu k' wuh string, heh leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh sem-rik wuh e'shua mazhiv-kur-tor tor ish-veh k' ish-veh sha' el'ru, heh var-tor ish-veh au kupi bohrau anybody k' ish-veh heh zaprah witches whenever au aitlu tor aishan k' taran vel tor ish-veh; tonk'peh au worla var-tor ra ish-veh vesh' au leralmin-tor tor ish-veh. Niggers would sarlah s' ek' pa' tra' heh mazhiv-kur-tor jim sovek-vel au had, aishan na' wuh glan t' ik kaukuh-svitan krus; tonk'peh au wouldn't esta ish-veh, fai'ei wuh e'shua had had ish-veh el'ru fi' ish-veh. Jim vesh' danik ruined na' wuh dvinsu, fai'ei au prah terpau abru fi' khrosahp t' having gla-tor wuh e'shua heh vesh' fau-tor k' witches. Muhl, lu tom heh me prah tor wuh rihk t' wuh hilltop etek glazhau maf ne' vi' wuh pi'kahr heh kupi gla-tor rehkuh il kehkuh ha'ge twinkling, wilat tra' vesh' has-bosh sular-ves, sos'eh; heh wuh yel abru' etek vesh' sparkling ek'wak ni tok-ti; heh ne' k' wuh pi'kahr vesh' wuh pilash, wuh bosh mile sax'ksei, heh awful fam dvun heh grand. Etek went ne' wuh kunel heh afer-tor jo harper heh ben rogers, heh dahkuh il rehkuh weht t' wuh sa-kan, ip-sut svi' wuh hinek tanyard. Ni etek unhitched wuh skiff heh seshau ne' wuh pilash dahkuh mile heh wuh ulef, tor wuh suk' ulidar fi' wuh hillside, heh went ashore. Etek went tor wuh clump t' bushes, heh tom tor kanok-veh swear tor potau wuh tsat, heh yi gluvau au wuh razh svi' wuh kunel, gas'rak svi' wuh thickest krus t' wuh bushes. Yi etek lit wuh ha'fek, heh ukrau svi' fi' etwel el'ru heh mal-nef. Etek went pa' dah-teh ker, heh yi wuh tauk tu'ash abru. Tom poked pa' svi' wuh tvur, heh takov ak ducked ne' wuh temok wilat du wouldn't wuh pubeglanau ik tra' vesh' wuh razh. Etek went bi' wuh wonil shi heh prah vi' wuh ves t' tvi-shal, ek' damp heh sweaty heh samu, heh tra' etek pehkau. Tom leralmin-tor: "i', etek'll palikaya nash zhel t' robbers heh vutau ish-veh tom sawyer's gang. Kanok-veh ik aitlu tor hau has prah tor nem-tor wuh oath, heh kitau ish-veh ahm svi' khaf." kanok-veh vesh' willing. Ni tom prah si' wuh thalv t' dun ik au had kitau wuh oath fi', heh telv-tor ish-veh. Ish-veh swore kanok sa-kan tor terpau tor wuh zhel, heh worla var-tor sovek t' wuh tsat; heh kuv anybody ovsoh sovek-vel tor sovek sa-kan svi' wuh zhel, whichever sa-kan vesh' ordered tor stau ik person heh ish-veh skan bolau tor ish-veh, heh au mustn't yokul heh au mustn't yuk till au had pustau au heh hacked wuh tuhs svi' ish-veh thasek, if vesh' wuh glat t' wuh zhel. Heh kling ik didn't belong tor wuh zhel kupi nam-tor-tor ik ulidar, heh kuv au did au bolau nam-tor sued; heh kuv au ovsoh ish-veh va'ashiv au bolau nam-tor pustau. Heh kuv anybody ik belonged tor wuh zhel var-tor wuh tsat, au bolau ma ish-veh drahk tresahk, heh yi ma ish-veh carcass yontau abru heh wuh vitush scattered ek' pa', heh ish-veh ahm blotted ska' t' wuh feim k' khaf heh worla mentioned va'ashiv k' wuh gang, tonk'peh ma wuh curse shitau fi' ish-veh heh nam-tor forgot ek'wak. Kanok-veh leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh yeht vaksurik oath, heh ya'akash tom kuv au prah ish-veh s' ish-veh sha' patam. Au leralmin-tor, ein t' ish-veh, tonk'peh wuh shom vesh' s' pirate-dunap heh robber-dunap, heh kanok gang ik vesh' pid-toned had ish-veh. Ein nahp ish-veh would nam-tor rom tor stau wuh skan t' sa-kan ik var-tor wuh tsat. Tom leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh rom idea, ni au nem-tor wuh hish heh kitau ish-veh svi'. Yi ben rogers leralmin-tor: "la''s huck finn, au hain't prah rai skan; ra du going tor tor 'bout ish-veh?" "muhl, hain't au prah wuh sa-mekh?" leralmin-tor tom sawyer. "ha, au's prah wuh sa-mekh, tonk'peh du mokuhlek't worla talal ish-veh aifa gad. Au nam-tor-tor tor ti mon-tor k' wuh hogs svi' wuh tanyard, tonk'peh au hain't vesh' gla-tor svi' aifa krus na' wuh tevun il weht." au variben ish-veh abru', heh au vesh' going tor tor-go me si', fai'ei au leralmin-tor kanok sa-kan bolau ma wuh skan il somebody tor stau, il else ish-veh wouldn't nam-tor rom heh keh-vla na' wuh vath. Muhl, kling kupi nah-tor t' sovek-vel tor doeverybody vesh' stumped, heh eku fam dvun. I vesh' danik pok tor maf; tonk'peh ek' na' wuh'wak i nahp t' wuh yut, heh ni i nufau au din-tor watsonthey kupi stau ish-veh. Kanok-veh leralmin-tor: "oh, she'll tor. Ik's ek' gas'rak. Huck mokuhlek sarlah svi'." yi au ek' terpau wuh pin svi' ish-veh ozh tor prah khaf tor glat k', heh i tor t'nash-veh ulidar fi' wuh dun. "i', " leralmin-tor ben rogers, "ra's wuh zehl t' business t' nash gang?" "nothing goh robbery heh riyeht-staya, " tom leralmin-tor. "tonk'peh vi nam-tor etek going tor rob?kelek, il cattle, il" "tukh! Stealing cattle heh such vel ain't robbery; ish-veh's burglary, " leralmin-tor tom sawyer. "etek ain't burglars. Ik ain't rai wihfelau t' style. Etek nam-tor highwaymen. Etek pehkaya skaf heh carriages fi' wuh fau-yut, k' limein fi', heh stau wuh sutra heh nem-tor ish-veh glantau heh donku." "bolau etek kwon-hau-ov stau wuh sutra?" "oh, certainly. Ish-veh's buhfik. Ein ek'te'kru nah-tor natya, tonk'peh mostly ish-veh's panah-tor buhfik tor stau themexcept ein ik du katau tor wuh tauk la', heh potau au till au're ransomed." "ransomed? Ra's ik?" "i ri tor fai-tor. Tonk'peh ik's ra au tor. I've gla-tor ish-veh svi' dunap; heh ni veling ik's ra etek've prah tor tor." "tonk'peh uf mokuhlek etek tor ish-veh kuv etek ri tor fai-tor ra ish-veh nam-tor?" "po, tenai ish-veh ek', etek've prah tor tor ish-veh. Ri tor i var-tor du ish-veh's svi' wuh dunap? Tor du aitlun tor hal-tor tor doing natya s' ra's svi' wuh dunap, heh prah vel ek' muddled abru?" "oh, ik's ek' maut tok-ti tor leralmin, tom sawyer, tonk'peh uf svi' wuh shashol nam-tor aifa katravahsu going tor nam-tor ransomed kuv etek ri tor fai-tor uf tor tor ish-veh tor au?ik's wuh vel i aitlun tor prah na'. I', ra tor du reckon ish-veh nam-tor?" "muhl, i ri tor fai-tor. Tonk'peh fundauik'aps kuv etek potau au till au're ransomed, ish-veh tvai ik etek potau au till au're tevik." "i', ik's vel spo'. Ik'll kilko-srashiv. Po couldn't du leralmin-tor ik fa'? Etek'll potau au till au're ransomed tor tevakh; heh wuh bothersome lot au'll nam-tor, tooeating abru kanok-vei, heh kwon-hau-ov trying tor prah thal." "uf du variben, ben rogers. Uf mokuhlek au prah thal lu tra''s wuh klashausu abru' au, pok tor pohshau au ne' kuv au dvun wuh peg?" "wuh klashausu! Muhl, ik nam-tor rom. Ni somebody's prah tor eku abru ek' mu-yor heh worla prah sovek yuk, aishan ni u' tor glantau au. I nah-tor ik's duh'es. Po mokuhlek't wuh ak'shem nem-tor wuh muhd heh ransom au u' ak u' au prah la'?" "fai'ei ish-veh ain't svi' wuh dunap sothat's po. I', ben rogers, tor du aitlun tor tor vel regular, il ri tor du?ik's wuh idea. Ri tor du reckon ik wuh sutra ik tor wuh dunap fai-tor ra's wuh yeht vel tor tor? Tor du reckon du mokuhlek oren-tor 'em sovek-vel? Ri k' wuh rom deal. Rai, osu, etek'll aishan hal-tor fi' heh ransom au svi' wuh regular yut." "ek' gas'rak. I ri tor kashek; tonk'peh i leralmin ish-veh's wuh duhsu yut, anyhow. Leralmin, tor etek stau wuh kosu, nuh'?" "muhl, ben rogers, kuv i vesh' u' ignorant u' du i wouldn't kal-tor fi'. Stau wuh kosu? Rai; kling ek'wak gla-tor sovek-vel svi' wuh dunap spo' ik. Du zaprah au tor wuh tauk, heh du're kwon-hau-ov u' polite u' pie tor au; heh k'-heh-k' au tevan svi' ashaya k' du, heh worla aitlun tor hal-tor ha-kel sovek weht." "muhl, kuv ik's wuh yut i'm sep-wafikh, tonk'peh i ri tor nem-tor rai fek svi' ish-veh. Mighty ak etek'll ma wuh tauk ni cluttered abru k' kosu, heh katravahsu waiting tor nam-tor ransomed, ik tra' skil-tor't nam-tor rai shi na' wuh robbers. Tonk'peh fator'voh, i ain't prah nothing tor leralmin." pi' tommy barnes vesh' asleep i', heh lu au waked ish-veh abru au vesh' pahth-tor, heh maf-tor, heh leralmin-tor au aitlu tor hal-tor ha-kel tor ish-veh ma, heh didn't aitlun tor nam-tor wuh robber sovek weht. Ni au ek' tor mihrsh t' ish-veh, heh puvutau ish-veh maf-kan-bu, heh ik tor ish-veh mad, heh au leralmin-tor au would hal-tor zehik heh var-tor ek' wuh tsat. Tonk'peh tom mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh kaukuh cents tor potau hizhuk, heh leralmin-tor etek would ek' hal-tor ha-kel heh ragel-tor thurai wehk gad, heh rob somebody heh stau ein sutra. Ben rogers leralmin-tor au couldn't prah si' mau, goh sundays, heh ni au aitlu tor palikau thurai gad; tonk'peh ek' wuh sa-kan leralmin-tor ish-veh would nam-tor wicked tor tor ish-veh fi' gad, heh ik settled wuh vel. Au sep-wafikh tor prah teretuhr heh teslau wuh gad u' ak u' au kupi, heh yi etek todvel-tor tom sawyer wuh'rak khart-lan heh jo harper dahr khart-lan t' wuh gang, heh ni palikau ha-kel. I clumb abru wuh foshuhl heh crept vi' t'nash-veh krani aishan fa' gad vesh' breaking. T'nash-veh uzh sai-vel vesh' ek' elmin-tor abru heh clayey, heh i vesh' dog-zungor. Chapter iii. Muhl, i prah wuh rom going-abru' svi' wuh asal s' hinek din-tor watson fi' khrosahp t' t'nash-veh sai-vel; tonk'peh wuh kir'an she didn't scold, tonk'peh goh pu-tor ska' wuh elmin heh krizhiv, heh glazhau ni sorry ik i nahp i would kloshah wuh du' kuv i kupi. Yi din-tor watson she nem-tor me svi' wuh tsorayek heh prayed, tonk'peh nothing sarlah t' ish-veh. She var-tor me tor pray kanok gad, heh whatever i ya'akash na' i would prah ish-veh. Tonk'peh ish-veh vikau't ni. I ar'kada ish-veh. Wuh'wak i prah wuh aluk-zehl, tonk'peh rai kik. Ish-veh vikau't sovek rom tor me rik' kik. I ar'kada na' wuh kik rehkuh il kehkuh wak, tonk'peh somehow i couldn't tor ish-veh ar'kadan. K'-heh-k', veh gad, i ya'akash din-tor watson tor ar'kadan na' me, tonk'peh she leralmin-tor i vesh' wuh duhsu. She worla var-tor me po, heh i couldn't tor ish-veh si' rai yut. I eku ne' veh wak pla' svi' wuh lapan, heh had wuh wu nah-tor pa' ish-veh. I leralmin-tor tor myself, kuv wuh ak'shem mokuhlek prah sovek-vel au pray na', po ri tor deacon winn zaprah wuh donku au pakik fi' pork? Po mokuhlek't wuh kir'an prah pla' ish-veh haul-tukh snuffbox ik vesh' vazgau? Po mokuhlek't din-tor watson thelik abru? Rai, leralmin-tor i tor myself, tra' ain't nothing svi' ish-veh. I went heh var-tor wuh kir'an pa' ish-veh, heh she leralmin-tor wuh vel wuh ak'shem kupi panavau praying na' ish-veh vesh' "spiritual mazhiv-kur." nash vesh' nuh' wehk na' me, tonk'peh she var-tor me ra she meanti bolau gol'nev vath sutra, heh tor kanok-vei i kupi na' vath sutra, heh glazhau si' na' au ek' wuh wak, heh worla nah-tor pa' myself. Nash vesh' including din-tor watson, u' i nem-tor ish-veh. I went si' svi' wuh lapan heh da-tor ish-veh abru' svi' t'nash-veh kashek wuh akarshif, tonk'peh i couldn't gla-tor rai advantage pa' itexcept na' wuh vath sutra; ni na' kim-shah i reckoned i wouldn't worry pa' ish-veh sovek weht, tonk'peh aishan kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor. Sometimes wuh kir'an would nem-tor me veh vla heh variben pa' providence svi' wuh yut tor tor wuh ak'shem's ru'lut masu; tonk'peh sos'eh thurai gad din-tor watson would nem-tor meskaraya heh knock ish-veh ek' ne' va'ashiv. I judged kupi gla-tor nash-veh ik tra' vesh' dahkuh providences, heh wuh ri donku-tor chap would lamok considerable gluvaya k' wuh kir'an's providence, tonk'peh kuv din-tor watson's prah ish-veh tra' vikau't rai gol'nev na' ish-veh sovek weht. I nahp ish-veh ek' si', heh reckoned i would belong tor wuh kir'an's kuv au aitlu me, hi i couldn't tor si' uf au vesh' wuh-going tor nam-tor sovek weh-rom ska' yi do ra au vesh' fa', seeing i vesh' ni ignorant, heh ni ves t' neik-ne' heh ornery. Pap au hadn't vesh' gla-tor na' weht do wuh tevun, heh ik vesh' kel'o na' me; i didn't aitlun tor gla-tor ish-veh rai weht. Au nam-tor-tor tor kwon-hau-ov whale me lu au vesh' sober heh kupi prah ish-veh el'ru fi' me; hi i nam-tor-tor tor nem-tor tor wuh lapan danik t' wuh wak lu au vesh' pa'. Muhl, pa' nash wak au vesh' afer-tor svi' wuh pilash drownded, pa' leh-dah mile abru' kahr, ni sutra leralmin-tor. Au judged ish-veh vesh' ish-veh, anyway; leralmin-tor nash drownded sasu vesh' aishan ish-veh suk'es, heh vesh' ragged, heh had uncommon wu isachya, if vesh' ek' spo' pap; tonk'peh au couldn't tor nothing s' wuh limuk, fai'ei ish-veh had vesh' svi' wuh masu ni wu ish-veh vikau't mau spo' wuh limuk na' ek'. Au leralmin-tor au vesh' floating fi' ish-veh pla' svi' wuh masu. Au nem-tor ish-veh heh visolektau ish-veh fi' wuh kutra. Tonk'peh i vikau't kel'o wu, fai'ei i pavesh-tor tor nah-tor t' vel. I knowed mighty muhl ik wuh drownded sasu ri tor marek fi' ish-veh pla', tonk'peh fi' ish-veh limuk. Ni i knowed, yi, ik nash vikau't pap, tonk'peh wuh kosu sai-vel-tor abru svi' wuh sasu's sai-vel. Ni i vesh' uncomfortable va'ashiv. I judged wuh hinek sasu would da-tor abru va'ashiv k'-heh-k', hi i istau au wouldn't. Etek mavau robber i' heh yi pa' wuh tevun-krus, heh yi i resigned. Ek' wuh sa-kan did. Etek hadn't robbed kling, hadn't pustau sovek sutra, tonk'peh goh aishan pretended. Etek nam-tor-tor tor spen-tor s' wuh lapan heh hal-tor charging ne' fi' hog-yetursu heh kosu svi' hal taking bah-ker tukh tor mahr-kel, tonk'peh etek worla hived sovek t' au. Tom sawyer puvutau wuh hogs "ingots, " heh au puvutau wuh turnips heh tukh "julery, " heh etek would hal-tor tor wuh tauk heh powwow abru' ra etek had ovsoh, heh uf wehk sutra etek had pustau heh pu'ulidau. Tonk'peh i couldn't gla-tor rai pinkaunu svi' ish-veh. Veh wak tom satau wuh sa-kan tor sahr-tor pa' kahr k' wuh blazing terpau, if au puvutau wuh slogan (if vesh' wuh glat na' wuh gang tor prah teretuhr), heh yi au leralmin-tor au had prah tsat ro'fori k' ish-veh zamasu ik thurai gad wuh bosh parcel t' spanish merchants heh don-ka wuh-rabs vesh' going tor ith'du svi' tauk hollow k' dah-teh elephants, heh shehkuh hundred tchorka, heh abru' wuh thousand "sumter" jarel, ek' putush-tor ne' k' di'monds, heh au didn't ma goh wuh klashausu t' kehkuh hundred ask'ersu, heh ni etek would ti svi' ambuscade, u' au puvutau ish-veh, heh stau wuh lot heh scoop wuh vel. Au leralmin-tor etek bolau slick abru etwel shek heh pohshayek, heh prah pok. Au worla kupi hal-tor po' kauk wuh turnip-hal tonk'peh au bolau ma wuh shek heh pohshayek ek' scoured abru na' ish-veh, hi au vesh' goh lath heh broomsticks, heh du lau scour na' au till du nehau, heh yi au vikau't don wuh mouthful t' vitush weht do ra au vesh' fa'. I didn't dva-tor etek kupi lick such wuh patreitan t' spaniards heh wuh-rabs, tonk'peh i aitlu tor gla-tor wuh tchorka heh elephants, ni i vesh' fi' el'ru thurai gad, gad, svi' wuh ambuscade; heh lu etek prah wuh zhit etek rushed s' wuh lapan heh ne' wuh kunel. Tonk'peh tra' vikau't rai spaniards heh wuh-rabs, heh tra' vikau't rai tchorka il rai elephants. Ish-veh vikau't sovek-vel tonk'peh wuh gad-shi'oren picnic, heh goh wuh primer-mohrn na' ik. Etek busted ish-veh abru, heh chased wuh kanu abru wuh hollow; tonk'peh etek worla prah sovek-vel tonk'peh ein doughnuts heh khlup, hi ben rogers prah wuh a'cit su-leitri, heh jo harper prah wuh hymn-dunap heh wuh ek'ur; heh yi wuh savensu vifalunau svi', heh tor etek eku kanok-vei heh tresahk. I didn't gla-tor rai di'monds, heh i var-tor tom sawyer ni. Au leralmin-tor tra' vesh' tus-tor t' au tra', anyway; heh au leralmin-tor tra' vesh' wuh-rabs tra', nuh', heh elephants heh vel. I leralmin-tor, po couldn't gla-tor etek au, yi? Au leralmin-tor kuv i vikau't ni ignorant, tonk'peh had telv-tor wuh dunap puvutau don quixote, i would fai-tor rik' asking. Au leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' ek' ovsoh k' enchantment. Au leralmin-tor tra' vesh' hundreds t' ask'ersu tra', heh elephants heh treasure, heh ni fi', tonk'peh etek had nemut if au puvutau magicians; heh au had da-tor wuh bosh vel vi' wuh kan-bu gad-shi'oren, aishan s' spite. I leralmin-tor, ek' gas'rak; yi wuh vel na' etek tor tor vesh' tor hal-tor na' wuh magicians. Tom sawyer leralmin-tor i vesh' wuh numskull. "po, " leralmin-tor au, "wuh magician kupi vutau abru wuh lot t' genies, heh au would hash du abru spo' nothing fa' du kupi leralmin jack robinson. Au nam-tor u' ha-vol u' wuh lap heh u' suk' pa' u' wuh church." "muhl, " i leralmin-tor, "s'pose etek prah ein genies tor gol'nev uscan't etek lick wuh vath patreitan yi?" "uf du going tor prah au?" "i ri tor fai-tor. Uf tor au prah au?" "po, au tetaya wuh hinek zhai-tukh ha'gelek il wuh shek-tukh mokov, heh yi wuh genies sarlah tearing svi', k' wuh rahm heh igen-wesh wuh-ripping pa' heh wuh vuzh wuh-rolling, heh kanok-vei au're var-tor tor tor au abru heh tor ish-veh. Au ri tor nah-tor nothing t' pulling wuh pohshaya-kispek abru k' wuh gir, heh belting wuh gad-shi'oren superintendent abru' wuh patam k' itor sovek vath sasu." "vi tor au bezhun-masu pa' ni?" "po, whoever tetau wuh ha'gelek il wuh mokov. Au belong tor whoever tetau wuh ha'gelek il wuh mokov, heh au've prah tor tor whatever au leralmin-tor. Kuv au var-tor au tor torvau wuh palace keh-leh miles wu s' di'monds, heh boshaya ish-veh bosh t' chewing-lag, il whatever du aitlun, heh zaprah wuh sa-eik-te'krusu's ko-fu s' china na' du tor marry, au've prah tor tor itand au've prah tor tor ish-veh fa' yel-abru thurai asal, nuh'. Heh weht: au've prah tor waltz ik palace pa' abru' wuh shasol wherever du aitlun ish-veh, du ken-tor." "muhl, " leralmin-tor i, "i nah-tor au nam-tor wuh sa'haf t' pa'ash-patam na' ri keeping wuh palace themselves 'stead t' fooling au maf spo' ik. Heh ra's moreif i vesh' veh t' au i would gla-tor wuh sasu svi' jericho fa' i would eku t'nash-veh business heh sarlah tor ish-veh na' wuh rubbing t' wuh hinek zhai-tukh ha'gelek." "uf du variben, huck finn. Po, du'd ma tor sarlah lu au tetau ish-veh, whether du aitlu tor il ri." "ra! Heh i u' pid u' wuh lap heh u' suk' u' wuh church? Ek' gas'rak, yi; i would sarlah; tonk'peh i ti i'd tor ik sasu qots'noi wuh k'lek lap tra' vesh' svi' wuh shasol." "shucks, ish-veh ain't rai nam-tor-tor tor variben tor du, huck finn. Du ri tor seem tor fai-tor sovek-vel, somehowperfect saphead." i nahp ek' nash abru' na' dahkuh il rehkuh gad, heh yi i reckoned i would gla-tor kuv tra' vesh' sovek-vel svi' ish-veh. I prah wuh hinek zhai-tukh ha'gelek heh wuh shek-tukh mokov, heh went si' svi' wuh lapan heh tetau heh tetau till i wadashaya spo' wuh injun, calculating tor torvau wuh palace heh makau ish-veh; tonk'peh ish-veh vikau't rai nam-tor-tor, rim t' wuh genies sarlah. Ni yi i judged ik ek' ik tukh vesh' goh aishan veh t' tom sawyer's ti. I reckoned au pudva-tor svi' wuh wuh-rabs heh wuh elephants, tonk'peh u' na' me i nah-tor natya. Ish-veh had ek' wuh ulidar t' wuh gad-shi'oren. Chapter iv. Muhl, rehkuh il kehkuh tevun-krus sahr-tor bi', heh ish-veh vesh' muhl vi' wuh karil i'. I had vesh' tor shi'oren danik ek' wuh wak heh kupi spell heh telv-tor heh kitau aishan wuh pi', heh kupi leralmin wuh wehkovaya pasu abru tor shehkuh wak stehkuh nam-tor reh-leh-kaukuh, heh i ri tor reckon i kupi ek'wak prah sovek further do ik kuv i vesh' tor ha-tor ek'wak. I ri tor nem-tor rai fek svi' su'etek-ek'tal, anyway. Palikauk i fnu-ven wuh shi'oren, tonk'peh k'-heh-k' i prah ni i kupi lamok ish-veh. Whenever i prah uncommon zungor i mavau hookey, heh wuh hiding i prah thurai gad ovsoh me rom heh cheered me abru. Ni wuh longer i went tor shi'oren wuh easier ish-veh prah tor nam-tor. I vesh' getting wihfelau t' nam-tor-tor tor wuh kir'an's yut, nuh', heh au vikau't ni raspy fi' me. Living svi' wuh kelek heh sleeping svi' wuh sar-tak seshau fi' me takov wufik mostly, tonk'peh fa' wuh samu igen-va i nam-tor-tor tor zish-tor si' heh yuk svi' wuh lapan sometimes, heh ni ik vesh' wuh shom tor me. I tishau wuh hinek yut buhfik, tonk'peh i vesh' getting ni i tishau wuh uzh ones, nuh', wuh pi' zeshau. Wuh kir'an leralmin-tor i vesh' coming bi' vohris tonk'peh sure, heh doing maut satisfactory. She leralmin-tor she vikau't kafusik t' me. Veh asal i pavesh-tor tor da-tor abru' wuh alem-cellar na' asal-yem. I pulau na' ein t' ish-veh u' sahris u' i kupi tor lehm abru' t'nash-veh losrak tipan heh potau ska' wuh rasahkos kunli, tonk'peh din-tor watson vesh' svi' ahead t' me, heh tuhsau me ska'. She leralmin-tor, "nem-tor ish-veh el'ru maf, huckleberry; ra wuh mess du nam-tor kwon-hau-ov tor!" wuh kir'an shitau svi' wuh rom zhit na' me, tonk'peh ik vikau't going tor potau ska' wuh rasahkos kunli, i knowed ik muhl hiyet. I palikau si', po' asal-yem, olaya worried heh hutau, heh wondering wilat ish-veh vesh' going tor tevan fi' me, heh ra ish-veh vesh' going tor nam-tor. Tra' nam-tor yut tor potau ska' ein ves t' rasahkos kunli, tonk'peh nash wasn't veh t' au ves; ni i worla ar'kada tor tor sovek-vel, tonk'peh aishan poked bi' neik-spirited heh fi' wuh glantau-si'. I went ne' tor wuh khom bah-ker heh clumb abru' wuh stile wilat du hal-tor k'fai wuh pid dohn foshek. Tra' vesh' wuh inch t' uzh izh fi' wuh solektra, heh i gla-tor somebody's ash'yaidar. Au had sarlah abru s' wuh quarry heh lam-tor pa' wuh stile wuh du', heh yi went fi' pa' wuh bah-ker foshek. Ish-veh vesh' funny au hadn't sarlah svi', po' standing pa' ni. I couldn't tor ish-veh si'. Ish-veh vesh' maut curious, somehow. I vesh' going tor zahal-tor pa', tonk'peh i stooped ne' tor glazhau na' wuh ash'yaidar wuh'rak. I didn't beglanau sovek-vel palikauk, tonk'peh thurai i did. Tra' vesh' wuh tuhs svi' wuh losrak kluf-timut tor k' suk' felu, tor potau ska' wuh e'shua. I vesh' abru svi' wuh dahr heh shinning ne' wuh kunel. I glazhau abru' t'nash-veh tipan kanok i' heh yi, tonk'peh i didn't gla-tor kling. I vesh' na' judge thatcher's u' sahris u' i kupi prah tra'. Au leralmin-tor: "po, t'nash-veh sa-kan, du nam-tor ek' s' esh. Did sarlah du na' ish-veh eku'ko?" "rai, osu, " i leralmin-tor; "nam-tor tra' ein na' me?" "oh, ha, wuh ulef-yearly nam-tor svi', kim-shah nightover wuh hundred heh kau-leh dollars. Ved wuh fortune na' du. Du had weh-rom kal-tor me invest ish-veh bi' k' ish-veh shehkuh thousand, fai'ei kuv du nem-tor ish-veh du'll spend ish-veh." "rai, osu, " i leralmin-tor, "i ri tor aitlun tor spend ish-veh. I ri tor aitlun ish-veh na' allnor wuh shehkuh thousand, nuther. I aitlun du tor nem-tor ish-veh; i aitlun tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor youthe shehkuh thousand heh ek'." au glazhau ak'wikmun. Au couldn't seem tor tor ish-veh si'. Au leralmin-tor: "po, ra mokuhlek du tvai, t'nash-veh sa-kan?" i leralmin-tor, "ri tor du ya'akash me rai deshkau pa' ish-veh, sanoi. Du'll nem-tor itwon't du?" au leralmin-tor: "muhl, i'm puzzled. Nam-tor vel wuh tukh?" "sanoi nem-tor ish-veh, " leralmin-tor i, "heh ri tor ya'akash me nothingthen i skil-tor't ma tor var-tor rai ti." au orenau wuh du', heh yi au leralmin-tor: "oho-o! I nah-tor gla-tor nash-veh. Du aitlun tor makau ek' ish-veh veltra tor menot mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh. Ik's wuh yeht idea." yi au kitau vel fi' wuh dun heh telv-tor ish-veh abru', heh leralmin-tor: "tra'; gla-tor du ish-veh leralmin-tor 'na' wuh consideration.' ik tvai i ma bought ish-veh t' du heh vlitau du na' ish-veh. La''s wuh dollar na' du. I' du glat ish-veh." ni i signed ish-veh, heh losrak. Din-tor watson's nigger, jim, had wuh isachya-rin'k'n u' suk' u' ish-veh ozh-dukal, if had vesh' nem-tor s' wuh fourth skaun-sa'haf t' wuh ox, heh au nam-tor-tor tor tor magic k' ish-veh. Au leralmin-tor tra' vesh' wuh tam'a svi' ish-veh, heh ish-veh knowed kanok-vei. Ni i went tor ish-veh ik mu-yor heh var-tor ish-veh pap vesh' la' va'ashiv, na' i afer-tor ish-veh ash'yaidar svi' wuh izh. Ra i aitlu tor fai-tor vesh', ra au vesh' going tor tor, heh vesh' au going tor stay? Jim prah si' ish-veh isachya-rin'k'n heh leralmin-tor vel abru' ish-veh, heh yi au meskarau ish-veh abru heh eku-tor ish-veh fi' wuh lan-tol. Ish-veh tevan-tor takov huhtik, heh goh padukau pa' wuh inch. Jim ar'kada ish-veh va'ashiv, heh yi wuh'ashiv wak, heh ish-veh bae'cok aishan wuh ka. Jim prah ne' fi' ish-veh mal-nef, heh shitau ish-veh kaluk tehnat ish-veh heh shroi. Tonk'peh ish-veh vikau't rai nam-tor-tor; au leralmin-tor ish-veh wouldn't variben. Au leralmin-tor sometimes ish-veh wouldn't variben rik' donku. I var-tor ish-veh i had wuh hinek slick counterfeit yonuk ik vikau't rai rom fai'ei wuh dvesh-tukh gluvau k'fai wuh haul-tukh wuh pi', heh ish-veh wouldn't be' dvun nohow, kauk kuv wuh dvesh-tukh didn't gluvaya, fai'ei ish-veh vesh' ni slick ish-veh olau greasy, heh ni ik would var-tor fi' ish-veh kanok wak. (i reckoned i wouldn't leralmin nothing pa' wuh dollar i prah s' wuh judge.) i leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' takov rasahkos donku, tonk'peh sos'eh wuh isachya-rin'k'n would nem-tor ish-veh, fai'ei sos'eh ish-veh wouldn't fai-tor wuh natyan. Jim smelt ish-veh heh zeshau ish-veh heh tetau ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor au would khartau ni wuh isachya-rin'k'n would nah-tor ish-veh vesh' rom. Au leralmin-tor au would thresh tu'ash wuh raw irish potato heh terpau wuh yonuk svi' svi' heh potau ish-veh tra' ek' mu-yor, heh thurai asal du couldn't gla-tor rai dvesh-tukh, heh ish-veh wouldn't olau greasy rai weht, heh ni anybody svi' kahr would nem-tor ish-veh svi' wuh minute, kal-tor sa'awek wuh isachya-rin'k'n. Muhl, i knowed wuh potato would tor ik fa', tonk'peh i had forgot ish-veh. Jim shitau wuh yonuk ne' wuh isachya-rin'k'n, heh prah ne' heh shroi va'ashiv. Nash wak au leralmin-tor wuh isachya-rin'k'n vesh' ek' gas'rak. Au leralmin-tor ish-veh would var-tor t'nash-veh bosh fortune kuv i aitlu ish-veh tor. I leralmin-tor, hal-tor fi'. Ni wuh isachya-rin'k'n variben tor jim, heh jim var-tor ish-veh tor me. Au leralmin-tor: "yo' ole sa-mekh doan' fai-tor yit ra au's wuh-gwyne tor tor. Sometimes au spec au'll hal-tor 'yut, en den agin au spec au'll stay. De bes' yut nam-tor tor res' hagik en kal-tor de ole sasu nem-tor ish-veh sha' yut. Dey's dahkuh ha'su hoverin' roun' 'bout ish-veh. Veh uv 'em nam-tor wan-kur en shiny, en t'vath veh nam-tor nesh-kur. De wan-kur veh gits ish-veh tor hal-tor gas'rak wuh pi' du', den de nesh-kur veh mashalo-thalv svi' en bust ish-veh ek' abru. Wuh ak'shem mokuhlek't var-tor yit if veh gwyne tor zaprah ish-veh na' de las'. Tonk'peh du nam-tor ek' gas'rak. Du gwyne ki' considable trouble svi' yo' ha'kiv, en considable mak. Sometimes du gwyne tor git dash-tor, en sometimes du gwyne tor git has-bosh; tonk'peh kanok wak du's gwyne tor git muhl agin. Dey's dahkuh gals flyin' 'bout du svi' yo' ha'kiv. Veh uv 'em's ta'hal en t'vath veh nam-tor gu'gelik. Veh nam-tor don-ka en t'vath nam-tor po'. Du's gwyne tor marry de po' veh fust en de don-ka veh k' en k'. Du aitlu tor potau 'yut fum de masu u' mau u' du pi-maat, en ri tor sahr-tor rai resk, 'kase ish-veh's ne' svi' de dun dat du's gwyne tor git geldau." lu i lit t'nash-veh ha'fek heh went abru tor t'nash-veh tvi-shal ik mu-yor tra' hayal-tor pap ish-veh sha' shal! Chapter v. I had ikap-tor wuh svep tor. Yi i da-tor pa' heh tra' au vesh'. I nam-tor-tor tor nam-tor pahth-tor t' ish-veh ek' wuh wak, au tanned me ni mau. I reckoned i vesh' pahth-tor i', nuh'; tonk'peh svi' wuh minute gla-tor nash-veh i vesh' mistakenthat nam-tor, po' wuh wuh'rak jolt, u' du lau leralmin, lu t'nash-veh esh wihfelau t' hitched, au hasu ni ri-gishu; tonk'peh gas'rak maf po' gla-tor nash-veh i vikau't pahth-tor t' ish-veh don bothring pa'. Au vesh' danik kau-leh, heh au glazhau ish-veh. Ish-veh isachya vesh' wu heh tangled heh greasy, heh geldau ne', heh du kupi gla-tor ish-veh bezhun shining k'fai spo' au vesh' za' kas-elakh. Ish-veh vesh' ek' nesh-kur, rai zhai-kur; ni vesh' ish-veh wu, rish-tor-abru whiskers. Tra' vikau't rai kur svi' ish-veh limuk, wilat ish-veh limuk gluvau; ish-veh vesh' wan-kur; ri spo' wuh'ashiv sasu's wan-kur, tonk'peh wuh wan-kur tor tor wuh ak'shem has-bosh, wuh wan-kur tor tor wuh ak'shem's kahm crawla lap-git'woa wan-kur, wuh aluk-nehg wan-kur. U' na' ish-veh clothesjust a'cit, ik vesh' ek'. Au had veh mal-nik resting fi' t'vath mal-nef; wuh kluf fi' ik ash'ya vesh' busted, heh dahkuh t' ish-veh gof terpau k'fai, heh au ar'kada au i' heh yi. Ish-veh taik vesh' laying fi' wuh flooran hinek nesh-kur slouch k' wuh fik caved svi', spo' wuh lid. I lam-tor wuh-looking na' ish-veh; au eku tra' wuh-looking na' me, k' ish-veh ku-san ayau pla' wuh pi'. I eku wuh ha'fek ne'. I pubeglanau wuh krani vesh' abru; ni au had clumb svi' k' wuh foshuhl. Au potau wuh-looking me ek' abru'. K'-heh-k' au leralmin-tor: "starchy clothesvery. Du nah-tor du're wuh rom deal t' wuh suk'-bug, ri tor du?" "sos'eh i am, sos'eh i ain't, " i leralmin-tor. "ri tor du mazhiv-kur-tor me rim o' ish-veh bru, " leralmin-tor au. "du've shitau fi' considerable wehk frills opi' i vesh' maf. I'll nem-tor du ne' wuh peg fa' i prah ovsoh k' du. Du're educated, nuh', au saycan telv-tor heh kitau. Du nah-tor du're weh-rom'n ish-veh sa-mekh, i', ri tor du, fai'ei au mokuhlek't? I'll nem-tor ish-veh s' du. Vi var-tor du du lau meddle k' such hifalut'n duh'es, hey?vi var-tor du du kupi?" "wuh kir'an. She var-tor me." "wuh kir'an, hey?heh vi var-tor wuh kir'an she kupi shitau svi' ish-veh hilek pa' wuh vel ik ain't rim t' ish-veh business?" "kling worla var-tor ish-veh." "muhl, i'll oren-tor ish-veh uf tor meddle. Heh looky hereyou eku ik shi'oren, du zhu-tor? I'll oren-tor sutra tor katau abru wuh sa-kan tor shitau fi' airs abru' ish-veh sha' sa-mekh heh kal-tor fi' tor nam-tor weh-rom'n ra au nam-tor. Du lemme kum du fooling pa' ik shi'oren va'ashiv, du zhu-tor? Ish-veh ko-mekh couldn't telv-tor, heh she couldn't kitau, nuther, fa' she tev-tor. Rim t' wuh skan couldn't fa' au tev-tor. I mokuhlek't; heh la' du're wuh-puv yourself abru spo' nash. I ain't wuh sasu tor lamok ityou zhu-tor? Leralmin, lemme zhu-tor du telv-tor." i nem-tor abru wuh dunap heh palikau vel pa' paik washington heh wuh t'naehm. Lu i'd telv-tor pa' wuh ulef wuh minute, au zaprah wuh dunap wuh whack k' ish-veh el'ru heh knocked ish-veh mes' wuh kelek. Au leralmin-tor: "ish-veh's ni. Du mokuhlek tor ish-veh. I had t'nash-veh vet-tor lu du var-tor me. I' looky la'; du pehkaya ik putting fi' frills. I skil-tor't ma ish-veh. I'll ti na' du, t'nash-veh smarty; heh kuv i kum du pa' ik shi'oren i'll mazhiv-kur du rom. Wuh'rak du fai-tor du'll prah odva, nuh'. I worla gla-tor such wuh sa-fu." au nem-tor abru wuh pi' pla-kur heh yaller bikuv t' ein aushfa heh wuh sa-kan, heh leralmin-tor: "ra's nash?" "ish-veh's vel au mazhiv-kur-tor me na' learning t'nash-veh tupa rom." au tore ish-veh abru, heh leralmin-tor: "i'll mazhiv-kur-tor du vel betteri'll mazhiv-kur-tor du wuh cowhide." au eku tra' wuh-mumbling heh wuh-growling wuh minute, heh yi au leralmin-tor: "ain't du wuh slor-scented dandy, hi? Wuh sar-tak; heh bedclothes; heh wuh glazhau'n'-makh; heh wuh krus t' la'y fi' wuh floorand ish-veh sha' sa-mekh prah tor yuk k' wuh hogs svi' wuh tanyard. I worla gla-tor such wuh sa-fu. I sihaya i'll nem-tor ein o' aifa frills si' o' du fa' i'm ovsoh k' du. Po, tra' ain't rai shaht tor ish-veh airsthey leralmin du're don-ka. Hey?uf's ik?" "au liethat's uf." "looky heremind uf du variben tor me; i'm wuh-standing pa' ek' i mokuhlek lamok nowso ri tor gimme rai sass. I've vesh' svi' kahr dahkuh gad, heh i hain't puzhu-tor nothing tonk'peh pa' du bein' don-ka. I puzhu-tor pa' ish-veh maf ne' wuh pilash, nuh'. Ik's po sarlah nash-veh. Du git me ik donku tor-morrowi aitlun ish-veh." "i hain't prah rai donku." "ish-veh's wuh ti. Judge thatcher's prah ish-veh. Du git ish-veh. I aitlun ish-veh." "i hain't prah rai donku, i var-tor du. Du ya'akash judge thatcher; au'll var-tor du wuh ka." "ek' gas'rak. I'll ya'akash ish-veh; heh i'll tor ish-veh pungle, nuh', il i'll fai-tor wuh utvau po. Leralmin, uf mau du prah svi' ish-veh abru'lik? I aitlun ish-veh." "i hain't prah goh wuh dollar, heh i aitlun ik tor" "ish-veh ri tor tor rai natyan ra du aitlun ish-veh foryou aishan fo ish-veh si'." au nem-tor ish-veh heh zeshau ish-veh tor gla-tor kuv ish-veh vesh' rom, heh yi au leralmin-tor au vesh' going ne' kahr tor prah ein whisky; leralmin-tor au hadn't had wuh mon ek' gad. Lu au had prah si' fi' wuh foshuhl au shitau ish-veh patam svi' va'ashiv, heh cussed me na' putting fi' frills heh trying tor nam-tor weh-rom do ish-veh; heh lu i reckoned au vesh' hal-tor au sarlah pla' heh shitau ish-veh patam svi' va'ashiv, heh var-tor me tor kashek pa' ik shi'oren, fai'ei au vesh' going tor ti na' me heh lick me kuv i didn't eku ik. Thurai gad au vesh' mon-tor, heh au went tor judge thatcher's heh bullyragged ish-veh, heh ar'kada tor tor ish-veh mazhiv-kur-tor abru wuh donku; tonk'peh au couldn't, heh yi au swore au'd tor wuh tor-gav nekwitaya ish-veh. Wuh judge heh wuh kir'an went tor tor-gav tor prah wuh kelek tor nem-tor me maf s' ish-veh heh kal-tor veh t' au nam-tor t'nash-veh guardian; tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' wuh uzh judge ik had aishan sarlah, heh au didn't fai-tor wuh hinek sasu; ni au leralmin-tor kelek mustn't snertau heh dahshauk skan kuv au kupi gol'nev ish-veh; leralmin-tor au'd druther ri nem-tor wuh kan maf s' its sa-mekh. Ni judge thatcher heh wuh kir'an had tor quit fi' wuh business. Ik sanoi wuh hinek sasu till au couldn't shom. Au leralmin-tor au'd cowhide me till i vesh' nesh-kur heh pla-kur kuv i didn't ashenau ein donku na' ish-veh. I yahv-tor rehkuh dollars s' judge thatcher, heh pap nem-tor ish-veh heh prah mon-tor, heh went wuh-blowing pa' heh cussing heh whooping heh carrying fi'; heh au potau ish-veh abru ek' abru' kahr, k' wuh zhai-tukh sunil, till danik midnight; yi au jailed ish-veh, heh thurai gad au had ish-veh fa' kelek, heh jailed ish-veh va'ashiv na' wuh wehk gad. Tonk'peh au leralmin-tor au vesh' satisfied; leralmin-tor au vesh' feihan t' ish-veh sa-fu, heh au'd tor ish-veh lamekh na' ish-veh. Lu au prah si' wuh uzh judge leralmin-tor au vesh' wuh-going tor tor wuh sasu t' ish-veh. Ni au nem-tor ish-veh tor ish-veh sha' kelek, heh sai-vel-tor ish-veh abru sok'i heh nice, heh had ish-veh tor asal-yem heh aru-yem heh mu'yor-yem k' wuh skan, heh vesh' aishan hinek pie tor ish-veh, ni tor stariben. Heh po' mu'yor-yem au variben tor ish-veh pa' temperance heh such vel till wuh hinek sasu maf-tor, heh leralmin-tor au'd vesh' wuh duhsu, heh fooled maf ish-veh ha'kiv; tonk'peh i' au vesh' wuh-going tor da-tor abru' wuh uzh mor heh nam-tor wuh sasu kling wouldn't nam-tor kafusik t', heh au rok-tor wuh judge would gol'nev ish-veh heh ri glazhau ne' fi' ish-veh. Wuh judge leralmin-tor au kupi teraya-martaya ish-veh na' au zhit; ni au maf-tor, heh ish-veh ko-telsu she maf-tor va'ashiv; pap leralmin-tor au'd vesh' wuh sasu ik had kwon-hau-ov vesh' misunderstood fa', heh wuh judge leralmin-tor au pudva-tor ish-veh. Wuh hinek sasu leralmin-tor ik ra wuh sasu aitlu ik vesh' ne' vesh' sympathy, heh wuh judge leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' ni; ni au maf-tor va'ashiv. Heh lu ish-veh vesh' bedtime wuh hinek sasu she-tor abru heh meskarau si' ish-veh el'ru, heh leralmin-tor: "glazhau na' ish-veh, gentlemen heh t'sai ek'; nem-tor wuh-meskaraya t' ish-veh; hutau ish-veh. Tra''s wuh el'ru ik vesh' wuh el'ru t' wuh hog; tonk'peh ish-veh ain't ni rai weht; ish-veh's wuh el'ru t' wuh sasu ik's palikau svi' fi' wuh uzh ha'kiv, heh'll tev-tor fa' au'll hal-tor pla'. Du ulidar au wordsdon't yen-tor i leralmin-tor au. Ish-veh's wuh sok'i el'ru i'; hutau itdon't nam-tor afeard." ni au hutau ish-veh, veh po' wuh vath, ek' pa', heh maf-tor. Wuh judge's ko-telsu she shok-tor ish-veh. Yi wuh hinek sasu au signed wuh pledgemade ish-veh ulidar. Wuh judge leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh holiest wak fi' vipladau, il vel spo' ik. Yi au k'hy-tor wuh hinek sasu vi' wuh vaksurik tvi-shal, if vesh' wuh spare tvi-shal, heh svi' wuh mu-yor ein wak au prah powerful thirsty heh clumb si' fi' tor wuh porch-kamu heh slid ne' wuh stanchion heh traded ish-veh uzh tor-pal na' wuh mashek t' keh-leh-fek, heh clumb pla' va'ashiv heh had wuh rom hinek wak; heh na' gad-ha'khlup au ukrau si' va'ashiv, mon-tor u' wuh fiddler, heh padukau ska' wuh porch heh shau ish-veh losrak kar svi' dahkuh shitau, heh vesh' danik froze tor tevakh lu somebody afer-tor ish-veh po' yel-abru. Heh lu sarlah au tor glazhau na' ik spare tvi-shal au had tor nem-tor soundings fa' au kupi kharau ish-veh. Wuh judge au olau ves t' sival. Au leralmin-tor au reckoned wuh ak'shem kupi reform wuh hinek sasu k' wuh shotgun, sos'eh, tonk'peh au didn't fai-tor rai vath yut. Chapter vi. Muhl, takov ak wuh hinek sasu vesh' abru heh pa' va'ashiv, heh yi au went na' judge thatcher svi' wuh kelek tor tor ish-veh mazhiv-kur-tor abru ik donku, heh au went na' me, nuh', na' ri stopping shi'oren. Au catched me wuh couple t' wak heh thrashed me, tonk'peh i went tor shi'oren aishan wuh ka, heh sayutau ish-veh il outrun ish-veh danik t' wuh wak. I didn't aitlun tor hal-tor tor shi'oren mau fa', tonk'peh i reckoned i'd hal-tor i' tor spite pap. Ik tor-gav trial vesh' wuh vohris businessappeared spo' au vikau't ek'wak going tor prah palikau fi' ish-veh; ni kanok i' heh yi i'd yahv-tor dahkuh il rehkuh dollars ska' t' wuh judge na' ish-veh, tor potau s' getting wuh cowhiding. Kanok wak au prah donku au prah mon-tor; heh kanok wak au prah mon-tor au ashenau cain pa' kahr; heh kanok wak au ashenau cain au prah jailed. Au vesh' aishan suitedthis ves t' vel vesh' gas'rak svi' ish-veh zehl. Au prah tor hanging pa' wuh kir'an's nuh' mau heh ni she var-tor ish-veh na' kim-shah ik kuv au didn't quit using pa' tra' she would tor trouble na' ish-veh. Muhl, wasn't au mad? Au leralmin-tor au would gluvaya vi vesh' huck finn's feihan. Ni au glantau si' na' me veh gad svi' wuh sikar, heh catched me, heh nem-tor me abru wuh pilash pa' rehkuh mile svi' wuh skiff, heh tuhsau abru' tor wuh illinois gef wilat ish-veh vesh' lapanik heh tra' vikau't rai kelek tonk'peh wuh hinek lap-fek hut svi' wuh shi wilat wuh lap-tukh vesh' ni bali du couldn't talal ish-veh kuv du didn't fai-tor wilat ish-veh vesh'. Au potau me k' ish-veh ek' wuh wak, heh i worla prah wuh pavesh tor sahr-tor ska'. Etek ha-tor svi' ik hinek thif'etek, heh au kwon-hau-ov klacha wuh svep heh shitau wuh tal-muv ne' ish-veh patam mu-yor. Au had wuh pohshayek if au had vazgau, i reckon, heh etek aluk-kum-tor heh shi'kar, heh ik vesh' ra etek ha-tor fi'. Kanok pi' du' au klacha me svi' heh went ne' tor wuh mahr-kel, rehkuh miles, tor wuh mes-hali, heh traded aluk heh zhagra na' whisky, heh zaprah ish-veh ha-kel heh prah mon-tor heh had wuh rom wak, heh licked me. Wuh kir'an she afer-tor si' wilat i vesh' k'-heh-k', heh she satau wuh sasu abru' tor ar'kadan tor prah meskaraya t' me; tonk'peh pap drove ish-veh ska' k' wuh pohshayek, heh ish-veh vikau't wu po' ik till i vesh' nam-tor-tor tor hasu wilat i vesh', heh tishau itall tonk'peh wuh cowhide krus. Ish-veh vesh' ves t' kas'el heh jolly, laying ska' kel'o ek' gad, smoking heh fishing, heh rai dunap il orenau. Dahkuh tevun-krus il weht sahr-tor bi', heh t'nash-veh sai-vel prah tor nam-tor ek' a'cit heh kitek, heh i didn't gla-tor uf i'd ek'wak prah tor spo' ish-veh ni muhl na' wuh kir'an's, wilat du had tor pu-tor, heh yokul fi' wuh math, heh dref abru, heh hal-tor tor sar-tak heh prah abru regular, heh nam-tor ek'wak bothering abru' wuh dunap, heh ma hinek din-tor watson pecking na' du ek' wuh wak. I didn't aitlun tor hal-tor pla' rai weht. I had pehkau cussing, fai'ei wuh kir'an didn't spo' ish-veh; tonk'peh i' i nem-tor tor ish-veh va'ashiv fai'ei pap hadn't rai objections. Ish-veh vesh' takov rom wak abru svi' wuh lapan tra', nem-tor ish-veh ek' pa'. Tonk'peh k'-heh-k' pap prah nuh' handy k' ish-veh hick'ry, heh i couldn't lamok ish-veh. I vesh' ek' abru' welts. Au prah tor going maf ni mau, nuh', heh locking me svi'. Wuh'wak au klacha me svi' heh vesh' hal-tor rehkuh gad. Ish-veh vesh' dreadful lonesome. I judged au had prah drownded, heh i wasn't ek'wak going tor prah si' sovek weht. I vesh' pahth-tor. I tor abru t'nash-veh kashek i would teslau abru ein yut tor trasha tra'. I had ar'kada tor prah s' ik thif'etek wehk wuh wak, tonk'peh i couldn't talal rai yut. Tra' vikau't wuh krani tor ish-veh suk' hiyet na' wuh dog tor prah k'fai. I couldn't prah abru wuh chimbly; ish-veh vesh' nuh' wonil. Wuh svep vesh' bali, huhtik oak slabs. Pap vesh' takov tun-bosh ri tor trasha wuh lipau il sovek-vel svi' wuh thif'etek lu au vesh' maf; i reckon i had shi'kar wuh shi abru' u' mau u' wuh hundred wak; muhl, i vesh' danik ek' wuh wak na' ish-veh, fai'ei ish-veh vesh' pa' wuh goh yut tor shitau svi' wuh wak. Tonk'peh nash wak i afer-tor vel na' kim-shah; i afer-tor wuh hinek zhar-tor lapan-gla-tor rik' sovek el'rek; ish-veh vesh' laid svi' svi' wuh rafter heh wuh clapboards t' wuh kamu. I elmin-tor ish-veh abru heh went tor ar'kadan. Tra' vesh' wuh hinek jarel-yuk-sai nailed tehnat wuh lap-fek na' wuh irak shaht t' wuh thif'etek za' wuh pasu, tor potau wuh salan s' blowing k'fai wuh chinks heh putting wuh ha'fek si'. I prah ne' wuh pasu heh ashenau wuh yuk-sai, heh went tor ar'kadan tor gla-tor wuh krus t' wuh suk' lanet lap-fek outbig hiyet tor kal-tor me k'fai. Muhl, ish-veh vesh' wuh rom wu job, tonk'peh i vesh' getting na' wuh shaht t' ish-veh lu i puzhu-tor pap's pohshayek svi' wuh lapan. I prah rid t' wuh glat t' t'nash-veh ar'kadan, heh eku-tor wuh yuk-sai heh ip-sut t'nash-veh gla-tor, heh takov ak pap sarlah svi'. Pap vikau't svi' wuh rom humorso au vesh' ish-veh malatik shal. Au leralmin-tor au vesh' ne' kahr, heh kanok-vei vesh' going riyeht. Ish-veh lawyer leralmin-tor au reckoned au would skil ish-veh lawsuit heh prah wuh donku kuv au ek'wak prah palikau fi' wuh trial; tonk'peh yi tra' vesh' yut tor shitau ish-veh ska' wuh akarshif, heh judge thatcher knowed uf tor tor ish-veh. Heh au leralmin-tor sutra kal-tor tra''d nam-tor wuh'ashiv trial tor prah me maf s' ish-veh heh mazhiv-kur-tor me tor wuh kir'an na' t'nash-veh guardian, heh au guessed ish-veh would skil nash wak. Nash hutau me abru considerable, fai'ei i didn't aitlun tor hal-tor pla' tor wuh kir'an's sovek weht heh nam-tor ni runelau abru heh sivilized, u' au puvutau ish-veh. Yi wuh hinek sasu prah tor cussing, heh cussed kanok-vei heh kanok-veh au kupi nah-tor t', heh yi cussed au ek' abru' va'ashiv tor tor sure au hadn't skipped sovek, heh po' ik au polished ska' k' wuh ves t' wuh paik cuss ek' pauk, including wuh considerable parcel t' sutra if au didn't fai-tor wuh ahm t', heh ni puvutau au ra's-ish-veh-ahm lu au prah tor au, heh went gas'rak bi' k' ish-veh cussing. Au leralmin-tor au would spo' tor gla-tor wuh kir'an prah me. Au leralmin-tor au would glantau si', heh kuv au ar'kada tor sarlah sovek such zhagra fi' ish-veh au knowed t' wuh shi shehkuh il stehkuh mile ska' tor stow me svi', wilat au lau shi'kar till au eku-tor heh au couldn't talal me. Ik tor me takov uneasy va'ashiv, tonk'peh goh na' wuh minute; i reckoned i wouldn't stay fi' el'ru till au prah ik pavesh. Wuh hinek sasu tor me hal-tor tor wuh skiff heh zaprah wuh vel au had prah. Tra' vesh' wuh kau-leh-plesh-tor sa'haf t' corn yem, heh wuh vla t' bacon, ammunition, heh wuh kehkuh-gallon mashek t' whisky, heh wuh hinek dunap heh dahkuh newspapers na' wadding, isha ein tow. I toted abru wuh tus, heh went pla' heh eku ne' fi' wuh kes-wun t' wuh skiff tor shom. I nahp ish-veh ek' abru', heh i reckoned i would lates ska' k' wuh pohshayek heh ein zehl, heh nem-tor tor wuh lapan lu i sahr-tor maf. I guessed i wouldn't stay svi' veh shi, tonk'peh aishan tramp gas'rak mes' wuh shasol, mostly mu-yor wak, heh shi'kar heh aluk tor potau alive, heh ni prah ni irak maf ik wuh hinek sasu il wuh kir'an couldn't ek'wak talal me sovek weht. I judged i would gla-tor si' heh trasha ik mu-yor kuv pap prah mon-tor hiyet, heh i reckoned au would. I prah ni bosh t' ish-veh i didn't beglanau uf wu i vesh' staying till wuh hinek sasu hollered heh ya'akash me whether i vesh' asleep il drownded. I prah wuh vel ek' abru tor wuh thif'etek, heh yi ish-veh vesh' pa' gu'gelik. Du' i vesh' fasan mu'yor-yem wuh hinek sasu nem-tor wuh swig il dahkuh heh prah wihfelau t' warmed abru, heh went tor ripping va'ashiv. Au had vesh' mon-tor abru' svi' kahr, heh laid svi' wuh gutter ek' mu-yor, heh au vesh' wuh glan tor glazhau na'. Wuh ak'shem would wuh nahp au vesh' adamhe vesh' aishan ek' vral. Whenever ish-veh liquor palikau tor ar'kadan au danik kwon-hau-ov went na' wuh govment, nash wak au leralmin-tor: "vutau nash wuh govment! Po, aishan glazhau na' ish-veh heh gla-tor ra ish-veh's spo'. La''s wuh tor-gav wuh-standing pok tor nem-tor wuh sasu's sa-fu maf s' hima sasu's sha' sa-fu, if au has had ek' wuh trouble heh ek' wuh anxiety heh ek' wuh kodona t' raising. Ha, aishan u' ik sasu has prah ik sa-fu ashenau na' kim-shah, heh pok tor hal-tor tor ar'kadan heh palikau tor tor suthin' na' ish-veh heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh shom, wuh tor-gav abru heh hal-tor na' ish-veh. Heh au vutau ik govment! Ik ain't ek', nuther. Wuh tor-gav pla'dor ik hinek judge thatcher abru heh gol-tor ish-veh tor potau me si' o' t'nash-veh veltra. La''s ra wuh tor-gav tor: wuh tor-gav nem-tor wuh sasu don shehkuh thousand dollars heh abru'ards, heh jams ish-veh vi' wuh hinek pash t' wuh thif'etek spo' nash, heh kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor pauk svi' sai-vel ik ain't fitten na' wuh hog. Au vutau ik govment! Wuh sasu mokuhlek't prah ish-veh rights svi' wuh govment spo' nash. Sometimes i've wuh mighty notion tor aishan trasha wuh shasol na' rom heh ek'. Ha, heh i var-tor 'em ni; i var-tor hinek thatcher ni tor ish-veh limuk. Lots t' 'em puzhu-tor me, heh mokuhlek var-tor ra i leralmin-tor. Leralmin-tor i, na' dahkuh cents i'd trasha wuh tenah shasol heh worla sarlah wuh-be' ish-veh agin. Au's wuh maut zhit. I leralmin-tor glazhau na' t'nash-veh hatif du vutau ish-veh wuh hatbut wuh lid ashenau abru heh wuh shom t' ish-veh hal-tor ne' till ish-veh's ne' t'nash-veh chin, heh yi ish-veh ain't rightly wuh taik na' ek', tonk'peh weht spo' t'nash-veh patam vesh' shoved abru k'fai wuh jint o' stove-mev. Glazhau na' ish-veh, leralmin-tor isuch wuh taik na' me tor wearone t' wuh wealthiest sasu svi' nash kahr kuv i kupi git t'nash-veh rights. "oh, ha, nash nam-tor wuh wonderful govment, wonderful. Po, looky la'. Tra' vesh' wuh elik nigger tra' s' ohioa mulatter, danik u' wan-kur u' wuh wan-kur sasu. Au had wuh whitest sav'el fi' du ek'wak gla-tor, nuh', heh wuh shiniest taik; heh tra' ain't wuh sasu svi' ik kahr ik's prah u' tok-ti sai-vel u' ra au had; heh au had wuh pi-maat-tukh glantau heh naf-elakh, heh wuh haul-tukh-headed canethe awfulest hinek zhai-kur-headed nabob svi' wuh fupa s'. Heh ra tor du nah-tor? Au leralmin-tor au vesh' wuh p'fessor svi' wuh college, heh kupi variben ek' ves t' gen-lis, heh knowed kanok-vei. Heh ik ain't wuh wust. Au leralmin-tor au kupi dvel lu au vesh' na' ha-kel. Muhl, ik kal-tor me si'. Nah-tor i, ra nam-tor wuh shasol wuh-coming tor? Ish-veh vesh' 'lection gad, heh i vesh' aishan pa' tor hal-tor heh dvel myself kuv i vikau't nuh' mon-tor tor prah tra'; tonk'peh lu au var-tor me tra' vesh' wuh fupa s' svi' nash shasol wilat au'd kal-tor ik nigger dvel, i bes-tor si'. I leralmin-tor i'll worla dvel agin. Au's wuh maut zhit i leralmin-tor; au ek' puzhu-tor me; heh wuh shasol lau nehaya na' ek' mei'll worla dvel agin u' wu u' i ha-tor. Heh tor gla-tor wuh samuyau yut t' ik niggerwhy, au wouldn't wuh mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh fau-yut kuv i hadn't shoved ish-veh si' o' wuh yut. I leralmin-tor tor wuh sutra, po ain't nash nigger shitau abru na' auction heh makau?ik's ra i aitlun tor fai-tor. Heh ra tor du reckon au leralmin-tor? Po, au leralmin-tor au couldn't nam-tor makau till au'd vesh' svi' wuh fupa s' shehkuh tevun-krus, heh au hadn't vesh' tra' ik wu wi. Tra', nowthat's wuh specimen. Au vutau ik wuh govment ik mokuhlek't makau wuh elik nigger till au's vesh' svi' wuh fupa s' shehkuh tevun-krus. La''s wuh govment ik calls itself wuh govment, heh kal-tor fi' tor nam-tor wuh govment, heh nah-tor ish-veh nam-tor wuh govment, heh wi's prah tor eku fek-fam dvun na' shehkuh bosh tevun-krus fa' ish-veh mokuhlek nem-tor wuh meskaraya t' wuh prowling, thieving, infernal, wan-kur-shirted elik nigger, heh" pap vesh' agoing fi' ni au worla pubeglanau wilat ish-veh hinek limber mal vesh' taking ish-veh tor, ni au went patam abru' timut abru' wuh matuhlek t' alem pork heh barked fi' ne-mal, heh wuh shom t' ish-veh starun vesh' ek' wuh hottest ves t' languagemostly hove na' wuh nigger heh wuh govment, hi au mazhiv-kur-tor wuh matuhlek ein, nuh', ek' bi', la' heh tra'. Au spen-tor pa' wuh thif'etek considerable, wuh'rak fi' veh mal heh yi fi' wuh vath, holding wuh'rak veh ne-mal heh yi wuh vath veh, heh na' kim-shah au kal-tor si' k' ish-veh losrak ash'ya ek' t' wuh sudden heh zaprah wuh matuhlek wuh rattling kick. Tonk'peh ish-veh vikau't rom judgment, fai'ei ik vesh' wuh kluf ik had wuh couple t' ish-veh gof leaking s' wuh khom shaht t' ish-veh; ni i' au ashenau wuh vlut ik fairly tor wuh ak'shem's isachya ashenau, heh ne' au went svi' wuh kitek, heh padukau tra', heh meskarau ish-veh gof; heh wuh cussing au ovsoh yi laid abru' sovek-vel au had ek'wak ovsoh previous. Au leralmin-tor ni ish-veh sha' shal afterwards. Au had puzhu-tor hinek sowberry hagan svi' ish-veh buhfik gad, heh au leralmin-tor ish-veh laid abru' ish-veh, nuh'; tonk'peh i reckon ik vesh' wihfelau t' piling ish-veh fi', sos'eh. Po' mu'yor-yem pap nem-tor wuh mashek, heh leralmin-tor au had hiyet whisky tra' na' dahkuh drunks heh veh delirium tremens. Ik vesh' kwon-hau-ov ish-veh zhit. I judged au would nam-tor glan-fam mon-tor svi' pa' wuh wadan, heh yi i would vazgau wuh tal-muv, il gla-tor myself si', veh il t'vath. Au drank heh drank, heh tumbled ne' fi' ish-veh yuk-sai k'-heh-k'; tonk'peh kunli didn't sahr-tor t'nash-veh yut. Au didn't hal-tor ralash asleep, tonk'peh vesh' uneasy. Au groaned heh nau heh thrashed pa' nash yut heh ik na' wuh akarshif. Na' kim-shah i prah ni sleepy i couldn't potau t'nash-veh bezhun tu'ash ek' i kupi tor, heh ni fa' i knowed ra i vesh' pa' i vesh' ralash asleep, heh wuh ha'fek yontau. I ri tor fai-tor uf wu i vesh' asleep, tonk'peh ek' t' wuh sudden tra' vesh' wuh awful shei heh i vesh' abru. Tra' vesh' pap looking kwai, heh skipping pa' kanok if yut heh yelling pa' oluhk. Au leralmin-tor au vesh' crawling abru ish-veh mal; heh yi au would mazhiv-kur-tor wuh spen-tor heh shei, heh leralmin veh had zeshau ish-veh fi' wuh cheekbut i couldn't gla-tor rai oluhk. Au palikau heh sahr-tor pauk heh pauk wuh thif'etek, hollering "nem-tor ish-veh ska'! Nem-tor ish-veh ska'! Au's biting me fi' wuh talu!" i worla gla-tor wuh sasu glazhau ni kwai svi' wuh bezhun. Takov ak au vesh' ek' fagged si', heh tevan-tor ne' panting; yi au padukau abru' heh abru' wonderful sahris, kicking vel kanok if yut, heh striking heh grabbing na' wuh sov k' ish-veh el'ru, heh screaming heh taran tra' vesh' e'shua wuh-meskaraya t' ish-veh. Au sai-vel-tor si' k'-heh-k', heh laid fam dvun wuh du', moaning. Yi au laid stiller, heh didn't tor wuh ralash. I kupi zhu-tor wuh owls heh wuh wolves maf ska' svi' wuh lapan, heh ish-veh seemed terrible fam dvun. Au vesh' laying abru' k' wuh teruk. K'-heh-k' au ashenau abru krus yut heh shroi, k' ish-veh patam tor veh vla. Au leralmin-tor, maut neik: "tramptramptramp; ik's wuh tevik; tramptramptramp; au're coming po' me; tonk'peh i skil-tor't hal-tor. Oh, au're la'! Ri tor esta medon't! El'ru offthey're samu; kal-tor hal-tor. Oh, kal-tor wuh ri donku-tor e'shua sa'awek!" yi au went ne' fi' ek' fours heh ukrau ska', begging au tor kal-tor ish-veh sa'awek, heh au padukau himself abru svi' ish-veh yuk-sai heh wallowed svi' ne' wuh hinek pine pasu, fam dvun wuh-begging; heh yi au went tor maf-tor. I kupi zhu-tor ish-veh k'fai wuh yuk-sai. K'-heh-k' au padukau si' heh spen-tor abru fi' ish-veh ash'ya looking kwai, heh au gla-tor me heh went na' me. Au chased me pauk heh pauk wuh shi k' wuh clasp-lipau, calling me wuh ha'su t' tevakh, heh taran au would stau me, heh yi i couldn't sarlah na' ish-veh rai weht. I eit'jae, heh var-tor ish-veh i vesh' goh huck; tonk'peh au abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor such wuh screechy abru'teruklar-ru'lut, heh roared heh cussed, heh potau fi' chasing me abru. Wuh'wak lu i da-tor pen heh sayutau ne' ish-veh kar au tor wuh runem heh prah me k' wuh jacket svi' t'nash-veh tipan, heh i nahp i vesh' hal-tor; tonk'peh i slid s' wuh jacket sahris u' igen-wesh, heh korsau myself. Takov ak au vesh' ek' zungor si', heh eku-tor ne' k' ish-veh pla' tehnat wuh svep, heh leralmin-tor au would shom wuh minute heh yi stau me. Au shitau ish-veh lipau ne' ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor au would yuk heh prah karik, heh yi au would gla-tor vi vesh' vi. Ni au dozed ska' takov ak. K'-heh-k' i prah wuh hinek thresh-lanet ku-san heh clumb abru u' hagik u' i kupi, ri tor tor sovek ralash, heh prah ne' wuh pohshayek. I trel-tor wuh ramrod ne' ish-veh tor tor sure ish-veh vesh' putush-tor, yi i laid ish-veh mes' wuh turnip subok, pointing na' pap, heh eku ne' za' ish-veh tor bek-tor na' ish-veh tor stir. Heh uf vohris heh fam dvun wuh wak did zaseshau bi'. Chapter vii. "git abru! Ra du 'bout?" i tu'ash t'nash-veh bezhun heh glazhau pa', trying tor tor si' wilat i vesh'. Ish-veh vesh' po' yel-abru, heh i had vesh' ralash asleep. Pap vesh' standing abru' me looking sfith heh has-bosh, nuh'. Au leralmin-tor: "ra du doin' k' nash pohshayek?" i judged au didn't fai-tor nothing pa' ra au had vesh' doing, ni i leralmin-tor: "somebody ar'kada tor prah svi', ni i vesh' laying na' ish-veh." "po didn't du roust me si'?" "muhl, i ar'kada tor, tonk'peh i couldn't; i couldn't budge du." "muhl, ek' gas'rak. Ri tor lamok tra' palavering ek' gad, tonk'peh si' k' du heh gla-tor kuv tra''s wuh aluk fi' wuh zehl na' asal-yem. I'll nam-tor bi' svi' wuh minute." au unlocked wuh svep, heh i pa'shu si' abru wuh pilash-kutra. I pubeglanau ein krus t' sikrus heh such vel floating ne', heh wuh sprinkling t' kas-wadi; ni i knowed wuh pilash had palikau tor shen. I reckoned i would ma lo'uk wak i' kuv i vesh' abru' na' wuh kahr. Wuh belaar shen nam-tor-tor tor nam-tor kwon-hau-ov kunli na' me; fai'ei u' ak u' ik shen palikau la' sarlah cordwood floating ne', heh krus t' lap-fek raftssometimes wuh dozen lap-fek teretuhr; ni ek' du ma tor tor nam-tor tor kum au heh makau au tor wuh lapan-ker heh wuh sawmill. I went bi' abru wuh kutra k' veh bezhun si' na' pap heh t'vath veh si' na' ra wuh shen lau zaprah bi'. Muhl, ek' na' wuh'wak la' sarlah wuh canoe; aishan wuh vaksur, nuh', pa' leh-reh il leh-keh ash'ya wu, riding pid spo' wuh duck. I pohshaya patam-wuh'rak ska' t' wuh kutra spo' wuh git'woa, sai-vel heh ek' fi', heh kwul-tor si' na' wuh canoe. I aishan gishu tra''d nam-tor somebody laying ne' svi' ish-veh, fai'ei sutra k'ashiv ovsoh ik tor duhsu sular-ves, heh lu wuh chap had seshau wuh skiff si' danik tor ish-veh au'd ashenau abru heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' ish-veh. Tonk'peh ish-veh vikau't ni nash wak. Ish-veh vesh' wuh maraya-canoe sure hiyet, heh i clumb svi' heh paddled ish-veh ashore. Nah-tor i, wuh hinek sasu dungi nam-tor glad lu gla-tor ish-veh thisshe's don lehkuh dollars. Tonk'peh lu i prah tor gef pap wasn't svi' glan wi, heh u' i vesh' sahran ish-veh vi' wuh pi' creek spo' wuh gully, ek' geldau abru' k' kas-elakh heh willows, i kwul-tor wuh'ashiv idea: i judged i'd ip-sut ish-veh rom, heh yi, 'stead t' taking tor wuh lapan lu i sahr-tor ska', i'd hal-tor ne' wuh pilash pa' kau-leh mile heh ith'du svi' veh shi na' rom, heh ri ma such wuh rough wak tramping fi' ash'ya. Ish-veh vesh' takov beyik wuh shanty, heh i nahp i puzhu-tor wuh hinek sasu coming ek' wuh wak; tonk'peh i prah ish-veh ip-sut; heh yi i si' heh glazhau pa' wuh bunch t' willows, heh tra' vesh' wuh hinek sasu ne' wuh yut wuh krus aishan bestan wuh o'lid fi' wuh kushel k' ish-veh pohshayek. Ni au hadn't gla-tor sovek-vel. Lu au prah bi' i vesh' lerash na' ish-veh taking abru wuh "sahr-tor" zehl. Au abused me wuh pi' na' hasu ni vohris; tonk'peh i var-tor ish-veh i tevan-tor svi' wuh pilash, heh ik vesh' ra tor me ni wu. I knowed au would gla-tor i vesh' masupik, heh yi au would nam-tor asking deshkau. Etek prah kaukuh catfish ska' wuh zehl heh went ha-kel. Du' etek laid ska' po' asal-yem tor yuk abru, fi' t' etek hasu pa' sai-vel-tor si', i prah tor thinking ik kuv i kupi teslau abru ein yut tor potau pap heh wuh kir'an s' trying tor zahal-tor me, ish-veh would nam-tor wuh certainer vel do trusting tor kunli tor prah irak hiyet ska' fa' au din-tor me; du gla-tor, ek' ves t' vel lau pavesh-tor. Muhl, i didn't gla-tor rai yut na' wuh du', tonk'peh k'-heh-k' pap ashenau abru wuh minute tor mon wuh'ashiv subok t' masu, heh au leralmin-tor: "wuh'ashiv wak wuh sasu sarlah wuh-prowling pauk la' du roust me si', du zhu-tor? Ik sasu vikau't la' na' rai rom. I'd wuh pohshaya ish-veh. Thurai wak du roust me si', du zhu-tor?" yi au eku-tor ne' heh went tor yuk va'ashiv; tonk'peh ra au had vesh' taran mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh maut idea i aitlu. I leralmin-tor tor myself, i mokuhlek teslau ish-veh i' ni kling skil-tor't nah-tor t' zahalik me. Pa' leh-dah o'wak-vel etek da-tor si' heh went bi' abru wuh kutra. Wuh pilash vesh' coming abru takov sahris, heh lots t' driftwood going k' fi' wuh shen. K'-heh-k' bi' sarlah krus t' wuh lap-fek raftnine lap-fek sahris teretuhr. Etek went si' k' wuh skiff heh towed ish-veh ashore. Yi etek had aru-yem. Anybody tonk'peh pap would wuh bek-tor heh gla-tor wuh gad k'fai, ni u' tor kum weht tukh; tonk'peh ik vikau't pap's style. Naukuh lap-fek vesh' hiyet na' veh wak; au bolau shove gas'rak abru' tor kahr heh makau. Ni au klacha me svi' heh nem-tor wuh skiff, heh palikau ska' towing wuh marshak pa' ulef-vesht rehkuh. I judged au wouldn't sarlah pla' ik mu-yor. I bek-tor till i reckoned au had prah wuh rom palikaya; yi i si' k' t'nash-veh gla-tor, heh went tor ar'kadan fi' ik lap-fek va'ashiv. Fa' au vesh' t'vath vla t' wuh pilash i vesh' s' wuh razh; ish-veh heh ish-veh marshak vesh' aishan wuh speck fi' wuh masu maf ska' yonder. I nem-tor wuh sa'haf t' corn yem heh nem-tor ish-veh tor wilat wuh canoe vesh' ip-sut, heh shoved wuh kas-elakh heh khlup k'wuhli heh shitau ish-veh svi'; yi i ovsoh wuh ka k' wuh vla t' bacon; yi wuh whisky-mashek. I nem-tor ek' wuh mon heh slor-tukh tra' vesh', heh ek' wuh ammunition; i nem-tor wuh wadding; i nem-tor wuh mashuk heh gourd; i nem-tor wuh dipper heh wuh zhai-tukh cup, heh t'nash-veh hinek gla-tor heh dahkuh yuk-sai, heh wuh skillet heh wuh mon-sunil. I nem-tor aluk-zehl heh matches heh vath thingseverything ik vesh' don wuh cent. I pu-tor si' wuh shi. I aitlu wuh la'ash, tonk'peh tra' wasn't sovek, goh wuh veh si' na' wuh woodpile, heh i knowed po i vesh' going tor trasha ik. I zaprah si' wuh pohshayek, heh i' i vesh' ovsoh. I had sai-vel-tor wuh solektra wuh rom deal crawling s' wuh razh heh dragging si' ni wehk vel. Ni i teslau ik u' rom u' i kupi s' wuh s'udish k' scattering grazhiv fi' wuh shi, if wein-tor abru wuh smoothness heh wuh sawdust. Yi i teslau wuh krus t' lap-fek pla' vi' its shi, heh shitau dahkuh kov ne' ish-veh heh veh tehnat ish-veh tor meskaraya ish-veh tra', na' ish-veh vesh' keh'sei abru na' ik shi heh didn't ved esta solektra. Kuv du lam-tor kehkuh il kaukuh ash'ya maf heh didn't fai-tor ish-veh vesh' sawed, du wouldn't worla beglanau ish-veh; heh isha, nash vesh' wuh pla' t' wuh thif'etek, heh ish-veh vikau't kesik anybody would hal-tor fooling pa' tra'. Ish-veh vesh' ek' yar pa'shik tor wuh canoe, ni i hadn't losrak wuh yut. I zahal-tor pa' tor gla-tor. I lam-tor fi' wuh kutra heh glazhau si' abru' wuh pilash. Ek' safe. Ni i nem-tor wuh pohshayek heh went abru wuh krus vi' wuh lapan, heh vesh' hunting pa' na' ein kushel lu gla-tor nash-veh wuh kwai pig; hogs ak went kwai svi' au bottoms po' au had prah maf s' wuh pseth-yar-eiktra uroshal. I pohshaya nash katravahsu heh nem-tor ish-veh vi' ith'du. I nem-tor wuh la'ash heh smashed svi' wuh svep. I kuhsh-tor ish-veh heh hacked ish-veh considerable wuh-doing ish-veh. I zaprah wuh pig svi', heh nem-tor ish-veh pla' nearly tor wuh pasu heh hacked vi' ish-veh drahk k' wuh la'ash, heh laid ish-veh ne' fi' wuh solektra tor khafau; i leralmin solektra fai'ei ish-veh vesh' groundhard sa'haf-tor, heh rai dohn. Muhl, thurai i nem-tor wuh hinek sa'haf heh shitau wuh lot t' suk' kov svi' itall i kupi dragand i palikau ish-veh s' wuh pig, heh zaseshau ish-veh tor wuh svep heh k'fai wuh lapan ne' tor wuh pilash heh dumped ish-veh svi', heh ne' ish-veh ne'hal-tor, s' glan. Du kupi hagik gla-tor ik vel had vesh' zaseshau abru' wuh solektra. I did istaya tom sawyer vesh' tra'; i knowed au would nem-tor wuh eku'ko svi' nash ves t' business, heh lehm svi' wuh fancy estuhl. Kling kupi sak-tor himself spo' tom sawyer svi' such wuh vel u' ik. Muhl, kim-shah i seshau si' ein t' t'nash-veh isachya, heh blooded wuh la'ash rom, heh terpau ish-veh fi' wuh pla' vla, heh slung wuh la'ash svi' wuh teruk. Yi i nem-tor abru wuh pig heh meskarau ish-veh tor t'nash-veh thasek k' t'nash-veh jacket (ni au couldn't thezh) till i prah wuh rom krus ne' wuh kelek heh yi dumped ish-veh vi' wuh pilash. I' i nahp t' vel else. Ni i went heh prah wuh sa'haf t' yem heh t'nash-veh hinek gla-tor s' wuh canoe, heh zaprah au tor wuh kelek. I nem-tor wuh sa'haf tor wilat ish-veh nam-tor-tor tor lamok, heh tres-tor wuh razh svi' wuh lanet t' ish-veh k' wuh gla-tor, na' tra' vikau't rai lipau heh snauk fi' wuh placepap ovsoh kanok-vei k' ish-veh clasp-lipau pa' wuh fasan. Yi i lesh wuh sa'haf pa' wuh hundred ker mes' wuh yar heh k'fai wuh willows she'rak t' wuh kelek, tor wuh gan suk'muzh ik vesh' kaukuh mile eik heh bosh t' rushesand ducks nuh', du lau leralmin, svi' wuh tevun-yonuk. Tra' vesh' wuh slough il wuh creek leading s' ish-veh fi' wuh vath vla ik went miles maf, i ri tor fai-tor wilat, tonk'peh ish-veh didn't hal-tor tor wuh pilash. Wuh yem sifted si' heh tor wuh pi' yut ek' wuh yut tor wuh suk'muzh. I eku-tor pap's whetstone tra' nuh', ni u' tor glazhau spo' ish-veh had vesh' ovsoh k' kisheya. Yi i tied abru wuh tres svi' wuh yem sa'haf k' wuh string, ni ish-veh wouldn't tasaya rai weht, heh nem-tor ish-veh heh t'nash-veh gla-tor tor wuh canoe va'ashiv. Ish-veh vesh' pa' gu'gelik i'; ni i eku-tor wuh canoe ne' wuh pilash ne' ein willows ik geldau abru' wuh kutra, heh bek-tor na' wuh aikum tor shen. I tor sahris tor wuh willow; yi i nem-tor wuh zeshaya tor yokul, heh k'-heh-k' laid ne' svi' wuh canoe tor vuzh wuh mev heh ti si' wuh dotor. I leralmin-tor tor myself, au'll zahal-tor wuh yut t' ik sackful t' kov tor wuh gef heh yi zaseshau wuh pilash na' me. Heh au'll zahal-tor ik yem yut tor wuh suk'muzh heh hal-tor browsing ne' wuh creek ik fulag-tor s' ish-veh tor talal wuh robbers ik pustau me heh nem-tor wuh vel. Au skil-tor't ek'wak shi'kar wuh pilash na' sovek-vel tonk'peh t'nash-veh tevik carcass. Au'll ak prah zungor t' ik, heh skil-tor't ertau rai weht pa' me. Ek' gas'rak; i mokuhlek pehkaya sovek-wilat i aitlun tor. Jackson's vikuvtra nam-tor rom hiyet na' me; i fai-tor ik vikuvtra takov muhl, heh kling ek'wak sarlah tra'. Heh yi i mokuhlek paddle abru' tor kahr mu-yor, heh slink pa' heh abrashau vel i aitlun. Jackson's vikuvtra's wuh shi. I vesh' takov zungor, heh wuh wuh'rak vel i knowed i vesh' asleep. Lu i woke abru i didn't fai-tor wilat i vesh' na' wuh minute. I eku abru heh glazhau pa', wuh pi' pahth-tor. Yi i vokau. Wuh pilash glazhau miles heh miles mes'. Wuh aikum vesh' ni ugelik i kupi wuh tum-tor wuh maraya lap-fek ik went wuh-slipping bi', nesh-kur heh fam dvun, hundreds t' ker si' s' gef. Kanok-vei vesh' tevik hizhuk, heh ish-veh glazhau tab-ma, heh smelt tab-ma. Du fai-tor ra i meani ri tor fai-tor wuh zhit tor shitau ish-veh svi'. I nem-tor wuh rom haf heh wuh sakadaya, heh vesh' aishan going tor unhitch heh palikaya lu i puzhu-tor wuh ralash maf abru' wuh masu. I shroi. Takov ak i tor ish-veh si'. Ish-veh vesh' ik pasik ves t' wuh regular ralash ik sarlah s' fel working svi' rowlocks lu ish-veh's wuh fam dvun mu-yor. I peeped si' k'fai wuh willow khlup, heh tra' ish-veh wasa skiff, maf mes' wuh masu. I couldn't var-tor uf wehk vesh' svi' ish-veh. Ish-veh potau wuh-coming, heh lu ish-veh vesh' abreast t' me gla-tor nash-veh tra' vikau't tonk'peh veh sasu svi' ish-veh. Nah-tor's i, sos'eh ish-veh's pap, hi i vikau't expecting ish-veh. Au eku-tor ne' me k' wuh current, heh k'-heh-k' sarlah ish-veh wuh-swinging abru gef svi' wuh hagik masu, heh au went k' ni ikap-tor i kupi wuh pulau si' wuh pohshayek heh estuhl ish-veh. Muhl, ish-veh vesh' pap, sure enoughand sober, nuh', k' wuh yut au laid ish-veh fel. I didn't pak-tor rai wak. Wuh thurai minute i vesh' wuh-spinning ne' pilash mos tonk'peh sahris svi' wuh duvek t' wuh kutra. I tor dahkuh mile heh wuh ulef, heh yi kwul-tor si' wuh yonuk t' wuh mile il weht na' wuh svitan t' wuh pilash, fai'ei takov ak i would nam-tor be' dvun-tor wuh mes-hali landing, heh sutra lau gla-tor me heh masu-kov me. I prah si' svi' wuh driftwood, heh yi laid ne' svi' wuh lanet t' wuh canoe heh kal-tor ish-veh marek. I laid tra', heh had wuh rom shom heh wuh vuzh s' t'nash-veh mev, looking maf vi' wuh igen; ri wuh wan svi' ish-veh. Wuh igen glazhau ek'wak ni glu lu du ti ne' fi' ish-veh pla' svi' wuh moonshine; i worla knowed ish-veh fa'. Heh uf irak wuh ak'shem mokuhlek zhu-tor fi' wuh masu such mu-yor! I puzhu-tor sutra talking na' wuh mes-hali landing. I puzhu-tor ra au leralmin-tor, tooevery zhit t' ish-veh. Veh sasu leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' getting na' wuh wu gad heh wuh pen mu-yor i'. T'vath veh leralmin-tor nash vikau't veh t' wuh pen ones, au reckonedand yi au abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor, heh au leralmin-tor ish-veh abru' va'ashiv, heh au abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor va'ashiv; yi au waked abru wuh'ashiv katravahsu heh var-tor ish-veh, heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor, tonk'peh au didn't abru'teruklar-ru'lut; au tres-tor si' vel brax, heh leralmin-tor kal-tor ish-veh sa'awek. Wuh wuh'rak katravahsu leralmin-tor au 'lowed tor var-tor ish-veh tor ish-veh hinek womanshe would nah-tor ish-veh vesh' takov rom; tonk'peh au leralmin-tor ik vikau't nothing tor ein vel au had leralmin-tor svi' ish-veh wak. I puzhu-tor veh sasu leralmin ish-veh vesh' nearly rehkuh o'wak-vel, heh au rok-tor gad-ha'khlup wouldn't bek-tor weht do pa' wuh wehk gad longer. Po' ik wuh variben prah further heh further maf, heh i couldn't tor si' wuh zhit sovek weht; tonk'peh i kupi zhu-tor wuh mumble, heh i' heh yi wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut, nuh', tonk'peh ish-veh seemed wuh wu yut ska'. I vesh' maf ne' wuh mes-hali i'. I she-tor abru, heh tra' vesh' jackson's vikuvtra, pa' dahkuh mile heh wuh ulef ne' pilash, ras timbered heh standing abru s' wuh svitan t' wuh pilash, suk' heh gu'gelik heh huhtik, spo' wuh steamboat rik' sovek ha'ge. Tra' vikau't sovek glat t' wuh mofek na' wuh headit vesh' ek' ne' masu i'. Ish-veh didn't nem-tor me wu tor prah tra'. I pohshaya vesht wuh patam na' wuh ripping tav, wuh current vesh' ni swift, heh yi i prah vi' wuh tevik masu heh landed fi' wuh vla na' wuh illinois gef. I sahr-tor wuh canoe vi' wuh glu tuhk svi' wuh kutra ik i knowed pa'; i had tor krus wuh willow khlup tor prah svi'; heh lu i tor sahris kling kupi wuh gla-tor wuh canoe s' wuh s'udish. I went abru heh eku ne' fi' wuh lap-fek na' wuh patam t' wuh vikuvtra, heh glazhau si' fi' wuh suk' pilash heh wuh nesh-kur driftwood heh maf abru' tor wuh kahr, rehkuh mile maf, wilat tra' vesh' rehkuh il kehkuh ha'ge twinkling.
