Wuh monstrous suk' lumber-marshak vesh' pa' wuh mile abru pilash, coming bi' ne', k' wuh makh-yonet svi' wuh svitan t' ish-veh. I glantau ish-veh sarlah creeping ne', heh lu ish-veh vesh' danik abreast t' wilat i lam-tor i puzhu-tor wuh sasu leralmin, "harr-krus fel, tra'! Heave ish-veh patam tor stabboard!" i puzhu-tor ik aishan u' eiktra u' kuv wuh sasu vesh' k' t'nash-veh vla. Tra' vesh' wuh pi' zhai-kur svi' wuh igen i'; ni i ash-tor vi' wuh lapan, heh laid ne' na' wuh nap fa' asal-yem. Chapter viii. Wuh yel vesh' abru ni pid lu i waked ik i judged ish-veh vesh' po' ohkuh o'wak-vel. I laid tra' svi' wuh yar heh wuh samuyau duvek thinking pa' vel, heh olaya shom-tor heh ruther kel'o heh satisfied. I kupi gla-tor wuh yel si' na' veh il dahkuh razh, tonk'peh mostly ish-veh vesh' suk' lap ek' pa', heh gloomy svi' tra' ekhlami. Tra' vesh' freckled shitau fi' wuh solektra wilat wuh ta'hal sifted ne' k'fai wuh mor, heh wuh freckled shitau swapped pa' wuh pi', showing tra' vesh' wuh pi' pi'salan abru tra'. Wuh couple t' squirrels eku fi' wuh sikrus heh jabbered na' me maut friendly. I vesh' powerful kas'el heh comfortabledidn't aitlun tor prah abru heh fas-tor asal-yem. Muhl, i vesh' dozing ska' va'ashiv lu i nah-tor i zhu-tor wuh glu ralash t' "ork!" maf abru wuh pilash. I kastorilau abru, heh shom-tor fi' t'nash-veh kar-nef heh shroi; takov ak i zhu-tor ish-veh va'ashiv. I spen-tor abru, heh went heh glazhau si' na' wuh razh svi' wuh mor, heh gla-tor nash-veh wuh bunch t' vuzh laying fi' wuh masu wuh wu yut upabout abreast wuh mes-hali. Heh tra' vesh' wuh mes-hali-masu-hali bosh t' sutra floating bi' ne'. I knowed ra vesh' wuh tukh i'. "ork!" gla-tor nash-veh wuh wan-kur vuzh squirt s' wuh mes-hali-masu-hali's vla. Gla-tor du, au vesh' firing thorshun abru' wuh masu, trying tor tor t'nash-veh carcass sarlah tor wuh fik. I vesh' takov k'avon, tonk'peh ish-veh vikau't going tor tor na' me tor palikaya wuh yon, fai'ei au lau gla-tor wuh vuzh. Ni i eku tra' heh glantau wuh thorshun-vuzh heh shroi tor wuh ork. Wuh pilash vesh' wuh mile eik tra', heh ish-veh kwon-hau-ov glazhau takov fi' wuh belaar morningso i vesh' having wuh rom hiyet wak seeing au shi'kar na' t'nash-veh hafayat kuv i goh had wuh zeshaya tor yokul. Muhl, yi i pavesh-tor tor nah-tor uf au kwon-hau-ov shitau quicksilver svi' loaves t' kap heh marek au ska', fai'ei au kwon-hau-ov hal-tor gas'rak tor wuh drownded carcass heh pehkaya tra'. Ni, leralmin-tor i, i'll potau wuh lookout, heh kuv sovek t' au's floating pa' po' me i'll mazhiv-kur-tor au wuh gluvaya. I rubai tor wuh illinois rihk t' wuh vikuvtra tor gla-tor ra kunli i kupi ma, heh i vikau't disappointed. Wuh suk' dahtau loaf sarlah bi', heh i danik prah ish-veh k' wuh wu terpau, tonk'peh t'nash-veh ash'ya trel-tor heh she markau si' further. Veling i vesh' wilat wuh current eku svi' wuh closest tor wuh shorei knowed hiyet na' ik. Tonk'peh k'-heh-k' bi' sarlah wuh'ashiv veh, heh nash wak i skil-tor. I nem-tor si' wuh plug heh hutau si' wuh pi' dab t' quicksilver, heh eku t'nash-veh zud svi'. Ish-veh vesh' "leipausu's kap"ra wuh quality yokul; rim t' ish-veh neik-ne' corn-pone. I prah wuh rom shi svi' wuh mor, heh eku tra' fi' wuh lap-fek, munching wuh kap heh watching wuh mes-hali-masu-hali, heh maut muhl satisfied. Heh yi vel kwul-tor me. I leralmin-tor, i' i reckon wuh kir'an il wuh parson il somebody prayed ik nash kap would talal me, heh la' ish-veh has hal-tor heh ovsoh ish-veh. Ni tra' ain't rai vet tonk'peh tra' nam-tor vel svi' ik thingthat nam-tor, tra''s vel svi' ish-veh lu wuh ak'shem spo' wuh kir'an il wuh parson prays, tonk'peh ish-veh ri tor ar'kadan na' me, heh i reckon ish-veh ri tor ar'kadan na' goh aishan wuh gas'rak ves. I lit wuh mev heh had wuh rom wu vuzh, heh went fi' watching. Wuh mes-hali-masu-hali vesh' floating k' wuh current, heh i kal-tor i'd ma wuh pavesh tor gla-tor vi vesh' aboard lu she sarlah bi', fai'ei she would sarlah svi' ikap-tor, wilat wuh kap did. Lu she'd prah takov muhl bi' ne' na' me, i shitau si' t'nash-veh mev heh went tor wilat i aluk-kum-tor si' wuh kap, heh laid ne' za' wuh lap-fek fi' wuh kutra svi' wuh pi' tu'ash shi. Wilat wuh lap-fek forked i kupi peep k'fai. K'-heh-k' she sarlah bi', heh she marau svi' ni ikap-tor ik au kupi wuh sahr-tor si' wuh plank heh lates-tor ashore. Danik kanok-veh vesh' fi' wuh masu-hali. Pap, heh judge thatcher, heh bessie thatcher, heh jo harper, heh tom sawyer, heh ish-veh hinek ezyet polly, heh sid heh mary, heh plenty weht. Kanok-veh vesh' talking pa' wuh riyeht-staya, tonk'peh wuh khart-lan shau svi' heh leralmin-tor: "glazhau nasik, i'; wuh current dvolau svi' wuh closest la', heh sos'eh au's pu-tor ashore heh prah tangled svi' wuh achut na' wuh masu's rihk. I rok ni, anyway." i didn't rok ni. Au ek' crowded abru heh gal-tor abru' wuh rails, nearly svi' t'nash-veh limuk, heh potau fam dvun, watching k' ek' ish-veh lau. Kupi gla-tor nash-veh au wuh'rak-tav, tonk'peh au couldn't gla-tor me. Yi wuh khart-lan uralau si': "lamok maf!" heh wuh thorshun kal-tor ska' such wuh thorshaya gas'rak fa' me ik ish-veh tor me deef k' wuh ralash heh takov be' glan-fam k' wuh vuzh, heh i judged i vesh' hal-tor. Kuv au'd wuh had ein bullets svi', i reckon au'd wuh prah wuh tevikeh au vesh' po'. Muhl, gla-tor nash-veh i vikau't dash-tor, itaren tor goodness. Wuh masu-hali markau fi' heh went s' glan pa' wuh tipan t' wuh vikuvtra. I kupi zhu-tor wuh booming i' heh yi, further heh further ska', heh k'-heh-k', po' wuh wadan, i didn't zhu-tor ish-veh rai weht. Wuh vikuvtra vesh' rehkuh mile wu. I judged au had prah tor wuh ash'ya, heh vesh' giving ish-veh abru. Tonk'peh au didn't wi wuh du'. Au da-tor pa' wuh ash'ya t' wuh vikuvtra heh palikau abru wuh mashyut fi' wuh missouri vla, ne' zhis, heh booming wuh'wak svi' wuh du' u' au went. I tuhsau abru' tor ik vla heh glantau au. Lu au prah abreast wuh patam t' wuh vikuvtra au quit shooting heh eku-tor abru' tor wuh missouri gef heh went ha-kel tor wuh kahr. I knowed i vesh' ek' gas'rak i'. Kling else would sarlah wuh-hunting po' me. I prah t'nash-veh pash-tor s' wuh canoe heh tor me wuh nice ith'du svi' wuh bali lapan. I tor wuh ves t' wuh ith'du s' t'nash-veh yuk-sai tor shitau t'nash-veh vel ne' ni wuh sov-masu couldn't prah na' au. I catched wuh catfish heh haggled ish-veh tu'ash k' t'nash-veh gla-tor, heh na' sundown i palikau t'nash-veh ith'du yon heh had mu'yor-yem. Yi i eku si' wuh zehl tor kum ein aluk na' asal-yem. Lu ish-veh vesh' gu'gelik i eku k' t'nash-veh ith'du yon smoking, heh olaya takov muhl satisfied; tonk'peh k'-heh-k' ish-veh prah wihfelau t' lonesome, heh ni i went heh eku fi' wuh kutra heh shroi tor wuh current swashing bi', heh tum-tor wuh yel heh maraya lap-fek heh marshak ik sarlah ne', heh yi went tor sar-tak; tra' ain't rai weh-rom yut tor shitau svi' wak lu du nam-tor lonesome; du mokuhlek't stay ni, du ak prah abru' ish-veh. Heh ni na' rehkuh gad heh mu-yor. Rai differencejust wuh ka vel. Tonk'peh wuh thurai gad i went exploring pa' ne' k'fai wuh vikuvtra. I vesh' feihan t' ish-veh; ish-veh ek' belonged tor me, ni tor leralmin, heh i aitlu tor fai-tor ek' pa' ish-veh; tonk'peh mainly i aitlu tor shitau svi' wuh wak. I afer-tor plenty strawberries, piyah heh nenat; heh yar-kur belaar grapes, heh yar-kur razberries; heh wuh yar-kur blackberries vesh' aishan palikaya tor gluvaya. Au would ek' sarlah handy k'-heh-k', i judged. Muhl, i went fooling bi' svi' wuh glu lapan till i judged i vikau't irak s' wuh ash'ya t' wuh vikuvtra. I had t'nash-veh pohshayek bi', tonk'peh i hadn't pohshaya nothing; ish-veh vesh' na' protection; nahp i would stau ein zhagra nigh ha-kel. Pa' nash wak i mighty be' ash-tor fi' wuh rom-sized oluhk, heh ish-veh went sliding ska' k'fai wuh yar heh svai, heh i po' ish-veh, trying tor prah wuh pohshaya na' ish-veh. I clipped bi', heh ek' t' wuh sudden i bounded gas'rak fi' tor wuh vitush t' wuh ith'du yon ik vesh' fam dvun smoking. T'nash-veh khaf-spol spen-tor abru svi' t'nash-veh esh-sa'haf. I worla bek-tor na' tor glazhau further, tonk'peh uncocked t'nash-veh pohshayek heh went sneaking pla' fi' t'nash-veh tiptoes u' sahris u' ek'wak i kupi. Kanok i' heh yi i pehkau wuh dahr svi' wuh bali mor heh shroi, tonk'peh t'nash-veh esh sarlah ni lerash i couldn't zhu-tor nothing else. I slunk bi' wuh'ashiv krus further, yi shroi va'ashiv; heh ni fi', heh ni fi'. Kuv gla-tor nash-veh wuh stump, i nem-tor ish-veh na' wuh sasu; kuv i sahr-tor fi' wuh terpau heh shau ish-veh, ish-veh tor me olau spo' wuh person had tresahk veh t' t'nash-veh esh svi' dahkuh heh i goh prah ulef, heh wuh pen ulef, nuh'. Lu i prah tor ith'du i vikau't olaya maut brash, tra' vikau't mau mazhiv svi' t'nash-veh craw; tonk'peh i leralmin-tor, nash ain't rai wak tor nam-tor fooling pa'. Ni i prah ek' t'nash-veh pash-tor vi' t'nash-veh canoe va'ashiv ni u' ki' au s' glan, heh i shitau si' wuh yon heh scattered wuh vitush pa' tor glazhau spo' wuh hinek kim-shah tevun's ith'du, heh yi clumb wuh lap. I reckon i vesh' abru svi' wuh lap dahkuh wadan; tonk'peh i didn't gla-tor nothing, i didn't zhu-tor nothingi goh nahp i puzhu-tor heh gla-tor u' mau u' wuh thousand vel. Muhl, i couldn't stay abru tra' ek'wak; ni na' kim-shah i prah ne', tonk'peh i potau svi' wuh bali lapan heh fi' wuh lookout ek' wuh wak. Ek' i kupi prah tor yokul vesh' nei-savas heh ra vesh' losrak abru' s' asal-yem. K' wuh wak ish-veh vesh' mu-yor i vesh' takov k'avon. Ni lu ish-veh vesh' rom heh gu'gelik i slid si' s' gef fa' moonrise heh paddled abru' tor wuh illinois bankabout wuh yonuk t' wuh mile. I went si' svi' wuh lapan heh pufas-tor wuh mu'yor-yem, heh i had pa' tor abru t'nash-veh kashek i would stay tra' ek' mu-yor lu i zhu-tor wuh plunkety-plunk, plunkety-plunk, heh leralmin-tor tor myself, jarel coming; heh thurai i zhu-tor sutra's spes. I prah kanok-vei vi' wuh canoe u' sahris u' i kupi, heh yi went creeping k'fai wuh lapan tor gla-tor ra i kupi talal si'. I hadn't prah irak lu i zhu-tor wuh sasu leralmin: "etek weh-rom ith'du la' kuv etek mokuhlek talal wuh rom shi; wuh jarel nam-tor pa' kuhsh-tor si'. Kal-tor's glazhau pa'." i didn't bek-tor, tonk'peh shoved si' heh paddled maf hagik. I tied abru svi' wuh hinek shi, heh reckoned i would yuk svi' wuh canoe. I didn't yuk mau. I couldn't, somehow, na' thinking. Heh kanok wak i waked abru i nahp somebody had me k' wuh talu. Ni wuh yuk didn't tor me rai rom. K'-heh-k' i leralmin-tor tor myself, i mokuhlek't ha-tor nash yut; i'm wuh-going tor talal si' vi ish-veh nam-tor ik's la' fi' wuh vikuvtra k' me; i'll talal ish-veh si' il bust. Muhl, i olau weh-rom gas'rak ska'. Ni i nem-tor t'nash-veh paddle heh slid si' s' gef aishan wuh ash il dahkuh, heh yi kal-tor wuh canoe eku bi' ne' svi' wuh duv. Wuh aikum vesh' shining, heh si' wuh duv ish-veh tor ish-veh danik u' ta'hal u' gad. I poked bi' muhl fi' tor wuh wadan, kanok-vei fam dvun u' kov heh ralash asleep. Muhl, k' nash wak i vesh' danik ne' tor wuh ash'ya t' wuh vikuvtra. Wuh pi' ripply, samuyau pi'salan palikau tor salur, heh ik vesh' u' rom u' taran wuh mu-yor vesh' pa' ovsoh. I mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh da-tor k' wuh paddle heh brung ish-veh han tor gef; yi i prah t'nash-veh pohshayek heh trel-tor si' heh vi' wuh rihk t' wuh lapan. I hayal-tor ne' tra' fi' wuh lap-fek, heh glazhau si' k'fai wuh mor. Gla-tor nash-veh wuh aikum hal-tor ska' glantau, heh wuh mu'khlup'es palikau tor yuk-sai wuh pilash. Tonk'peh svi' wuh pi' du' gla-tor nash-veh wuh spoh wesh abru' wuh treetops, heh knowed wuh gad vesh' coming. Ni i nem-tor t'nash-veh pohshayek heh trel-tor ska' na' wilat i had sahr-tor mes' ik ith'du yon, stopping kanok minute il dahkuh tor shroi. Tonk'peh i hadn't rai kunli somehow; i couldn't seem tor talal wuh shi. Tonk'peh k'-heh-k', sure hiyet, i catched wuh glimpse t' yon maf k'fai wuh lap. I went na' ish-veh, cautious heh vohris. K'-heh-k' i vesh' ikap-tor hiyet ki' wuh glazhau, heh tra' laid wuh sasu fi' wuh solektra. Ish-veh danik mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh sovek-tods. Au had wuh yuk-sai pa' ish-veh patam, heh ish-veh patam vesh' nearly svi' wuh yon. I eku tra' za' wuh clump t' bushes, svi' pa' shehkuh ash'ya t' ish-veh, heh potau t'nash-veh bezhun fi' ish-veh br'xan. Ish-veh vesh' getting zhai-kur gad-ha'khlup i'. Takov ak au gapped heh sakadau himself heh hove ska' wuh yuk-sai, heh ish-veh vesh' din-tor watson's jim! I sihaya i vesh' glad tor gla-tor ish-veh. I leralmin-tor: "tonk'peh, jim!" heh skipped si'. Au rukau abru heh nantau na' me kwai. Yi au eku-tor ne' fi' ish-veh mal-nef, heh shitau ish-veh el'ru teretuhr heh leralmin-tor: "doan' dash-tor medon't! I hain't ek'wak ovsoh rai klau tor wuh ghos'. I alwuz tishau tevik sutra, en ovsoh ek' i kupi na' 'em. Du hal-tor en git svi' de pilash agin, whah du b'longs, en doan' tor nuffn tor ole jim, 'na' 'uz awluz yo' fren'." muhl, i vikau't wu tor ish-veh ken-tor i vikau't tevik. I vesh' ek'wak ni glad tor gla-tor jim. I vikau't lonesome i'. I var-tor ish-veh i vikau't kwes t' ish-veh telling wuh sutra wilat i vesh'. I variben bi', tonk'peh au goh eku tra' heh glazhau na' me; worla leralmin-tor nothing. Yi i leralmin-tor: "ish-veh's rom gad-ha'khlup. Le's prah asal-yem. Tor abru ish-veh ith'du yon rom." "ra's de nam-tor-tor er makin' abru de ith'du yon tor fas-tor strawbries en sich truck? Tonk'peh du prah wuh pohshayek, hain't du? Den etek pi-maat git sumfn weh-rom den strawbries." "strawberries heh such truck, " i leralmin-tor. "nam-tor ik ra du ha-tor fi'?" "i couldn' git nuffn else, " au leralmin-tor. "po, uf wu du vesh' fi' wuh vikuvtra, jim?" "sarlah nash-veh heah de mu-yor arter du's pustau." "ra, ek' ik wak?" "yesindeedy." "heh ain't du had nothing tonk'peh ik ves t' rubbage tor yokul?" "rai, sahnuffn else." "muhl, du bolau nam-tor danik starved, ain't du?" "i reck'n i kupi yokul wuh hoss. I nah-tor i kupi. Uf wu du ben fi' de islan'?" "opi' wuh mu-yor i prah pustau." "rai! W'y, ra has du ha-tor fi'? Tonk'peh du prah wuh pohshayek. Oh, ha, du prah wuh pohshayek. Dat's rom. I' du stau sumfn en i'll tor abru de yon." ni etek went abru' tor wilat wuh canoe vesh', heh du' au torvau wuh yon svi' wuh grassy tu'ash shi svi' wuh lap, i zaprah yem heh bacon heh mon, heh mon-sunil heh frying-sunil, heh slor-tukh heh zhai-tukh cups, heh wuh nigger vesh' eku pla' considerable, fai'ei au reckoned ish-veh vesh' ek' ovsoh k' witchcraft. I catched wuh rom suk' catfish, nuh', heh jim pu-tor ish-veh k' ish-veh lipau, heh pupol-tor ish-veh. Lu asal-yem vesh' pok etek lolled fi' wuh yar heh yokul ish-veh smoking fal. Jim laid ish-veh svi' k' ek' ish-veh lau, na' au vesh' danik pa' starved. Yi lu etek had prah takov muhl tukh-tor, etek laid ska' heh lazied. K'-heh-k' jim leralmin-tor: "tonk'peh looky la', huck, vi wuz ish-veh dat 'uz pustau svi' dat shanty ef ish-veh vikau't du?" yi i var-tor ish-veh wuh bosh vel, heh au leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' klon. Au leralmin-tor tom sawyer couldn't prah abru rai weh-rom dotor do ra i had. Yi i leralmin-tor: "uf tor sarlah du tor nam-tor la', jim, heh uf'd du prah la'?" au glazhau takov uneasy, heh didn't leralmin nothing na' wuh minute. Yi au leralmin-tor: "sos'eh i weh-rom ri var-tor." "po, jim?" "muhl, dey's utvau. Tonk'peh du wouldn' var-tor fi' me ef i uz tor var-tor du, would du, huck?" "tenah kuv i would, jim." "muhl, i b'lieve du, huck. Ii sahr-tor ska'." "jim!" "tonk'peh kashek, du leralmin-tor du wouldn' tellyou fai-tor du leralmin-tor du wouldn' var-tor, huck." "muhl, i did. I leralmin-tor i wouldn't, heh i'll terpau tor ish-veh. Trau injun, i dungi. Sutra would vutau me wuh neik-ne' abolitionist heh despise me na' keeping mumbut ik ri tor tor rai natyan. I ain't wuh-going tor var-tor, heh i ain't wuh-going pla' tra', anyways. Ni, i', le's fai-tor ek' pa' ish-veh." "muhl, gla-tor du, ish-veh 'uz dis yut. Ole missusdat's din-tor watsonshe pecks fi' me ek' de wak, en skasau me pooty rough, tonk'peh she awluz leralmin-tor she wouldn' makau me ne' tor orleans. Tonk'peh i pubeglanau dey wuz wuh nigger trader roun' de shi considable lately, en i palikau tor git oneasy. Muhl, veh mu-yor i creeps tor de tor' pooty tab-ma, en de tor' vikau't ved shet, en i zhu-tor hinek missus var-tor de widder she gwyne tor makau me ne' tor orleans, tonk'peh she didn' aitlun tor, tonk'peh she kupi git ohkuh hund'd dollars na' me, en ish-veh 'uz sich wuh suk' tuh o' donku she couldn' resis'. De widder she ar'kadan tor git ish-veh tor leralmin she wouldn' tor ish-veh, tonk'peh i worla bek-tor tor zhu-tor de res'. I lit si' mighty sahris, i var-tor du. "i k'hy si' en ne-mal ne' de kunel, en 'spec tor vazgau wuh skift 'wu de sho' som'ers 'bove de kahr, tonk'peh dey wuz sutra wuh-stirring yit, ni i ip-sut svi' de ole tumble-ne' cooper-mahr-kel fi' de kutra tor bek-tor na' kanok-veh tor hal-tor 'yut. Muhl, i wuz dah ek' mu-yor. Dey wuz somebody roun' ek' de wak. 'wu 'bout shehkuh svi' de mawnin' skifts palikau tor hal-tor k', en 'bout ohkuh er naukuh kanok skift dat went 'wu wuz talkin' 'bout uf yo' pap sarlah abru' tor de kahr en leralmin du's pustau. Dese las' skifts wuz bosh o' t'sai en genlmen wuh-goin' abru' na' tor gla-tor de shi. Sometimes dey'd seshaya abru na' de sho' en nem-tor wuh res' b'fo' dey palikau acrost, ni k' de variben i prah tor fai-tor ek' 'bout de killin'. I 'uz powerful sorry du's pustau, huck, tonk'peh i ain't rai mo' i'. "i laid dah ne' de shavin's ek' gad. I 'uz k'avon, tonk'peh i vikau't afeard; bekase i knowed ole missus en de widder wuz goin' tor palikaya tor de ith'du-ragel-tor'n' gas'rak arter breakfas' en nam-tor hal-tor ek' gad, en dey fai-tor i hal-tor ska' wid de cattle 'bout gad-ha'khlup, ni dey wouldn' 'spec tor gla-tor me roun' de shi, en ni dey wouldn' din-tor me var-tor arter gu'gelik svi' de evenin'. De yuther dvinsu wouldn' din-tor me, kase dey'd ne-mal si' en nem-tor holiday ak u' de ole sular-ves 'uz si''n de yut. "muhl, lu ish-veh sarlah gu'gelik i k'hy si' abru de pilash fau-yut, en went 'bout dahkuh mile er weht tor whah dey vikau't rai kelek. I'd tor abru t'nash-veh t'nash-veh 'bout ra i's agwyne tor tor. Gla-tor du, ef i kep' fi' tryin' tor git maf aisha, de dogs 'ud yut me; ef i vazgau wuh skift tor tuhs abru', dey'd din-tor dat skift, gla-tor du, en dey'd fai-tor 'bout whah i'd lan' fi' de yuther vla, en whah tor abrashau t'nash-veh yut. Ni i leralmin-tor, wuh raff nam-tor ra i's arter; ish-veh doan' tor rai yut. "gla-tor nash-veh wuh ta'hal wuh-comin' roun' de p'int bymeby, ni i masu-tor' svi' en shove' wuh lap-fek ahead o' me en mahal-tor weht'n ulef yut acrost de pilash, en prah svi' 'mongst de maraya-lapan, en kep' t'nash-veh patam ne' neik, en kinder mahal-tor agin de current var-tor de raff sarlah bi'. Den i mahal-tor tor de harr-krus uv ish-veh en k'hy wuh-holt. Ish-veh clouded abru en 'uz pooty gu'gelik na' wuh pi' du'. Ni i clumb abru en laid ne' fi' de planks. De sasu 'uz ek' 'yut yonder svi' de svitan, whah de makh-yonet wuz. De pilash wuz wuh-risin', en dey wuz wuh rom current; ni i reck'n'd 'na' k' fo' svi' de mawnin' i'd nam-tor dah-leh-kaukuh mile ne' de pilash, en den i'd trel svi' jis b'fo' gad-ha'khlup en mahal-tor asho', en nem-tor tor de lapan fi' de illinois vla. "tonk'peh i didn' ma rai kunli. Lu etek 'uz mos' ne' tor de patam er de islan' wuh sasu palikau tor sarlah aft wid de makh-yonet, gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh vikau't rai nam-tor-tor fer tor bek-tor, ni i slid overboard en kwul-tor si' fer de islan'. Muhl, i had wuh notion i kupi lan' mos' anywhers, tonk'peh i couldn'tbank nuh' bluff. I 'uz mos' tor de ash'ya er de islan' b'fo' i afer-tor' wuh rom shi. I went vi' de lapan en jedged i wouldn' duhsu wid raffs rai mo', wu u' dey dvun de makh-yonet roun' ni. I had t'nash-veh mev en wuh plug er dog-mal, en ein matches svi' t'nash-veh taik, en dey vikau't masupik, ni i 'uz ek' gas'rak." "heh ni du ain't had rai kahm il kap tor yokul ek' nash wak? Po didn't du prah vral-turkles?" "uf du gwyne tor git 'm? Du mokuhlek't trel abru fi' um en runem um; en uf's wuh ak'shem gwyne tor kwul um wid wuh kov? Uf kupi wuh ak'shem tor ish-veh svi' de mu-yor? En i vikau't gwyne tor gluvaya mysef fi' de kutra svi' de gad-wakik." "muhl, ik's ni. Du've had tor potau svi' wuh lapan ek' wuh wak, t' rivak. Did du zhu-tor 'em shooting wuh thorshun?" "oh, ha. I knowed dey vesh' arter du. Gla-tor nash-veh um hal-tor k' heahwatched um thoo de bushes." ein nu'ri kushel sarlah bi', hashan wuh ker il dahkuh na' wuh wak heh ha'gelan. Jim leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh glat ish-veh vesh' going tor sov-masu. Au leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh glat lu nu'ri kahm flew ik yut, heh ni au reckoned ish-veh vesh' wuh ka yut lu nu'ri kushel ovsoh ish-veh. I vesh' going tor kum ein t' au, tonk'peh jim wouldn't kal-tor me. Au leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' tevakh. Au leralmin-tor ish-veh sa-mekh laid mighty has-bosh wuh'wak, heh ein t' au catched wuh kushel, heh ish-veh hinek granny leralmin-tor ish-veh sa-mekh would tev-tor, heh au did. Heh jim leralmin-tor du mustn't tum-tor wuh vel du nam-tor going tor fas-tor na' aru-yem, fai'ei ik would katau rasahkos kunli. Wuh ka kuv du hutau wuh pasu-sai po' sundown. Heh au leralmin-tor kuv wuh sasu puma wuh beehive heh ik sasu tev-tor, wuh bees bolau nam-tor var-tor pa' ish-veh fa' yel-abru thurai asal, il else wuh bees would ek' kobatau ne' heh quit ar'kadan heh tev-tor. Jim leralmin-tor bees wouldn't rakus idiots; tonk'peh i didn't dva-tor ik, fai'ei i had ar'kada au lots t' wak myself, heh au wouldn't rakus me. I had puzhu-tor pa' ein t' aifa vel fa', tonk'peh ri ek' t' au. Jim knowed ek' ves t' glat. Au leralmin-tor au knowed danik kanok-vei. I leralmin-tor ish-veh glazhau tor me spo' ek' wuh glat vesh' pa' rasahkos kunli, heh ni i ya'akash ish-veh kuv tra' vikau't sovek rom-kunli glat. Au leralmin-tor: "mighty fewan' dey ain't rai nam-tor-tor tor wuh ak'shem. Ra du aitlun tor fai-tor lu rom kunli's wuh-comin' na'? Aitlun tor potau ish-veh ska'?" heh au leralmin-tor: "ef du's prah hairy kar en wuh hairy breas', ish-veh's wuh glat dat du's agwyne tor nam-tor don-ka. Muhl, dey's ein nam-tor-tor svi' wuh glat spo' dat, 'kase ish-veh's ni ausachya ahead. Gla-tor du, sos'eh du's prah tor nam-tor po' wuh akarshif fust, en ni du lau git discourage' en stau yo'sef 'f du didn' fai-tor k' de glat dat du gwyne tor nam-tor don-ka bymeby." "ma du prah hairy kar heh wuh hairy thasek, jim?" "ra's de nam-tor-tor tor la'ash dat deshker? Ri tor gla-tor du i has?" "muhl, nam-tor du don-ka?" "rai, tonk'peh i ben don-ka wunst, heh gwyne tor nam-tor don-ka agin. Wunst i had foteen dollars, tonk'peh i k'hy tor specalat'n', en prah busted si'." "ra did du speculate svi', jim?" "muhl, fust i tackled fek." "ra ves t' fek?" "po, ha-tor stockcattle, du fai-tor. I shitau lehkuh dollars svi' wuh aushfa. Tonk'peh i ain' gwyne tor resk rai mo' donku svi' fek. De aushfa abru 'n' tev-tor fi' t'nash-veh han's." "ni du pakik wuh lehkuh dollars." "rai, i didn't pak-tor ish-veh ek'. I fi''y los' 'bout naukuh t' ish-veh. I lad de ip-sut en taller na' wuh dollar en lehkuh cents." "du had kaukuh dollars heh lehkuh cents losrak. Did du speculate sovek weht?" "ha. Du fai-tor ish-veh-laigged nigger dat b'longs tor hinek misto bradish? Muhl, au sot abru wuh kutra, en leralmin anybody dat shitau svi' wuh dollar would git fo' dollars mo' na' de en' er de tevun. Muhl, ek' de niggers went svi', tonk'peh dey didn't ma mau. I wuz de fi''y veh dat had mau. Ni i terpau si' na' mo' dan fo' dollars, en i leralmin-tor 'f i didn' git ish-veh i'd palikaya wuh kutra mysef. Muhl, o' rivak dat nigger aitlun' tor potau me si' er de business, bekase au leralmin-tor dey vikau't business 'nough na' dahkuh kutra, ni au leralmin i kupi shitau svi' t'nash-veh kaukuh dollars en au vlitau me reh-leh-kaukuh na' de en' er de tevun. "ni i ovsoh ish-veh. Den i reck'n'd i'd inves' de reh-leh-kaukuh dollars gas'rak ska' en potau vel wuh-movin'. Dey wuz wuh nigger ahm' bob, dat had ketched wuh lapan-pa'ash, en ish-veh marster didn' fai-tor ish-veh; en i bought ish-veh ska''n ish-veh en var-tor ish-veh tor nem-tor de reh-leh-kaukuh dollars lu de en' er de tevun sarlah; tonk'peh somebody vazgau de lapan-pa'ash dat mu-yor, en nex gad de veh-laigged nigger leralmin de kutra's busted. Ni dey didn' rim uv etek git rai donku." "ra did du tor k' wuh lehkuh cents, jim?" "muhl, i 'uz gwyne tor spen' ish-veh, tonk'peh i had wuh sahr-tor, en de sahr-tor tole me tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor wuh nigger ahm' balumbalum's ass dey vutau ish-veh na' pen; au's veh er dem chuckleheads, du fai-tor. Tonk'peh au's kunli, dey leralmin, en i gla-tor i vikau't kunli. De sahr-tor leralmin kal-tor balum inves' de lehkuh cents en au'd tor wuh ashenau na' me. Muhl, balum au k'hy de donku, en lu au wuz svi' church au zhu-tor de preacher leralmin dat whoever mazhiv-kur-tor tor de po' len' tor de s'haile, en boun' tor git ish-veh donku pla' wuh hund'd wak. Ni balum au k'hy en mazhiv-kur-tor de lehkuh cents tor de po', en laid neik tor gla-tor ra wuz gwyne tor sarlah t' ish-veh." "muhl, ra did sarlah t' ish-veh, jim?" "nuffn worla sarlah t' ish-veh. I couldn' khartau tor k'leck dat donku rai yut; en balum au couldn'. I ain' gwyne tor len' rai mo' donku 'dout gla-tor nash-veh de shar'es. Boun' tor git yo' donku pla' wuh hund'd wak, de preacher leralmin-tor! Ef i kupi git de lehkuh cents pla', i'd vutau ish-veh squah, en nam-tor glad er de chanst." "muhl, ish-veh's ek' gas'rak anyway, jim, wu u' du're going tor nam-tor don-ka va'ashiv ein wak il vath." "ha; en i's don-ka i', sarlah tor glazhau na' ish-veh. I ma mysef, en i's wuth ohkuh hund'd dollars. I wisht i had de donku, i wouldn' aitlun rai mo'." chapter ix. I aitlu tor hal-tor heh glazhau na' wuh shi gas'rak pa' wuh svitan t' wuh vikuvtra ik i'd afer-tor lu i vesh' exploring; ni etek palikau heh ak prah tor ish-veh, fai'ei wuh vikuvtra vesh' goh rehkuh miles wu heh wuh yonuk t' wuh mile eik. Nash shi vesh' wuh tolerable wu, menal kunel il tauf pa' keh-leh ash'ya pid. Etek had wuh rough wak getting tor wuh fik, wuh vla vesh' ni menal heh wuh bushes ni bali. Etek tramped heh clumb pa' ek' abru' ish-veh, heh k'-heh-k' afer-tor wuh rom suk' suk-tauk svi' wuh kov, danik abru tor wuh fik fi' wuh vla na' illinois. Wuh suk-tauk vesh' u' suk' u' dahkuh il rehkuh tvi-shal bunched teretuhr, heh jim kupi lamok abru zehik svi' ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' samuyau svi' tra'. Jim vesh' na' putting etwel pash-tor svi' tra' gas'rak maf, tonk'peh i leralmin-tor etek didn't aitlun tor nam-tor climbing abru heh ne' tra' ek' wuh wak. Jim leralmin-tor kuv etek had wuh canoe ip-sut svi' wuh rom shi, heh had ek' wuh pash-tor svi' wuh suk-tauk, etek kupi rush tra' kuv anybody vesh' tor sarlah tor wuh vikuvtra, heh au would worla talal etek rik' dogs. Heh, isha, au leralmin-tor au pi' kushel had leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' going tor sov-masu, heh did i aitlun wuh vel tor prah masupik? Ni etek went pla' heh prah wuh canoe, heh paddled abru abreast wuh suk-tauk, heh lugged ek' wuh pash-tor abru tra'. Yi etek shi'kar abru wuh shi beyik tor ip-sut wuh canoe svi', svi' wuh bali willows. Etek nem-tor ein aluk ska' t' wuh zehl heh eku au va'ashiv, heh palikau tor prah pok na' aru-yem. Wuh svep t' wuh suk-tauk vesh' suk' hiyet tor padukau wuh hogshead svi', heh fi' veh vla t' wuh svep wuh lan-tol terpau si' wuh pi' zeshau, heh vesh' pa'ash heh wuh rom shi tor torvau wuh yon fi'. Ni etek torvau ish-veh tra' heh pufas-tor aru-yem. Etek sak-tor wuh yuk-sai svi'udish na' wuh la'y, heh yokul etwel aru-yem svi' tra'. Etek shitau ek' wuh vath vel handy na' wuh pla' t' wuh suk-tauk. Takov ak ish-veh mu'glau abru, heh palikau tor rahm heh lighten; ni wuh kushel vesh' gas'rak pa' ish-veh. Directly ish-veh palikau tor sov-masu, heh ish-veh sov-mashau spo' ek' fury, nuh', heh i worla gla-tor wuh salan salur ni. Ish-veh vesh' veh t' aifa regular belaar sahriv. Ish-veh would prah ni gu'gelik ik ish-veh glazhau ek' pla-kur-nesh-kur s'udish, heh lovely; heh wuh sov-masu would thrash bi' k' ni bali ik wuh lap ska' wuh pi' yut glazhau neik-ha'khlup heh a'lazb-webby; heh la' would sarlah wuh thorshaya t' salan ik would vulaya wuh lap ne' heh da-tor abru wuh spoh underside t' wuh mor; heh yi wuh buhfik ripper t' wuh gust would zahal-tor bi' heh eku wuh khlup tor tossing ish-veh kar u' kuv au vesh' aishan kwai; heh thurai, lu ish-veh vesh' aishan pa' wuh bluest heh blackestfst! Ish-veh vesh' u' ugelik u' glory, heh du'd ma wuh pi' glimpse t' lap-fik wuh-taul-tor pa' maf ska' yonder svi' wuh sahriv, hundreds t' ker further do du kupi gla-tor fa'; gu'gelik u' sin va'ashiv svi' wuh dahr, heh i' du'd zhu-tor wuh rahm kal-tor hal-tor k' wuh awful tevul, heh yi hal-tor rumbling, grumbling, tumbling, ne' wuh igen na' wuh ne' vla t' wuh panu, spo' rolling herbosh subok ne' stairswhere ish-veh's wu kaiden heh au rukaya wuh rom deal, du fai-tor. "jim, nash nam-tor nice, " i leralmin-tor. "i wouldn't aitlun tor nam-tor nowhere else tonk'peh la'. Be' dvun me bi' wuh'ashiv hunk t' aluk heh ein fal corn-kap." "muhl, du wouldn't wuh ben la' 'f ish-veh hadn't wuh ben na' jim. Du'd wuh ben ne' dah svi' de lapan widout sovek aru-yem, en gittn' mos' drownded, nuh'; dat du would, honey. Kahm fai-tor lu ish-veh's gwyne tor sov-masu, en ni tor de kushel, chile." wuh pilash went fi' raising heh raising na' lehkuh il leh-dah gad, till na' kim-shah ish-veh vesh' abru' wuh kutra. Wuh masu vesh' rehkuh il kehkuh ash'ya glu fi' wuh vikuvtra svi' wuh neik shitau heh fi' wuh illinois lanet. Fi' ik vla ish-veh vesh' wuh rom wehk miles eik, tonk'peh fi' wuh missouri vla ish-veh vesh' wuh ka hinek ir acrossa ulef wuh milebecause wuh missouri gef vesh' aishan wuh temok t' pid bluffs. Daytimes etek paddled ek' abru' wuh vikuvtra svi' wuh canoe, ish-veh vesh' mighty samuyau heh shady svi' wuh glu lapan, kauk kuv wuh yel vesh' blazing s'udish. Etek went kuvoran svi' heh si' svi' wuh lap, heh sometimes wuh kas-elakh geldau ni bali etek had tor pla' maf heh hal-tor ein vath yut. Muhl, fi' kanok hinek pushau-ne' lap du kupi gla-tor rabbits heh oluhk heh such vel; heh lu wuh vikuvtra had vesh' overflowed wuh gad il dahkuh au prah ni fnau, fi' khrosahp t' hasu k'avon, ik du kupi paddle gas'rak abru heh shitau ish-veh el'ru fi' au kuv du aitlu tor; tonk'peh ri wuh oluhk heh turtlesthey would zish-tor ska' svi' wuh masu. Wuh tauf etwel suk-tauk vesh' svi' vesh' bosh t' au. Etek kupi wuh had kelek-aushfa hiyet kuv etek'd aitlu au. Veh mu-yor etek catched wuh pi' krus t' wuh lumber raftnice pine planks. Ish-veh vesh' leh-dah ash'ya eik heh pa' leh-kau il leh-sheh ash'ya wu, heh wuh fik lam-tor abru' masu shehkuh il stehkuh inchesa huhtik, volik lan-tol. Etek kupi gla-tor gla-tor-lap-fek hal-tor k' svi' wuh gad-ha'khlup sometimes, tonk'peh etek kal-tor au hal-tor; etek didn't gluvaya ourselves svi' gad-ha'khlup. Wuh'ashiv mu-yor lu etek vesh' abru na' wuh patam t' wuh vikuvtra, aishan fa' gad-ha'khlup, la' sarlah wuh nentu-kelek ne', fi' wuh tev'rak vla. She vesh' wuh dahkuh-var, heh ayau abru' considerable. Etek paddled si' heh prah aboardclumb svi' na' wuh upstairs krani. Tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' nuh' gu'gelik tor gla-tor wi, ni etek tor wuh canoe sahris heh eku svi' ish-veh tor bek-tor na' gad-ha'khlup. Wuh ta'hal palikau tor sarlah fa' etek prah tor wuh ash'ya t' wuh vikuvtra. Yi etek glazhau svi' na' wuh krani. Etek kupi tor si' wuh sar-tak, heh wuh pasu, heh dahkuh hinek ku-san, heh lots t' vel pa' pa' fi' wuh lan-tol, heh tra' vesh' sai-vel hanging tehnat wuh temok. Tra' vesh' vel laying fi' wuh lan-tol svi' wuh irak teruk ik glazhau spo' wuh sasu. Ni jim leralmin-tor: "tonk'peh, du!" tonk'peh ish-veh didn't budge. Ni i hollered va'ashiv, heh yi jim leralmin-tor: "de sasu ain't asleephe's tevik. Du meskaraya stilli'll hal-tor en gla-tor." au went, heh keh'sei ne' heh glazhau, heh leralmin-tor: "ish-veh's wuh tevik sasu. Ha, indeedy; sai-fam, nuh'. Au's ben pohshaya svi' de pla'. I reck'n au's ben tevik dahkuh er rehkuh gad. Sarlah svi', huck, tonk'peh doan' glazhau na' ish-veh faceit's nuh' gashly." i didn't glazhau na' ish-veh na' ek'. Jim throwed ein hinek a'cit abru' ish-veh, tonk'peh au needn't ovsoh ish-veh; i didn't aitlun tor gla-tor ish-veh. Tra' vesh' heaps t' hinek greasy nop scattered pa' abru' wuh lan-tol, heh hinek whisky mashek, heh wuh couple t' limein tor s' nesh-kur sai; heh ek' abru' wuh temok vesh' wuh ignorantest ves t' zhit heh bikuv tor k' yonol-tukh. Tra' vesh' dahkuh hinek kitork calico sai-vel, heh wuh yel-bonnet, heh ein kosu's underclothes hanging tehnat wuh temok, heh ein sasu's sai-vel, nuh'. Etek shitau wuh lot vi' wuh canoeit lau sarlah rom. Tra' vesh' wuh sa-kan's hinek speckled terp taik fi' wuh lan-tol; i nem-tor ik, nuh'. Heh tra' vesh' wuh mashek ik had had thas svi' ish-veh, heh ish-veh had wuh a'cit stopper na' wuh kan-bu tor suck. Etek would wuh nem-tor wuh mashek, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' shau. Tra' vesh' wuh seedy hinek tuf, heh wuh hinek isachya lap-fek k' wuh tu'adayek shau. Au lam-tor tu'ash, tonk'peh tra' vikau't nothing losrak svi' au ik vesh' sovek khrosahp. Wuh yut vel vesh' scattered pa' etek reckoned wuh sutra losrak svi' wuh brax, heh vikau't teslau ni u' tor lesh ska' danik t' ish-veh tukh. Etek prah wuh hinek zhai-tukh makh-yonet, heh wuh butcher-lipau rik' sovek el'rek, heh wuh bran-uzh barlow lipau don dahkuh bits svi' sovek mahr-kel, heh wuh lot t' tallow ha'fek, heh wuh zhai-tukh ha'fek, heh wuh gourd, heh wuh zhai-tukh cup, heh wuh ratty hinek bedquilt ska' wuh sar-tak, heh wuh reticule k' og-lum heh pins heh beeswax heh gonaf heh og-elakh heh ek' such truck svi' ish-veh, heh wuh hatchet heh ein felu, heh wuh fishline u' bali u' t'nash-veh wuhr-ozh k' ein monstrous kik fi' ish-veh, heh wuh padukau t' buckskin, heh wuh duf dog-hmoi'neks, heh wuh horseshoe, heh ein vials t' haseret ik didn't ma rai label fi' au; heh aishan u' etek vesh' leaving i afer-tor wuh tolerable rom curry-dref, heh jim au afer-tor wuh ratty hinek fiddle-kes-wun, heh wuh wooden mal. Wuh zhel vesh' shau ska' t' ish-veh, tonk'peh, barring ik, ish-veh vesh' wuh rom hiyet mal, hi ish-veh vesh' nuh' wu na' me heh ri wu hiyet na' jim, heh etek couldn't talal wuh vath veh, hi etek shi'kar ek' pa'. Heh ni, nem-tor ish-veh ek' pa', etek tor wuh rom haul. Lu etek vesh' pok tor shove ska' etek vesh' wuh yonuk t' wuh mile ne' wuh vikuvtra, heh ish-veh vesh' takov sax'ksei gad; ni i tor jim ti ne' svi' wuh canoe heh wein abru k' wuh quilt, fai'ei kuv au eku abru sutra kupi var-tor au vesh' wuh nigger wuh rom yut ska'. I paddled abru' tor wuh illinois gef, heh marau ne' danik wuh ulef wuh mile doing ish-veh. I crept abru wuh tevik masu ne' wuh kutra, heh hadn't rai kisheya heh didn't gla-tor kling. Etek prah ha-kel ek' safe. Chapter x. Po' asal-yem i aitlu tor variben pa' wuh tevik sasu heh guess si' uf au sarlah tor nam-tor pustau, tonk'peh jim didn't aitlun tor. Au leralmin-tor ish-veh would zaprah rasahkos kunli; heh isha, au leralmin-tor, au lau sarlah heh ha'nt etek; au leralmin-tor wuh sasu ik vikau't visolektau vesh' weht kesik tor hal-tor wuh-ha'nting pa' do veh ik vesh' kastkau heh kel'o. Ik sounded takov reasonable, ni i didn't leralmin rai weht; tonk'peh i couldn't potau s' studying abru' ish-veh heh wishing i knowed vi pohshaya wuh sasu, heh ra au ovsoh ish-veh na'. Etek rummaged wuh sai-vel etek'd prah, heh afer-tor ohkuh dollars svi' haul-tukh og-tor abru svi' wuh tvitaya t' wuh hinek yuk-sai overcoat. Jim leralmin-tor au reckoned wuh sutra svi' ik kelek vazgau wuh tor-pal, fai'ei kuv au'd wuh knowed wuh donku vesh' tra' au wouldn't wuh losrak ish-veh. I leralmin-tor i reckoned au pustau ish-veh, nuh'; tonk'peh jim didn't aitlun tor variben pa' ik. I leralmin-tor: "i' du nah-tor ish-veh's rasahkos kunli; tonk'peh ra did du leralmin lu i zaprah svi' wuh oluhk-wadi ik i afer-tor fi' wuh fik t' wuh tauf gad fa' za-gad? Du leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh rasahkos rasahkos kunli svi' wuh panu tor esta wuh oluhk-wadi k' t'nash-veh el'ru. Muhl, la''s ish-veh rasahkos kunli! Etek've dref-tor svi' ek' nash truck heh ohkuh dollars isha. I istaya etek kupi ma ein rasahkos kunli spo' nash kanok gad, jim." "worla du kashek, honey, worla du kashek. Ri tor du git nuh' peart. Ish-veh's wuh-comin'. Kashek i var-tor du, ish-veh's wuh-comin'." ish-veh did sarlah, nuh'. Ish-veh vesh' wuh gad ik etek had ik variben. Muhl, po' aru-yem gad etek vesh' laying pa' svi' wuh yar na' wuh upper shaht t' wuh tauf, heh prah s' tobacco. I went tor wuh suk-tauk tor prah ein, heh afer-tor wuh rattlesnake svi' tra'. I pustau ish-veh, heh tcha-tor ish-veh abru fi' wuh ash'ya t' jim's yuk-sai, ek'wak ni malatik, thinking tra''d nam-tor ein mihrsh lu jim afer-tor ish-veh tra'. Muhl, k' mu-yor i forgot ek' pa' wuh oluhk, heh lu jim flung himself ne' fi' wuh yuk-sai du' i kwul-tor wuh ta'hal wuh oluhk's katelau vesh' tra', heh zeshau ish-veh. Au spen-tor abru yelling, heh wuh wuh'rak vel wuh ta'hal gluvau vesh' wuh varmint tcha-tor abru heh pok na' wuh'ashiv sikar. I laid ish-veh si' svi' wuh dahr k' wuh terpau, heh jim runem-tor pap's whisky-mashek heh palikau tor mukau ish-veh ne'. Au vesh' barefooted, heh wuh oluhk zeshau ish-veh gas'rak fi' wuh timut. Ik ek' sarlah t' t'nash-veh hasu such wuh duhsu u' tor ri vokau ik wherever du trasha wuh tevik oluhk its katelau kwon-hau-ov sarlah tra' heh tcha-tor pa' ish-veh. Jim var-tor me tor chop ska' wuh oluhk's patam heh lehm ish-veh maf, heh yi wadi wuh ak'shem heh roast wuh krus t' ish-veh. I ovsoh ish-veh, heh au yokul ish-veh heh leralmin-tor ish-veh would gol'nev bohrau ish-veh. Au tor me nem-tor ska' wuh rattles heh tie au pa' ish-veh kar-nik, nuh'. Au leralmin-tor ik ik would gol'nev. Yi i slid si' hizhuk heh throwed wuh oluhk pa'shik maf svi' wuh bushes; na' i vikau't going tor kal-tor jim talal si' ish-veh vesh' ek' t'nash-veh lafot, ri kuv i kupi gol'nev ish-veh. Jim sucked heh sucked na' wuh mashek, heh i' heh yi au prah s' ish-veh patam heh pitched pa' heh saul-tor; tonk'peh kanok wak au sarlah tor himself au went tor sucking na' wuh mashek va'ashiv. Ish-veh ash'ya puv-tor abru takov suk', heh ni did ish-veh mal; tonk'peh k'-heh-k' wuh mon-tor palikau tor sarlah, heh ni i judged au vesh' ek' gas'rak; tonk'peh i'd druther vesh' zeshau k' wuh oluhk do pap's whisky. Jim vesh' laid abru na' kehkuh gad heh mu-yor. Yi wuh puv vesh' ek' hal-tor heh au vesh' pa' va'ashiv. I tor abru t'nash-veh kashek i wouldn't ek'wak nem-tor wuh-holt t' wuh oluhk-wadi va'ashiv k' t'nash-veh el'ru, i' ik gla-tor nash-veh ra had sarlah t' ish-veh. Jim leralmin-tor au reckoned i would dva-tor ish-veh thurai wak. Heh au leralmin-tor ik handling wuh oluhk-wadi vesh' such awful rasahkos kunli ik sos'eh etek hadn't prah tor wuh shaht t' ish-veh wi. Au leralmin-tor au druther gla-tor wuh uzh aikum abru' ish-veh losrak tipan u' mau u' wuh thousand wak do nem-tor abru wuh oluhk-wadi svi' ish-veh el'ru. Muhl, i vesh' getting tor olau ik yut myself, hi i've kwon-hau-ov reckoned ik looking na' wuh uzh aikum abru' ish-veh losrak tipan nam-tor veh t' wuh carelessest heh foolishest vel wuh ak'shem mokuhlek tor. Hinek hank bunker ovsoh ish-veh wuh'wak, heh bragged pa' ish-veh; heh svi' lehkuh tor dahkuh tevun au prah mon-tor heh tevan-tor ska' t' wuh pohshaya-kispek, heh sak-tor himself si' ni ik au vesh' aishan wuh ves t' wuh zhai-tukh, u' du lau leralmin; heh au slid ish-veh edgeways svi' dahkuh aushfa-kel svep na' wuh tevikeh-natuhn, heh visolektau ish-veh ni, ni au leralmin, tonk'peh i didn't gla-tor ish-veh. Pap var-tor me. Tonk'peh anyway ish-veh ek' sarlah t' looking na' wuh aikum ik yut, spo' wuh duhsu. Muhl, wuh gad went bi', heh wuh pilash went ne' svi' its kutra va'ashiv; heh pa' wuh wuh'rak vel etek ovsoh vesh' tor bait veh t' wuh suk' kik k' wuh skinned rabbit heh eku ish-veh heh kum wuh catfish ik vesh' u' suk' u' wuh sasu, hasu shehkuh ash'ya dahkuh inches wu, heh rasathau abru' dahkuh hundred plesh-tor. Etek couldn't el'rek ish-veh, veling; au would wuh flung etek vi' illinois. Etek aishan eku tra' heh glantau ish-veh tres heh bezhun-masu pa' till au drownded. Etek afer-tor wuh dvesh-tukh gonaf svi' ish-veh skaun-sa'haf heh wuh pauk rin'k'n, heh lots t' rubbage. Etek thresh wuh rin'k'n tu'ash k' wuh hatchet, heh tra' vesh' wuh spool svi' ish-veh. Jim leralmin-tor au'd had ish-veh tra' wuh akarshif, tor tor-pal ish-veh abru' ni heh tor wuh rin'k'n t' ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' u' suk' wuh aluk u' vesh' ek'wak catched svi' wuh mississippi, i reckon. Jim leralmin-tor au hadn't ek'wak gla-tor wuh bigger veh. Au would wuh vesh' don wuh rom deal abru' na' wuh pi'kahr. Au peddle si' such wuh aluk u' ik k' wuh plesh-tor svi' wuh mahr-kel-kelek tra'; kanok-veh buys ein t' ish-veh; ish-veh kahm's u' wan-kur u' izh heh tor wuh rom pol-tor. Thurai asal i leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' getting vohris heh pasik, heh i aitlu tor prah wuh stirring abru ein yut. I leralmin-tor i reckoned i would trel abru' wuh pilash heh talal si' ra vesh' going fi'. Jim tishau ik notion; tonk'peh au leralmin-tor i bolau hal-tor svi' wuh gu'gelik heh glazhau nasik. Yi au orenau ish-veh abru' heh leralmin-tor, couldn't i shitau fi' ein t' au hinek vel heh sai-vel abru spo' wuh ko-kan? Ik vesh' wuh rom notion, nuh'. Ni etek pen-tor abru veh t' wuh calico gowns, heh i da-tor abru t'nash-veh trouser-mal tor t'nash-veh mal-nef heh prah vi' ish-veh. Jim hitched ish-veh za' k' wuh kik, heh ish-veh vesh' wuh rom nunau. I shitau fi' wuh yel-bonnet heh tied ish-veh ne' t'nash-veh chin, heh yi na' wuh ak'shem tor glazhau svi' heh gla-tor t'nash-veh limuk vesh' spo' looking ne' wuh joint t' stove-mev. Jim leralmin-tor kling would fai-tor me, kauk svi' wuh gad-wakik, hardly. I practiced pa' ek' gad tor prah wuh geldau t' wuh vel, heh k'-heh-k' i kupi tor takov muhl svi' au, goh jim leralmin-tor i didn't lates spo' wuh ko-kan; heh au leralmin-tor i bolau quit pulling abru t'nash-veh gown tor prah na' t'nash-veh britches-abru'lik. I nem-tor beglanau, heh ovsoh weh-rom. I palikau abru wuh illinois gef svi' wuh canoe aishan po' gu'gelik. I palikau mes' tor wuh kahr s' wuh pi' ne' wuh mes-hali-landing, heh wuh maraya t' wuh current zaprah me svi' na' wuh lanet t' wuh kahr. I tied abru heh palikau bi' wuh kutra. Tra' vesh' wuh ta'hal yontau svi' wuh pi' shanty ik hadn't vesh' ha-tor svi' na' wuh akarshif, heh i wondered vi had nem-tor abru ha-shal tra'. I trel-tor abru heh peeped svi' na' wuh krani. Tra' vesh' wuh kosu pa' keh-leh tevun hinek svi' tra' knitting k' wuh ha'fek ik vesh' fi' wuh pine pasu. I didn't fai-tor ish-veh limuk; she vesh' wuh ri-fainusu, na' du couldn't palikaya wuh limuk svi' ik kahr ik i didn't fai-tor. I' nash vesh' kunli, fai'ei i vesh' weakening; i vesh' getting kwes i had sarlah; sutra lau fai-tor t'nash-veh spes heh talal me si'. Tonk'peh kuv nash kosu had vesh' svi' such wuh pi' kahr dahkuh gad she kupi var-tor me ek' i aitlu tor fai-tor; ni i knocked na' wuh svep, heh tor abru t'nash-veh kashek i wouldn't yen-tor i vesh' wuh ko-kan. Chapter xi. "sarlah svi', " leralmin-tor wuh kosu, heh i did. She leralmin-tor: "nem-tor wuh cheer." i ovsoh ish-veh. She glazhau me ek' abru' k' ish-veh pi' shiny bezhun, heh leralmin-tor: "ra lau ish-veh ahm nam-tor?" "sarah williams." "wilat 'bouts tor du ha-tor? Svi' nash neighborhood?' "rai'm. Svi' hookerville, stehkuh mile ne'. I've lates-tor ek' wuh yut heh i'm ek' zungor si'." "k'avon, nuh', i reckon. I'll talal du vel." "rai'm, i ain't k'avon. I vesh' ni k'avon i had tor pehkaya dahkuh miles ne' la' na' wuh uroshal; ni i ain't k'avon rai weht. Ish-veh's ra tor me ni tab-ma. T'nash-veh ko-mekh's ne' has-bosh, heh s' donku heh kanok-vei, heh sarlah nash-veh tor var-tor t'nash-veh sa-kuk abner moore. Au ha-tor na' wuh upper shaht t' wuh kahr, she leralmin-tor. I hain't ek'wak vesh' la' fa'. Tor du fai-tor ish-veh?" "rai; tonk'peh i ri tor fai-tor kanok-veh wi. I haven't ha-tor la' ved dahkuh wehk gad. Ish-veh's wuh considerable yut tor wuh upper shaht t' wuh kahr. Du weh-rom stay la' ek' mu-yor. Nem-tor ska' ish-veh bonnet." "rai, " i leralmin-tor; "i'll shom wuh du', i reckon, heh hal-tor fi'. I ain't afeared t' wuh gu'gelik." she leralmin-tor she wouldn't ti'amah k' myself, tonk'peh ish-veh sa-telsu would nam-tor svi' k'-heh-k', sos'eh svi' wuh wadan heh wuh ulef, heh she'd satau ish-veh bi' k' me. Yi she prah tor talking pa' ish-veh sa-telsu, heh pa' ish-veh relations abru wuh pilash, heh ish-veh relations ne' wuh pilash, heh pa' uf mau weh-rom ska' au nam-tor-tor tor vesh', heh uf au didn't fai-tor tonk'peh au'd tor wuh lafosh coming tor etwel kahr, instead t' letting muhl aloneand ni fi' heh ni fi', till i vesh' afeard i had tor wuh lafosh coming tor ish-veh tor talal si' ra vesh' going fi' svi' wuh kahr; tonk'peh k'-heh-k' she eku-tor fi' tor pap heh wuh riyeht-staya, heh yi i vesh' takov willing tor kal-tor ish-veh clatter gas'rak bi'. She var-tor pa' me heh tom sawyer finding wuh shehkuh thousand dollars (goh she prah ish-veh lehkuh) heh ek' pa' pap heh ra wuh lerash lot au vesh', heh ra wuh lerash lot i vesh', heh na' kim-shah she prah ne' tor wilat i vesh' riyeht-stau. I leralmin-tor: "vi ovsoh ish-veh? Etek've puzhu-tor considerable pa' aifa goings fi' ne' svi' hookerville, tonk'peh etek ri tor fai-tor vi 'twas ik pustau huck finn." "muhl, i reckon tra''s wuh gas'rak klon pavesh t' sutra la' ik'd spo' tor fai-tor vi pustau ish-veh. Ein nah-tor hinek finn ovsoh ish-veh himself." "nois ik ni?" "danik kanok-veh nahp ish-veh palikauk. Au'll worla fai-tor uf nigh au sarlah tor getting lynched. Tonk'peh fa' mu-yor au rubai pa' heh judged ish-veh vesh' ovsoh k' wuh runaway nigger ahmau jim." "po au" i pehkau. I reckoned i weh-rom potau fam dvun. She sahr-tor fi', heh worla pubeglanau i had shitau svi' na' ek': "wuh nigger sahr-tor ska' wuh maut mu-yor huck finn vesh' pustau. Ni tra''s wuh reward si' na' himthree hundred dollars. Heh tra''s wuh reward si' na' hinek finn, tootwo hundred dollars. Gla-tor du, au sarlah tor kahr wuh asal po' wuh riyeht-staya, heh var-tor pa' ish-veh, heh vesh' si' k' 'em fi' wuh mes-hali-masu-hali shi'kar, heh gas'rak maf po' au abru heh losrak. Fa' mu-yor au aitlu tor lynch ish-veh, tonk'peh au vesh' hal-tor, gla-tor du. Muhl, thurai gad au afer-tor si' wuh nigger vesh' hal-tor; au afer-tor si' au hadn't ben gla-tor sence lehkuh o'wak-vel wuh mu-yor wuh riyeht-staya vesh' ovsoh. Ni yi au shitau ish-veh fi' ish-veh, gla-tor du; heh du' au vesh' bosh t' ish-veh, thurai gad, pla' sarlah hinek finn, heh went boo-hooing tor judge thatcher tor prah donku tor shi'kar na' wuh nigger ek' abru' illinois k'. Wuh judge mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ein, heh ik khru au prah mon-tor, heh vesh' pa' till po' midnight k' wuh couple t' mighty lerash-looking ri-fainusu, heh yi went ska' k' au. Muhl, au hain't sarlah pla' sence, heh au ain't looking na' ish-veh pla' till nash vel salur abru' wuh pi', na' sutra nah-tor i' ik au pustau ish-veh sa-kan heh teslau vel ni sular-ves would nah-tor robbers ovsoh ish-veh, heh yi au'd prah huck's donku rik' having tor ertau wuh akarshif k' wuh lawsuit. Sutra tor leralmin au vikau't sovek nuh' rom tor tor ish-veh. Oh, au's sly, i reckon. Kuv au ri tor sarlah pla' na' wuh tevun au'll nam-tor ek' gas'rak. Du mokuhlek't skan-tor sovek-vel fi' ish-veh, du fai-tor; kanok-vei dungi nam-tor quieted ne' yi, heh au'll lates svi' huck's donku u' hagik u' nothing." "ha, i reckon ni, 'm. I ri tor gla-tor nothing svi' wuh yut t' ish-veh. Has kanok-veh quit thinking wuh nigger ovsoh ish-veh?" "oh, rai, ri kanok-veh. Wuh rom wehk nah-tor au ovsoh ish-veh. Tonk'peh au'll prah wuh nigger takov ak i', heh sos'eh au mokuhlek pahth ish-veh s' ish-veh." "po, nam-tor au po' ish-veh wi?" "muhl, du're innocent, ain't du! Tor rehkuh hundred dollars ti pa' kanok gad na' sutra tor abrashau? Ein sular-ves nah-tor wuh nigger ain't irak s' la'. I'm veh t' thembut i hain't variben ish-veh pa'. Wuh zamu gad ago i vesh' talking k' wuh hinek couple ik ha-tor thurai svep svi' wuh lap-fek shanty, heh au pavesh-tor tor leralmin hardly anybody ek'wak hal-tor tor ik vikuvtra abru' yonder ik au vutau jackson's vikuvtra. Ri tor anybody ha-tor tra'? Leralmin-tor i. Rai, kling, leralmin-tor au. I didn't leralmin sovek weht, tonk'peh i ovsoh ein thinking. I vesh' takov be' ac'ruth i'd gla-tor vuzh abru' tra', pa' wuh patam t' wuh vikuvtra, wuh gad il dahkuh fa' ik, ni i leralmin-tor tor myself, spo' u' ri ik nigger's hiding abru' tra'; anyway, leralmin-tor i, ish-veh's don wuh trouble tor mazhiv-kur-tor wuh shi wuh shi'kar. I hain't gla-tor sovek vuzh sence, ni i reckon sos'eh au's hal-tor, kuv ish-veh vesh' ish-veh; tonk'peh sa-telsu's going abru' tor seehim heh wuh'ashiv sasu. Au vesh' hal-tor abru wuh pilash; tonk'peh au zaprah tor-gad, heh i var-tor ish-veh u' ak u' au prah la' dahkuh wadan ago." i had prah ni uneasy i couldn't eku fam dvun. I had tor tor vel k' t'nash-veh el'ru; ni i nem-tor abru wuh og-lum ska' t' wuh pasu heh went tor threading ish-veh. T'nash-veh el'ru hutau, heh i vesh' tor wuh rasahkos job t' ish-veh. Lu wuh kosu pehkau talking i glazhau abru, heh she vesh' looking na' me takov curious heh smiling wuh pi'. I shitau ne' wuh og-lum heh og-elakh, heh kal-tor fi' tor nam-tor interestedand i vesh', tooand leralmin-tor: "rehkuh hundred dollars nam-tor wuh tepul t' donku. I istaya t'nash-veh ko-mekh kupi prah ish-veh. Nam-tor ish-veh sa-telsu going abru' tra' tor-mu-yor?" "oh, ha. Au went abru-kahr k' wuh sasu i vesh' telling du t', tor prah wuh masu-hali heh gla-tor kuv au kupi yahv-tor wuh'ashiv pohshayek. Au'll hal-tor abru' po' midnight." "couldn't gla-tor au weh-rom kuv au vesh' tor bek-tor till gad-wakik?" "ha. Heh couldn't wuh nigger gla-tor weh-rom, nuh'? Po' midnight au'll kesik nam-tor asleep, heh au mokuhlek trel pa' k'fai wuh lapan heh shi'kar abru ish-veh ith'du yon ek' wuh weh-rom na' wuh gu'gelik, kuv au's prah veh." "i didn't nah-tor t' ik." wuh kosu potau looking na' me takov curious, heh i didn't olau wuh zeshau kel'o. Takov ak she leralmin-tor, "ra did du leralmin ish-veh ahm vesh', honey?" "mmary williams." somehow ish-veh didn't seem tor me ik i leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' mary fa', ni i didn't glazhau upseemed tor me i leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' sarah; ni i olau wihfelau t' cornered, heh vesh' afeared sos'eh i vesh' looking ish-veh, nuh'. I istau wuh kosu would leralmin vel weht; wuh longer she eku fam dvun wuh uneasier i vesh'. Tonk'peh i' she leralmin-tor: "honey, i nahp du leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' sarah lu du wuh'rak sarlah svi'?" "oh, ha'm, i did. Sarah mary williams. Sarah's t'nash-veh wuh'rak ahm. Ein calls me sarah, ein calls me mary." "oh, ik's wuh yut t' ish-veh?" "ha'm." i vesh' olaya weh-rom yi, tonk'peh i istau i vesh' s' tra', anyway. I couldn't glazhau abru wi. Muhl, wuh kosu tevan-tor tor talking pa' uf lerash wak vesh', heh uf ri donku-tor au had tor ha-tor, heh uf wuh rats vesh' u' elik u' kuv au puma wuh shi, heh ni forth heh ni fi', heh yi i prah hagik va'ashiv. She vesh' gas'rak pa' wuh rats. Du'd gla-tor veh terpau ish-veh han s' wuh razh svi' wuh teruk kanok pi' du'. She leralmin-tor she had ki' vel handy tor lehm na' au lu she vesh' sa'awek, il au wouldn't mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh rai sochya. She gluvau me wuh mofek t' ras-tukh kuvoran-tor abru vi' wuh knot, heh leralmin-tor she vesh' wuh rom pohshaya k' ish-veh generly, tonk'peh she'd wrenched ish-veh kar wuh gad il dahkuh ago, heh didn't fai-tor whether she kupi lehm yeht i'. Tonk'peh she glantau na' wuh pavesh, heh directly banged maf na' wuh rat; tonk'peh she din-tor ish-veh eik, heh leralmin-tor "ouch!" ish-veh dash-tor ish-veh kar ni. Yi she var-tor me tor ar'kadan na' wuh thurai veh. I aitlu tor nam-tor getting maf fa' wuh hinek sasu zaprah, tonk'peh t' rivak i didn't kal-tor fi'. I prah wuh vel, heh wuh wuh'rak rat ik gluvau ish-veh han i kal-tor yetur, heh kuv au'd wuh stayed wilat au vesh' au'd wuh vesh' wuh tolerable has-bosh rat. She leralmin-tor ik vesh' wuh'rak-tav, heh she reckoned i would hive wuh thurai veh. She went heh prah wuh vihk t' ras-tukh heh zaprah ish-veh pla', heh katau bi' wuh hank t' yarn if she aitlu me tor gol'nev ish-veh k'. I meskarau abru t'nash-veh dahkuh el'ru heh she shitau wuh hank abru' au, heh went fi' talking pa' ish-veh heh ish-veh sa-telsu's tukh. Tonk'peh she shau ska' tor leralmin: "potau ish-veh bezhun fi' wuh rats. Du weh-rom ma wuh ras-tukh svi' ish-veh lap, handy." ni she eku-tor wuh vihk vi' t'nash-veh lap aishan na' ik moment, heh i clapped t'nash-veh mal teretuhr fi' ish-veh heh she went fi' talking. Tonk'peh goh pa' wuh minute. Yi she nem-tor ska' wuh hank heh glazhau me zehik svi' wuh limuk, heh maut vaksurik, heh leralmin-tor: "sarlah, i', ra's ish-veh yeht ahm?" "whwhat, mum?" "ra's ish-veh yeht ahm? Nam-tor ish-veh dun, il tom, il bob?il ra nam-tor ish-veh?" i reckon i hutau spo' wuh mor, heh i didn't fai-tor hardly ra tor tor. Tonk'peh i leralmin-tor: "sanoi tor ri tor poke mihrsh na' wuh ri donku-tor ko-kan spo' me, mum. Kuv i'm svi' wuh yut la', i'll" "rai, du skil-tor't. Eku ne' heh stay wilat du nam-tor. I ain't going tor dash-tor du, heh i ain't going tor var-tor fi' du, nuther. Du aishan var-tor me ish-veh tsat, heh sahrafel me. I'll potau ish-veh; heh, ra's weht, i'll gol'nev du. Ni'll t'nash-veh hinek sasu kuv du aitlun ish-veh tor. Gla-tor du, du're wuh runaway 'prentice, ik's ek'. Ish-veh ain't sovek-vel. Tra' ain't rai klau svi' ish-veh. Du've vesh' skasau rasahkos, heh du tor abru ish-veh kashek tor tresahk. Kudau du, kan, i wouldn't var-tor fi' du. Var-tor me ek' pa' ish-veh i', ik's wuh rom sa-kan." ni i leralmin-tor ish-veh wouldn't nam-tor rai nam-tor-tor tor ar'kadan tor mavau ish-veh sovek longer, heh i would aishan tor wuh sok'i thasek heh var-tor ish-veh kanok-vei, tonk'peh she musn't hal-tor pla' fi' ish-veh ugaya. Yi i var-tor ish-veh t'nash-veh sa-mekh heh ko-mekh vesh' tevik, heh wuh tor-gav had bound me si' tor wuh tvai hinek uroshitausu svi' wuh shasol reh-leh mile pla' s' wuh pilash, heh au skasau me ni rasahkos i couldn't lamok ish-veh rai longer; au went maf tor nam-tor hal-tor wuh couple t' gad, heh ni i nem-tor t'nash-veh pavesh heh vazgau ein t' ish-veh ko-fu's hinek sai-vel heh pa'shu si', heh i had vesh' rehkuh mu-yor coming wuh reh-leh miles. I halovau mu-yor, heh ip-sut daytimes heh yuk-tor, heh wuh sa'haf t' kap heh kahm i lesh s' ha-kel palesh-tor me ek' wuh yut, heh i had wuh-plenty. I leralmin-tor i pudva-tor t'nash-veh sa-kuk abner moore would nem-tor tun t' me, heh ni ik vesh' po i kwul-tor si' na' nash kahr t' goshen. "goshen, kan? Nash ain't goshen. Nash nam-tor st. Petersburg. Goshen's lehkuh mile further abru wuh pilash. Vi var-tor du nash vesh' goshen?" "po, wuh sasu i ragel-tor na' gad-keshtan nash asal, aishan u' i vesh' going tor da-tor vi' wuh lapan na' t'nash-veh regular yuk. Au var-tor me lu wuh fau-yut forked i bolau nem-tor wuh gas'rak el'ru, heh kaukuh mile would zaprah me tor goshen." "au vesh' mon-tor, i reckon. Au var-tor du aishan exactly riyeht." "muhl, au did bae'cok spo' au vesh' mon-tor, tonk'peh ish-veh ain't rai tukh i'. I prah tor nam-tor dvun-tor bi'. I'll zaprah goshen fa' gad-ha'khlup." "meskaraya fi' wuh minute. I'll shitau du abru wuh snack tor yokul. Du lau aitlun ish-veh." ni she shitau me abru wuh snack, heh leralmin-tor: "leralmin, lu wuh aushfa's laying ne', if shaht t' ish-veh prah abru wuh'rak? Kilko-srashiv abru prompt nowdon't pehkaya tor orenau abru' ish-veh. If shaht prah abru wuh'rak?" "wuh hind shaht, mum." "muhl, yi, wuh jarel?" "wuh na''rard shaht, mum." "if vla t' wuh lap tor wuh yekuhl tor'ovau fi'?" "desh'rak vla." "kuv leh-kau aushfa nam-tor browsing fi' wuh hillside, uf wehk t' au yokul k' ish-veh patam sfekau wuh ka kharat?" "wuh bosh leh-kau, mum." "muhl, i reckon du ma ha-tor svi' wuh shasol. I nahp sos'eh du vesh' trying tor hocus me va'ashiv. Ra's ish-veh yeht ahm, i'?" "george peters, mum." "muhl, ar'kadan tor vokau ish-veh, george. Ri tor yen-tor heh var-tor me ish-veh's elexander fa' du hal-tor, heh yi prah si' k' taran ish-veh's george elexander lu i kum du. Heh ri tor hal-tor pa' kosu svi' ik hinek calico. Du tor wuh ko-kan tolerable ri donku-tor, tonk'peh du lau duhsu sasu, sos'eh. Kudau du, kan, lu du eku si' tor og-elakh wuh og-lum ri tor meskaraya wuh og-elakh fam dvun heh zaprah wuh og-lum abru tor ish-veh; meskaraya wuh og-lum fam dvun heh poke wuh og-elakh na' ish-veh; ik's wuh yut wuh kosu danik kwon-hau-ov tor, tonk'peh wuh sasu kwon-hau-ov tor t'vath yut. Heh lu du lehm na' wuh rat il sovek-vel, hitch yourself abru wuh tiptoe heh zaprah ish-veh el'ru abru abru' ish-veh patam u' awkward u' du mokuhlek, heh din-tor ish-veh rat pa' shehkuh il stehkuh ash'ya. Lehm stegel-armed s' wuh tipan, spo' tra' vesh' wuh da-sfek tra' na' ish-veh tor da-tor fi', spo' wuh ko-kan; ri s' wuh kar-nik heh kar-nef, k' ish-veh kar si' tor veh vla, spo' wuh sa-kan. Heh, kashek du, lu wuh ko-kan ar'kada tor kum sovek-vel svi' ish-veh lap she lehm-tor ish-veh mal-nef k'wuhli; she ri tor clap au teretuhr, wuh yut du did lu du catched wuh vihk t' ras-tukh. Po, i gla-tor du na' wuh sa-kan lu du vesh' threading wuh og-lum; heh i contrived wuh vath vel aishan tor tor ac'ruth. I' sahr-tor bi' tor ish-veh sa-kuk, sarah mary williams george elexander peters, heh kuv du prah vi' trouble du satau zhit tor mrs. Judith loftus, if nam-tor me, heh i'll tor ra i mokuhlek tor prah du s' ish-veh. Potau wuh pilash fau-yut ek' wuh yut, heh thurai wak du tramp nem-tor ash'el heh ash'ai k' du. Wuh pilash fau-yut's wuh rocky veh, heh ish-veh ash'ya'll nam-tor svi' wuh nosh lu du prah tor goshen, i reckon." i went abru wuh kutra pa' kau-leh ker, heh yi i dahtau fi' t'nash-veh ash'yaidar heh trel-tor pla' tor wilat t'nash-veh canoe vesh', wuh rom krus ne' wuh kelek. I spen-tor svi', heh vesh' ska' svi' wuh brax. I went abru-pilash irak hiyet tor tor wuh patam t' wuh vikuvtra, heh yi palikau mes'. I nem-tor ska' wuh yel-bonnet, na' i didn't aitlun rai blinders fi' yi. Lu i vesh' pa' wuh svitan i puzhu-tor wuh wak-vel palikau tor kwul, ni i pehkau heh shroi; wuh ralash sarlah faint abru' wuh masu tonk'peh cleareleven. Lu i kwul-tor wuh patam t' wuh vikuvtra i worla bek-tor tor salur, hi i vesh' danik kuvor-tor, tonk'peh i shoved gas'rak vi' wuh lap-tukh wilat t'nash-veh hinek ith'du nam-tor-tor tor nam-tor, heh palikau wuh rom yon tra' fi' wuh pid heh pseth gla-tor. Yi i spen-tor svi' wuh canoe heh hil-tor si' na' etwel shi, wuh mile heh wuh ulef ne', u' lerash u' i kupi hal-tor. I landed, heh slopped k'fai wuh lap-tukh heh abru wuh tauf heh vi' wuh suk-tauk. Tra' jim laid, ralash asleep fi' wuh solektra. I kastorilau ish-veh si' heh leralmin-tor: "git abru heh hump yourself, jim! Tra' ain't wuh minute tor pak-tor. Au're po' etek!" jim worla ya'akash rai deshkau, au worla leralmin-tor wuh zhit; tonk'peh wuh yut au ar'kada na' wuh thurai ulef wuh wadan gluvau pa' uf au vesh' pahth-tor. K' ik wak kanok-vei etek had svi' wuh panu vesh' fi' etwel marshak, heh she vesh' pok tor nam-tor shoved si' s' wuh willow pi'tchol wilat she vesh' ip-sut. Etek shitau si' wuh ith'du yon na' wuh suk-tauk wuh wuh'rak vel, heh didn't gluvaya wuh ha'fek s'udish po' ik. I nem-tor wuh canoe si' s' wuh gef wuh pi' krus, heh nem-tor wuh glazhau; tonk'peh kuv tra' vesh' wuh masu-hali pa' i couldn't gla-tor ish-veh, na' yel heh duv ain't rom tor gla-tor k'. Yi etek prah si' wuh marshak heh trel-tor bi' ne' svi' wuh duvek, vesht wuh ash'ya t' wuh vikuvtra tevik stillnever taran wuh zhit. Chapter xii. Ish-veh bolau wuh vesh' ikap-tor fi' tor veh o'wak-vel lu etek prah ne' wuh vikuvtra na' kim-shah, heh wuh marshak did seem tor hal-tor mighty vohris. Kuv wuh masu-hali vesh' tor sarlah bi' etek vesh' going tor nem-tor tor wuh canoe heh shaya na' wuh illinois gef; heh ish-veh vesh' muhl wuh masu-hali didn't sarlah, na' etek hadn't ek'wak nahp tor shitau wuh pohshayek svi' wuh canoe, il wuh fishing-zehl, il sovek-vel tor yokul. Etek vesh' svi' ruther nuh' mau t' wuh wadashaya tor nah-tor t' ni wehk vel. Ish-veh vikau't rom judgment tor shitau kanok-vei fi' wuh marshak. Kuv wuh sasu went tor wuh vikuvtra i aishan gish au afer-tor wuh ith'du yon i torvau, heh glantau ish-veh ek' mu-yor na' jim tor sarlah. Anyways, au stayed maf s' etek, heh kuv t'nash-veh kelek wuh yon worla fooled au ish-veh vikau't rai lafot t' t'nash-veh. I mavau ish-veh u' neik ne' fi' au u' i kupi. Lu wuh wuh'rak wesh t' gad began tor gluvaya etek tied abru tor wuh tow-patam svi' wuh suk' vulaya fi' wuh illinois vla, heh hacked ska' cottonwood khlup k' wuh hatchet, heh wein-tor abru wuh marshak k' au ni she glazhau spo' tra' had vesh' wuh tauk-svi' svi' wuh kutra tra'. Wuh tow-patam nam-tor wuh mazhiv-zehl ik has cottonwoods fi' ish-veh u' bali u' harrow-zud. Etek had suk'kunel fi' wuh missouri gef heh ras lap-tukh fi' wuh illinois vla, heh wuh mashyut vesh' ne' wuh missouri gef na' ik shi, ni etek vikau't kwes t' anybody sahran mes' etek. Etek laid tra' ek' gad, heh glantau wuh marshak heh steamboats padan ne' wuh missouri gef, heh abru-bound steamboats puk wuh suk' pilash svi' wuh svitan. I var-tor jim ek' pa' wuh wak i had jabbering k' ik kosu; heh jim leralmin-tor she vesh' wuh klon veh, heh kuv she vesh' tor palikaya po' etek herself she wouldn't eku ne' heh glantau wuh ith'du fireno, osu, she'd zaprah wuh dog. Muhl, yi, i leralmin-tor, po couldn't she var-tor ish-veh sa-telsu tor zaprah wuh dog? Jim leralmin-tor au sihaya she did nah-tor t' ish-veh k' wuh wak wuh sasu vesh' pok tor palikaya, heh au pudva-tor au bolau wuh hal-tor abru-kahr tor prah wuh dog heh ni au pakik ek' ik wak, il else etek wouldn't nam-tor la' fi' wuh tow-patam leh-sheh il leh- steh mile ne' wuh villageno, indeedy, etek would nam-tor svi' ik ka hinek kahr va'ashiv. Ni i leralmin-tor i didn't tun ra vesh' wuh utvau au didn't prah etek u' wu u' au didn't. Lu ish-veh vesh' palikaya tor sarlah fi' gu'gelik etek poked etwel patam s' wuh cottonwood pi'laptra, heh glazhau abru heh ne' heh mes'; nothing svi' glan; ni jim nem-tor abru ein t' wuh fik planks t' wuh marshak heh torvau wuh snug wigwam tor prah ne' svi' blazing igen-va heh sov-masuyanik, heh tor potau wuh vel pseth. Jim tor wuh lan-tol na' wuh wigwam, heh ashenau ish-veh wuh ash'ya il weht abru' wuh volik t' wuh marshak, ni i' wuh yuk-sai heh ek' wuh pash-tor vesh' s' pulau t' steamboat pral. Gas'rak svi' wuh svitan t' wuh wigwam etek tor wuh zhai-tukh t' kitek pa' kaukuh il shehkuh inches glu k' wuh nentu pa' ish-veh na' tor meskaraya ish-veh tor its shi; nash vesh' tor torvau wuh yon fi' svi' sloppy igen-va il chilly; wuh wigwam would potau ish-veh s' hasu gla-tor. Etek tor wuh hayaik steering-fel, nuh', fai'ei veh t' wuh vath lau prah shau fi' wuh snag il vel. Etek teslau abru wuh pen forked terpau tor geldau wuh hinek makh-yonet fi', fai'ei etek bolau kwon-hau-ov ta'hal wuh makh-yonet whenever gla-tor etek wuh steamboat coming ne'-pilash, tor potau s' getting sahr-tor abru'; tonk'peh etek wouldn't ma tor ta'hal ish-veh na' abru-pilash masu-hali vita gla-tor etek etek vesh' svi' ra au vutau wuh "mes"; na' wuh pilash vesh' takov pid wi, maut neik kutra hasu fam dvun wuh pi' ne' masu; ni abru-bound masu-hali didn't kwon-hau-ov sahr-tor wuh mashyut, tonk'peh shi'kar hagik masu. Nash dahr mu-yor etek sahr-tor svi' stehkuh heh ohkuh wadan, k' wuh current ik vesh' tor abru' kehkuh mile wuh wadan. Etek catched aluk heh variben, heh etek nem-tor wuh mahal-tor i' heh yi tor potau ska' sleepiness. Ish-veh vesh' ves t' solemn, drifting ne' wuh suk', fam dvun pilash, laying fi' etwel pla'dor looking abru na' wuh yel, heh etek didn't ek'wak olau spo' talking ral, heh ish-veh vikau't k'ashiv ik etek laughedonly wuh pi' ves t' wuh neik chuckle. Etek had mighty rom igen-va u' wuh paik vel, heh nothing ek'wak pavesh-tor tor etek na' allthat mu-yor, il wuh thurai, il wuh thurai. Kanok mu-yor etek be' dvun-tor kahr, ein t' au maf abru fi' nesh-kur hillsides, nothing tonk'peh aishan wuh shiny sar-tak t' ha'ge; ri wuh kelek kupi gla-tor du. Wuh fifth mu-yor etek be' dvun-tor st. Louis, heh ish-veh vesh' spo' wuh bosh panu lit abru. Svi' st. Petersburg au nam-tor-tor tor leralmin tra' vesh' dah-leh il reh-leh thousand sutra svi' st. Louis, tonk'peh i worla pudva-tor ish-veh till gla-tor nash-veh ik wonderful sak-tor t' ha'ge na' dahkuh o'wak-vel ik fam dvun mu-yor. Tra' vikau't wuh ralash tra'; kanok-veh vesh' asleep. Kanok mu-yor i' i nam-tor-tor tor trel ashore na' lehkuh o'wak-vel na' ein pi' pi'kahr, heh mahr-tor lehkuh il leh-kau cents' don t' yem il bacon il vath tukh tor yokul; heh sometimes i abertau wuh kahm ik vikau't roosting kel'o, heh nem-tor ish-veh bi'. Pap kwon-hau-ov leralmin-tor, nem-tor wuh kahm lu du prah wuh pavesh, fai'ei kuv du ri tor aitlun ish-veh yourself du mokuhlek hagik talal somebody ik tor, heh wuh rom deed ain't ek'wak forgot. I worla gla-tor pap lu au didn't aitlun wuh kahm himself, tonk'peh ik nam-tor ra au nam-tor-tor tor leralmin, anyway. Asal fa' gad-ha'khlup i trel-tor vi' cornfields heh yahv-tor wuh watermelon, il wuh mushmelon, il wuh punkin, il ein uzh corn, il vel t' ik ves. Pap kwon-hau-ov leralmin-tor ish-veh vikau't rai klau tor yahv-tor vel kuv du vesh' meaning tor vlitau au pla' ein wak; tonk'peh wuh kir'an leralmin-tor ish-veh vikau't sovek-vel tonk'peh wuh mos ahm na' stealing, heh rai tevan ak'shem would tor ish-veh. Jim leralmin-tor au reckoned wuh kir'an vesh' partly gas'rak heh pap vesh' partly gas'rak; ni wuh buhfik yut would nam-tor na' etek tor pick si' dahkuh il rehkuh vel s' wuh feim heh leralmin etek wouldn't yahv-tor au sovek morethen au reckoned ish-veh wouldn't nam-tor rai klau tor yahv-tor wuh vath. Ni etek variben ish-veh abru' ek' veh mu-yor, drifting bi' ne' wuh pilash, trying tor tor abru etwel kashkau whether tor eku wuh watermelons, il wuh cantelopes, il wuh mushmelons, il ra. Tonk'peh na' gad-ha'khlup etek prah ish-veh ek' settled satisfactory, heh concluded tor eku crabapples heh p'simmons. Etek vikau't olaya aishan gas'rak fa' ik, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' ek' kel'o i'. I vesh' glad wuh yut ish-veh sasarlah, nuh', fai'ei crabapples ain't ek'wak rom, heh wuh p'simmons wouldn't nam-tor piyah na' dahkuh il rehkuh tevun-krus wi. Etek pohshaya wuh masu-kushel, i' heh, yi ik prah abru nuh' lehkuh-mal svi' wuh asal il didn't hal-tor tor sar-tak lehkuh-mal hiyet svi' wuh khru. Nem-tor ish-veh ek' pauk, etek ha-tor takov pid. Wuh fifth mu-yor ne' st. Louis etek had wuh suk' sahriv po' midnight, k' wuh tepul t' rahm heh igen-wesh, heh wuh sov-masu mukau ne' svi' wuh huhtik thalv. Etek stayed svi' wuh wigwam heh kal-tor wuh marshak nem-tor tun t' itself. Lu wuh igen-wesh glared si' etek kupi gla-tor wuh suk' zehik pilash ahead, heh pid, rocky bluffs fi' fi' vla. K'-heh-k' leralmin-tor i, "hel-lo, jim, looky yonder!" ish-veh vesh' wuh steamboat ik had pustau herself fi' wuh kov. Etek vesh' drifting zehik ne' na' ish-veh. Wuh igen-wesh gluvau ish-veh maut natya. She vesh' leaning abru', k' krus t' ish-veh upper lan-tol abru' masu, heh du kupi gla-tor kanok pi' chimbly-sasu sok'i heh pa'shik, heh wuh ku-san k' wuh suk' kus-vakh, k' wuh hinek slouch taik hanging fi' wuh pla' t' ish-veh, lu wuh kahai sarlah. Muhl, ish-veh hasu maf svi' wuh mu-yor heh stormy, heh ek' ni mysterious-spo', i olau aishan wuh yut sovek vath sa-kan would wuh olau lu i gla-tor ik vashau laying tra' ni mournful heh lonesome svi' wuh svitan t' wuh pilash. I aitlu tor prah aboard t' ish-veh heh slink pa' wuh pi', heh gla-tor ra tra' vesh' tra'. Ni i leralmin-tor: "le's solektra fi' ish-veh, jim." tonk'peh jim vesh' tevik tehnat ish-veh palikauk. Au leralmin-tor: "i doan' aitlun tor hal-tor duhsu'n 'wu er rai wrack. Etek's doin' tenai' muhl, en etek weh-rom kal-tor tenai' muhl sa'awek, u' de rom dunap leralmin-tor. Spo' u' ri dey's wuh watchman fi' dat wrack." "watchman ish-veh ko'mekh-il, " i leralmin-tor; "tra' ain't nothing tor glantau tonk'peh wuh texas heh wuh hashsu-kelek; heh tor du reckon anybody's going tor resk ish-veh ha'kiv na' wuh texas heh wuh hashsu-kelek such wuh mu-yor u' nash, lu ish-veh's kesik tor shaya abru heh pu-tor ska' ne' wuh pilash sovek minute?" jim couldn't leralmin nothing tor ik, ni au didn't ar'kadan. "heh isha, " i leralmin-tor, "etek lau yahv-tor vel don having s' wuh khart-lan's stateroom. Seegars, i sihaya youand kodona kaukuh cents apiece, huhtik cash. Steamboat khart-lan nam-tor kwon-hau-ov don-ka, heh prah sheh-leh dollars wuh tevun-krus, heh au ri tor tun wuh cent ra wuh vel kodona-tor, du fai-tor, wu u' au aitlun ish-veh. Terpau wuh ha'fek svi' ish-veh abru'lik; i mokuhlek't shom, jim, till etek mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh rummaging. Tor du reckon tom sawyer would ek'wak hal-tor k' nash vel? Ri na' pie, au wouldn't. Au'd vutau ish-veh wuh adventurethat's ra au'd vutau ish-veh; heh au'd solektra fi' ik vashau kuv ish-veh vesh' ish-veh kim-shah bae'cok. Heh wouldn't au lehm style vi' ish-veh?wouldn't au sak-tor himself, il nothing? Po, du'd nah-tor ish-veh vesh' christopher c'lumbus discovering kingdom-sarlah. I istaya tom sawyer vesh' la'." jim au grumbled wuh pi', tonk'peh mazhiv-kur-tor svi'. Au leralmin-tor etek mustn't variben sovek weht do etek kupi gol'nev, heh yi variben mighty neik. Wuh igen-wesh gluvau etek wuh vashau va'ashiv aishan svi' wak, heh etek zaprah wuh stabboard aberofek, heh tor sahris tra'. Wuh lan-tol vesh' pid si' la'. Etek went sneaking ne' wuh vul t' ish-veh tor labboard, svi' wuh gu'gelik, na' wuh texas, olaya etwel yut vohris k' etwel ash'ya, heh spreading etwel el'ru si' tor fend ska' wuh sasu, na' ish-veh vesh' ni gu'gelik etek couldn't gla-tor rai glat t' au. Takov ak etek kwul-tor wuh fa'rak shaht t' wuh ha'gel-razh, heh clumb fi' tor ish-veh; heh wuh thurai ash zaprah etek svi' khom t' wuh khart-lan's svep, if vesh' tu'ash, heh k' jimminy, maf ne' k'fai wuh texas-tvur gla-tor etek wuh ta'hal! Heh ek' svi' wuh ka dahr etek seem tor zhu-tor neik spes svi' yonder! Jim zhal-tor heh leralmin-tor au vesh' olaya powerful has-bosh, heh var-tor me tor sarlah bi'. I leralmin-tor, ek' gas'rak, heh vesh' going tor palikaya na' wuh marshak; tonk'peh aishan yi i puzhu-tor wuh spes wail si' heh leralmin: "oh, sanoi ri tor, sa-kan; i swear i skil-tor't ek'wak var-tor!" wuh'ashiv spes leralmin-tor, takov ral: "ish-veh's wuh ti, jim turner. Du've bae'cok nash yut fa'. Du kwon-hau-ov aitlun weht'n ish-veh thresh t' wuh truck, heh du've kwon-hau-ov prah ish-veh, nuh', fai'ei du've swore 't kuv du didn't du'd var-tor. Tonk'peh nash wak du've leralmin-tor ish-veh jest veh wak nuh' wehk. Du're wuh meanest, treacherousest hound svi' nash shasol." k' nash wak jim vesh' hal-tor na' wuh marshak. I vesh' aishan wuh-biling k' curiosity; heh i leralmin-tor tor myself, tom sawyer wouldn't pla' si' i', heh ni i skil-tor't either; i'm wuh-going tor gla-tor ra's going fi' la'. Ni i eku-tor fi' t'nash-veh el'ru heh mal-nef svi' wuh pi' tvur, heh crept aft svi' wuh gu'gelik till tra' vikau't tonk'peh veh stateroom betwixt me heh wuh tuhs-tvur t' wuh texas. Yi svi' tra' gla-tor nash-veh wuh sasu sakadau fi' wuh lan-tol heh tied el'ru heh ash'ya, heh dahkuh sasu standing abru' ish-veh, heh veh t' au had wuh neik-ha'khlup makh-yonet svi' ish-veh el'ru, heh wuh vath veh had wuh el'ru-pohshayek. Nash-veh potau pointing wuh el'ru-pohshayek na' wuh sasu's patam fi' wuh lan-tol, heh taran: "i'd spo' tor! Heh i orter, tooa tvai skunk!" wuh sasu fi' wuh lan-tol would shrivel abru heh leralmin, "oh, sanoi ri tor, dun; i hain't ek'wak goin' tor var-tor." heh kanok wak au leralmin-tor ik wuh sasu k' wuh makh-yonet would abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh leralmin: "'deed du ain't! Du worla leralmin-tor rai truer vel 'n ik, du sihaya du." heh wuh'wak au leralmin-tor: "zhu-tor ish-veh eit'jae! Heh yit kuv etek hadn't prah wuh buhfik t' ish-veh heh tied ish-veh au'd wuh pustau etek fi'. Heh ra na'? Jist na' noth'n. Jist fai'ei etek lam-tor fi' etwel rightsthat's ra na'. Tonk'peh i ti du ain't wuh-goin' tor nan-tor kling sovek weht, jim turner. Shitau abru ik el'ru-pohshayek, dun." dun leralmin-tor: "i ri tor aitlun tor, jake packard. I'm na' killin' himand didn't au stau hinek hatfield jist wuh ka wayand ri tor au nazh ish-veh?" "tonk'peh i ri tor aitlun ish-veh pustau, heh i've prah t'nash-veh utvau na' ish-veh." "kudau yo' khaf-spol na' au zhit, jake packard! I'll worla forgit du wu's i ha-tor!" leralmin-tor wuh sasu fi' wuh lan-tol, wihfelau t' blubbering. Packard didn't nem-tor rai beglanau t' ik, tonk'peh geldau abru ish-veh makh-yonet fi' wuh felu heh palikau na' wilat i vesh' tra' svi' wuh gu'gelik, heh motioned dun tor sarlah. I crawfished u' sahris u' i kupi pa' dahkuh ker, tonk'peh wuh masu-hali vul-tor ni ik i couldn't tor maut rom wak; ni tor potau s' getting sahr-tor abru' heh catched i ukrau vi' wuh stateroom fi' wuh upper vla. Wuh sasu sarlah wuh-pawing bi' svi' wuh gu'gelik, heh lu packard prah tor t'nash-veh stateroom, au leralmin-tor: "herecome svi' la'." heh svi' au sarlah, heh dun po' ish-veh. Tonk'peh fa' au prah svi' i vesh' abru svi' wuh upper berth, cornered, heh sorry sarlah nash-veh. Yi au lam-tor tra', k' ish-veh el'ru fi' wuh ledge t' wuh berth, heh variben. I couldn't gla-tor au, tonk'peh i kupi var-tor wilat au vesh' k' wuh whisky au'd vesh' having. I vesh' glad i didn't mon whisky; tonk'peh ish-veh wouldn't tor mau natyan anyway, fai'ei danik t' wuh wak au couldn't wuh treed me fai'ei i didn't esh-tor. I vesh' nuh' pahth-tor. Heh, isha, wuh ak'shem couldn't esh-tor heh zhu-tor such variben. Au variben neik heh earnest. Dun aitlu tor stau turner. Au leralmin-tor: "au's leralmin-tor au'll var-tor, heh au dungi. Kuv etek vesh' tor mazhiv-kur-tor fi' etwel thresh-tor tor ish-veh i' ish-veh wouldn't tor rai natyan po' wuh zehl heh wuh yut etek've dvin-tor ish-veh. Gef's du're pukeshta, au'll da-tor fupa s''s evidence; i' du zhu-tor me. I'm na' putting ish-veh s' ish-veh troubles." "ni'm i, " leralmin-tor packard, maut hizhuk. "tenai ish-veh, i'd sorter palikau tor nah-tor du wasn't. Muhl, yi, ik's ek' gas'rak. Le's hal-tor heh tor ish-veh." "meskaraya fi' wuh minute; i hain't had t'nash-veh leralmin yit. Du shroi tor me. Shooting's rom, tonk'peh tra''s quieter yut kuv wuh vel's prah tor nam-tor ovsoh. Tonk'peh ra i leralmin nam-tor nash: ish-veh ain't rom kash-ral tor hal-tor kelek'n pa' po' wuh halter kuv du mokuhlek git na' ra du're abru tor svi' ein yut ik's jist u' rom heh na' wuh ka wak ri tor katau du vi' rai resks. Ain't ik ni?" "du sihaya ish-veh nam-tor. Tonk'peh uf du goin' tor khartau ish-veh nash wak?" "muhl, t'nash-veh idea nam-tor nash: etek'll rustle pa' heh hoknau abru whatever pickins etek've overlooked svi' wuh staterooms, heh shove na' gef heh ip-sut wuh truck. Yi etek'll bek-tor. I' i leralmin ish-veh ain't wuh-goin' tor nam-tor weht'n dahkuh wadan befo' nash wrack breaks abru heh pu-tor ska' ne' wuh pilash. Gla-tor? Au'll nam-tor drownded, heh skil-tor't ma kling tor tenai na' ish-veh tonk'peh ish-veh sha' shal. I reckon ik's wuh considerble glan weh-rom 'n killin' t' ish-veh. I'm unfavorable tor killin' wuh sasu u' wu u' du mokuhlek git aroun' ish-veh; ish-veh ain't rom kash-ral, ish-veh ain't rom morals. Ain't i gas'rak?" "ha, i reck'n du nam-tor. Tonk'peh s'pose she ri tor shaya abru heh pu-tor ska'?" "muhl, etek mokuhlek bek-tor wuh dahkuh wadan anyway heh gla-tor, mokuhlek't etek?" "ek' gas'rak, yi; sarlah bi'." ni au palikau, heh i lit si', ek' svi' wuh samu wadashaya, heh parish-tor fa'rak. Ish-veh vesh' gu'gelik u' ralash tra'; tonk'peh i leralmin-tor, svi' wuh ves t' wuh dirik zhal, "jim!" heh au kilko-tor abru, gas'rak na' t'nash-veh kar-nef, k' wuh wihfelau t' wuh naya, heh i leralmin-tor: "sahris, jim, ish-veh ain't rai wak na' fooling pa' heh moaning; tra''s wuh gang t' murderers svi' yonder, heh kuv etek ri tor shi'kar abru ish-veh masu-hali heh eku ish-veh drifting ne' wuh pilash ni aifa katravahsu mokuhlek't prah maf s' wuh vashau tra''s veh t' 'em going tor nam-tor svi' wuh rasahkos teslau. Tonk'peh kuv etek talal ish-veh masu-hali etek mokuhlek shitau ek' t' 'em svi' wuh rasahkos fixfor wuh sheriff 'll prah 'em. Quickhurry! I'll shi'kar wuh labboard vla, du shi'kar wuh stabboard. Du palikaya na' wuh marshak, heh" "oh, t'nash-veh lordy, lordy! Raf'? Dey ain' rai raf' rai mo'; she ovsoh shau thal en hal-tor ien la' etek nam-tor!" chapter xiii. Muhl, i catched t'nash-veh esh heh danik fainted. Ikap'uh t'du ru'lut fi' wuh vashau k' such wuh gang u' ik! Tonk'peh ish-veh vikau't rai wak tor nam-tor sentimentering. Etek'd prah tor talal ik masu-hali nowhad ki' ish-veh na' ourselves. Ni etek went wuh-quaking heh shaking ne' wuh stabboard vla, heh vohris ar'kadan ish-veh vesh', tooseemed wuh wehk gad fa' etek prah tor wuh harr-krus. Rai glat t' wuh masu-hali. Jim leralmin-tor au didn't dva-tor au kupi hal-tor sovek furtherso pahth-tor au hadn't hardly sovek karik'es losrak, au leralmin-tor. Tonk'peh i leralmin-tor, sarlah fi', kuv etek prah losrak fi' nash vashau etek nam-tor svi' wuh teslau, sure. Ni fi' etek prowled va'ashiv. Etek kwul-tor na' wuh harr-krus t' wuh texas, heh afer-tor ish-veh, heh yi scrabbled bi' fa'rak fi' wuh ha'gel-razh, hanging fi' s' fe-wein tor fe-wein, na' wuh rihk t' wuh ha'gel-razh vesh' svi' wuh masu. Lu etek prah takov beyik wuh tuhs-tvur svep, tra' vesh' wuh skiff, sure hiyet! I kupi aishan barely gla-tor ish-veh. I olau ek'wak ni itar-bosh. Svi' wuh'ashiv dahr i would wuh vesh' aboard t' ish-veh, tonk'peh aishan yi wuh svep tu'ash. Veh t' wuh sasu terpau ish-veh patam si' goh pa' wuh couple t' ash'ya s' me, heh i nahp i vesh' hal-tor; tonk'peh au hutau ish-veh svi' va'ashiv, heh leralmin-tor: "heave ik tenai makh-yonet si' o' glan, dun!" au flung wuh sa'haf t' vel vi' wuh masu-hali, heh yi prah svi' himself heh eku ne'. Ish-veh vesh' packard. Yi dun au sasarlah heh prah svi'. Packard leralmin-tor, svi' wuh neik spes: "ek' readyshove ska'!" i couldn't hardly geldau fi' tor wuh fe-wein, i vesh' ni kobat. Tonk'peh dun leralmin-tor: "meskaraya fi''d du hal-tor k'fai ish-veh?" "rai. Didn't du?" "rai. Ni au's prah ish-veh thresh o' wuh cash wi." "muhl, yi, sarlah bi'; rai nam-tor-tor tor nem-tor truck heh trasha donku." "leralmin, skil-tor't au suspicion ra etek're abru tor?" "sos'eh au skil-tor't. Tonk'peh etek prah ki' ish-veh anyway. Sarlah bi'." ni au prah si' heh went svi'. Wuh svep slammed tor fai'ei ish-veh vesh' fi' wuh careened vla; heh svi' wuh ulef dahr i vesh' svi' wuh masu-hali, heh jim sarlah tumbling po' me. I si' k' t'nash-veh lipau heh tresahk wuh man-elakh, heh maf etek went! Etek didn't esta wuh fel, heh etek didn't stariben il zhal, il hardly kauk esh-tor. Etek went gliding swift bi', tevik ralash-fam, vesht wuh um t' wuh paddle-natuhn, heh vesht wuh harr-krus; yi svi' wuh dahr il dahkuh weht etek vesh' wuh hundred ker ne' wuh vashau, heh wuh mu'khlup'es soaked ish-veh abru, kanok kim-shah glat t' ish-veh, heh etek vesh' safe, heh knowed ish-veh. Lu etek vesh' rehkuh il kehkuh hundred ker ne'-pilash gla-tor etek wuh makh-yonet gluvaya spo' wuh pi' kil na' wuh texas svep na' wuh dahr, heh etek knowed k' ik ik wuh rascals had din-tor ish-veh masu-hali, heh vesh' palikaya tor ken-tor ik au vesh' svi' aishan u' mau trouble i' u' jim turner vesh'. Yi jim manned wuh fel, heh etek nem-tor si' po' etwel marshak. I' vesh' wuh wuh'rak wak ik i palikau tor worry pa' wuh meni reckon i hadn't had wak tor fa'. I palikau tor nah-tor uf dreadful ish-veh vesh', kauk na' murderers, tor nam-tor svi' such wuh teslau. I leralmin-tor tor myself, tra' ain't rai telling tonk'peh i lau sarlah tor nam-tor wuh murderer myself wi, heh yi uf would i spo' ish-veh?
