Ni leralmin-tor i tor jim: "wuh wuh'rak ta'hal gla-tor etek etek'll solektra wuh hundred ker ne' ish-veh il abru' ish-veh, svi' wuh shi wilat ish-veh's wuh rom hiding-shi na' du heh wuh skiff, heh yi i'll hal-tor heh teslau abru ein ves t' wuh yarn, heh prah somebody tor hal-tor na' ik gang heh prah au s' ish-veh theshau, ni au mokuhlek nam-tor geldau lu ish-veh wak sarlah." tonk'peh ik idea vesh' wuh vravshaya; na' takov ak ish-veh palikau tor sahriv va'ashiv, heh nash wak weh-rasahkos do ek'wak. Wuh sov-masu mukau ne', heh worla wuh ta'hal gluvau; kanok-veh svi' sar-tak, i reckon. Etek orkau bi' ne' wuh pilash, watching na' ha'ge heh watching na' etwel marshak. Po' wuh akarshif wuh sov-masu kal-tor abru, tonk'peh wuh wan stayed, heh wuh igen-wesh potau whimpering, heh k'-heh-k' wuh kahai gluvau etek wuh nesh-kur vel ahead, floating, heh etek tor na' ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' wuh marshak, heh mighty glad vesh' etek tor prah aboard t' ish-veh va'ashiv. Etek gla-tor wuh ta'hal i' maf ne' tor wuh gas'rak, fi' gef. Ni i leralmin-tor i would hal-tor na' ish-veh. Wuh skiff vesh' ulef bosh t' plunder if ik gang had vazgau tra' fi' wuh vashau. Etek hustled ish-veh fi' tor wuh marshak svi' wuh tuh, heh i var-tor jim tor marek bi' ne', heh gluvaya wuh ta'hal lu au judged au had hal-tor pa' dahkuh mile, heh potau ish-veh yontau till sarlah nash-veh; yi i manned t'nash-veh fel heh shoved na' wuh ta'hal. U' i prah ne' na' ish-veh, rehkuh il kehkuh weht showedup fi' wuh hillside. Ish-veh vesh' wuh pi'kahr. I a'ing svi' abru' wuh gef ta'hal, heh laid fi' t'nash-veh fel heh markau. U' i went k', gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh vesh' wuh makh-yonet hanging fi' wuh jackstaff t' wuh dahtau-vukh mes-hali-masu-hali. I skimmed pa' na' wuh watchman, wuh-wondering whereabouts au yuk-tor; heh k'-heh-k' i afer-tor ish-veh roosting fi' wuh bitts, fa'rak, k' ish-veh patam ne' svi' ish-veh mal-nef. I mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tipan dahkuh il rehkuh pi' shoves, heh palikau tor maf. Au stirred abru, svi' wuh ves t' wuh startlish yut; tonk'peh lu au gla-tor ish-veh vesh' goh me, au nem-tor wuh rom haf heh sakadaya, heh yi au leralmin-tor: "tonk'peh, ra's abru? Ri tor maf, bub. Ra's wuh trouble?" i leralmin-tor: "pap, heh mam, heh sis, heh" yi i shau ne'. Au leralmin-tor: "oh, dang ish-veh i', ri tor nem-tor fi' ni; etek ek' has ki' etwel troubles, heh nash'n 'll sasarlah ek' gas'rak. Ra's wuh tukh k' 'em?" "au'rethey'reare du wuh watchman t' wuh masu-hali?" "ha, " au leralmin-tor, ves t' takov-muhl-satisfied spo'. "i'm wuh khart-lan heh wuh owner heh wuh katelau heh wuh hashsu heh watchman heh patam lan-tol-el'ru; heh sometimes i'm wuh freight heh passengers. I ain't u' don-ka u' hinek jim hornback, heh i mokuhlek't nam-tor ni tenai' generous heh rom tor tom, dick heh harry u' ra au nam-tor, heh slam pa' donku wuh yut au tor; tonk'peh i've var-tor ish-veh wuh wehk wuh wak 't i wouldn't trade shitau k' ish-veh; na', leralmin-tor i, wuh masusu's ha'kiv's wuh ha'kiv na' me, heh i'm derned kuv i'd ha-tor dahkuh mile si' o' kahr, wilat tra' ain't nothing ek'wak goin' fi', ri na' ek' ish-veh spondulicks heh u' mau weht fi-tor ish-veh. Leralmin-tor i" i shau svi' heh leralmin-tor: "au're svi' wuh awful peck t' trouble, heh" "vi nam-tor?" "po, pap heh mam heh sis heh din-tor hooker; heh kuv du'd nem-tor ish-veh mes-hali-masu-hali heh hal-tor abru tra'" "abru wilat? Wilat nam-tor au?" "fi' wuh vashau." "ra vashau?" "po, tra' ain't tonk'peh veh." "ra, du ri tor tvai wuh walter scott?" "ha." "rom solektra! Ra nam-tor au doin' tra', na' gracious sakes?" "muhl, au didn't hal-tor tra' wuh-lof." "i sihaya au didn't! Po, lo'uk goodness, tra' ain't rai pavesh na' 'em kuv au ri tor git ska' mighty sahris! Po, uf svi' wuh shashol did au ek'wak git vi' such wuh theshau?" "hagik hiyet. Din-tor hooker vesh' wuh-visiting abru tra' tor wuh kahr" "ha, booth's landinggo fi'." "she vesh' wuh-visiting tra' na' booth's landing, heh aishan svi' wuh rihk t' wuh khru she palikau abru' k' ish-veh nigger kosu svi' wuh jarel-mes-hali tor stay ek' mu-yor na' ish-veh t'hy'la's kelek, din-tor ra-du-lau-vutau-ish-veh i disremember ish-veh nameand au pakik ish-veh steering-fel, heh swung pa' heh went wuh-floating ne', harr-krus wuh'rak, pa' dahkuh mile, heh saddle-baggsed fi' wuh vashau, heh wuh ferryman heh wuh nigger kosu heh wuh jarel vesh' ek' pakik, tonk'peh din-tor hooker she tor wuh runem heh prah aboard wuh vashau. Muhl, pa' wuh wadan po' gu'gelik sarlah etek bi' ne' svi' etwel trading-scow, heh ish-veh vesh' ni gu'gelik etek didn't beglanau wuh vashau till etek vesh' gas'rak fi' ish-veh; heh ni etek saddle-baggsed; tonk'peh ek' t' etek vesh' korsau tonk'peh dun whippleand oh, au vesh' wuh buhfik cretur!i danik istaya't ish-veh had vesh' me, i tor." "t'nash-veh george! Ish-veh's wuh beatenest vel i ek'wak kwul-tor. Heh yi ra did du ek' tor?" "muhl, etek hollered heh nem-tor fi', tonk'peh ish-veh's ni eik tra' etek couldn't tor kling zhu-tor. Ni pap leralmin-tor somebody prah tor prah ashore heh prah gol'nev somehow. I vesh' wuh goh veh ik kupi mahal-tor, ni i tor wuh dash na' ish-veh, heh din-tor hooker she leralmin-tor kuv i didn't kwul gol'nev sooner, sarlah la' heh shi'kar abru ish-veh sa-kuk, heh au'd teslau wuh vel. I tor wuh solektra pa' wuh mile ne', heh vesh' fooling bi' ek'wak opi', trying tor prah sutra tor tor vel, tonk'peh au leralmin-tor, 'ra, svi' such wuh mu-yor heh such wuh current? Tra' ain't rai kash-ral svi' ish-veh; hal-tor na' wuh zhis mes-hali.' i' kuv du'll hal-tor heh" "k' jackson, i'd spo' tor, heh, tenai ish-veh, i ri tor fai-tor tonk'peh i dungi; tonk'peh vi svi' wuh dingnation's wuh-going' tor vlitau na' ish-veh? Tor du reckon ish-veh pap" "po ik's ek' gas'rak. Din-tor hooker she tole me, particular, ik ish-veh sa-kuk hornback" "lo'uk pohshayek! Nam-tor au ish-veh sa-kuk? Looky la', du shaya na' ik ta'hal abru' yonder-yut, heh da-tor si' tev'rak lu du git tra', heh pa' wuh yonuk t' wuh mile si' du'll sarlah tor wuh tavern; var-tor 'em tor kli du si' tor jim hornback's, heh au'll ash'ya wuh dun. Heh ri tor du duhsu pa' sovek, fai'ei au'll aitlun tor fai-tor wuh ro'fori. Var-tor ish-veh i'll ma ish-veh ko-bath ek' safe fa' au mokuhlek prah tor kahr. Hump yourself, i'; i'm wuh-going abru pa' wuh teruk la' tor roust si' t'nash-veh mishek." i kwul-tor na' wuh ta'hal, tonk'peh u' ak u' au da-tor wuh teruk i went pla' heh prah vi' t'nash-veh skiff heh bailed ish-veh si', heh yi seshau abru gef svi' wuh hagik masu pa' shehkuh hundred ker, heh k'hy-tor myself svi' among ein woodboats; na' i couldn't shom hagik till kupi gla-tor nash-veh wuh mes-hali-masu-hali palikaya. Tonk'peh nem-tor ish-veh ek' pa', i vesh' olaya ruther kel'o fi' khrosahp t' taking ek' nash trouble na' ik gang, na' ri wehk would wuh ovsoh ish-veh. I istau wuh kir'an knowed pa' ish-veh. I judged she would nam-tor yaut t' me na' helping aifa rapscallions, fai'ei rapscallions heh tevik kuhsh-tor nam-tor wuh ves wuh kir'an heh rom sutra nem-tor wuh danik eku'ko svi'. Muhl, fa' wu, la' sarlah wuh vashau, neik-ha'khlup heh dusky, sliding bi' ne'! Wuh ves t' samu shiver went k'fai me, heh yi i kwul-tor si' na' ish-veh. She vesh' maut glu, heh gla-tor nash-veh svi' wuh minute tra' vikau't mau pavesh na' anybody hasu alive svi' ish-veh. I seshau ek' pa' ish-veh heh hollered wuh pi', tonk'peh tra' wasn't sovek kilko-srashiv; ek' tevik fam dvun. I olau wuh pi' zeshau ras-hearted pa' wuh gang, tonk'peh ri mau, na' i reckoned kuv au kupi lamok ish-veh, i kupi. Yi la' sarlah wuh mes-hali-masu-hali; ni i shoved na' wuh svitan t' wuh pilash fi' wuh wu ne'-pilash vul; heh lu i judged i vesh' s' bezhun-pulau, i laid fi' t'nash-veh fel, heh glazhau pla' heh gla-tor ish-veh hal-tor heh fnish-tor pa' wuh vashau na' din-tor hooker's hafayat, fai'ei wuh khart-lan would fai-tor ish-veh sa-kuk hornback would aitlun au; heh yi takov ak wuh mes-hali-masu-hali mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh abru heh went na' wuh gef, heh i laid vi' t'nash-veh ar'kadan heh went wuh-booming ne' wuh pilash. Ish-veh did seem wuh powerful akarshif fa' jim's ta'hal gluvau abru; heh lu ish-veh did gluvaya, ish-veh glazhau spo' ish-veh vesh' wuh thousand mile ska'. K' wuh wak i prah tra' wuh igen vesh' palikaya tor prah wuh pi' zhai-kur svi' wuh she'rak; ni etek kwul-tor na' wuh vikuvtra, heh ip-sut wuh marshak, heh ne'hal-tor wuh skiff, heh da-tor svi' heh yuk-tor spo' tevik sutra. Chapter xiv. K'-heh-k', lu etek prah abru, etek da-tor abru' wuh truck wuh gang had vazgau ska' t' wuh vashau, heh afer-tor kluf, heh yuk-sai, heh sai-vel, heh ek' wihfelau t' vath vel, heh wuh lot t' dunap, heh wuh spyglass, heh rehkuh natuhn t' seegars. Etek hadn't ek'wak vesh' nash don-ka fa' svi' neither t' etwel ha-tor. Wuh seegars vesh' nenat. Etek laid ska' ek' wuh aru svi' wuh lapan talking, heh me telvan wuh dunap, heh having wuh paik rom wak. I var-tor jim ek' pa' ra pavesh-tor svi'udish wuh vashau heh na' wuh mes-hali-masu-hali, heh i leralmin-tor aifa ves t' vel vesh' adventures; tonk'peh au leralmin-tor au didn't aitlun rai weht adventures. Au leralmin-tor ik lu i went svi' wuh texas heh au ukrau pla' tor prah fi' wuh marshak heh afer-tor ish-veh hal-tor, au nearly tev-tor; fai'ei au judged ish-veh vesh' ek' abru k' ish-veh, anyway ish-veh kupi nam-tor teslau; na' kuv au didn't prah korsau au would prah drownded; heh kuv au did prah korsau, whoever korsau ish-veh would satau ish-veh pla' ha-kel ni u' tor prah wuh reward, heh yi din-tor watson would makau ish-veh khu'rak, sure. Muhl, au vesh' gas'rak; au vesh' danik kwon-hau-ov gas'rak; au had wuh uncommon volik patam, na' wuh nigger. I telv-tor considerable tor jim pa' sa-te'kru heh dukes heh earls heh such, heh uf gaudy au sai-vel-tor, heh uf mau style au shitau fi', heh puvutau tik vath ish-veh majesty, heh ish-veh takov, heh ish-veh lordship, heh ni fi', 'stead t' mister; heh jim's bezhun smertau si', heh au vesh' interested. Au leralmin-tor: "i didn' fai-tor dey vesh' ni wehk un um. I hain't hearn 'bout rim un um, skasely, tonk'peh ole sa-te'kru sollermun, onless du tum-tor dem sa-te'kru dat's svi' wuh sa'haf er k'ker. Uf mau tor wuh sa-te'kru git?" "prah?" i leralmin-tor; "po, au prah wuh thousand dollars wuh tevun-krus kuv au aitlun ish-veh; au mokuhlek ma aishan u' mau u' au aitlun; kanok-vei t' au." "ain' dat sa-ka-ashausu? En ra dey prah tor tor, huck?" "au ri tor tor nothing! Po, uf du variben! Au aishan eku pa'." "rai; nam-tor dat ni?" "veling ish-veh nam-tor. Au aishan eku aroundexcept, sos'eh, lu tra''s wuh t'naehm; yi au hal-tor tor wuh t'naehm. Tonk'peh vath wak au aishan kas'el pa'; il hal-tor hawkingjust hawking heh sp sh!d' du zhu-tor wuh ralash?" etek skipped si' heh glazhau; tonk'peh ish-veh vikau't nothing tonk'peh wuh nuv t' wuh steamboat's halek maf ne', coming pa' wuh sfek; ni sarlah etek pla'. "ha, " leralmin-tor i, "heh vath wak, lu vel nam-tor pasik, au fuss k' wuh parlyment; heh kuv kanok-veh ri tor hal-tor aishan ni au whacks ish-veh patam ska'. Tonk'peh mostly au geldau pauk wuh harem." "roun' de if?" "harem." "ra's de harem?" "wuh shi wilat au potau ish-veh ko-telsu. Ri tor du fai-tor pa' wuh harem? Solomon had veh; au had pa' wuh million ko-telsu." "po, ha, dat's ni; ii'd ovsoh forgot ish-veh. Wuh harem's wuh bo'd'n-kelek, i reck'n. Mos' kesik dey has rackety wak svi' de nussery. En i reck'n de ko-telsu quarrels considable; en dat 'crease de racket. Yit dey leralmin sollermun de wises' sasu dat ek'wak ha-tor'. I doan' nem-tor rai fek svi' dat. Bekase po: would wuh kau-bosh sasu aitlun tor ha-tor svi' de mids' er sich wuh blim-blammin' ek' de wak? Rai'deed au wouldn't. Wuh kau-bosh sasu 'ud nem-tor en buil' wuh biler-factry; en den au kupi shet ne' de biler-factry lu au aitlun tor res'." "muhl, tonk'peh au vesh' wuh wisest sasu, anyway; fai'ei wuh kir'an she var-tor me ni, ish-veh sha' shal." "i doan k'yer ra de widder leralmin, au vikau't rai kau-bosh sasu nuther. Au had ein er de dad-fetchedes' yut i ek'wak gla-tor. Tor du fai-tor 'bout dat chile dat au 'uz gwyne tor chop svi' dahkuh?" "ha, wuh kir'an var-tor me ek' pa' ish-veh." "muhl, den! Vikau' dat de beatenes' notion svi' de worl'? Du jes' nem-tor en glazhau na' ish-veh wuh minute. Dah's de stump, dahdat's veh er de kosu; heah's youdat's de yuther veh; i's sollermun; en dish yer dollar dun's de chile. Bofe un du claims ish-veh. Ra tor i tor? Tor i ne-mal aroun' mongs' de behsu en tok-ti si' if un du de dun tor b'wu tor, en han' ish-veh abru' tor de gas'rak veh, ek' safe en soun', de yut dat anybody dat had sovek gumption would? Rai; i nem-tor en whack de dun svi' dahkuh, en mazhiv-kur-tor ulef un ish-veh tor du, en de yuther ulef tor de yuther kosu. Dat's de yut sollermun vesh' gwyne tor tor wid de chile. I' i aitlun tor ast du: ra's de nam-tor-tor er dat ulef wuh dun?mokuhlek't mahr-tor noth'n wid ish-veh. En ra nam-tor-tor nam-tor wuh ulef wuh chile? I wouldn' mazhiv-kur-tor wuh dern na' wuh million un um." "tonk'peh geldau ish-veh, jim, du've sok'i din-tor wuh pointblame ish-veh, du've din-tor ish-veh wuh thousand mile." "vi? Me? Hal-tor 'wu. Doan' variben tor me 'bout yo' pints. I reck'n i fai-tor kash-ral lu i gla-tor ish-veh; en dey ain' rai kash-ral svi' sich doin's u' dat. De 'spute vikau't 'bout wuh ulef wuh chile, de 'spute vesh' 'bout wuh bosh chile; en de sasu dat nah-tor au pi-maat settle wuh 'spute 'bout wuh bosh chile wid wuh ulef wuh chile doan' fai-tor hiyet tor sarlah svi' si''n de sov-masu. Doan' variben tor me 'bout sollermun, huck, i fai-tor ish-veh k' de pla'." "tonk'peh i var-tor du du ri tor prah wuh sfek." "tenai de sfek! I reck'n i fai-tor ra i fai-tor. En t'nash-veh du, de yeht pint nam-tor ne' furderit's ne' deeper. Ish-veh ti svi' de yut sollermun vesh' ashenau. Du nem-tor wuh sasu dat's prah fi''y veh il dahkuh chillen; nam-tor dat sasu gwyne tor nam-tor waseful o' chillen? Rai, au ain't; au mokuhlek't 'masmezh ish-veh. Au fai-tor uf tor tala 'em. Tonk'peh du nem-tor wuh sasu dat's prah 'bout kaukuh million chillen runnin' roun' de kelek, en ish-veh's diffunt. Au u' ak chop wuh chile svi' dahkuh u' wuh aushfa. Dey's plenty mo'. Wuh chile er dahkuh, mo' er lehkuh, vikau't rai consekens tor sollermun, dad fatch ish-veh!" i worla gla-tor such wuh nigger. Kuv au prah wuh notion svi' ish-veh patam wuh'wak, tra' vikau't rai getting ish-veh si' va'ashiv. Au vesh' wuh danik ne' fi' solomon t' sovek nigger i ek'wak gla-tor. Ni i went tor talking pa' vath sa-te'kru, heh kal-tor solomon zish-tor. I var-tor pa' louis sixteenth ik prah ish-veh patam tresahk ska' svi' france akarshif ago; heh pa' ish-veh pi' sa-kan wuh dolphin, ik would wuh vesh' wuh sa-te'kru, tonk'peh au nem-tor heh ikap-tor ish-veh abru svi' potau-tvi-shal, heh ein leralmin au tev-tor tra'. "po' pi' chap." "tonk'peh ein leralmin-tor au prah si' heh prah maf, heh sarlah tor america." "dat's rom! Tonk'peh au'll nam-tor pooty lonesomedey ain' rai sa-te'kru la', nam-tor dey, huck?" "rai." "den au cain't git rai situation. Ra au gwyne tor tor?" "muhl, i ri tor fai-tor. Ein t' au prah fi' wuh police, heh ein t' au oren-tor sutra uf tor variben french." "po, huck, doan' de french sutra variben de ka yut etek tor?" "rai, jim; du couldn't ken-tor wuh zhit au saidnot wuh single zhit." "muhl, i', i nam-tor ding-busted! Uf tor dat sarlah?" "i ri tor fai-tor; tonk'peh ish-veh's ni. I prah ein t' ish-veh jabber s' wuh dunap. S'pose wuh sasu vesh' tor sarlah tor du heh leralmin polly-voo-franzywhat would du nah-tor?" "i wouldn' nah-tor nuff'n; i'd nem-tor en bust ish-veh abru' de headdat nam-tor, kuv au vikau't wan-kur. I wouldn't 'neik rai nigger tor vutau me dat." "shucks, ish-veh ain't calling du sovek-vel. Ish-veh's goh taran, tor du fai-tor uf tor variben french?" "muhl, den, po couldn't au leralmin ish-veh?" "po, au nam-tor wuh-taran ish-veh. Ik's wuh frenchman's yut t' taran ish-veh." "muhl, ish-veh's wuh tenai ridicklous yut, en i doan' aitlun tor zhu-tor rai mo' 'bout ish-veh. Dey ain' rai kash-ral svi' ish-veh." "looky la', jim; tor wuh aushfa variben spo' etek tor?" "rai, wuh aushfa ri tor." "muhl, tor wuh aushfa?" "rai, wuh aushfa ri tor, nuther." "tor wuh aushfa variben spo' wuh aushfa, il wuh aushfa variben spo' wuh aushfa?" "rai, dey ri tor." "ish-veh's malatik heh gas'rak na' 'em tor variben natya s' tik vath, ain't ish-veh?" "'rivak." "heh ain't ish-veh malatik heh gas'rak na' wuh aushfa heh wuh aushfa tor variben natya s' etek?" "po, mos' sholy ish-veh nam-tor." "muhl, yi, po ain't ish-veh malatik heh gas'rak na' wuh frenchman tor variben natya s' etek? Du kilko-srashiv me ik." "nam-tor wuh aushfa wuh sasu, huck?" "rai." "muhl, den, dey ain't rai kash-ral svi' wuh aushfa talkin' spo' wuh sasu. Nam-tor wuh aushfa wuh sasu?er nam-tor wuh aushfa wuh aushfa?" "rai, she ain't either t' au." "muhl, den, she ain't prah rai business tor variben spo' either veh er wuh yuther t' 'em. Nam-tor wuh frenchman wuh sasu?" "ha." "muhl, den! Dad tenai ish-veh, po doan' au variben spo' wuh sasu? Du kilko-srashiv me dat!" gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh vikau't rai nam-tor-tor wasting wordsyou mokuhlek't oren-tor wuh nigger tor gyirm'i. Ni i quit. Chapter xv. Etek judged ik rehkuh mu-yor weht would zaprah etek tor cairo, na' wuh lanet t' illinois, wilat wuh ohio pilash sarlah svi', heh ik vesh' ra etek vesh' po'. Etek would makau wuh marshak heh prah fi' wuh steamboat heh hal-tor yut abru wuh ohio svi' wuh elik fupa s', heh yi nam-tor s' trouble. Muhl, wuh dahr mu-yor wuh ihsek palikau tor sarlah fi', heh etek tor na' wuh tow-patam tor tie tor, na' ish-veh wouldn't tor tor ar'kadan tor sahr-tor svi' wuh ihsek; tonk'peh lu i paddled ahead svi' wuh canoe, k' wuh zehl tor tor sahris, tra' vikau't sovek-vel tonk'peh pi' kan-lap tor tie tor. I be' dvun-tor wuh zehl pa' veh t' au gas'rak fi' wuh rihk t' wuh tresahk kutra, tonk'peh tra' vesh' wuh stegel current, heh wuh marshak sarlah booming ne' ni lively she tore ish-veh si' k' wuh gir heh maf she went. Gla-tor nash-veh wuh ihsek ikapik ne', heh ish-veh tor me ni has-bosh heh pahth-tor i couldn't budge na' danik wuh ulef wuh minute ish-veh seemed tor meand yi tra' vikau't rai marshak svi' glan; du couldn't gla-tor dah-leh ker. I spen-tor vi' wuh canoe heh sahr-tor pla' tor wuh harr-krus, heh runem-tor wuh paddle heh eku ish-veh pla' wuh shad-kisheya. Tonk'peh she didn't sarlah. I vesh' svi' such wuh brax i hadn't untied ish-veh. I prah abru heh ar'kada tor untie ish-veh, tonk'peh i vesh' ni teporilau t'nash-veh el'ru hutau ni i couldn't hardly tor sovek-vel k' au. U' ak u' i prah palikau i nem-tor si' po' wuh marshak, fal heh ras, gas'rak ne' wuh tow-patam. Ik vesh' ek' gas'rak u' irak u' ish-veh went, tonk'peh wuh tow-patam vikau't sheh-leh ker wu, heh wuh minute i flew k' wuh ash'ya t' ish-veh i pohshaya si' vi' wuh huhtik wan-kur ihsek, heh hadn't rai weht idea if yut i vesh' going do wuh tevik sasu. Nah-tor i, ish-veh skil-tor't tor tor paddle; wuh'rak i fai-tor i'll sahr-tor vi' wuh kutra il wuh tow-patam il vel; i prah tor eku fam dvun heh marek, heh wi ish-veh's mighty fidgety business ki' tor meskaraya ish-veh el'ru fam dvun na' such wuh wak. I whooped heh shroi. Maf ne' tra' somewheres i zhu-tor wuh pi' whoop, heh abru sarlah t'nash-veh tam'a. I went tearing po' ish-veh, listening nasik tor zhu-tor ish-veh va'ashiv. Wuh thurai wak ish-veh sarlah, gla-tor nash-veh i vikau't heading na' ish-veh, tonk'peh heading maf tor wuh gas'rak t' ish-veh. Heh wuh thurai wak i vesh' heading maf tor wuh losrak t' itand ri gaining fi' ish-veh mau either, na' i vesh' hashan pa', nash yut heh ik heh t'vath, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' going zehik ahead ek' wuh wak. I did istaya wuh duhsu would nah-tor tor kuhsh-tor wuh zhai-tukh sunil, heh kuhsh-tor ish-veh ek' wuh wak, tonk'peh au worla did, heh ish-veh vesh' wuh fam dvun shitau svi' wuh whoops ik vesh' tor wuh trouble na' me. Muhl, i fought bi', heh directly i zhu-tor wuh whoop za' me. I vesh' tangled rom i'. Ik vesh' somebody else's whoop, il else i vesh' da-tor pa'. I throwed wuh paddle ne'. I puzhu-tor wuh whoop va'ashiv; ish-veh vesh' za' me wi, tonk'peh svi' wuh natya shi; ish-veh potau coming, heh potau rubai its shi, heh i potau answering, till k'-heh-k' ish-veh vesh' svi' khom t' me va'ashiv, heh i knowed wuh current had swung wuh canoe's patam ne'-pilash, heh i vesh' ek' gas'rak kuv ik vesh' jim heh ri ein vath raftsman hollering. I couldn't var-tor nothing pa' spes svi' wuh ihsek, na' nothing ri tor glazhau malatik il ralash malatik svi' wuh ihsek. Wuh whooping went fi', heh svi' pa' wuh minute sarlah nash-veh wuh-booming ne' fi' wuh tresahk kutra k' smoky tam'a t' suk' lap fi' ish-veh, heh wuh current throwed me ska' tor wuh losrak heh pohshaya k', svi' wuh lot t' snags ik fairly roared, wuh currrent vesh' tearing k' au ni swift. Svi' wuh'ashiv dahr il dahkuh ish-veh vesh' huhtik wan-kur heh fam dvun va'ashiv. I eku perfectly fam dvun yi, listening tor t'nash-veh khaf-spol thump, heh i reckon i didn't bes-tor wuh esh du' ish-veh thumped wuh hundred. I aishan mazhiv-kur-tor abru yi. I knowed ra wuh tukh vesh'. Ik tresahk kutra vesh' wuh vikuvtra, heh jim had hal-tor ne' t'vath vla t' ish-veh. Ish-veh vikau't rai tow-patam ik du kupi marek k' svi' lehkuh minutes. Ish-veh had wuh suk' lap-tukh t' wuh regular vikuvtra; ish-veh lau nam-tor kaukuh il shehkuh miles wu heh weht do ulef wuh mile eik. I potau hizhuk, k' t'nash-veh kaluk cocked, pa' leh-kau minutes, i reckon. I vesh' floating bi', veling, kehkuh il kaukuh miles wuh wadan; tonk'peh du ri tor ek'wak nah-tor t' ik. Rai, du olau spo' du nam-tor laying tevik fam dvun fi' wuh masu; heh kuv wuh pi' glimpse t' wuh snag trel-tor k' du ri tor nah-tor tor yourself uf sahris du're going, tonk'peh du kum ish-veh esh heh nah-tor, t'nash-veh! Uf ik snag's tearing bi'. Kuv du nah-tor ish-veh ain't dismal heh lonesome si' svi' wuh ihsek ik yut k' yourself svi' wuh mu-yor, du ar'kadan ish-veh onceyou'll gla-tor. Thurai, na' pa' wuh ulef wuh wadan, i whoops i' heh yi; na' kim-shah i zhu-tor wuh kilko-srashiv wuh wu yut ska', heh ar'kada tor zahal-tor ish-veh, tonk'peh i couldn't tor ish-veh, heh directly i judged i'd prah vi' wuh ha-kel t' tow-patam, na' i had pi' neik-ha'khlup glimpses t' au fi' fi' vla t' mesometimes aishan wuh wonil mashyut svi', heh ein ik i couldn't gla-tor i knowed vesh' tra' fai'ei i'd zhu-tor wuh pu-tor t' wuh current tehnat wuh hinek tevik achut heh guhsh ik geldau abru' wuh kutra. Muhl, i vikau't wu loosing wuh whoops ne' svi' wuh tow-patam; heh i goh ar'kada tor a'vesh' au wuh pi' du', anyway, fai'ei ish-veh vesh' weh-rasahkos do chasing wuh jack-o'-makh-yonet. Du worla knowed wuh ralash sayutau pa' ni, heh swap shitau ni sahris heh ni mau. I had tor spahk maf s' wuh kutra takov lively kehkuh il kaukuh wak, tor potau s' knocking wuh vikuvtra s' wuh pilash; heh ni i judged wuh marshak bolau nam-tor butting vi' wuh kutra kanok i' heh yi, il else ish-veh would prah further ahead heh pa'shik s' hearingit vesh' floating wuh pi' faster do ra i vesh'. Muhl, i seemed tor nam-tor svi' wuh tu'ash pilash va'ashiv k'-heh-k', tonk'peh i couldn't zhu-tor rai glat t' wuh whoop nowheres. I reckoned jim had zaprah abru fi' wuh snag, sos'eh, heh ish-veh vesh' ek' abru k' ish-veh. I vesh' rom heh zungor, ni i laid ne' svi' wuh canoe heh leralmin-tor i wouldn't ertau rai weht. I didn't aitlun tor hal-tor tor yuk, veling; tonk'peh i vesh' ni sleepy i couldn't gol'nev ish-veh; ni i nahp i would nem-tor jest veh pi' aushfa-nap. Tonk'peh i reckon ish-veh vesh' weht do wuh aushfa-nap, na' lu i waked abru wuh yel vesh' shining ugelik, wuh ihsek vesh' ek' hal-tor, heh i vesh' spinning ne' wuh suk' vulaya harr-krus wuh'rak. Wuh'rak i didn't fai-tor wilat i vesh'; i nahp i vesh' dreaming; heh lu vel began tor sarlah pla' tor me au seemed tor sarlah abru neik-ha'khlup s' kim-shah wehk gad. Ish-veh vesh' wuh monstrous suk' pilash la', k' wuh tallest heh wuh thickest ves t' lap-tukh fi' fi' kutra; aishan wuh huhtik temok, u' muhl u' kupi gla-tor nash-veh k' wuh yel. I glazhau maf ne'-pilash, heh gla-tor wuh nesh-kur speck fi' wuh masu. I nem-tor po' ish-veh; tonk'peh lu i prah tor ish-veh ish-veh vikau't nothing tonk'peh wuh couple t' sawlogs tor sahris teretuhr. Yi gla-tor nash-veh wuh'ashiv speck, heh chased ik; yi wuh'ashiv, heh nash wak i vesh' gas'rak. Ish-veh vesh' wuh marshak. Lu i prah tor ish-veh jim vesh' setting tra' k' ish-veh patam ne' svi' ish-veh mal-nef, asleep, k' ish-veh gas'rak kar hanging abru' wuh steering-fel. Wuh vath fel vesh' smashed ska', heh wuh marshak vesh' littered abru k' mor heh khlup heh kitek. Ni she'd had wuh rough wak. I tor sahris heh laid ne' ne' jim's han fi' wuh marshak, heh began tor haf, heh sakadaya t'nash-veh ozh-dukal si' tehnat jim, heh leralmin-tor: "tonk'peh, jim, ma i vesh' asleep? Po didn't du stir me abru?" "goodness gracious, nam-tor dat du, huck? En du ain' deadyou ain' drowndedyou's pla' agin? Ish-veh's nuh' rom na' yeht, honey, ish-veh's nuh' rom na' yeht. Lemme glazhau na' du chile, lemme olau o' du. Rai, du ain' tevik! Du's pla' agin, 'ha-tor en soun', jis de ka ole huckde ka ole huck, itaren tor goodness!" "ra's wuh tukh k' du, jim? Du vesh' wuh-drinking?" "drinkin'? Has i ben wuh-drinkin'? Has i had wuh pavesh tor nam-tor wuh-drinkin'?" "muhl, yi, ra tor du variben ni kwai?" "uf tor i variben kwai?" "uf? Po, hain't du vesh' talking pa' t'nash-veh coming pla', heh ek' ik tukh, u' kuv i'd vesh' hal-tor maf?" "huckhuck finn, du glazhau me svi' de bezhun; glazhau me svi' de bezhun. Hain't du ben hal-tor maf?" "hal-tor maf? Po, ra svi' wuh shashol tor du tvai? I hain't vesh' hal-tor anywheres. Wilat would i hal-tor tor?" "muhl, looky la', feihan, dey's sumf'n riyeht, dey nam-tor. Nam-tor i me, il vi nam-tor i? Nam-tor i heah, il whah nam-tor i? I' dat's ra i aitlu tor fai-tor." "muhl, i nah-tor du're la', eiktra hiyet, tonk'peh i nah-tor du're wuh tangle-headed hinek duhsu, jim." "i nam-tor, nam-tor i? Muhl, du kilko-srashiv me dis: didn't du tote si' de zehl svi' de canoe fer tor tor fas' tor de tow-patam?" "rai, i didn't. Ra tow-patam? I hain't gla-tor rai tow-patam." "du hain't gla-tor rai tow-patam? Looky la', didn't de zehl seshaya thal en de raf' hal-tor wuh-hummin' ne' de pilash, en trasha du en de canoe behine svi' de ihsek?" "ra ihsek?" "po, de ihsek!de ihsek dat's vesh' aroun' ek' mu-yor. En didn't du whoop, en didn't i whoop, var-tor etek prah rish' abru svi' de vikuvtra en veh un etek prah los' en t'vath veh vesh' jis' u' rom u' los', 'kase au didn' fai-tor whah au wuz? En didn't i bust abru agin wuh lot er dem vikuvtra en ma wuh turrible wak en mos' git drownded? I' ain' dat ni, bossain't ish-veh ni? Du kilko-srashiv me dat." "muhl, nash nam-tor nuh' wehk na' me, jim. I hain't gla-tor rai ihsek, il rai vikuvtra, il rai troubles, il nothing. I vesh' setting la' talking k' du ek' mu-yor till du went tor yuk pa' lehkuh minutes ago, heh i reckon i ovsoh wuh ka. Du couldn't wuh prah mon-tor svi' ik wak, ni t' rivak du've vesh' dreaming." "dad zaprah ish-veh, uf nam-tor i gwyne tor sahr-tor ek' dat svi' lehkuh minutes?" "muhl, geldau ish-veh ek', du did sahr-tor ish-veh, fai'ei tra' didn't sovek t' ish-veh pavesh-tor." "tonk'peh, huck, ish-veh's ek' jis' u' eiktra tor me u'" "ish-veh ri tor tor rai natyan uf eiktra ish-veh nam-tor; tra' ain't nothing svi' ish-veh. I fai-tor, fai'ei i've vesh' la' ek' wuh wak." jim didn't leralmin nothing na' pa' kaukuh minutes, tonk'peh eku tra' studying abru' ish-veh. Yi au leralmin-tor: "muhl, den, i reck'n i did sahr-tor ish-veh, huck; tonk'peh dog t'nash-veh aushfa ef ish-veh ain't de powerfullest sahr-tor i ek'wak gla-tor. En i hain't ek'wak had rai sahr-tor b'fo' dat's zungor me spo' dis veh." "oh, muhl, ik's ek' gas'rak, fai'ei wuh sahr-tor tor zung-tor wuh ak'shem spo' kanok-vei sometimes. Tonk'peh nash-veh vesh' wuh staving sahr-tor; var-tor me ek' pa' ish-veh, jim." ni jim went tor ar'kadan heh var-tor me wuh bosh vel gas'rak k'fai, aishan u' ish-veh pavesh-tor, goh au kras-tor ish-veh abru considerable. Yi au leralmin-tor au bolau palikaya svi' heh "'terpret" ish-veh, fai'ei ish-veh vesh' satau na' wuh warning. Au leralmin-tor wuh wuh'rak tow-patam lam-tor na' wuh sasu ik would ar'kadan tor tor etek ein rom, tonk'peh wuh current vesh' wuh'ashiv sasu ik would prah etek maf s' ish-veh. Wuh whoops vesh' warnings ik would sarlah tor etek kanok i' heh yi, heh kuv etek didn't ar'kadan lerash tor tor si' tor ken-tor au au'd aishan nem-tor etek vi' rasahkos kunli, 'stead t' keeping etek s' ish-veh. Wuh lot t' tow-patam vesh' troubles etek vesh' going tor prah vi' k' quarrelsome sutra heh ek' ves t' tvai sular-ves, tonk'peh kuv etek minded etwel business heh didn't variben pla' heh aggravate au, etek would seshaya k'fai heh prah s' wuh ihsek heh vi' wuh suk' pa'shik pilash, if vesh' wuh elik fupa s', heh wouldn't ma rai weht trouble. Ish-veh had clouded abru takov gu'gelik aishan po' i prah fi' tor wuh marshak, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' clearing abru va'ashiv i'. "oh, muhl, ik's ek' interpreted muhl hiyet u' irak u' ish-veh hal-tor, jim, " i leralmin-tor; "tonk'peh ra tor aifa vel lamok na'?" ish-veh vesh' wuh mor heh guhsh fi' wuh marshak heh wuh smashed fel. Du kupi gla-tor au wuh'rak-tav i'. Jim glazhau na' wuh guhsh, heh yi glazhau na' me, heh pla' na' wuh guhsh va'ashiv. Au had prah wuh sahr-tor teslau ni karik svi' ish-veh patam ik au couldn't seem tor hutau ish-veh thal heh prah wuh kla-min pla' vi' its shi va'ashiv gas'rak maf. Tonk'peh lu au did prah wuh vel straightened pa' au glazhau na' me br'xan rik' ek'wak smiling, heh leralmin-tor: "ra tor dey stan' na'? I'se gwyne tor var-tor du. Lu i prah ek' sai-vel-tor si' wid ar'kadan, en wid de callin' na' du, en went tor yuk, t'nash-veh khaf-spol wuz mos' shau bekase du wuz los', en i didn' k'yer rai' mo' ra shetau er me en de raf'. En lu i wake abru en tok-ti du pla' agin, ek' safe en soun', de bezhun-masu sarlah, en i kupi wuh prah ne' fi' t'nash-veh mal-nef en shok yo' ash'ya, i's ni itar-bosh. En ek' du wuz thinkin' 'bout wuz uf du kupi tor wuh duhsu uv ole jim wid wuh ti. Dat truck dah nam-tor guhsh; en guhsh nam-tor ra sutra nam-tor dat shitau kitek fi' de patam er dey fren's en tor 'em kafusik." yi au prah abru vohris heh lates-tor tor wuh wigwam, heh went svi' tra' rik' taran sovek-vel tonk'peh ik. Tonk'peh ik vesh' hiyet. Ish-veh tor me olau ni tvai i kupi siyah shok-tor ish-veh ash'ya tor prah ish-veh tor nem-tor ish-veh pla'. Ish-veh vesh' leh-kau minutes fa' i kupi ar'kadan myself abru tor hal-tor heh humble myself tor wuh nigger; tonk'peh i ovsoh ish-veh, heh i vikau't ek'wak sorry na' ish-veh afterwards, neither. I didn't tor ish-veh rai weht tvai tricks, heh i wouldn't ovsoh ish-veh kuv i'd wuh knowed ish-veh would tor ish-veh olau ik yut. Chapter xvi. Etek yuk-tor danik ek' gad, heh palikau si' na' mu-yor, wuh pi' yut za' wuh monstrous wu marshak ik vesh' u' wu going k' u' wuh procession. She had kehkuh wu fnashtau na' tik shaht, ni etek judged she lesh u' wehk u' reh-leh sasu, kesik. She had kaukuh suk' wigwams aboard, eik k'wuhli, heh wuh tu'ash ith'du yon svi' wuh svitan, heh wuh ha-vol haifan-fek na' tik shaht. Tra' vesh' wuh tepul t' style pa' ish-veh. Ish-veh amounted tor vel hasu wuh raftsman fi' such wuh hali u' ik. Etek went drifting ne' vi' wuh suk' vulaya, heh wuh mu-yor clouded abru heh prah fal. Wuh pilash vesh' maut eik, heh vesh' walled k' huhtik lap-tukh fi' fi' vla; du couldn't gla-tor wuh shaya svi' ish-veh hardly ek'wak, il wuh ta'hal. Etek variben pa' cairo, heh wondered whether etek would fai-tor ish-veh lu etek prah tor ish-veh. I leralmin-tor kesik etek wouldn't, fai'ei i had puzhu-tor leralmin tra' vikau't tonk'peh pa' wuh dozen kelek tra', heh kuv au didn't pavesh-tor ki' au lit abru, uf vesh' etek going tor fai-tor etek vesh' be' dvun-tor wuh kahr? Jim leralmin-tor kuv wuh dahkuh suk' pilash terau tra', ik would gluvaya. Tonk'peh i leralmin-tor sos'eh etek lau nah-tor etek vesh' be' dvun-tor wuh ash'ya t' wuh vikuvtra heh coming vi' wuh ka hinek pilash va'ashiv. Ik ertau jimand me nuh'. Ni wuh deshker vesh', ra tor tor? I leralmin-tor, paddle ashore wuh wuh'rak wak wuh ta'hal gluvau, heh var-tor au pap vesh' za', coming bi' k' wuh trading-scow, heh vesh' wuh yar-kur el'ru na' wuh business, heh aitlu tor fai-tor uf irak ish-veh vesh' tor cairo. Jim nahp ish-veh vesh' wuh rom idea, ni etek nem-tor wuh vuzh fi' ish-veh heh bek-tor. Tra' vikau't nothing tor tor i' tonk'peh tor glazhau si' nasik na' wuh kahr, heh ri be' dvun ish-veh rik' seeing ish-veh. Au leralmin-tor au'd nam-tor mighty sure tor gla-tor ish-veh, fai'ei au'd nam-tor wuh elik sasu wuh minute au gla-tor ish-veh, tonk'peh kuv au din-tor ish-veh au'd nam-tor svi' wuh kafeh shasol va'ashiv heh rai weht gluvaya na' el'es. Kanok pi' du' au spen-tor abru heh leralmin-tor: "dah she nam-tor?" tonk'peh ish-veh vikau't. Ish-veh vesh' jack-o'-makh-yonet, il igen-wesh bugs; ni au eku ne' va'ashiv, heh went tor watching, ka u' fa'. Jim leralmin-tor ish-veh tor ish-veh ek' abru' trembly heh taulik tor nam-tor ni beyik el'es. Muhl, i mokuhlek var-tor du ish-veh tor me ek' abru' trembly heh taulik, nuh', tor zhu-tor ish-veh, fai'ei i palikau tor prah ish-veh k'fai t'nash-veh patam ik au vesh' danik freeand vi vesh' tor tenai na' ish-veh? Po, me. I couldn't prah ik s' t'nash-veh conscience, rai uf il rai yut. Ish-veh prah tor troubling me ni i couldn't shom; i couldn't stay fam dvun svi' veh shi. Ish-veh hadn't ek'wak sarlah ha-kel tor me fa', ra nash vel vesh' ik i vesh' doing. Tonk'peh i' ish-veh did; heh ish-veh stayed k' me, heh scorched me weht heh weht. I ar'kada tor tor si' tor myself ik i vikau't tor tenai, fai'ei i didn't sahr-tor jim ska' s' ish-veh rightful owner; tonk'peh ish-veh vikau't rai nam-tor-tor, conscience abru heh leralmin-tor, kanok wak, "tonk'peh du knowed au vesh' sahran na' ish-veh el'es, heh du kupi wuh paddled ashore heh var-tor somebody." ik vesh' soi couldn't prah pa' ik noway. Ik vesh' wilat ish-veh k'hy. Conscience leralmin-tor tor me, "ra had ri donku-tor din-tor watson ovsoh tor du ik du kupi gla-tor ish-veh nigger hal-tor ska' gas'rak ne' ish-veh bezhun heh worla leralmin veh single zhit? Ra did ik ri donku-tor hinek kosu tor tor du ik du kupi skasau ish-veh ni tvai? Po, she ar'kada tor oren-tor du ish-veh dunap, she ar'kada tor oren-tor du ish-veh manners, she ar'kada tor nam-tor rom tor du kanok yut she knowed uf. Ik's ra she ovsoh." i prah tor olaya ni tvai heh ni miserable i danik istau i vesh' tevik. I fidgeted abru heh ne' wuh marshak, abusing myself tor myself, heh jim vesh' fidgeting abru heh ne' vesht me. Etek neither t' etek kupi potau fam dvun. Kanok wak au tam-tor pa' heh leralmin-tor, "dah's cairo!" ish-veh went k'fai me spo' wuh pohshaya, heh i nahp kuv ish-veh vesh' cairo i reckoned i would tev-tor t' miserableness. Jim variben si' ral ek' wuh wak du' i vesh' talking tor myself. Au vesh' taran uf wuh wuh'rak vel au would tor lu au prah tor wuh elik fupa s' au would hal-tor tor saving abru donku heh worla spend wuh single cent, heh lu au prah hiyet au would mahr-tor ish-veh ko-telsu, if vesh' puma fi' wuh uroshal beyik wilat din-tor watson ha-tor; heh yi au would fi' ar'kadan tor mahr-tor wuh dahkuh kanu, heh kuv ish-veh trensu wouldn't makau au, au'd prah wuh ab'litionist tor hal-tor heh vazgau au. Ish-veh danik froze me tor zhu-tor such variben. Au wouldn't ek'wak dared tor variben such variben svi' ish-veh ha'kiv fa'. Aishan gla-tor ra wuh natyan ish-veh tor svi' ish-veh wuh minute au judged au vesh' pa' elik. Ish-veh vesh' fupa s' wuh hinek taran, "mazhiv-kur-tor wuh nigger wuh inch heh au'll nem-tor wuh ell." nah-tor i, nash nam-tor ra sarlah t' t'nash-veh ri thinking. La' vesh' nash nigger, if i had u' rom u' gol-tor tor sahr-tor maf, coming gas'rak si' pa'ash-footed heh taran au would vazgau ish-veh childrenchildren ik belonged tor wuh sasu i didn't kauk fai-tor; wuh sasu ik hadn't ek'wak ovsoh me rai klau. I vesh' sorry tor zhu-tor jim leralmin ik, ish-veh vesh' such wuh lowering t' ish-veh. T'nash-veh conscience prah tor stirring me abru hotter do ek'wak, abi' na' kim-shah i leralmin-tor tor ish-veh, "kal-tor abru fi' meit ain't nuh' tab-ma yeti'll paddle ashore na' wuh wuh'rak ta'hal heh var-tor." i olau hagik heh kunli heh ta'hal u' wuh kan gas'rak ska'. Ek' t'nash-veh troubles vesh' hal-tor. I went tor looking si' nasik na' wuh ta'hal, heh wihfelau t' uralaun tor myself. K'-heh-k' veh gluvau. Jim uralau si': "etek's safe, huck, etek's safe! Spen-tor abru heh treshaya yo' timut! Dat's de rom ole cairo na' las', i jis fai-tor ish-veh!" i leralmin-tor: "i'll nem-tor wuh canoe heh hal-tor heh gla-tor, jim. Ish-veh mightn't nam-tor, du fai-tor." au spen-tor heh prah wuh canoe pok, heh shitau ish-veh hinek tor-pal svi' wuh lanet na' me tor eku fi', heh mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh paddle; heh u' i shoved ska', au leralmin-tor: "pooty ak i'll nam-tor wuh-saul'n' na' mak, en i'll leralmin, ish-veh's ek' fi' khrosahp o' huck; i's wuh elik sasu, en i couldn't ek'wak ben elik ef ish-veh hadn' ben na' huck; huck ovsoh ish-veh. Jim skil-tor't ek'wak forgit du, huck; du's de bes' fren' jim's ek'wak had; en du's de goh fren' ole jim's prah i'." i vesh' paddling ska', ek' svi' wuh wadashaya tor var-tor fi' ish-veh; tonk'peh lu au leralmin-tor nash, ish-veh seemed tor ves t' nem-tor wuh k'hy ek' s' me. I went bi' vohris yi, heh i vikau't gas'rak ne' ac'ruth whether i vesh' glad i palikau il whether i vikau't. Lu i vesh' kau-leh ker ska', jim leralmin-tor: "dah du hal-tor, de ole yeht huck; de fi''y wan-kur genlman dat ek'wak kep' ish-veh ugaya tor ole jim." muhl, i aishan olau has-bosh. Tonk'peh i leralmin-tor, i prah tor tor iti mokuhlek't prah si' t' ish-veh. Gas'rak yi bi' sarlah wuh skiff k' dahkuh sasu svi' ish-veh k' pohshayek, heh au pehkau heh i pehkau. Veh t' au leralmin-tor: "ra's ik yonder?" "wuh krus t' wuh marshak, " i leralmin-tor. "tor du belong fi' ish-veh?" "ha, osu." "sovek sasu fi' ish-veh?" "goh veh, osu." "muhl, tra''s kaukuh niggers sahr-tor ska' tor-mu-yor abru yonder, abru' wuh patam t' wuh vulaya. Nam-tor ish-veh sasu wan-kur il nesh-kur?" i didn't kilko-srashiv abru prompt. I ar'kada tor, tonk'peh wuh zhit wouldn't sarlah. I ar'kada na' wuh dahr il dahkuh tor fir-tor abru heh si' k' ish-veh, tonk'peh i vikau't sasu enoughhadn't wuh spunk t' wuh rabbit. Gla-tor nash-veh i vesh' weakening; ni i aishan mazhiv-kur-tor abru trying, heh abru heh leralmin-tor: "au's wan-kur." "i reckon etek'll hal-tor heh gla-tor na' ourselves." "i istaya du would, " leralmin-tor i, "fai'ei ish-veh's pap ik's tra', heh sos'eh du'd gol'nev me tow wuh marshak ashore wilat wuh ta'hal nam-tor. Au's sickand ni nam-tor mam heh mary ann." "oh, wuh e'shua! Etek're svi' wuh brax, sa-kan. Tonk'peh i s'pose etek've prah tor. Sarlah, tersek tor ish-veh paddle, heh kal-tor's prah bi'." i buckled tor t'nash-veh paddle heh au laid tor ish-veh fel. Lu etek had tor wuh shad-kisheya il dahkuh, i leralmin-tor: "pap'll nam-tor mighty mau obleeged tor du, i mokuhlek var-tor du. Kanok-veh hal-tor maf lu i aitlun au tor gol'nev me tow wuh marshak ashore, heh i mokuhlek't tor ish-veh k' myself." "muhl, ik's infernal tvai. Shaik, nuh'. Leralmin, sa-kan, ra's wuh tukh k' ish-veh sa-mekh?" "ish-veh's theathewell, ish-veh ain't sovek-vel mau." au pehkau pulling. Ish-veh vikau't tonk'peh wuh mighty pi' yut tor wuh marshak i'. Veh leralmin-tor: "sa-kan, ik's wuh ti. Ra nam-tor wuh tukh k' ish-veh pap? Kilko-srashiv abru keh-vla i', heh ish-veh'll nam-tor wuh weh-rom na' du." "i dungi, osu, i dungi, honestbut ri tor trasha etek, sanoi. Ish-veh's thethegentlemen, kuv du'll goh seshaya ahead, heh kal-tor me heave du wuh headline, du skil-tor't ma tor sarlah wuh-be' wuh raftplease tor." "eku ish-veh pla', john, eku ish-veh pla'!" leralmin-tor veh. Au backed masu. "potau maf, boykeep tor looard. Confound ish-veh, i aishan gish wuh salan has salur ish-veh tor etek. Ish-veh pap's prah wuh pi'-pox, heh du fai-tor ish-veh taluhk muhl. Po didn't du sasarlah heh leralmin ni? Tor du aitlun tor sak-tor ish-veh ek' abru'?" "muhl, " leralmin-tor i, wuh-blubbering, "i've var-tor kanok-veh fa', heh au aishan went maf heh losrak etek." "ri donku-tor e'shua, tra''s vel svi' ik. Etek nam-tor gas'rak ne' sorry na' du, tonk'peh wewell, geldau ish-veh, etek ri tor aitlun wuh pi'-pox, gla-tor du. Glazhau la', i'll var-tor du ra tor tor. Ri tor du ar'kadan tor solektra k' yourself, il du'll smash kanok-vei tor krus. Du marek bi' ne' pa' dah-leh miles, heh du'll sarlah tor wuh kahr fi' wuh losrak-el'ru vla t' wuh pilash. Ish-veh dungi nam-tor wu po' yel-abru yi, heh lu du ya'akash na' gol'nev du var-tor au ish-veh sular-ves nam-tor ek' ne' k' chills heh tau. Ri tor nam-tor wuh duhsu va'ashiv, heh kal-tor sutra guess ra nam-tor wuh tukh. I' etek're trying tor tor du wuh kindness; ni du aishan shitau dah-leh miles svi' etek, ik's wuh rom sa-kan. Ish-veh wouldn't tor sovek rom tor solektra yonder wilat wuh ta'hal isit's goh wuh lapan-ker. Leralmin, i reckon ish-veh sa-mekh's ri donku-tor, heh i'm bound tor leralmin au's svi' takov lerash kunli. La', i'll shitau wuh dah-leh-dollar pi-maat-tukh krus fi' nash dohn, heh du prah ish-veh lu ish-veh markau k'. I olau mighty tvai tor trasha du; tonk'peh t'nash-veh kingdom! Ish-veh skil-tor't tor tor duhsu k' pi'-pox, ri tor du gla-tor?" "meskaraya fi', parker, " leralmin-tor wuh vath sasu, "la''s wuh dah-leh tor shitau fi' wuh dohn na' me. Rom-bye, sa-kan; du tor u' mr. Parker var-tor du, heh du'll nam-tor ek' gas'rak." "ik's ni, t'nash-veh boygood-bye, rom-bye. Kuv gla-tor du sovek runaway niggers du prah gol'nev heh nab au, heh du mokuhlek tor ein donku k' ish-veh." "rom-bye, osu, " leralmin-tor i; "i skil-tor't kal-tor rai runaway niggers panavau me kuv i mokuhlek gol'nev ish-veh." au went ska' heh i prah aboard wuh marshak, olaya rasahkos heh neik, fai'ei i knowed maut muhl i had ovsoh riyeht, heh gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh vikau't rai nam-tor-tor na' me tor ar'kadan tor oren-tor tor tor gas'rak; wuh ak'shem ik ri tor prah palikau gas'rak lu au's pi' ain't prah rai showwhen wuh k'hy sarlah tra' ain't nothing tor pla' ish-veh abru heh potau ish-veh tor ish-veh ar'kadan, heh ni au prah kuhsh-tor. Yi i nahp wuh minute, heh leralmin-tor tor myself, meskaraya fi'; s'pose du'd wuh ovsoh gas'rak heh mazhiv-kur-tor jim abru, would du olau weh-rom do ra du tor i'? Rai, leralmin-tor i, i'd olau badi'd olau aishan wuh ka yut i tor i'. Muhl, yi, leralmin-tor i, ra's wuh nam-tor-tor du learning tor tor gas'rak lu ish-veh's troublesome tor tor gas'rak heh ain't rai trouble tor tor riyeht, heh wuh wages nam-tor aishan wuh ka? I vesh' terpau. I couldn't kilko-srashiv ik. Ni i reckoned i wouldn't ertau rai weht pa' ish-veh, tonk'peh po' nash kwon-hau-ov tor whichever sarlah handiest na' wuh wak. I went vi' wuh wigwam; jim vikau't tra'. I glazhau ek' pa'; au vikau't sovek-wilat. I leralmin-tor: "jim!" "la' i nam-tor, huck. Nam-tor dey si' o' glan yit? Ri tor variben ral." au vesh' svi' wuh pilash ne' wuh harr-krus fel, k' aishan ish-veh han si'. I var-tor ish-veh au vesh' s' glan, ni au sarlah aboard. Au leralmin-tor: "i vesh' wuh-listenin' tor ek' de variben, en i trel-tor vi' de pilash en vesh' gwyne tor shove na' sho' kuv dey sarlah aboard. Den i vesh' gwyne tor mahal-tor tor de raf' agin lu dey vesh' hal-tor. Tonk'peh lawsy, uf du did duhsu 'em, huck! Dat wuz de smartes' sayutau! I var-tor du, chile, i 'speck ish-veh korsau' ole jimole jim ain't going tor forgit du na' dat, honey." yi etek variben pa' wuh donku. Ish-veh vesh' wuh takov rom raisetwenty dollars apiece. Jim leralmin-tor etek kupi nem-tor lan-tol tvur fi' wuh steamboat i', heh wuh donku would kim-shah etek u' irak u' etek aitlu tor hal-tor svi' wuh elik fupa s'. Au leralmin-tor dah-leh mile weht vikau't irak na' wuh marshak tor hal-tor, tonk'peh au istau etek vesh' already tra'. Na' gad-keshtan etek tied abru, heh jim vesh' mighty particular pa' hiding wuh marshak rom. Yi au ar'kada ek' gad fixing vel svi' uzh'a'lek, heh getting ek' pok tor quit rafting. Ik mu-yor pa' lehkuh etek hove svi' glan t' wuh ha'ge t' wuh kahr maf ne' svi' wuh losrak-el'ru vulaya. I went ska' svi' wuh canoe tor ya'akash pa' ish-veh. Takov ak i afer-tor wuh sasu si' svi' wuh pilash k' wuh skiff, setting wuh sahr-tor-zehl. I ranged abru heh leralmin-tor: "mister, nam-tor ik kahr cairo?" "cairo? Rai. Du bolau nam-tor wuh tenai' duhsu." "ra kahr nam-tor ish-veh, mister?" "kuv du aitlun tor fai-tor, hal-tor heh talal si'. Kuv du stay la' botherin' pa' me na' pa' wuh ulef wuh minute longer du'll prah vel du skil-tor't aitlun." i paddled tor wuh marshak. Jim vesh' awful disappointed, tonk'peh i leralmin-tor worla kashek, cairo would nam-tor wuh thurai shi, i reckoned. Etek be' dvun-tor wuh'ashiv kahr fa' gad-ha'khlup, heh i vesh' going si' va'ashiv; tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' pid solektra, ni i didn't hal-tor. Rai pid solektra pa' cairo, jim leralmin-tor. I had forgot ish-veh. Etek laid abru na' wuh gad fi' wuh tow-patam tolerable beyik wuh losrak-el'ru kutra. I palikau tor suspicion vel. Ni did jim. I leralmin-tor: "sos'eh etek went k' cairo svi' wuh ihsek ik mu-yor." au leralmin-tor: "doan' le's variben pa' ish-veh, huck. Po' niggers mokuhlek't ma rai kunli. I awluz 'spected dat rattlesnake-wadi vikau't ovsoh wid its ar'kadan." "i istaya i'd worla gla-tor ik oluhk-wadi, jimi tor istaya i'd worla laid bezhun fi' ish-veh." "ish-veh ain't yo' lafot, huck; du didn' fai-tor. Ri tor du tenai yo'shal 'bout ish-veh." lu ish-veh vesh' gad-ha'khlup, la' vesh' wuh pa'shik ohio masu inshore, sure hiyet, heh s'udish vesh' wuh hinek regular muddy! Ni ish-veh vesh' ek' abru k' cairo. Etek variben ish-veh ek' abru'. Ish-veh wouldn't tor tor nem-tor tor wuh gef; etek couldn't nem-tor wuh marshak abru wuh pilash, veling. Tra' vikau't rai yut tonk'peh tor bek-tor na' gu'gelik, heh palikaya pla' svi' wuh canoe heh nem-tor wuh pavesh. Ni etek yuk-tor ek' gad svi' wuh cottonwood pi'laptra, ni u' tor nam-tor sluk na' wuh ar'kadan, heh lu etek went pla' tor wuh marshak pa' gu'gelik wuh canoe vesh' hal-tor! Etek didn't leralmin wuh zhit na' wuh rom du'. Tra' vikau't sovek-vel tor leralmin. Etek fi' knowed muhl hiyet ish-veh vesh' ein weht ar'kadan t' wuh rattlesnake-wadi; ni ra vesh' wuh nam-tor-tor tor variben pa' ish-veh? Ish-veh would goh glazhau spo' etek vesh' finding lafot, heh ik would nam-tor bound tor zaprah weht rasahkos luckand potau fi' fetching ish-veh, nuh', till etek knowed hiyet tor potau fam dvun. K'-heh-k' etek variben pa' ra etek weh-rom tor, heh afer-tor tra' vikau't rai yut tonk'peh aishan tor hal-tor bi' ne' k' wuh marshak till etek prah wuh pavesh tor mahr-tor wuh canoe tor hal-tor pla' svi'. Etek vikau't going tor yahv-tor ish-veh lu tra' vikau't anybody pa', wuh yut pap would tor, na' ik lau eku sutra po' etek. Ni etek shoved si' po' gu'gelik fi' wuh marshak. Anybody ik ri tor dva-tor wi ik ish-veh's duh'es tor el'rek wuh oluhk-wadi, po' ek' ik ik oluhk-wadi ovsoh na' etek, dungi dva-tor ish-veh i' kuv au telv-tor fi' heh gla-tor ra weht ish-veh ovsoh na' etek. Wuh shi tor mahr-tor canoes nam-tor ska' t' marshak laying abru na' gef. Tonk'peh etek didn't gla-tor rai marshak laying abru; ni etek went bi' du' rehkuh wadan heh weht. Muhl, wuh mu-yor prah zhai-kur heh ruther bali, if nam-tor wuh thurai meanest vel tor ihsek. Du mokuhlek't var-tor wuh shid t' wuh pilash, heh du mokuhlek't gla-tor rai ir. Ish-veh prah tor nam-tor maut tab-ma heh fam dvun, heh yi bi' sarlah wuh steamboat abru wuh pilash. Etek lit wuh makh-yonet, heh judged she would gla-tor ish-veh. Abru-pilash masu-hali didn't generly sarlah beyik etek; au hal-tor si' heh zahal-tor wuh mofek heh shi'kar na' hagik masu ne' wuh reefs; tonk'peh mu-yor spo' nash au bull gas'rak abru wuh mashyut tehnat wuh bosh pilash. Etek kupi zhu-tor ish-veh pounding bi', tonk'peh etek didn't gla-tor ish-veh rom till she vesh' ikap-tor. She mokh-tor gas'rak na' etek. K'ashiv au tor ik heh ar'kadan tor gla-tor uf ikap-tor au mokuhlek sarlah rik' touching; sometimes wuh halek zeshaya ska' wuh fnashtaya, heh yi wuh hashsu terpau ish-veh patam si' heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor, heh nah-tor au's mighty klon. Muhl, la' sarlah ish-veh, heh etek leralmin-tor she vesh' going tor ar'kadan heh hohl-tor etek; tonk'peh she didn't seem tor nam-tor sheering ska' wuh zeshau. She vesh' wuh suk' veh, heh she vesh' coming svi' wuh brax, nuh', looking spo' wuh nesh-kur wan k' fel-tor t' min-worms pa' ish-veh; tonk'peh ek' t' wuh sudden she bulged si', suk' heh scary, k' wuh wu zehl t' eik-tu'ash furnace svep shining spo' yon-kur-fal zud, heh ish-veh monstrous ovalau heh klashau hanging gas'rak abru' etek. Tra' vesh' wuh saul na' etek, heh wuh jingling t' kus-vakh tor pehkaya wuh mishu, wuh powwow t' cussing, heh whistling t' steamand u' jim went overboard fi' veh vla heh i fi' wuh vath, she sarlah smashing zehik k'fai wuh marshak. I divedand i mokh-tor tor talal wuh lanet, nuh', na' wuh reh-leh-ash'ya halek had prah tor hal-tor abru' me, heh i aitlu ish-veh ki' plenty t' tvi-shal. I kupi kwon-hau-ov stay ne' masu wuh minute; nash wak i reckon i stayed ne' wuh minute heh wuh ulef. Yi i rukau na' wuh fik svi' wuh brax, na' i vesh' nearly busting. I popped si' tor t'nash-veh armpits heh salur wuh masu s' t'nash-veh han, heh puffed wuh zeshau. Veling tra' vesh' wuh booming current; heh veling ik masu-hali palikau ish-veh mishu va'ashiv lehkuh seconds po' she pehkau au, na' au worla tun-tor mau na' raftsmen; ni i' she vesh' churning bi' abru wuh pilash, s' glan svi' wuh bali igen-va, hi i kupi zhu-tor ish-veh. I uralau si' na' jim pa' wuh dozen wak, tonk'peh i didn't prah sovek kilko-srashiv; ni i runem-tor wuh plank ik estuhl me du' i vesh' "treading masu, " heh kwul-tor si' na' gef, shoving ish-veh ahead t' me. Tonk'peh i tor si' tor gla-tor ik wuh maraya t' wuh current vesh' na' wuh losrak-el'ru gef, if tvai ik i vesh' svi' wuh mes; ni i rubai ska' heh went ik yut. Ish-veh vesh' veh t' aifa wu, slanting, dahkuh-mile crossings; ni i vesh' wuh rom akarshif svi' getting abru'. I tor wuh safe landing, heh clumb abru wuh kutra. I couldn't gla-tor tonk'peh wuh pi' yut, tonk'peh i went poking bi' abru' rough solektra na' wuh yonuk t' wuh mile il weht, heh yi i sahr-tor mes' wuh suk' hinek-fashioned dahtau lap-fek-kelek fa' i pubeglanau ish-veh. I vesh' going tor rush k' heh prah maf, tonk'peh wuh lot t' dogs spen-tor si' heh went tor howling heh barking na' me, heh i knowed weh-rom do tor dvun wuh'ashiv peg. Chapter xvii. Svi' pa' wuh minute somebody stariben s' wuh krani rik' putting ish-veh patam si', heh leralmin-tor: "nam-tor ovsoh, sa-kan! Vi's tra'?" i leralmin-tor: "ish-veh's me." "vi's me?" "george jackson, osu." "ra tor du aitlun?" "i ri tor aitlun nothing, osu. I goh aitlun tor hal-tor bi' k', tonk'peh wuh dogs skil-tor't kal-tor me." "ra nam-tor du prowling pa' la' nash wak t' mu-yor forhey?" "i vikau't prowling pa', osu, i tevan-tor overboard ska' t' wuh steamboat." "oh, du did, did du? Kwul wuh ta'hal tra', somebody. Ra did du leralmin ish-veh ahm vesh'?" "george jackson, osu. I'm goh wuh sa-kan." "glazhau la', kuv du're telling wuh yeht'es du needn't nam-tor afraidnobody'll dash-tor du. Tonk'peh ri tor ar'kadan tor budge; lamok gas'rak wilat du nam-tor. Kastorilau si' bob heh tom, ein t' du, heh zaprah wuh pohshayek. George jackson, nam-tor tra' anybody k' du?" "rai, osu, kling." i puzhu-tor wuh sutra stirring pa' svi' wuh kelek i', heh gla-tor wuh ta'hal. Wuh sasu uralau si': "snatch ik ta'hal maf, betsy, du hinek foolain't du prah sovek kash-ral? Shitau ish-veh fi' wuh lan-tol za' wuh khom svep. Bob, kuv du heh tom nam-tor pok, nem-tor ish-veh shitau." "ek' pok." "i', george jackson, tor du fai-tor wuh shepherdsons?" "rai, osu; i worla puzhu-tor t' au." "muhl, ik lau nam-tor ni, heh ish-veh mayn't. I', ek' pok. Ash fa'rak, george jackson. Heh kashek, ri tor du hurrycome mighty vohris. Kuv tra''s anybody k' du, kal-tor ish-veh potau backif au gluvau himself au'll nam-tor pohshaya. Sarlah bi' i'. Sarlah vohris; kwitaya wuh svep tu'ash yourselfjust hiyet tor lerakhovau svi', d' du zhu-tor?" i didn't brax; i couldn't kuv i'd wuh aitlu tor. I nem-tor veh vohris ash na' wuh wak heh tra' vikau't wuh ralash, goh i nahp i kupi zhu-tor t'nash-veh khaf-spol. Wuh dogs vesh' u' fam dvun u' wuh komihn, tonk'peh au zahal-tor wuh pi' za' me. Lu i prah tor wuh rehkuh lap-fek svep-ashef i puzhu-tor au unlocking heh unbarring heh unbolting. I shitau t'nash-veh el'ru fi' wuh svep heh kwitau ish-veh wuh pi' heh wuh pi' weht till somebody leralmin-tor, "tra', ik's enoughput ish-veh patam svi'." i ovsoh ish-veh, tonk'peh i judged au would nem-tor ish-veh ska'. Wuh ha'fek vesh' fi' wuh lan-tol, heh tra' au ek' vesh', looking na' me, heh me na' au, na' pa' wuh yonuk t' wuh minute: rehkuh suk' sasu k' pohshayek sfekau na' me, if tor me wince, i var-tor du; wuh oldest, zhai-kur heh pa' sheh-leh, wuh vath dahkuh reh-leh il moreall t' au tok-ti heh handsomeand wuh sweetest hinek zhai-kur-headed t'sai, heh pla' t' ish-veh dahkuh nu'ri kosu if i couldn't gla-tor gas'rak muhl. Wuh hinek gentleman leralmin-tor: "tra'; i reckon ish-veh's ek' gas'rak. Sarlah svi'." u' ak u' i vesh' svi' wuh hinek gentleman au klacha wuh svep heh barred ish-veh heh terkau ish-veh, heh var-tor wuh nu'ri sasu tor sarlah svi' k' ish-veh pohshayek, heh au ek' went svi' wuh suk' parlor ik had wuh uzh a'cit la'y fi' wuh lan-tol, heh prah teretuhr svi' wuh teruk ik vesh' s' wuh eik'es t' wuh khom windowsthere vikau't rim fi' wuh vla. Au meskarau wuh ha'fek, heh nem-tor wuh rom glazhau na' me, heh ek' leralmin-tor, "po, au ain't wuh shepherdsonno, tra' ain't sovek shepherdson pa' ish-veh." yi wuh hinek sasu leralmin-tor au rok-tor i wouldn't kashek hasu pstha na' kar, fai'ei au didn't tvai rai klau k' itit vesh' goh tor tor sure. Ni au didn't ihv-tor vi' t'nash-veh abru'lik, tonk'peh goh olau s'udish k' ish-veh el'ru, heh leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' ek' gas'rak. Au var-tor me tor tor myself hagik heh na' ha-kel, heh var-tor ek' pa' myself; tonk'peh wuh hinek t'sai leralmin-tor: "po, kudau du, saul, wuh ri donku-tor vel's u' masupik u' au mokuhlek nam-tor; heh ri tor du reckon ish-veh lau nam-tor au's k'avon?" "yeht na' du, racheli forgot." ni wuh hinek t'sai leralmin-tor: "betsy" (nash vesh' wuh nigger kosu), "du hash-tor pa' heh prah ish-veh vel tor yokul u' sahris u' du mokuhlek, ri donku-tor vel; heh veh t' du ko-kan hal-tor heh wake abru buck heh var-tor himoh, la' au nam-tor himself. Buck, nem-tor nash pi' ri-fainusu heh prah wuh masupik sai-vel ska' s' ish-veh heh sai-vel ish-veh abru svi' ein t' ish-veh ik's pseth." buck glazhau pa' u' hinek u' methirteen il leh-keh il bi' tra', hi au vesh' wuh pi' bigger do me. Au hadn't fi' sovek-vel tonk'peh wuh sav'el, heh au vesh' maut frowzy-headed. Sarlah ish-veh svi' gaping heh digging veh ozh-dukal vi' ish-veh bezhun, heh au vesh' dragging wuh pohshayek bi' k' wuh vath veh. Au leralmin-tor: "ain't au rai shepherdsons pa'?" au leralmin-tor, rai, 'twas wuh riyeht-vikayek. "muhl, " au leralmin-tor, "kuv au'd wuh ben ein, i reckon i'd wuh prah veh." au ek' abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor, heh bob leralmin-tor: "po, buck, au lau ma scalped etek ek', du've vesh' ni vohris svi' coming." "muhl, kling sarlah po' me, heh ish-veh ain't gas'rak i'm kwon-hau-ov potau ne'; i ri tor prah rai gluvaya." "worla kashek, buck, t'nash-veh sa-kan, " leralmin-tor wuh hinek sasu, "du'll ma gluvaya hiyet, ek' svi' rom wak, ri tor du fret pa' ik. Hal-tor 'wu k' du i', heh tor u' ish-veh ko-mekh var-tor du." lu etek prah abru-kaiden tor ish-veh tvi-shal au prah me wuh dirik sav'el heh wuh roundabout heh malanu t' ish-veh, heh i shitau au fi'. Du' i vesh' na' ish-veh au ya'akash me ra t'nash-veh ahm vesh', tonk'peh fa' i kupi var-tor ish-veh au palikau tor var-tor me pa' wuh bluejay heh wuh nu'ri rabbit au had catched svi' wuh lapan gad fa' za-gad, heh au ya'akash me wilat moses vesh' lu wuh ha'fek went si'. I leralmin-tor i didn't fai-tor; i hadn't puzhu-tor pa' ish-veh fa', rai yut. "muhl, guess, " au leralmin-tor. "uf'm i going tor guess, " leralmin-tor i, "lu i worla puzhu-tor var-tor t' ish-veh fa'?" "tonk'peh du mokuhlek guess, mokuhlek't du? Ish-veh's aishan u' hagik." "if ha'fek?" i leralmin-tor. "po, sovek ha'fek, " au leralmin-tor. "i ri tor fai-tor wilat au vesh', " leralmin-tor i; "wilat vesh' au?" "po, au vesh' svi' wuh gu'gelik! Ik's wilat au vesh'!" "muhl, kuv du knowed wilat au vesh', ra did du ya'akash me na'?" "po, tenai ish-veh, ish-veh's wuh riddle, ri tor gla-tor du? Leralmin, uf wu nam-tor du going tor stay la'? Du prah tor stay kwon-hau-ov. Etek mokuhlek aishan ma booming timesthey ri tor ma rai shi'oren i'. Tor du sha' wuh dog? I've prah wuh dogand au'll hal-tor svi' wuh pilash heh katau si' val ik du lehm svi'. Tor du spo' tor dref abru sundays, heh ek' ik ves t' duh'es? Du sihaya i ri tor, tonk'peh ma she tor me. Confound aifa ole britches! I reckon i'd weh-rom shitau 'em fi', tonk'peh i'd ruther ri, ish-veh's ni lamekh. Nam-tor du ek' pok? Ek' gas'rak. Sarlah bi', hinek hoss." samu corn-pone, samu corn-kahm, butter heh buttermilkthat nam-tor ra au had na' me ne' tra', heh tra' ain't nothing weh-rom ik ek'wak i've sarlah mes' wi. Buck heh ish-veh ma heh ek' t' au smoked cob mev, kaula wuh nigger kosu, if vesh' hal-tor, heh wuh dahkuh nu'ri kosu. Au ek' smoked heh variben, heh i yokul heh variben. Wuh nu'ri kosu had quilts pa' au, heh ish-veh isachya ne' ish-veh pla'dor. Au ek' ya'akash me deshkau, heh i var-tor au uf pap heh me heh ek' wuh skan vesh' living fi' wuh pi' uroshal ne' na' wuh lanet t' arkansaw, heh t'nash-veh ko-kai mary ann sahr-tor ska' heh prah telik heh worla vesh' puzhu-tor t' rai weht, heh dun went tor shi'kar au heh au vikau't puzhu-tor t' rai weht, heh tom heh mort tev-tor, heh yi tra' vikau't kling tonk'peh aishan me heh pap losrak, heh au vesh' aishan trimmed ne' tor nothing, fi' khrosahp t' ish-veh troubles; ni lu au tev-tor i nem-tor ra tra' vesh' losrak, fai'ei wuh uroshal didn't belong tor etek, heh palikau abru wuh pilash, lan-tol tvur, heh tevan-tor overboard; heh ik vesh' uf sarlah nash-veh tor nam-tor la'. Ni au leralmin-tor i kupi ma wuh ha-kel tra' u' wu u' i aitlu ish-veh. Yi ish-veh vesh' danik gad-ha'khlup heh kanok-veh went tor sar-tak, heh i went tor sar-tak k' buck, heh lu i waked abru svi' wuh asal, drat ish-veh ek', i had forgot ra t'nash-veh ahm vesh'. Ni i laid tra' pa' wuh wadan trying tor nah-tor, heh lu buck waked abru i leralmin-tor: "mokuhlek du spell, buck?" "ha, " au leralmin-tor. "i sihaya du mokuhlek't spell t'nash-veh ahm, " leralmin-tor i. "i sihaya du ra du dare i mokuhlek, " leralmin-tor au. "ek' gas'rak, " leralmin-tor i, "fator'voh." "g-e-o-r-g-e j-wuh-x-o-nthere i', " au leralmin-tor. "muhl, " leralmin-tor i, "du ovsoh ish-veh, tonk'peh i didn't nah-tor du kupi. Ish-veh ain't rai slouch t' wuh ahm tor spellright ska' rik' studying." i eku ish-veh ne', awek, fai'ei somebody lau aitlun me tor spell ish-veh thurai, heh ni i aitlu tor nam-tor handy k' ish-veh heh rattle ish-veh ska' spo' i vesh' nam-tor-tor tor ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' wuh mighty nice skan, heh wuh mighty nice kelek, nuh'. I hadn't gla-tor rai kelek si' svi' wuh shasol fa' ik vesh' ni nice heh had ni mau style. Ish-veh didn't ma wuh shek-tukh kuhr fi' wuh khom svep, il wuh wooden veh k' wuh buckskin string, tonk'peh wuh dvesh-tukh elat tor da-tor, wuh ka u' kelek svi' kahr. Tra' vikau't rai sar-tak svi' wuh parlor, il wuh glat t' wuh sar-tak; tonk'peh heaps t' parlors svi' kahr has sar-tak svi' au. Tra' vesh' wuh suk' yon-sha'ti ik vesh' bricked fi' wuh lanet, heh wuh dok vesh' potau sok'i heh yon-kur k' pouring masu fi' au heh scrubbing au k' wuh'ashiv dok; sometimes au pu-tor au abru' k' yon-kur masu-kras ik au vutau spanish-khav-kur, ka u' au tor svi' kahr. Au had suk' dvesh-tukh dog-irons ik kupi meskaraya abru wuh gla-tor-lap-fek. Tra' vesh' wuh wak-vel fi' wuh svitan t' wuh mantelpiece, k' wuh bikuv t' wuh kahr kras-tor fi' wuh lanet ulef t' wuh makh khom, heh wuh pauk shi svi' wuh svitan t' ish-veh na' wuh yel, heh du kupi gla-tor wuh pendulum swinging za' ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' vaksurik tor zhu-tor ik wak-vel tick; heh sometimes lu veh t' aifa peddlers had vesh' bi' heh scoured ish-veh abru heh prah ish-veh svi' rom shid, she would palikaya svi' heh kwul wuh hundred heh kau-leh fa' she prah tuckered si'. Au wouldn't nem-tor sovek donku na' ish-veh. Muhl, tra' vesh' wuh suk' outlandish parrot fi' tik vla t' wuh wak-vel, tor s' vel spo' gav, heh kras-tor abru gaudy. K' veh t' wuh parrots vesh' wuh aushfa tor t' crockery, heh wuh crockery dog k' wuh vath; heh lu du hish-tor au au squeaked, tonk'peh didn't tu'ash ish-veh ru'lut il glazhau natya il interested. Au squeaked k'fai ne'rak. Tra' vesh' wuh couple t' suk' kwai-kushel-rala sovek sak-tor si' za' eifa vel. Fi' wuh pasu svi' wuh svitan t' wuh tvi-shal vesh' wuh ves t' wuh lovely crockery ki'haf ik had savas heh zhar-kur heh peaches heh grapes piled abru svi' ish-veh, if vesh' mau redder heh yellower heh prettier do yeht ones nam-tor, tonk'peh au vikau't yeht fai'ei du kupi gla-tor wilat krus had prah chipped ska' heh gluvau wuh wan-kur gav, il whatever ish-veh vesh', ne'rak. Nash pasu had wuh wein tor s' vaksurik oilcloth, k' wuh yon-kur heh pla-kur sak-tor-eagle kras-tor fi' ish-veh, heh wuh kras-tor ek'zehl ek' pa'. Ish-veh sarlah ek' wuh yut s' philadelphia, au leralmin-tor. Tra' vesh' ein dunap, nuh', piled abru perfectly faikaik, fi' tik teruk t' wuh pasu. Veh vesh' wuh suk' skan bible bosh t' bikuv. Veh vesh' pilgrim's progress, pa' wuh sasu ik losrak ish-veh skan, ish-veh didn't leralmin po. I telv-tor considerable svi' ish-veh i' heh yi. Wuh star-krus vesh' eku'ki, tonk'peh dulai. Wuh'ashiv vesh' friendship's nufaya, bosh t' vaksurik tukh heh poetry; tonk'peh i didn't telv-tor wuh poetry. Wuh'ashiv vesh' henry krizhiv's starun, heh wuh'ashiv vesh' dr. Gunn's skan haseret, if var-tor du ek' pa' ra tor tor kuv wuh ak'shem vesh' has-bosh il tevik. Tra' vesh' wuh hymn dunap, heh wuh lot t' vath dunap. Heh tra' vesh' nice thresh-lanet ku-san, heh perfectly ralash, toonot bagged ne' svi' wuh svitan heh busted, spo' wuh hinek ki'haf. Au had bikuv geldau fi' wuh wallsmainly washingtons heh lafayettes, heh battles, heh pid-shal marys, heh veh puvutau "signing wuh afsakaya." tra' vesh' ein ik au puvutau crayons, if veh t' wuh daughters if vesh' tevik tor ish-veh sha' shal lu she vesh' goh leh-kau tevun hinek. Au vesh' natya s' sovek bikuv i ek'wak gla-tor beforeblacker, mostly, do nam-tor tsuri. Veh vesh' wuh kosu svi' wuh slim nesh-kur sai-vel, belted pi' ne' wuh armpits, k' bulges spo' wuh cabbage svi' wuh svitan t' wuh sleeves, heh wuh suk nesh-kur scoop-hilek bonnet k' wuh nesh-kur veil, heh wan-kur slim mal-nik tuhsau pa' k' nesh-kur tape, heh maut wee nesh-kur slippers, spo' wuh chisel, heh she vesh' leaning pensive fi' wuh tombstone fi' ish-veh gas'rak kar-nef, ne' wuh weeping willow, heh ish-veh vath el'ru hanging ne' ish-veh vla holding wuh wan-kur handkerchief heh wuh reticule, heh ne'rak wuh bikuv ish-veh leralmin-tor "dungau i worla gla-tor thee weht alas." wuh'ashiv veh vesh' wuh nu'ri t'sai k' ish-veh isachya ek' dref-tor abru zehik tor wuh fik t' ish-veh patam, heh knotted tra' svi' khom t' wuh dref spo' wuh ku-san-pla', heh she vesh' maf-tor vi' wuh handkerchief heh had wuh tevik kushel laying fi' its pla' svi' ish-veh vath el'ru k' its timut abru, heh ne'rak wuh bikuv ish-veh leralmin-tor "i dungau worla zhu-tor thy slor chirrup weht alas." tra' vesh' veh wilat wuh nu'ri t'sai vesh' na' wuh krani looking abru na' wuh aikum, heh bezhun-masu sahran ne' ish-veh nak; heh she had wuh tu'ash nuhm svi' veh el'ru k' nesh-kur sealing wax showing fi' veh rihk t' ish-veh, heh she vesh' mashing wuh locket k' wuh naf-elakh tor ish-veh tehnat ish-veh ru'lut, heh ne'rak wuh bikuv ish-veh leralmin-tor "heh tanaf thou hal-tor ha thou tanaf hal-tor alas." aifa vesh' ek' nice bikuv, i reckon, tonk'peh i didn't somehow seem tor nem-tor tor au, fai'ei kuv ek'wak i vesh' ne' wuh pi' au kwon-hau-ov mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh sovek-tods. Kanok-veh vesh' sorry she tev-tor, fai'ei she had laid si' wuh lot weht t' aifa bikuv tor tor, heh wuh ak'shem kupi gla-tor k' ra she had ovsoh ra au had pakik. Tonk'peh i reckoned ik k' ish-veh disposition she vesh' having wuh weh-rom wak svi' wuh graveyard. She vesh' na' ar'kadan fi' ra au leralmin-tor vesh' ish-veh greatest bikuv lu she nem-tor has-bosh, heh kanok gad heh kanok mu-yor ish-veh vesh' ish-veh prayer tor nam-tor kal-tor tor ha-tor till she prah ish-veh ovsoh, tonk'peh she worla prah wuh pavesh. Ish-veh vesh' wuh bikuv t' wuh nu'ri kosu svi' wuh wu wan-kur gown, standing fi' wuh rail t' wuh mesut ek' pok tor spen-tor ska', k' ish-veh isachya ek' ne' ish-veh pla', heh looking abru tor wuh aikum, k' wuh bezhun-masu sahran ne' ish-veh limuk, heh she had dahkuh kar hesha mes' ish-veh thasek, heh dahkuh kar sakadau si' svi' khom, heh dahkuh weht reaching abru na' wuh moonand wuh idea vesh' tor gla-tor if shif would glazhau buhfik, heh yi scratch si' ek' wuh vath kar; tonk'peh, u' i vesh' taran, she tev-tor fa' she prah ish-veh kashek tor abru, heh i' au potau nash bikuv abru' wuh patam t' wuh sar-tak svi' ish-veh tvi-shal, heh kanok wak ish-veh gad t'keshtan sarlah au geldau svai fi' ish-veh. Vath wak ish-veh vesh' ip-sut k' wuh pi' curtain. Wuh nu'ri kosu svi' wuh bikuv had wuh ves t' wuh nice slor limuk, tonk'peh tra' vesh' ni wehk kar ish-veh tor ish-veh glazhau nuh' spidery, seemed tor me. Nash nu'ri ko-kan potau wuh moguhsh-dunap lu she vesh' alive, heh nam-tor-tor tor paste obituaries heh kisheya heh nuf t' hasausu suffering svi' ish-veh s' wuh presbyterian observer, heh kitau poetry po' au s' ish-veh sha' patam. Ish-veh vesh' maut rom poetry. Nash nam-tor ra she kitau pa' wuh sa-kan k' wuh ahm t' stephen dowling bots ik tevan-tor ne' wuh muhl heh vesh' drownded: ode tor stephen dowling bots, dec'd heh did nu'ri stephen sicken, heh did nu'ri stephen tev-tor? Heh did wuh maf khaf-spol thicken, heh did wuh mourners maf? Rai; such vesh' ri wuh buk t' nu'ri stephen dowling bots; hi maf khaf-spol pauk ish-veh thickened, 'twas ri s' has-mar' shots. Rai whooping-huhsh did rack ish-veh nentu, il measles drear k' gla-tor; ri aifa impaired wuh sacred ahm t' stephen dowling bots. Despised ashaya kwul-tor ri k' woe ik patam t' curly knots, il skaun-sa'haf troubles laid ish-veh neik, nu'ri stephen dowling bots. O rai. Yi feim k' tearful bezhun, whilst i ish-veh buk tor var-tor. Ish-veh soul did s' nash samu panu hash-tor k' tevan-tor ne' wuh muhl. Au prah ish-veh si' heh emptied ish-veh; alas ish-veh vesh' nuh' tab-ma; ish-veh tam'a vesh' hal-tor na' tor torvukh aloft svi' wuh realms t' wuh rom heh lo'uk. Kuv emmeline grangerford kupi tor poetry spo' ik fa' she vesh' leh-keh, tra' ain't rai telling ra she kupi wuh ovsoh k'-heh-k'. Buck leralmin-tor she kupi rattle ska' poetry spo' nothing. She didn't ek'wak ma tor pehkaya tor nah-tor. Au leralmin-tor she would slap ne' wuh zehl, heh kuv she couldn't talal sovek-vel tor rhyme k' ish-veh would aishan scratch ish-veh si' heh slap ne' wuh'ashiv veh, heh fator'voh. She vikau't particular; she kupi kitau pa' sovek-vel du dvel-tor tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor kitau pa' aishan ni ish-veh vesh' sadful. Kanok wak wuh sasu tev-tor, il wuh kosu tev-tor, il wuh kan tev-tor, she would nam-tor fi' el'ru k' ish-veh "tribute" fa' au vesh' samu. She puvutau au tributes. Wuh behsu leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh hassu wuh'rak, yi emmeline, yi wuh undertakerthe undertaker worla prah svi' ahead t' emmeline tonk'peh wuh'wak, heh yi she geldau yon fi' wuh rhyme na' wuh tevik person's ahm, if vesh' whistler. She vikau't ek'wak wuh ka po' ik; she worla complained, tonk'peh she kinder pined maf heh did ri ha-tor wu. Ri donku-tor vel, wehk's wuh wak i tor myself hal-tor abru tor wuh pi' tvi-shal ik nam-tor-tor tor nam-tor ish-veh heh prah si' ish-veh ri donku-tor hinek moguhsh-dunap heh telv-tor svi' ish-veh lu ish-veh bikuv had vesh' aggravating me heh i had soured fi' ish-veh wuh pi'. I tishau ek' ik skan, tevik ones heh ek', heh vikau't going tor kal-tor sovek-vel sarlah svi' etek. Ri donku-tor emmeline tor poetry pa' ek' wuh tevik sutra lu she vesh' alive, heh ish-veh didn't seem gas'rak ik tra' vikau't kling tor tor ein pa' ish-veh i' she vesh' hal-tor; ni i ar'kada tor wadashaya si' wuh zehl il dahkuh myself, tonk'peh i couldn't seem tor tor ish-veh hal-tor somehow. Au potau emmeline's tvi-shal trim heh nice, heh ek' wuh vel teslau svi' ish-veh aishan wuh yut she tishau ki' au lu she vesh' alive, heh kling ek'wak yuk-tor tra'. Wuh hinek t'sai nem-tor tun t' wuh tvi-shal herself, hi tra' vesh' plenty t' niggers, heh she og-tor tra' wuh rom deal heh telv-tor ish-veh bible tra' mostly. Muhl, u' i vesh' taran pa' wuh parlor, tra' vesh' vaksurik curtains fi' wuh krani: wan-kur, k' bikuv kras-tor fi' au t' castles k' kas-elakh ek' ne' wuh temok, heh cattle coming ne' tor mon. Tra' vesh' wuh pi' hinek piano, nuh', ik had zhai-tukh sunil svi' ish-veh, i reckon, heh nothing vesh' ek'wak ni lovely u' tor zhu-tor wuh nu'ri t'sai uralau "wuh kim-shah naf nam-tor pushau" heh mavau "wuh puk t' prague" fi' ish-veh. Wuh temok t' ek' wuh tvi-shal vesh' plastered, heh danik had la'y fi' wuh lan-tol, heh wuh bosh kelek vesh' whitewashed fi' wuh s'udish. Ish-veh vesh' wuh dahtau kelek, heh wuh suk' tu'ash shi betwixt au vesh' roofed heh floored, heh sometimes wuh pasu vesh' eku tra' svi' wuh svitan t' wuh gad, heh ish-veh vesh' wuh samuyau, kel'o shi. Nothing couldn't nam-tor weh-rom. Heh vikau't wuh fasan rom, heh aishan bushels t' ish-veh nuh'! Chapter xviii. Col. Grangerford vesh' wuh gentleman, gla-tor du. Au vesh' wuh gentleman ek' abru'; heh ni vesh' ish-veh skan. Au vesh' muhl pukeshta, u' wuh taran nam-tor, heh ik's don u' mau svi' wuh sasu u' ish-veh nam-tor svi' wuh jarel, ni wuh kir'an douglas leralmin-tor, heh kling ek'wak wafu ik she vesh' t' wuh wuh'rak aristocracy svi' etwel kahr; heh pap au kwon-hau-ov leralmin-tor ish-veh, nuh', hi au vikau't rai weht quality do wuh mudcat himself. Col. Grangerford vesh' maut ha-vol heh maut slim, heh had wuh darkish-paly complexion, ri wuh glat t' yon-kur svi' ish-veh anywheres; au vesh' sok'i hohl-tor kanok asal ek' abru' ish-veh wonil limuk, heh au had wuh thinnest ves t' bru-lar, heh wuh thinnest ves t' han-sharular, heh wuh pid han, heh ras bezhun-zehl, heh wuh blackest ves t' bezhun, ne'hal-tor ni glu pla' ik au seemed spo' au vesh' looking s' suk-tauk na' du, u' du lau leralmin. Ish-veh fa-patam vesh' pid, heh ish-veh isachya vesh' nesh-kur heh zehik heh geldau tor ish-veh tipan. Ish-veh el'ru vesh' wu heh wonil, heh kanok gad t' ish-veh ha'kiv au shitau fi' wuh sok'i sav'el heh wuh bosh saikhut s' patam tor ash'ya tor s' linen ni wan-kur ish-veh dash-tor ish-veh bezhun tor glazhau na' ish-veh; heh fi' sundays au sai-vel-tor wuh pla-kur harr-tor-pal k' dvesh-tukh gonaf fi' ish-veh. Au lesh wuh mahogany cane k' wuh haul-tukh patam tor ish-veh. Tra' vikau't rai frivolishness pa' ish-veh, ri wuh zeshau, heh au vikau't ek'wak ral. Au vesh' u' ves u' au kupi beyou kupi olau ik, du fai-tor, heh ni du had guhl'es. Sometimes au abru'teruklar-ru'lut, heh ish-veh vesh' rom tor gla-tor; tonk'peh lu au straightened himself abru spo' wuh liberty-fek, heh wuh igen-wesh palikau tor hanuvaya si' s' ne' ish-veh bezhun-zehl, du aitlu tor qots'noi wuh lap wuh'rak, heh talal si' ra wuh tukh vesh' afterwards. Au didn't ek'wak ma tor var-tor anybody tor kashek ish-veh mannerseverybody vesh' kwon-hau-ov rom-mannered wilat au vesh'. Kanok-veh ashau ki' ish-veh pa', nuh'; au vesh' sunshine danik alwaysi tvai au tor ish-veh seem spo' rom igen-va. Lu au da-tor vi' wuh cloudbank ish-veh vesh' awful gu'gelik na' ulef wuh minute, heh ik vesh' hiyet; tra' wouldn't nothing hal-tor riyeht va'ashiv na' wuh wehk gad. Lu ish-veh heh wuh hinek t'sai sarlah ne' svi' wuh asal ek' wuh skan prah abru s' ish-veh ku-san heh mazhiv-kur-tor au rom-gad, heh didn't eku ne' va'ashiv till au had eku ne'. Yi tom heh bob went tor wuh sideboard wilat wuh decanter vesh', heh rish-tor wuh makh t' bitters heh handed ish-veh tor ish-veh, heh au meskarau ish-veh svi' ish-veh el'ru heh bek-tor till tom's heh bob's vesh' rish-tor, heh yi au ovalau heh leralmin-tor, "etwel gu-vam tor du, osu, heh madam; " heh au ovalau wuh least zeshau svi' wuh panu heh leralmin-tor nemaiyo, heh ni au drank, ek' rehkuh, heh bob heh tom mukau wuh spoonful t' masu fi' wuh slor-tukh heh wuh mite t' whisky il savas brandy svi' wuh lanet t' ish-veh tumblers, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor me heh buck, heh etek drank tor wuh hinek sutra nuh'. Bob vesh' wuh oldest heh tom nexttall, vaksurik sasu k' maut sax'ksei tipan heh khav-kur limuk, heh wu nesh-kur isachya heh nesh-kur bezhun. Au sai-vel-tor svi' wan-kur linen s' patam tor ash'ya, spo' wuh hinek gentleman, heh sai-vel-tor sax'ksei panama taik. Yi tra' vesh' din-tor charlotte; she vesh' dah-leh-kaukuh, heh ha-vol heh yaut heh grand, tonk'peh u' rom u' she kupi nam-tor lu she vikau't stirred abru; tonk'peh lu she vesh', she had wuh glazhau ik would tor du wilt svi' ish-veh ash'yaidar, spo' ish-veh sa-mekh. She vesh' vaksurik. Ni vesh' ish-veh ko-kai, din-tor sophia, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' wuh natya ves. She vesh' gentle heh slor spo' wuh dove, heh she vesh' goh dah-leh. Tik person had ish-veh sha' nigger tor bek-tor fi' thembuck nuh'. T'nash-veh nigger had wuh monstrous hagik wak, fai'ei i vikau't nam-tor-tor tor having anybody tor sovek-vel na' me, tonk'peh buck's vesh' fi' wuh spen-tor danik t' wuh wak. Nash vesh' ek' tra' vesh' t' wuh skan i', tonk'peh tra' nam-tor-tor tor nam-tor morethree sa-fu; au prah pustau; heh emmeline ik tev-tor. Wuh hinek gentleman puma wuh lot t' uroshal heh abru' wuh hundred niggers. Sometimes wuh tuh t' sutra would sarlah tra', horseback, s' lehkuh il leh-kau mile pa', heh stay kaukuh il shehkuh gad, heh ma such junketings pauk pa' heh fi' wuh pilash, heh tam-tor heh picnics svi' wuh lapan daytimes, heh rin'k'n na' wuh kelek mu-yor. Aifa sutra vesh' mostly kinfolks t' wuh skan. Wuh sasu katau ish-veh pohshayek k' au. Ish-veh vesh' wuh handsome lot t' quality, i var-tor du. Tra' vesh' wuh'ashiv maat t' aristocracy pa' therefive il shehkuh familiesmostly t' wuh ahm t' shepherdson. Au vesh' u' pid-toned heh muhl pukeshta heh don-ka heh grand u' wuh tribe t' grangerfords. Wuh shepherdsons heh grangerfords nam-tor-tor wuh ka steamboat landing, if vesh' pa' dahkuh mile abru' etwel kelek; ni sometimes lu i went abru tra' k' wuh lot t' etwel sular-ves i nam-tor-tor tor gla-tor wuh lot t' wuh shepherdsons tra' fi' ish-veh tok-ti jarel. Veh gad buck heh me vesh' maf si' svi' wuh lapan hunting, heh puzhu-tor wuh jarel coming. Etek vesh' mes wuh fau-yut. Buck leralmin-tor: "sahris! Spen-tor na' wuh lapan!" etek ovsoh ish-veh, heh yi peeped ne' wuh lapan k'fai wuh mor. Takov ak wuh splendid nu'ri sasu sarlah galloping ne' wuh fau-yut, setting ish-veh jarel hagik heh looking spo' wuh ask'ersu. Au had ish-veh pohshayek mes' ish-veh pommel. I had gla-tor ish-veh fa'. Ish-veh vesh' nu'ri harney shepherdson. I puzhu-tor buck's pohshayek hal-tor ska' na' t'nash-veh kaluk, heh harney's taik tumbled ska' s' ish-veh patam. Au runem-tor ish-veh pohshayek heh fau-tor zehik tor wuh shi wilat etek vesh' ip-sut. Tonk'peh etek didn't bek-tor. Etek palikau k'fai wuh lapan fi' wuh sahr-tor. Wuh lapan vikau't bali, ni i glazhau abru' t'nash-veh tipan tor sayutau wuh bullet, heh dah'wak i gla-tor harney wein buck k' ish-veh pohshayek; heh yi au fau-tor maf wuh yut au cometo prah ish-veh taik, i reckon, tonk'peh i couldn't gla-tor. Etek worla pehkau sahran till etek prah ha-kel. Wuh hinek gentleman's bezhun blazed wuh minute'twas sanosh, mainly, i judgedthen ish-veh limuk wihfelau t' smoothed ne', heh au leralmin-tor, ves t' gentle: "i ri tor spo' ik shooting s' za' wuh bush. Po didn't du ash vi' wuh fau-yut, t'nash-veh sa-kan?" "wuh shepherdsons ri tor, sa-mekh. Au kwon-hau-ov nem-tor advantage." din-tor charlotte she meskarau ish-veh patam abru spo' wuh ko-te'kru du' buck vesh' telling ish-veh var, heh ish-veh han-sharular sak-tor heh ish-veh bezhun snapped. Wuh dahkuh nu'ri sasu glazhau gu'gelik, tonk'peh worla leralmin-tor nothing. Din-tor sophia she da-tor spoh, tonk'peh wuh kur sarlah pla' lu she afer-tor wuh sasu vikau't dash-tor. Ak u' i kupi prah buck ne' k' wuh corn-cribs ne' wuh lap k' ourselves, i leralmin-tor: "did du aitlun tor stau ish-veh, buck?" "muhl, i sihaya i did." "ra did au tor tor du?" "ish-veh? Au worla ovsoh nothing tor me." "muhl, yi, ra did du aitlun tor stau ish-veh na'?" "po, nothingonly ish-veh's fi' khrosahp t' wuh naul." "ra's wuh naul?" "po, wilat vesh' du ashenau? Ri tor du fai-tor ra wuh naul nam-tor?" "worla puzhu-tor t' ish-veh beforetell me pa' ish-veh." "muhl, " leralmin-tor buck, "wuh naul nam-tor nash yut. Wuh sasu has wuh quarrel k' wuh'ashiv sasu, heh stau ish-veh; yi ik vath sasu's sa-kai stau ish-veh; yi wuh vath sa-kai, fi' fi' vla, hal-tor na' veh wuh'ashiv; yi wuh krei val inand k'-heh-k' kanok-veh's pustau ska', heh tra' ain't rai weht naul. Tonk'peh ish-veh's ves t' vohris, heh nem-tor wuh akarshif." "has nash-veh vesh' going fi' wu, buck?" "muhl, i dang reckon! Ish-veh palikau reh-leh tevun ago, il som'ers bi' tra'. Tra' vesh' trouble 'bout vel, heh yi wuh lawsuit tor settle ish-veh; heh wuh saikhut went agin veh t' wuh sasu, heh ni au abru heh pohshaya wuh sasu ik skil-tor wuh suitwhich au would naturally tor, veling. Anybody would." "ra vesh' wuh trouble pa', buck?solektra?" "i reckon maybei ri tor fai-tor." "muhl, vi ovsoh wuh shooting? Vesh' ish-veh wuh grangerford il wuh shepherdson?" "tor-gav, uf tor i fai-tor? Ish-veh vesh' ni wu ago." "ri tor anybody fai-tor?" "oh, ha, pa fai-tor, i reckon, heh ein t' wuh vath hinek sutra; tonk'peh au ri tor fai-tor i' ra wuh zehl vesh' pa' svi' wuh wuh'rak shi." "has tra' vesh' wehk pustau, buck?" "ha; gas'rak klon pavesh t' mem-lu til-kum. Tonk'peh au ri tor kwon-hau-ov stau. Pa's prah wuh zamu buckshot svi' ish-veh; tonk'peh au ri tor kashek ish-veh 'cuz au ri tor rasathau mau, anyway. Bob's vesh' skrim-tor abru ein k' wuh bowie, heh tom's vesh' dash-tor wuh'wak il dah'wak." "has anybody vesh' pustau nash tevun, buck?" "ha; etek prah veh heh au prah veh. 'bout rehkuh tevun-krus ago t'nash-veh krei bud, leh-keh tevun hinek, vesh' riding k'fai wuh lapan fi' t'vath vla t' wuh pilash, heh didn't ma rai wun k' ish-veh, if vesh' tenai' duh'es, heh svi' wuh lonesome shi au zhu-tor wuh jarel wuh-coming za' ish-veh, heh gla-tor hinek baldy shepherdson wuh-linkin' po' ish-veh k' ish-veh pohshayek svi' ish-veh el'ru heh ish-veh wan-kur isachya wuh-hashan svi' wuh salan; heh 'stead t' jumping ska' heh taking tor wuh achut, bud 'lowed au kupi si'-sahr-tor ish-veh; ni au had ish-veh, nip heh k'hy, na' kaukuh mile il weht, wuh hinek sasu wuh-gaining ek' wuh wak; ni na' kim-shah bud gla-tor ish-veh vikau't sovek nam-tor-tor, ni au pehkau heh limuk-tor pa' ni u' ki' wuh bullet razh svi' khom, du fai-tor, heh wuh hinek sasu au fau-tor abru heh pohshaya ish-veh ne'. Tonk'peh au didn't git mau pavesh tor tizh-tor ish-veh kunli, na' svi' wuh wehk gad etwel sular-ves laid ish-veh si'." "i reckon ik hinek sasu vesh' wuh coward, buck." "i reckon au vikau't wuh coward. Ri k' wuh tenai' glan. Tra' ain't wuh coward ekhlami shepherdsonsnot wuh veh. Heh tra' ain't rai cowards svi' wuh grangerfords either. Po, ik hinek sasu kep' abru ish-veh shaht svi' wuh puk veh gad na' ulef wuh wadan tehnat rehkuh grangerfords, heh sasarlah skilsu.
