Au vesh' ek' wuh-horseback; au lit ska' t' ish-veh jarel heh prah za' wuh pi' woodpile, heh kep' ish-veh jarel fa' ish-veh tor pehkaya wuh bullets; tonk'peh wuh grangerfords stayed fi' ish-veh jarel heh capered pa' wuh hinek sasu, heh peppered maf na' ish-veh, heh au peppered maf na' au. Ish-veh heh ish-veh jarel fi' went ha-kel takov leaky heh crippled, tonk'peh wuh grangerfords had tor nam-tor zaprah homeand veh t' 'em vesh' tevik, heh wuh'ashiv tev-tor wuh thurai gad. Rai, osu; kuv wuh ak'shem's si' hunting na' cowards au ri tor aitlun tor duhsu maf sovek wak ekhlami shepherdsons, becuz au ri tor kosh-ves sovek t' ik ves." thurai gad etek ek' went tor church, pa' rehkuh mile, kanok-veh wuh-horseback. Wuh sasu nem-tor ish-veh pohshayek bi', ni did buck, heh potau au svi' ish-veh mal-nef il lam-tor au handy tehnat wuh temok. Wuh shepherdsons ovsoh wuh ka. Ish-veh vesh' takov ornery preachingall pa' brotherly ashaya, heh such-spo' tiresomeness; tonk'peh kanok-veh leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh rom sermon, heh au ek' variben ish-veh abru' going ha-kel, heh had such wuh powerful lot tor leralmin pa' odva heh rom ar'kada heh elik takov heh preforeordestination, heh i ri tor fai-tor ra ek', ik ish-veh did seem tor me tor nam-tor veh t' wuh roughest sundays i had sahr-tor mes' wi. Pa' wuh wadan po' aru-yem kanok-veh vesh' dozing pa', ein svi' ish-veh ku-san heh ein svi' ish-veh tvi-shal, heh ish-veh prah tor nam-tor takov pasik. Buck heh wuh dog vesh' sakadau si' fi' wuh yar svi' wuh yel ralash asleep. I went abru tor etwel tvi-shal, heh judged i would nem-tor wuh nap myself. I afer-tor ik slor din-tor sophia standing svi' ish-veh svep, if vesh' nam-tor' ours, heh she nem-tor me svi' ish-veh tvi-shal heh ikap-tor wuh svep maut mos, heh ya'akash me kuv i tishau ish-veh, heh i leralmin-tor i did; heh she ya'akash me kuv i would tor vel na' ish-veh heh ri var-tor anybody, heh i leralmin-tor i would. Yi she leralmin-tor she'd forgot ish-veh testament, heh losrak ish-veh svi' wuh ku-san na' church svi' dahkuh vath dunap, heh would i trel si' hizhuk heh hal-tor tra' heh zaprah ish-veh tor ish-veh, heh ri leralmin nothing tor kling. I leralmin-tor i would. Ni i slid si' heh trel-tor ska' abru wuh fau-yut, heh tra' vikau't anybody na' wuh church, kaula sos'eh wuh hog il dahkuh, na' tra' vikau't sovek klachek fi' wuh svep, heh hogs tishau wuh puncheon lan-tol svi' belaar-wak fai'ei ish-veh's samuyau. Kuv du beglanau, danik sular-ves ri tor hal-tor tor church goh lu au've prah tor; tonk'peh wuh hog nam-tor natya. Leralmin-tor i tor myself, vel's abru; ish-veh ain't malatik na' wuh ko-kan tor nam-tor svi' such wuh wadashaya pa' wuh testament. Ni i mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh hutau, heh si' eku-tor wuh pi' krus t' dun k' "ulef-vesht dahkuh" kitau fi' ish-veh k' wuh hish. I ransacked ish-veh, tonk'peh couldn't talal sovek-kitok. I couldn't tor sovek-vel s' ik, ni i shitau wuh dun svi' wuh dunap va'ashiv, heh lu i prah ha-kel heh upstairs tra' vesh' din-tor sophia svi' ish-veh svep waiting na' me. She seshau me svi' heh ikap-tor wuh svep; yi she glazhau svi' wuh testament till she afer-tor wuh dun, heh u' ak u' she telv-tor ish-veh she glazhau glad; heh fa' wuh ak'shem kupi nah-tor she runem-tor me heh mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh lerakhovau, heh leralmin-tor i vesh' wuh buhfik sa-kan svi' wuh panu, heh ri tor var-tor anybody. She vesh' mighty yon-kur svi' wuh limuk na' wuh minute, heh ish-veh bezhun lighted abru, heh ish-veh tor ish-veh powerful takov. I vesh' wuh rom deal astonished, tonk'peh lu i prah t'nash-veh esh i ya'akash ish-veh ra wuh dun vesh' pa', heh she ya'akash me kuv i had telv-tor ish-veh, heh i leralmin-tor rai, heh she ya'akash me kuv i kupi telv-tor kitaun, heh i var-tor ish-veh "rai, goh dirik-el'ru, " heh yi she leralmin-tor wuh dun vikau't sovek-vel tonk'peh wuh dunap-ulidar tor potau ish-veh shi, heh i lau hal-tor heh mavau i'. I went ska' ne' tor wuh pilash, studying abru' nash vel, heh takov ak i pubeglanau ik t'nash-veh nigger vesh' zahalik bi' za'. Lu etek vesh' s' glan t' wuh kelek au glazhau pla' heh pa' wuh dahr, heh yi sarlah wuh-sahran, heh leralmin-tor: "mars jawge, kuv du'll sarlah ne' vi' de flash i'll gluvaya du wuh bosh tuh o' masu-moccasins." nah-tor i, ik's mighty curious; au leralmin-tor ik za-gad. Au oughter fai-tor wuh ak'shem ri tor ashaya masu-moccasins hiyet tor hal-tor pa' hunting na' au. Ra nam-tor au abru tor, anyway? Ni i leralmin-tor: "ek' gas'rak; sahr-tor ahead." i zahal-tor wuh ulef wuh mile; yi au kwul-tor si' abru' wuh flash, heh masu-tor mal-nik glu u' mau u' wuh'ashiv ulef-mile. Sarlah etek tor wuh pi' pa'ash krus t' solektra if vesh' pseth heh maut bali k' lap heh bushes heh kas-elakh, heh au leralmin-tor: "du shove gas'rak svi' dah jist wuh zamu ash-tor, mars jawge; dah's whah dey nam-tor. I's nei 'm befo'; i ri tor k'yer tor gla-tor 'em rai mo'." yi au slopped gas'rak bi' heh went maf, heh takov ak wuh lap ip-sut ish-veh. I poked vi' wuh shi wuh-yut heh sarlah tor wuh pi' tu'ash patch u' suk' u' wuh shi'yuk ek' geldau pa' k' kas-elakh, heh afer-tor wuh sasu laying tra' asleepand, k' jings, ish-veh vesh' t'nash-veh hinek jim! I waked ish-veh abru, heh i reckoned ish-veh vesh' going tor nam-tor wuh grand ak'wikmun tor ish-veh tor gla-tor me va'ashiv, tonk'peh ish-veh vikau't. Au nearly maf-tor au vesh' ni glad, tonk'peh au vikau't ak'wikmun. Leralmin-tor au mahal-tor bi' za' me ik mu-yor, heh puzhu-tor me saul kanok wak, tonk'peh dasn't kilko-srashiv, fai'ei au didn't aitlun kling tor pick ish-veh abru heh nem-tor ish-veh vi' slavery va'ashiv. Leralmin-tor au: "i prah dash-tor wuh pi', en couldn't mahal-tor fas', ni i wuz wuh considable yut behine du na' de las'; lu du landed i reck'ned i kupi ketch abru wid du fi' de lan' 'dout havin' tor saul na' du, tonk'peh lu gla-tor nash-veh dat kelek i palikau tor hal-tor vohris. I 'uz ska' nuh' ausachya tor zhu-tor ra dey leralmin tor youi wuz 'fraid o' de dogs; tonk'peh lu ish-veh 'uz ek' hizhuk agin, i knowed du's svi' de kelek, ni i kwul-tor si' na' de lapan tor bek-tor na' gad. Lehkuh-mal svi' de mawnin' ein er de niggers sarlah bi', gwyne tor de vunai, en dey tuk me en gluvau me dis shi, whah de dogs mokuhlek't yut me fi' khrosahp o' de masu, en dey katau me truck tor yokul kanok mu-yor, en var-tor me uf du's wuh-gitt'n bi'." "po didn't du var-tor t'nash-veh jack tor zaprah me la' sooner, jim?" "muhl, 'twarn't rai nam-tor-tor tor 'sturb du, huck, var-tor etek kupi tor sumfnbut etek's ek' gas'rak i'. I ben wuh-buyin' sunil en sunil en vittles, u' i prah wuh chanst, en wuh-patchin' abru de raf' mu-yor lu" "ra marshak, jim?" "etwel ole raf'." "du tvai tor leralmin etwel hinek marshak vikau't smashed ek' tor flinders?" "rai, she vikau't. She vesh' tore abru wuh rom dealone en' t' ish-veh vesh'; tonk'peh dey vikau't rai lo'uk klau ovsoh, fi''y etwel pash-tor vesh' mos' ek' los'. Ef etek hadn' taul' ni glu en mahal-tor ni ausachya ne' masu, en de mu-yor hadn' ben ni gu'gelik, en etek vikau't ni sk'yerd, en ben sich punkin-patam, u' de sayin' nam-tor, etek'd wuh nei de raf'. Tonk'peh ish-veh's jis' u' muhl etek didn't, 'kase i' she's ek' teslau abru agin mos' u' rom u' uzh, en etek's prah wuh uzh lot o' tukh, svi' de shi o' ra 'uz los'." "po, uf did du prah meskaraya t' wuh marshak va'ashiv, jimdid du kum ish-veh?" "uf i gwyne tor ketch ish-veh en i si' svi' de lapan? Rai; ein er de niggers foun' ish-veh ketched fi' wuh snag bi' heah svi' de ben', en dey ip-sut ish-veh svi' wuh crick 'mongst de willows, en dey wuz ni mau jawin' 'bout if un 'um she b'wu tor de mos' dat sarlah nash-veh tor heah 'bout ish-veh pooty ak, ni i ups en settles de trouble k' tellin' 'um she ri tor b'wu tor rim uv um, tonk'peh tor du en me; en i ast 'm kuv dey gwyne tor runem wuh nu'ri wan-kur genlman's propaty, en git wuh ip-sut'n na' ish-veh? Den i gin 'm lehkuh cents apiece, en dey 'uz mighty muhl satisfied, en wisht ein mo' raf's 'ud sarlah bi' en tor 'm don-ka agin. Dey's mighty rom tor me, dese niggers nam-tor, en whatever i aitlu 'm tor tor ausachya me, i doan' ma tor ast 'm dah'wak, honey. Dat jack's wuh rom nigger, en pooty klon." "ha, au nam-tor. Au ain't ek'wak var-tor me du vesh' la'; var-tor me tor sarlah, heh au'd gluvaya me wuh lot t' masu-moccasins. Kuv sovek-vel pavesh-tor au ain't rish-tor abru svi' ish-veh. Au mokuhlek leralmin au worla gla-tor etek teretuhr, heh ish-veh'll nam-tor wuh yeht'es." i ri tor aitlun tor variben mau pa' wuh thurai gad. I reckon i'll tresahk ish-veh takov pen. I waked abru pa' gad-keshtan, heh vesh' wuh-going tor da-tor abru' heh hal-tor tor yuk va'ashiv, lu i pubeglanau uf fam dvun ish-veh wasdidn't seem tor nam-tor anybody stirring. Ik vikau't tsuri. Thurai i pubeglanau ik buck vesh' abru heh hal-tor. Muhl, i prah abru, wuh-wondering, heh hal-tor ne' stairsnobody pa'; kanok-vei u' fam dvun u' wuh aushfa. Aishan wuh ka s'udish. Nah-tor i, ra tor ish-veh tvai? Ne' k' wuh lapan-tuh i sarlah mes' t'nash-veh jack, heh leralmin-tor: "ra's ish-veh ek' pa'?" leralmin-tor au: "ri tor du fai-tor, mars jawge?" "rai, " leralmin-tor i, "i ri tor." "muhl, den, din-tor sophia's sahr-tor ska'! 'deed she has. She sahr-tor ska' svi' de mu-yor ein timenobody ri tor fai-tor jis' lu; sahr-tor ska' tor prah telik tor dat nu'ri harney shepherdson, du knowleastways, ni dey 'spec. De fambly foun' ish-veh si' 'bout ulef wuh wadan agomaybe wuh pi' mo'en' i var-tor du dey vikau't rai wak los'. Sich wuh'ashiv hurryin' abru pohshayek en hosses du worla gla-tor! De kosu sular-ves has hal-tor na' tor stir abru de relations, en ole mars saul en de sa-kan k'hy dey pohshayek en fau-tor abru de pilash fau-yut na' tor ar'kadan tor ketch dat nu'ri sasu en stau ish-veh 'fo' au pi-maat git acrost de pilash wid din-tor sophia. I reck'n dey's gwyne tor nam-tor mighty rough wak." "buck went ska' 'thout waking me abru." "muhl, i reck'n au did! Dey vikau't gwyne tor rish du abru svi' ish-veh. Mars buck au putush-tor abru ish-veh pohshayek en 'lowed au's gwyne tor zaprah ha-kel wuh shepherdson il bust. Muhl, dey'll nam-tor plenty un 'm dah, i reck'n, en du sihaya du au'll zaprah veh ef au gits wuh chanst." i nem-tor abru wuh pilash fau-yut u' lerash u' i kupi shitau. K'-heh-k' i palikau tor zhu-tor pohshayek wuh rom yut ska'. Lu sarlah nash-veh svi' glan t' wuh lap-fek mahr-kel heh wuh woodpile wilat wuh steamboats shasol, i ar'kada bi' ne' wuh lap heh achut till i prah tor wuh rom shi, heh yi i clumb abru vi' wuh snauk t' wuh cottonwood ik vesh' s' pulau, heh glantau. Tra' vesh' wuh lapan-lan kehkuh ash'ya pid wuh pi' yut svi' khom t' wuh lap, heh wuh'rak i vesh' going tor ip-sut za' ik; tonk'peh sos'eh ish-veh vesh' luckier i didn't. Tra' vesh' kehkuh il kaukuh sasu cavorting pa' fi' ish-veh jarel svi' wuh tu'ash shi fa' wuh lap-fek mahr-kel, cussing heh yelling, heh trying tor prah na' wuh couple t' nu'ri chaps ik vesh' za' wuh lapan-lan alongside t' wuh steamboat landing; tonk'peh au couldn't sarlah ish-veh. Kanok wak veh t' au gluvau himself fi' wuh pilash vla t' wuh woodpile au prah pohshaya na'. Wuh dahkuh sa-kan vesh' squatting pla' tor pla' za' wuh tuh, ni au kupi glantau fi' yut. K'-heh-k' wuh sasu pehkau cavorting pa' heh yelling. Au palikau riding na' wuh mahr-kel; yi abru prah veh t' wuh sa-kan, bes-tor wuh br'xan o'lid abru' wuh lapan-lan, heh eku-tor veh t' au s' ish-veh saddle. Ek' wuh sasu spen-tor ska' t' ish-veh jarel heh runem-tor wuh dash-tor veh heh palikau tor lesh ish-veh tor wuh mahr-kel; heh ik minute wuh dahkuh sa-kan palikau fi' wuh sahr-tor. Au prah ulef yut tor wuh lap i vesh' svi' fa' wuh sasu pubeglanau. Yi wuh sasu gla-tor au, heh spen-tor fi' ish-veh jarel heh nem-tor si' po' au. Au nazh-tor fi' wuh sa-kan, tonk'peh ish-veh didn't tor rai rom, wuh sa-kan had nuh' rom wuh palikaya; au prah tor wuh woodpile ik vesh' svi' khom t' t'nash-veh lap, heh trel-tor svi' za' ish-veh, heh ni au had wuh bulge fi' wuh sasu va'ashiv. Veh t' wuh sa-kan vesh' buck, heh wuh vath vesh' wuh slim nu'ri chap pa' leh-nau tevun hinek. Wuh sasu tres-tor pa' awhile, heh yi fau-tor maf. U' ak u' au vesh' s' glan i uralau si' tor buck heh var-tor ish-veh. Au didn't fai-tor ra tor tor t' t'nash-veh spes coming s' wuh lap palikauk. Au vesh' awful ak'wikmun. Au var-tor me tor glantau si' nasik heh kal-tor ish-veh fai-tor lu wuh sasu sarlah svi' glan va'ashiv; leralmin-tor au vesh' abru tor ein devilment il otherwouldn't nam-tor hal-tor wu. I istau i vesh' s' ik lap, tonk'peh i dasn't sarlah ne'. Buck palikau tor maf heh tres, heh 'lowed ik ish-veh heh ish-veh krei joe (ik vesh' wuh vath nu'ri chap) would tor abru na' nash gad wi. Au leralmin-tor ish-veh sa-mekh heh ish-veh dahkuh sa-kai vesh' pustau, heh dahkuh il rehkuh t' wuh nemut. Leralmin-tor wuh shepherdsons laid na' au svi' ambush. Buck leralmin-tor ish-veh sa-mekh heh sa-kai ought tor bek-tor na' ish-veh relationsthe shepherdsons vesh' nuh' karik na' au. I ya'akash ish-veh ra vesh' shetau t' nu'ri harney heh din-tor sophia. Au leralmin-tor au'd prah mes' wuh pilash heh vesh' safe. I vesh' glad t' ik; tonk'peh wuh yut buck did nem-tor fi' fai'ei au didn't khartau tor stau harney ik gad au pohshaya na' himi hain't ek'wak puzhu-tor sovek-vel spo' ish-veh. Ek' t' wuh sudden, bang! Bang! Bang! Hal-tor rehkuh il kehkuh gunsthe sasu had trel-tor pa' k'fai wuh lapan heh sarlah svi' s' za' rik' ish-veh jarel! Wuh sa-kan spen-tor na' wuh riverboth t' au hurtand u' au mahal-tor ne' wuh current wuh sasu sahr-tor bi' wuh kutra shooting na' au heh uralaun si', "stau au, stau au!" ish-veh tor me ni has-bosh i danik tevan-tor si' t' wuh lap. I ain't wuh-going tor var-tor ek' ik happenedit would tor me has-bosh va'ashiv kuv i vesh' tor tor ik. I istau i hadn't ek'wak sarlah ashore ik mu-yor tor gla-tor such vel. I ain't ek'wak going tor prah ikap-tor t' themlots t' wak i sahr-tor pa' au. I stayed svi' wuh lap till ish-veh palikau tor prah gu'gelik, kwes tor sarlah ne'. Sometimes i puzhu-tor pohshayek maf ska' svi' wuh lapan; heh dah'wak i gla-tor pi' gangs t' sasu ausahr vesht wuh lap-fek mahr-kel k' pohshayek; ni i reckoned wuh trouble vesh' fam dvun wuh-going fi'. I vesh' mighty downhearted; ni i tor abru t'nash-veh kashek i wouldn't ek'wak hal-tor anear ik kelek va'ashiv, fai'ei i reckoned i vesh' tor tenai, somehow. I judged ik ik krus t' dun tvai ik din-tor sophia vesh' tor ragel-tor harney somewheres na' ulef-vesht dahkuh heh sahr-tor ska'; heh i judged i ought tor var-tor ish-veh sa-mekh pa' ik dun heh wuh curious yut she bae'cok, heh yi sos'eh au would wuh klacha ish-veh abru, heh nash awful mess wouldn't ek'wak pavesh-tor. Lu i prah ne' s' wuh lap, i crept bi' ne' wuh pilash kutra wuh krus, heh afer-tor wuh dahkuh ak'shem laying svi' wuh rihk t' wuh masu, heh seshau na' au till i prah au ashore; yi i wein-tor abru ish-veh limuk, heh prah maf u' sahris u' i kupi. I maf-tor wuh pi' lu i vesh' covering abru buck's limuk, na' au vesh' mighty rom tor me. Ish-veh vesh' aishan gu'gelik i'. I worla went be' wuh kelek, tonk'peh kwul-tor k'fai wuh lapan heh tor na' wuh flash. Jim vikau't fi' ish-veh vikuvtra, ni i tramped ska' svi' wuh brax na' wuh crick, heh crowded k'fai wuh willows, yon-kur-fal tor spen-tor aboard heh prah s' ik awful shasol. Wuh marshak vesh' hal-tor! T'nash-veh souls, tonk'peh i vesh' pahth-tor! I couldn't prah t'nash-veh esh na' danik wuh minute. Yi i ashenau wuh saul. Wuh spes ri dah-leh-kaukuh ash'ya s' me leralmin-tor: "rom lan'! Nam-tor dat du, honey? Doan' tor rai ralash." ish-veh vesh' jim's voicenothing ek'wak sounded ni rom fa'. I sahr-tor bi' wuh kutra wuh krus heh prah aboard, heh jim au runem-tor me heh teraya-martaya me, au vesh' ni glad tor gla-tor me. Au leralmin-tor: "tor-gav kudau du, chile, i 'uz gas'rak ne' sho' du's tevik agin. Jack's vesh' heah; au leralmin au reck'n du's ben pohshaya, kase du didn' sarlah ha-kel rai mo'; ni i's jes' dis minute wuh startin' de raf' ne' na' de mouf er de crick, ni's tor nam-tor ek' pok na' tor shove si' en trasha ak u' jack sarlah agin en var-tor me na' ac'ruth du nam-tor tevik. Lawsy, i's mighty glad tor git du pla' agin, honey." i leralmin-tor: "ek' rightthat's mighty rom; au skil-tor't talal me, heh au'll nah-tor i've vesh' pustau, heh markau ne' wuh riverthere's vel abru tra' ik'll gol'nev au nah-tor soso ri tor du pak-tor rai wak, jim, tonk'peh aishan shove ska' na' wuh suk' masu u' sahris u' ek'wak du mokuhlek." i worla olau hagik till wuh marshak vesh' dahkuh mile ne' tra' heh si' svi' wuh svitan t' wuh mississippi. Yi etek geldau abru etwel glantokaya makh-yonet, heh judged ik etek vesh' elik heh safe wuh'wak weht. I hadn't had wuh zeshaya tor yokul opi' za-gad, ni jim au prah si' ein corn-dodgers heh buttermilk, heh pork heh cabbage heh greensthere ain't nothing svi' wuh panu ni rom lu ish-veh's pufas-tor rightand whilst i yokul t'nash-veh mu'yor-yem etek variben, heh had wuh rom wak. I vesh' powerful glad tor prah maf s' wuh naul-tor, heh ni vesh' jim tor prah maf s' wuh flash. Etek leralmin-tor tra' vikau't rai ha-kel spo' wuh marshak, po' ek'. Vath shitau tor seem ni runelau abru heh smothery, tonk'peh wuh marshak ri tor. Du olau mighty elik heh hagik heh kel'o fi' wuh marshak. Chapter xix. Dahkuh il rehkuh gad heh mu-yor went k'; i reckon i lau leralmin au mahal-tor k', au slid bi' ni hizhuk heh mos heh lovely. La' nam-tor wuh yut etek shitau svi' wuh wak. Ish-veh vesh' wuh monstrous suk' pilash ne' theresometimes wuh mile heh wuh ulef eik; etek sahr-tor mu-yor, heh laid abru heh ip-sut daytimes; ak u' mu-yor vesh' danik hal-tor etek pehkau navigating heh tied upnearly kwon-hau-ov svi' wuh tevik masu ne' wuh tow-patam; heh yi tresahk nu'ri cottonwoods heh willows, heh ip-sut wuh marshak k' au. Yi etek eku si' wuh zehl. Thurai etek slid vi' wuh pilash heh had wuh mahal-tor, ni u' tor freshen abru heh samuyau ska'; yi etek eku ne' fi' wuh mazhivik lanet wilat wuh masu vesh' pa' mal-nef glu, heh glantau wuh gad-ha'khlup sarlah. Ri wuh ralash anywheresperfectly stilljust spo' wuh bosh panu vesh' asleep, goh sometimes wuh bullfrogs wuh-cluttering, sos'eh. Wuh wuh'rak vel tor gla-tor, looking maf abru' wuh masu, vesh' wuh ves t' pasik linethat vesh' wuh lapan fi' t'vath vla; du couldn't tor nothing else si'; yi wuh spoh shi svi' wuh igen; yi weht paleness spreading pa'; yi wuh pilash softened abru maf ska', heh vikau't nesh-kur sovek weht, tonk'peh zhai-kur; du kupi gla-tor pi' gu'gelik gla-tor drifting bi' ek'wak ni irak awaytrading scows, heh such vel; heh wu nesh-kur streaksrafts; sometimes du kupi zhu-tor wuh fnashtaya screaking; il jumbled abru spes, ish-veh vesh' ni fam dvun, heh sounds sarlah ni irak; heh k'-heh-k' du kupi gla-tor wuh wesh fi' wuh masu if du fai-tor k' wuh glazhau t' wuh wesh ik tra''s wuh snag tra' svi' wuh swift current if breaks fi' ish-veh heh tor ik wesh glazhau ik yut; heh gla-tor du wuh mist tcha abru ska' t' wuh masu, heh wuh she'rak reddens abru, heh wuh pilash, heh du tor si' wuh lap-fek-thif'etek svi' wuh rihk t' wuh lapan, maf fi' wuh kutra fi' t'vath vla t' wuh pilash, hasu wuh woodyard, kesik, heh piled k' au kravau ni du mokuhlek lehm wuh dog k'fai ish-veh anywheres; yi wuh nice pi'salan sikar abru, heh sarlah fanning du s' abru' tra', ni samuyau heh sluk heh slor tor fnish-tor fi' khrosahp t' wuh lapan heh wuh svai; tonk'peh sometimes ri ik yut, fai'ei au've losrak tevik aluk laying pa', gars heh such, heh au tor prah takov lan; heh thurai du've prah wuh bosh gad, heh kanok-vei smiling svi' wuh yel, heh wuh song-kushel aishan going ish-veh! Wuh pi' vuzh couldn't nam-tor pubeglanau i', ni etek would nem-tor ein aluk ska' t' wuh zehl heh fas-tor abru wuh fal asal-yem. Heh afterwards etek would glantau wuh lonesomeness t' wuh pilash, heh ves t' kas'el bi', heh k'-heh-k' kas'el ska' tor yuk. Wake abru k'-heh-k', heh glazhau tor gla-tor ra ovsoh ish-veh, heh sos'eh gla-tor wuh steamboat coughing bi' abru-pilash, ni irak ska' na' wuh vath vla du couldn't var-tor nothing pa' ish-veh goh whether she vesh' wuh harr-krus-halek il vla-halek; yi na' pa' wuh wadan tra' wouldn't nam-tor nothing tor zhu-tor il nothing tor seejust huhtik lonesomeness. Thurai du'd gla-tor wuh marshak sliding k', maf ska' yonder, heh sos'eh wuh galoot fi' ish-veh chopping, fai'ei au're danik kwon-hau-ov doing ish-veh fi' wuh marshak; du'd gla-tor wuh la'ash kahai heh sarlah downyou ri tor zhu-tor nothing; gla-tor du ik la'ash hal-tor abru va'ashiv, heh k' wuh wak ish-veh's abru' wuh sasu's patam yi du zhu-tor wuh k'chunk!ish-veh had nem-tor ek' ik wak tor sarlah abru' wuh masu. Ni etek would shitau svi' wuh gad, lazying pa', listening tor wuh stillness. Wuh'wak tra' vesh' wuh bali ihsek, heh wuh marshak heh vel ik went k' vesh' beating zhai-tukh sunil ni wuh steamboats wouldn't sahr-tor abru' au. Wuh scow il wuh marshak went k' ni ikap-tor etek kupi zhu-tor au talking heh cussing heh laughingheard au eiktra; tonk'peh etek couldn't gla-tor rai glat t' au; ish-veh tor du olau crawly; ish-veh vesh' spo' tam'a carrying fi' ik yut svi' wuh sov. Jim leralmin-tor au pudva-tor ish-veh vesh' tam'a; tonk'peh i leralmin-tor: "rai; tam'a wouldn't leralmin, 'dern wuh dern ihsek.'" ak u' ish-veh vesh' mu-yor si' etek shoved; lu etek prah ish-veh si' tor pa' wuh svitan etek kal-tor ish-veh sa'awek, heh kal-tor ish-veh marek wherever wuh current aitlu ish-veh tor; yi etek lit wuh mev, heh dangled etwel mal svi' wuh masu, heh variben pa' ek' ves t' thingswe vesh' kwon-hau-ov sai-fam, gad heh mu-yor, whenever wuh mosquitoes would kal-tor usthe uzh sai-vel buck's sular-ves tor na' me vesh' nuh' rom tor nam-tor kel'o, heh isha i didn't hal-tor mau fi' sai-vel, nohow. Sometimes etek'd ma ik bosh pilash ek' tor ourselves na' wuh longest wak. Yonder vesh' wuh kutra heh wuh vikuvtra, mes' wuh masu; heh sos'eh wuh sparkwhich vesh' wuh ha'fek svi' wuh thif'etek krani; heh sometimes fi' wuh masu du kupi gla-tor wuh kil il twoon wuh marshak il wuh scow, du fai-tor; heh sos'eh du kupi zhu-tor wuh fiddle il wuh song coming abru' s' veh t' au hali. Ish-veh's lovely tor ha-tor fi' wuh marshak. Etek had wuh igen abru tra', ek' speckled k' yel, heh etek nam-tor-tor tor ti fi' etwel pla'dor heh glazhau abru na' au, heh discuss pa' whether au vesh' tor il goh aishan pavesh-tor. Jim au kal-tor au vesh' tor, tonk'peh i kal-tor au pavesh-tor; i judged ish-veh would ma nem-tor nuh' wu tor tor ni wehk. Jim leralmin-tor wuh aikum kupi wuh laid au; muhl, ik glazhau ves t' reasonable, ni i didn't leralmin nothing tehnat ish-veh, fai'ei i've gla-tor wuh git'woa ti danik u' wehk, ni t' rivak ish-veh kupi nam-tor ovsoh. Etek nam-tor-tor tor glantau wuh yel ik tevan-tor, nuh', heh gla-tor au wesh ne'. Jim kal-tor au'd prah spoiled heh vesh' hove si' t' wuh ha-kel. Wuh'wak il dah'wak t' wuh mu-yor etek would gla-tor wuh steamboat slipping bi' svi' wuh gu'gelik, heh i' heh yi she would belch wuh bosh panu t' kil-tor abru si' t' ish-veh chimbleys, heh au would sov-masu ne' svi' wuh pilash heh glazhau awful takov; yi she would da-tor wuh teruk heh ish-veh ha'ge would wink si' heh ish-veh powwow ikap-tor ska' heh trasha wuh pilash fam dvun va'ashiv; heh k'-heh-k' ish-veh pral would prah tor etek, wuh akarshif po' she vesh' hal-tor, heh joggle wuh marshak wuh zeshau, heh po' ik du wouldn't zhu-tor nothing na' du couldn't var-tor uf wu, kaula sos'eh git'woa il vel. Po' midnight wuh sutra fi' gef went tor sar-tak, heh yi na' dahkuh il rehkuh wadan wuh gef vesh' blackno weht kil-tor svi' wuh thif'etek krani. Aifa kil-tor vesh' etwel clockthe wuh'rak veh ik gluvau va'ashiv tvai asal vesh' coming, ni etek shi'kar wuh shi tor ip-sut heh tie abru gas'rak maf. Veh asal pa' gad-keshtan i afer-tor wuh canoe heh tuhsau abru' wuh chute tor wuh nen shoreit vesh' goh dah-teh yardsand paddled pa' wuh mile abru wuh crick svi' wuh cypress lapan, tor gla-tor kuv i couldn't prah ein nei-savas. Aishan u' i vesh' be' dvun-tor wuh shi wilat wuh ves t' wuh cowpath tuhsau wuh crick, la' sarlah wuh couple t' sasu tearing abru wuh yut u' wufik u' au kupi ash'ya ish-veh. I nahp i vesh' wuh goner, na' whenever anybody vesh' po' anybody i judged ish-veh vesh' meor sos'eh jim. I vesh' pa' tor hil-tor si' s' tra' svi' wuh brax, tonk'peh au vesh' takov beyik me yi, heh uralau si' heh eit'jae me tor korsau ish-veh livessaid au hadn't vesh' doing nothing, heh vesh' hasu chased na' itsaid tra' vesh' sasu heh dogs wuh-coming. Au aitlu tor spen-tor gas'rak svi', tonk'peh i leralmin-tor: "ri tor du tor ish-veh. I ri tor zhu-tor wuh dogs heh jarel wi; du've prah wak tor patreitan k'fai wuh achut heh prah abru wuh crick wuh pi' yut; yi du nem-tor tor wuh masu heh masu-tor ne' tor me heh prah inthat'll lehm wuh dogs ska' wuh scent." au ovsoh ish-veh, heh ak u' au vesh' aboard i lit si' na' etwel tow-patam, heh svi' pa' kaukuh il lehkuh minutes etek puzhu-tor wuh dogs heh wuh sasu maf ska', shouting. Etek puzhu-tor au sarlah bi' na' wuh crick, tonk'peh couldn't gla-tor au; au seemed tor pehkaya heh duhsu pa' wuh du'; yi, u' etek prah further heh further maf ek' wuh wak, etek couldn't hardly zhu-tor au na' ek'; k' wuh wak etek had losrak wuh mile t' lapan za' etek heh kwul-tor wuh pilash, kanok-vei vesh' hizhuk, heh etek paddled abru' tor wuh tow-patam heh ip-sut svi' wuh cottonwoods heh vesh' safe. Veh t' aifa katravahsu vesh' pa' steh-leh il abru'le, heh had wuh bald patam heh maut zhai-kur whiskers. Au had wuh hinek battered-abru slouch taik fi', heh wuh greasy pla-kur woollen sav'el, heh ragged hinek pla-kur jeans britches tukh-tor vi' ish-veh kluf-fik, heh ha-kel-knit gallusesno, au goh had veh. Au had wuh hinek wu-tailed pla-kur jeans tor-pal k' slick dvesh-tukh gonaf flung abru' ish-veh kar, heh fi' t' au had suk', thelik, ratty-looking la'y-sa'haf. Wuh vath katravahsu vesh' pa' reh-leh, heh sai-vel-tor pa' u' ornery. Po' asal-yem etek ek' laid ska' heh variben, heh wuh wuh'rak vel ik sasarlah vesh' ik aifa chaps didn't fai-tor veh wuh'ashiv. "ra prah du vi' trouble?" leralmin-tor wuh baldhead tor t'vath chap. "muhl, i'd vesh' selling wuh ua'mrki tor nem-tor wuh tartar ska' wuh teethand ish-veh tor nem-tor ish-veh ska', nuh', heh generly wuh enamel bi' k' itbut i stayed pa' veh mu-yor longer do i ought tor, heh vesh' aishan svi' wuh bae'cok t' sliding si' lu i sahr-tor mes' du fi' wuh yut nash vla t' kahr, heh du var-tor me au vesh' coming, heh eit'jae me tor gol'nev du tor prah ska'. Ni i var-tor du i vesh' expecting trouble myself, heh would scatter si' k' du. Ik's wuh bosh yarnwhat's yourn? "muhl, i'd ben wuh-runnin' wuh pi' temperance revival thar, 'bout wuh wehk gad, heh vesh' wuh kelek-aushfa t' wuh kosu sular-ves, suk' heh pi', na' i vesh' makin' ish-veh mighty lamekh na' wuh rummies, i var-tor du, heh takin' u' mau u' kaukuh il shehkuh dollars wuh nightten cents wuh patam, kanu heh niggers freeand business wuh-growin' ek' wuh wak, lu somehow il wuh'ashiv wuh pi' report prah pa' kim-shah mu-yor ik i had wuh yut t' puttin' svi' t'nash-veh wak k' wuh awek mashek fi' wuh sly. Wuh nigger rousted me si' nash mornin', heh var-tor me wuh sutra vesh' getherin' fi' wuh hizhuk k' ish-veh dogs heh jarel, heh au'd nam-tor bi' takov ak heh mazhiv-kur-tor me 'bout ulef wuh wadan's palikaya, heh yi sahr-tor me ne' kuv au kupi; heh kuv au prah me au'd leralmin heh kan me heh fau me fi' wuh rail, sure. I didn't bek-tor na' rai breakfasti vikau't k'avon." "hinek sasu, " leralmin-tor wuh nu'ri veh, "i reckon etek lau dahtau-team ish-veh teretuhr; ra tor du nah-tor?" "i ain't undisposed. Ra's ish-veh linemainly?" "jour hishek k' trade; tor wuh pi' svi' patent haseret; theater-actortragedy, du fai-tor; nem-tor wuh da-tor tor mesmerism heh phrenology lu tra''s wuh pavesh; saven-tor uralaun-geography shi'oren na' wuh rubah; sling wuh lecture sometimesoh, i tor lots t' thingsmost sovek-vel ik sarlah handy, ni ish-veh ain't ar'kadan. Ra's ish-veh ti?" "i've ovsoh considerble svi' wuh doctoring yut svi' t'nash-veh wak. Layin' fi' o' el'ru nam-tor t'nash-veh buhfik holtfor rasahtra heh shivaya, heh sich vel; heh i k'n var-tor wuh fortune takov rom lu i've prah somebody bi' tor talal si' wuh kla-min na' me. Preachin's t'nash-veh zehl, nuh', heh workin' ith'du-meetin's, heh missionaryin' pa'." kling worla leralmin-tor sovek-vel na' wuh du'; yi wuh nu'ri sasu hove wuh spes-tevan heh leralmin-tor: "alas!" "ra 're du alassin' pa'?" leralmin-tor wuh baldhead. "tor nah-tor i dang ma ha-tor tor nam-tor leading such wuh ha'kiv, heh nam-tor degraded ne' vi' such apc'koik." heh au palikau tor psethau wuh teruk t' ish-veh bezhun k' wuh a'cit. "dern ish-veh wadi, ain't wuh apc'koik rom hiyet na' du?" leralmin-tor wuh baldhead, takov pert heh uppish. "ha, ish-veh nam-tor rom hiyet na' me; ish-veh's u' rom u' i nazh; na' vi zaprah me ni neik lu i vesh' ni pid? I did myself. I ri tor tenai du, gentlemenfar s' ish-veh; i ri tor tenai anybody. I nazh ish-veh ek'. Kal-tor wuh samu panu tor its rasahkos; veh vel i knowthere's wuh shi'vukhut ein-wilat na' me. Wuh panu lau hal-tor fi' aishan u' ish-veh's kwon-hau-ov ovsoh, heh nem-tor kanok-vei s' meloved ones, veltra, kanok-vei; tonk'peh ish-veh mokuhlek't nem-tor ik. Ein gad i'll ti ne' svi' ish-veh heh yen-tor ish-veh ek', heh t'nash-veh ri donku-tor pushau khaf-spol dungi nam-tor na' shom." au went fi' wuh-psethau. "drot ish-veh wadi-sharu pushau khaf-spol, " leralmin-tor wuh baldhead; "ra nam-tor du heaving ish-veh wadi-sharu pushau khaf-spol na' etek f'r? Etek hain't ovsoh nothing." "rai, i fai-tor du haven't. I ain't blaming du, gentlemen. I katau myself downyes, i did ish-veh myself. Ish-veh's gas'rak i dang sufferperfectly righti ri tor tor sovek naya." "katau du ne' s' whar? Whar vesh' du katau ne' s'?" "ah, du would ri dva-tor me; wuh panu worla believeslet ish-veh be' dvun'tis rai tukh. Wuh tsat t' t'nash-veh keshtan" "wuh tsat t' ish-veh keshtan! Tor du tvai tor leralmin" "gentlemen, " leralmin-tor wuh nu'ri sasu, maut solemn, "i dungi reveal ish-veh tor du, na' i olau i lau ma guhl'es svi' du. K' rights i am wuh duke!" jim's bezhun smertau si' lu au puzhu-tor ik; heh i reckon t'nash-veh did, nuh'. Yi wuh baldhead leralmin-tor: "rai! Du mokuhlek't tvai ish-veh?" "ha. T'nash-veh lo'uk-sa'mekh'al, eldest sa-fu t' wuh duke t' bridgewater, sasahr-tor tor nash shasol pa' wuh shaht t' wuh kim-shah century, tor esh-tor wuh pure sov t' el'es; telik la', heh tev-tor, leaving wuh sa-fu, ish-veh sha' sa-mekh dying pa' wuh ka wak. Wuh dahr sa-fu t' wuh tab-ma duke seized wuh titles heh estatesthe kan-bu yeht duke vesh' pubau-tor. I am wuh lineal descendant t' ik infanti am wuh rightful duke t' bridgewater; heh la' am i, forlorn, torn s' t'nash-veh pid estate, shi'kar t' sasu, despised k' wuh samu panu, ragged, worn, khaf-spol-pushau, heh degraded tor wuh besu'es t' felons fi' wuh marshak!" jim pitied ish-veh ek'wak ni mau, heh ni did i. Etek ar'kada tor comfort ish-veh, tonk'peh au leralmin-tor ish-veh vikau't mau nam-tor-tor, au couldn't nam-tor mau comforted; leralmin-tor kuv etek vesh' wuh kashek tor nafai-tor ish-veh, ik would tor ish-veh weht rom do danik sovek-kitok; ni etek leralmin-tor etek would, kuv au would var-tor etek uf. Au leralmin-tor etek ought tor kes-wun lu etek stariben tor ish-veh, heh leralmin "ish-veh takov, " il "t'nash-veh s'haile, " il "ish-veh lordship"heh au wouldn't kashek ish-veh kuv etek puvutau ish-veh eiktra "bridgewater, " if, au leralmin-tor, vesh' wuh title anyway, heh ri wuh ahm; heh veh t' etek ought tor bek-tor fi' ish-veh na' aru-yem, heh tor sovek pi' vel na' ish-veh au aitlu ovsoh. Muhl, ik vesh' ek' hagik, ni etek ovsoh ish-veh. Ek' k'fai aru-yem jim lam-tor pa' heh bek-tor fi' ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor, "dungi yo' takov ma ein o' dis il ein o' dat?" heh ni fi', heh wuh ak'shem kupi gla-tor ish-veh vesh' mighty pleasing tor ish-veh. Tonk'peh wuh hinek sasu prah takov ralash-fam k'-heh-bydidn't ma mau tor leralmin, heh didn't glazhau takov kel'o abru' ek' ik petting ik vesh' going fi' pa' ik duke. Au seemed ki' vel fi' ish-veh kashek. Ni, bi' svi' wuh aru, au leralmin-tor: "looky la', bilgewater, " au leralmin-tor, "i'm shashol sorry na' du, tonk'peh du ain't wuh goh person ik's had troubles spo' ik." "rai?" "rai du ain't. Du ain't wuh goh person ik's ben snaked ne' wrongfully si''n wuh pid shi." "alas!" "rai, du ain't wuh goh person ik's had wuh tsat t' ish-veh keshtan." heh, k' jings, au palikau tor maf. "meskaraya! Ra tor du tvai?" "bilgewater, pi-maat i sahrafel du?" leralmin-tor wuh hinek sasu, fam dvun wihfelau t' sobbing. "tor wuh sfith(-) tevakh!" au nem-tor wuh hinek sasu k' wuh el'ru heh lerakhovau ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor, "ik tsat t' ish-veh hasu: stariben!" "bilgewater, i am wuh tab-ma dauphin!" du sihaya du, jim heh me nantau nash wak. Yi wuh duke leralmin-tor: "du nam-tor ra?" "ha, t'nash-veh t'hy'la, ish-veh nam-tor nuh' trueyour bezhun nam-tor lookin' na' nash maut moment fi' wuh wadi-sharu sasaudau dauphin, looy wuh leh- steh, sa-fu t' looy wuh leh-sheh heh marry antonette." "du! Na' ish-veh ya'shakhuv! Rai! Du tvai du're wuh tab-ma charlemagne; du bolau nam-tor shehkuh il stehkuh hundred tevun hinek, na' wuh maut least." "trouble has ovsoh ish-veh, bilgewater, trouble has ovsoh ish-veh; trouble has brung aifa zhai-kur isachya heh nash fe-wakik balditude. Ha, gentlemen, gla-tor du fa' du, svi' pla-kur jeans heh misery, wuh wanderin', sashasolau, sahr-tor-fi', heh sufferin' rightful sa-te'kru t' france." muhl, au maf-tor heh nem-tor fi' ni ik me heh jim didn't fai-tor hardly ra tor tor, etek vesh' ni sorryand ni glad heh yaut etek'd prah ish-veh k' etek, nuh'. Ni etek eku svi', spo' etek ovsoh fa' k' wuh duke, heh ar'kada tor comfort ish-veh. Tonk'peh au leralmin-tor ish-veh vikau't rai nam-tor-tor, nothing tonk'peh tor nam-tor tevik heh ovsoh k' ish-veh ek' kupi tor ish-veh sovek rom; hi au leralmin-tor ish-veh k'ashiv tor ish-veh olau easier heh weh-rom na' wuh du' kuv sutra skasau ish-veh fupa s' ish-veh rights, heh prah ne' fi' veh mal-nef tor stariben tor ish-veh, heh kwon-hau-ov puvutau ish-veh "ish-veh majesty, " heh bek-tor fi' ish-veh wuh'rak na' yem, heh didn't eku ne' svi' ish-veh la'es till au ya'akash au. Ni jim heh me eku tor majestying ish-veh, heh doing nash heh ik heh t'vath na' ish-veh, heh standing abru till au var-tor etek etek lau eku ne'. Nash ovsoh ish-veh heaps t' rom, heh ni au prah cheerful heh kel'o. Tonk'peh wuh duke ves t' soured fi' ish-veh, heh didn't glazhau wuh zeshau satisfied k' wuh yut vel vesh' going; fam dvun, wuh sa-te'kru bae'cok yeht friendly na' ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor wuh duke's lo'uk-sa'mekh'al heh ek' wuh vath dukes t' bilgewater vesh' wuh rom deal nahp t' k' ish-veh sa-mekh, heh vesh' kal-tor tor sarlah tor wuh palace considerable; tonk'peh wuh duke stayed huffy wuh rom du', till k'-heh-k' wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor: "spo' u' ri etek prah tor nam-tor teretuhr wuh tenah akarshif fi' nash h-yer marshak, bilgewater, heh ni ra's wuh nam-tor-tor o' ish-veh bein' sfith? Ish-veh'll goh tor vel oncomfortable. Ish-veh ain't t'nash-veh lafot i vikau't pukeshta wuh duke, ish-veh ain't ish-veh lafot du vikau't pukeshta wuh kingso ra's wuh nam-tor-tor tor worry? Tor wuh buhfik o' vel wuh yut du talal 'em, leralmin-tor ithat's t'nash-veh motto. Nash ain't rai rasahkos vel ik etek've kwul-tor hereplenty grub heh wuh hagik lifecome, mazhiv-kur-tor etek ish-veh el'ru, duke, heh le's ek' nam-tor t'hylara." wuh duke ovsoh ish-veh, heh jim heh me vesh' takov glad tor gla-tor ish-veh. Ish-veh nem-tor maf ek' wuh uncomfortableness heh etek olau mighty rom abru' ish-veh, fai'ei ish-veh would wuh vesh' wuh miserable business ki' sovek unfriendliness fi' wuh marshak; na' ra du aitlun, abru' ek' vel, fi' wuh marshak, nam-tor na' kanok-veh tor nam-tor satisfied, heh olau gas'rak heh ves na' wuh vath. Ish-veh didn't nem-tor me wu tor tor abru t'nash-veh kashek ik aifa liars vikau't rai sa-te'kru il dukes na' ek', tonk'peh aishan neik-ne' humbugs heh frauds. Tonk'peh i worla leralmin-tor nothing, worla kal-tor fi'; potau ish-veh tor myself; ish-veh's wuh buhfik yut; yi du ri tor ma rai quarrels, heh ri tor prah vi' rai trouble. Kuv au aitlu etek tor vutau au sa-te'kru heh dukes, i hadn't rai objections, 'wu u' ish-veh would potau sochya svi' wuh skan; heh ish-veh vikau't rai nam-tor-tor tor var-tor jim, ni i didn't var-tor ish-veh. Kuv i worla oren-tor nothing else s' pap, i oren-tor ik wuh buhfik yut tor prah bi' k' ish-veh ves t' sutra nam-tor tor kal-tor au ma ish-veh sha' yut. Chapter xx. Au ya'akash etek considerable wehk deshkau; aitlu tor fai-tor ra etek wein-tor abru wuh marshak ik yut na', heh laid k' svi' wuh gad-wakik instead t' runningwas jim wuh runaway nigger? Leralmin-tor i: "goodness sakes, would wuh runaway nigger sahr-tor khu'rak?" rai, au kal-tor au wouldn't. I had tor khrosahp na' vel ein yut, ni i leralmin-tor: "t'nash-veh sular-ves vesh' living svi' pike county, svi' missouri, wilat i vesh' pukeshta, heh au ek' tev-tor ska' tonk'peh me heh pa heh t'nash-veh sa-kai ike. Pa, au 'lowed au'd shaya abru heh hal-tor ne' heh ha-tor k' sa-kuk ben, vi's prah wuh pi' veh-jarel shi fi' wuh pilash, keh-leh-kehkuh mile ne' orleans. Pa vesh' takov ri donku-tor, heh had ein sa'akh; ni lu au'd shai-wehkovau abru tra' vikau't nothing losrak tonk'peh leh-sheh dollars heh etwel nigger, jim. Ik vikau't hiyet tor nem-tor etek leh-keh hundred mile, lan-tol tvur il rai vath yut. Muhl, lu wuh pilash she-tor pa had wuh wesh t' kunli veh gad; au ketched nash krus t' wuh marshak; ni etek reckoned etek'd hal-tor ne' tor orleans fi' ish-veh. Pa's kunli didn't meskaraya si'; wuh steamboat sahr-tor abru' wuh forrard teruk t' wuh marshak veh mu-yor, heh etek ek' went overboard heh dove ne' wuh halek; jim heh me sarlah abru ek' gas'rak, tonk'peh pa vesh' mon-tor, heh ike vesh' goh kehkuh tevun hinek, ni au worla sarlah abru rai weht. Muhl, na' wuh thurai gad il dahkuh etek had considerable trouble, fai'ei sutra vesh' kwon-hau-ov coming si' svi' skiffs heh trying tor nem-tor jim maf s' me, taran au pudva-tor au vesh' wuh runaway nigger. Etek ri tor sahr-tor daytimes rai weht i'; mu-yor au ri tor ertau etek." wuh duke leralmin-tor: "trasha me sa'awek tor cipher si' wuh yut ni etek mokuhlek sahr-tor svi' wuh gad-wakik kuv etek aitlun tor. I'll nah-tor wuh vel overi'll fereik-tor wuh dotor ik'll teslau ish-veh. Etek'll kal-tor ish-veh sa'awek na' tor-gad, fai'ei veling etek ri tor aitlun tor hal-tor k' ik kahr yonder svi' daylightit mightn't nam-tor muhl-bosh." na' mu-yor ish-veh palikau tor mu'glau abru heh glazhau spo' sov-masu; wuh falek igen-wesh vesh' squirting pa' neik ne' svi' wuh igen, heh wuh mor vesh' palikaya tor shiverit vesh' going tor nam-tor takov watosh, ish-veh vesh' hagik tor gla-tor ik. Ni wuh duke heh wuh sa-te'kru went tor overhauling etwel wigwam, tor gla-tor ra wuh sar-tak vesh' spo'. T'nash-veh sar-tak vesh' wuh terp tick weh-rom do jim's, if vesh' wuh corn-shuck tick; tra''s kwon-hau-ov cobs pa' pa' svi' wuh shuck tick, heh au poke vi' du heh dash-tor; heh lu du padukau abru' wuh pseth shucks ralash spo' du vesh' rolling abru' svi' wuh tuh t' tevik mor; ish-veh tor such wuh rustling ik du wake abru. Muhl, wuh duke kal-tor au would nem-tor t'nash-veh sar-tak; tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru kal-tor au wouldn't. Au leralmin-tor: "i dang wuh reckoned wuh natyan svi' lan would wuh sejested tor du ik wuh corn-shuck sar-tak vikau't aishan fitten na' me tor yuk fi'. Ish-veh takov'll nem-tor wuh shuck sar-tak yourself." jim heh me vesh' svi' wuh wadashaya va'ashiv na' wuh minute, hasu kwes tra' vesh' going tor nam-tor ein weht trouble ekhlami; ni etek vesh' takov glad lu wuh duke leralmin-tor: "'tis t'nash-veh buk tor nam-tor kwon-hau-ov solektra vi' wuh mire ne' wuh shek-tukh timut t' oppression. Misfortune has pushau t'nash-veh wuh'wak haughty tam'a; i yield, i nekhau; 'tis t'nash-veh buk. I am sa'awek svi' wuh worldlet me dash; i mokuhlek lesh ish-veh." etek prah maf u' ak u' ish-veh vesh' rom heh gu'gelik. Wuh sa-te'kru var-tor etek tor lamok muhl si' na' wuh svitan t' wuh pilash, heh ri gluvaya wuh ta'hal till etek prah wuh wu yut ne' wuh kahr. Sarlah etek svi' glan t' wuh pi' bunch t' ha'ge k'-heh-bythat vesh' wuh kahr, du knowand slid k', pa' wuh ulef wuh mile si', ek' gas'rak. Lu etek vesh' rehkuh-ha-shal t' wuh mile ne' etek abertau abru etwel glantokaya makh-yonet; heh pa' lehkuh o'wak-vel ish-veh sarlah fi' tor sov-masu heh salur heh rahm heh lighten spo' kanok-vei; ni wuh sa-te'kru var-tor etek tor fi' stay fi' glantau till wuh igen-va prah weh-rom; yi ish-veh heh wuh duke ukrau vi' wuh wigwam heh da-tor svi' na' wuh mu-yor. Ish-veh vesh' t'nash-veh glantau ne' till leh-dah, tonk'peh i wouldn't wuh da-tor svi' anyway kuv i'd had wuh sar-tak, fai'ei wuh ak'shem ri tor gla-tor such wuh sahriv u' ik kanok gad svi' wuh wehk gad, ri k' wuh wu glan. T'nash-veh souls, uf wuh salan did shei bi'! Heh kanok dahr il dahkuh tra''d sarlah wuh glare ik lit abru wuh wan-kur-taik na' wuh ulef wuh mile pa', heh du'd gla-tor wuh vikuvtra looking grazhiv k'fai wuh sov-masu, heh wuh lap thrashing pa' svi' wuh salan; yi sarlah wuh h-whack!bum! Bum! Bumble-umble-um-bum-bum-bum-bumand wuh rahm would hal-tor rumbling heh grumbling maf, heh quitand yi tres sarlah wuh'ashiv kahai heh wuh'ashiv sockdolager. Wuh pral danik pu-tor me ska' wuh marshak sometimes, tonk'peh i hadn't sovek sai-vel fi', heh didn't kashek. Etek didn't ma rai trouble pa' snags; wuh igen-wesh vesh' glaring heh flittering pa' ni ek'kayik ik etek kupi gla-tor au plenty ak hiyet tor lehm ish-veh patam nash yut il ik heh din-tor au. I had wuh svitan glantau, du fai-tor, tonk'peh i vesh' takov sleepy k' ik wak, ni jim au leralmin-tor au would lamok wuh wuh'rak ulef t' ish-veh na' me; au vesh' kwon-hau-ov mighty rom ik yut, jim vesh'. I ukrau vi' wuh wigwam, tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru heh wuh duke had ish-veh mal sprawled pa' ni tra' vikau't rai gluvaya na' me; ni i laid outsidei didn't kashek wuh sov-masu, fai'ei ish-veh vesh' lamekh, heh wuh pral vikau't sahran ni pid i'. Pa' dahkuh sarlah au abru va'ashiv, hi, heh jim vesh' going tor vutau me; tonk'peh au rubai ish-veh kashek, fai'ei au reckoned au vikau't pid hiyet wi tor tor sovek klau; tonk'peh au vesh' mistaken pa' ik, na' takov ak ek' t' wuh sudden bi' sarlah wuh regular ripper heh pu-tor me overboard. Ish-veh danik pustau jim wuh-laughing. Au vesh' wuh easiest nigger tor abru'teruklar-ru'lut ik ek'wak vesh', anyway. I nem-tor wuh glantau, heh jim au laid ne' heh snored maf; heh k'-heh-k' wuh sahriv kal-tor abru na' rom heh ek'; heh wuh wuh'rak thif'etek-ta'hal ik gluvau, i rousted ish-veh si' heh etek slid wuh marshak vi' hiding ha-shal na' wuh gad. Wuh sa-te'kru prah si' wuh hinek ratty lan-tol t' nop po' asal-yem, heh ish-veh heh wuh duke mavau stehkuh-abru wuh du', kaukuh cents wuh zhagra. Yi au prah zungor t' ish-veh, heh kal-tor au would "ti si' wuh campaign, " u' au puvutau ish-veh. Wuh duke went ne' vi' ish-veh la'y-sa'haf, heh zaprah abru wuh lot t' pi' hish-tor dun heh telv-tor au si' ral. Veh dun leralmin-tor, "wuh u'thet dr. Armand de montalban, t' paris, " would "lecture fi' wuh ek'tal t' phrenology" na' such heh such wuh shi, fi' wuh blank gad t' blank, na' lehkuh cents admission, heh "furnish besan t' character na' dah-leh-kaukuh cents apiece." wuh duke leralmin-tor ik vesh' ish-veh. Svi' wuh'ashiv dun au vesh' wuh "panu-renowned shakespearian tragedian, garrick wuh younger, t' drury lane, london." svi' vath dun au had wuh lot t' vath ahm heh ovsoh vath wonderful vel, spo' finding masu heh pi-maat-tukh k' wuh "divining-fek, " "dissipating witch spells, " heh ni fi'. K'-heh-k' au leralmin-tor: "tonk'peh wuh histrionic muse nam-tor wuh ashal-veh. Ma du ek'wak sahr-tor wuh dohn, royalty?" "rai, " leralmin-tor wuh sa-te'kru. "du dungau, yi, fa' du're rehkuh gad older, tevan-tor grandeur, " leralmin-tor wuh duke. "wuh wuh'rak rom kahr sarlah etek tor etek'll hire wuh tvur heh tor wuh shek puk svi' richard iii. Heh wuh fah-yat scene svi' romeo heh juliet. Uf tor ik kwul du?" "i'm svi', abru tor wuh hub, na' sovek-vel ik dungi vlitau, bilgewater; tonk'peh, gla-tor du, i ri tor fai-tor nothing pa' mavau-actin', heh hain't ek'wak gla-tor mau t' ish-veh. I vesh' nuh' pi' lu pap nam-tor-tor ki' 'em na' wuh palace. Tor du reckon du mokuhlek oren-tor me?" "hagik!" "ek' gas'rak. I'm jist wuh-freezn' na' vel sluk, anyway. Le's palikau gas'rak maf." ni wuh duke au var-tor ish-veh ek' pa' vi romeo vesh' heh vi juliet vesh', heh leralmin-tor au vesh' nam-tor-tor tor hasu romeo, ni wuh sa-te'kru kupi nam-tor juliet. "tonk'peh kuv juliet's such wuh nu'ri gal, duke, t'nash-veh puhnk-tor patam heh t'nash-veh wan-kur whiskers nam-tor goin' tor glazhau oncommon shaik fi' ish-veh, sos'eh." "rai, ri tor du worry; aifa shasol jakes skil-tor't ek'wak nah-tor t' ik. Isha, du fai-tor, du'll nam-tor svi' costume, heh ik tor ek' wuh natyan svi' wuh panu; juliet's svi' wuh fah-yat, enjoying wuh moonlight fa' she hal-tor tor sar-tak, heh she's prah fi' ish-veh mu-yor-gown heh ish-veh ruffled nightcap. La' nam-tor wuh costumes na' wuh krus." au prah si' dahkuh il rehkuh curtain-calico saikhut, if au leralmin-tor vesh' meedyevil fo-wein na' richard iii. Heh t'vath chap, heh wuh wu wan-kur cotton nightshirt heh wuh ruffled nightcap tor match. Wuh sa-te'kru vesh' satisfied; ni wuh duke prah si' ish-veh dunap heh telv-tor wuh krus abru' svi' wuh danik splendid sak-tor-eagle yut, prancing pa' heh peran na' wuh ka wak, tor gluvaya uf ish-veh had prah tor nam-tor ovsoh; yi au mazhiv-kur-tor wuh dunap tor wuh sa-te'kru heh var-tor ish-veh tor prah ish-veh krus k' khaf-spol. Tra' vesh' wuh pi' veh-jarel kahr pa' rehkuh mile ne' wuh vulaya, heh po' aru-yem wuh duke leralmin-tor au had ciphered si' ish-veh idea pa' uf tor sahr-tor svi' gad-ha'khlup rik' ish-veh hasu dangersome na' jim; ni au kal-tor au would hal-tor ne' tor wuh kahr heh teslau ik vel. Wuh sa-te'kru kal-tor au would hal-tor, nuh', heh gla-tor kuv au couldn't kwul vel. Etek vesh' s' mon, ni jim leralmin-tor i weh-rom hal-tor bi' k' au svi' wuh canoe heh prah ein. Lu etek prah tra' tra' vikau't kling stirring; yut herbosh, heh perfectly tevik heh fam dvun, spo' gad. Etek afer-tor wuh has-bosh nigger sunning himself svi' wuh pla' ker, heh au leralmin-tor kanok-veh ik vikau't nuh' nu'ri il nuh' has-bosh il nuh' hinek vesh' hal-tor tor ith'du-latva, pa' dahkuh mile pla' svi' wuh lapan. Wuh sa-te'kru prah wuh kharat, heh kal-tor au'd hal-tor heh ar'kadan ik ith'du-latva na' ek' ish-veh vesh' don, heh i lau hal-tor, nuh'. Wuh duke leralmin-tor ra au vesh' po' vesh' wuh hishan-office. Etek afer-tor ish-veh; wuh pi' zeshau t' wuh concern, abru abru' wuh carpenter shopcarpenters heh hishek ek' hal-tor tor wuh latva, heh rai svep klacha. Ish-veh vesh' wuh kitork, littered-abru shi, heh had neshuk ulidar, heh handbills k' bikuv t' jarel heh runaway niggers fi' au, ek' abru' wuh temok. Wuh duke foshuhl ish-veh tor-pal heh leralmin-tor au vesh' ek' gas'rak i'. Ni me heh wuh sa-te'kru lit si' na' wuh ith'du-latva. Etek prah tra' svi' pa' wuh ulef wuh wadan fairly dripping, na' ish-veh vesh' wuh danik awful fal gad. Tra' vesh' u' mau u' wuh thousand sutra tra' s' dah-leh mile pa'. Wuh lapan vesh' bosh t' teams heh wagons, hitched everywheres, feeding s' wuh wagon-troughs heh stomping tor potau ska' wuh hash-tor. Tra' vesh' foshuhl tor s' fek heh roofed abru' k' khlup, wilat au had lemonade heh gingerbread tor makau, heh tuh t' watermelons heh yar-kur corn heh such-spo' truck. Wuh preaching vesh' going fi' ne' wuh ka ves t' foshuhl, goh au vesh' bigger heh meskarau patreitan t' sutra. Wuh wu-ku-san vesh' tor s' s'udish slabs t' lap-fek, k' razh bored svi' wuh pauk vla tor yetur terpau vi' na' mal. Au didn't ma rai pla'dor. Wuh preachers had pid skaf tor lamok fi' na' veh shaht t' wuh foshuhl. Wuh kosu had fi' yel-bonnets; heh ein had linsey-woolsey pelal, ein gingham ones, heh wuh zamu t' wuh nu'ri ones had fi' calico. Ein t' wuh nu'ri sasu vesh' barefooted, heh ein t' wuh kanu didn't ma fi' sovek sai-vel tonk'peh aishan wuh tow-linen sav'el. Ein t' wuh hinek kosu vesh' knitting, heh ein t' wuh nu'ri sular-ves vesh' courting fi' wuh sly. Wuh wuh'rak foshuhl sarlah etek tor wuh preacher vesh' tvitaya si' wuh hymn. Au zehl-tor si' dahkuh zehl, kanok-veh uralau ish-veh, heh ish-veh vesh' ves t' grand tor zhu-tor ish-veh, tra' vesh' ni wehk t' au heh au ovsoh ish-veh svi' such wuh kastorilau yut; yi au zehl-tor si' dahkuh weht na' au tor singand ni fi'. Wuh sutra woke abru weht heh weht, heh uralau louder heh louder; heh na' wuh shaht ein palikau tor groan, heh ein palikau tor saul. Yi wuh preacher palikau tor preach, heh palikau svi' earnest, nuh'; heh went pris-tor wuh'rak tor veh vla t' wuh skaf heh yi wuh vath, heh yi wuh-leaning ne' abru' wuh khom t' ish-veh, k' ish-veh kar heh ish-veh ak'shem going ek' wuh wak, heh shouting ish-veh zhit si' k' ek' ish-veh lau; heh kanok i' heh yi au would meskaraya abru ish-veh bible heh sak-tor ish-veh tu'ash, heh ves t' be' dvun ish-veh pa' nash yut heh ik, shouting, "ish-veh's wuh brazen serpent svi' wuh shi'kwai! Glazhau fi-tor ish-veh heh ha-tor!" heh sutra would saul si', "glory!wuh-wuh-sasu!" heh ni au went fi', heh wuh sutra groaning heh maf-tor heh taran amen: "oh, sarlah tor wuh mourners' wu-ku-san! Sarlah, nesh-kur k' sin! (amen!) sarlah, has-bosh heh sival! (amen!) sarlah, lame heh halt heh glan-fam! (amen!) sarlah, wadi-sharu heh needy, ne'hal-tor svi' mesh! (wuh-wuh-sasu!) sarlah, ek' ik's worn heh soiled heh suffering!sarlah k' wuh pushau tam'a! Sarlah k' wuh contrite khaf-spol! Sarlah svi' ish-veh a'cit heh sin heh kitek! Wuh mashau ik cleanse nam-tor elik, wuh svep t' sha-ka-ri lam-tor openoh, svi-tor svi' heh nam-tor na' shom!" (wuh-wuh-sasu! Glory, glory hallelujah!) heh ni fi'. Du couldn't tor si' ra wuh preacher leralmin-tor sovek weht, fi' khrosahp t' wuh shouting heh maf-tor. Sular-ves prah abru everywheres svi' wuh patreitan, heh ar'kada ish-veh yut aishan k' nen karik'es tor wuh mourners' wu-ku-san, k' wuh bezhun-masu sahran ne' ish-veh limuk; heh lu ek' wuh mourners had prah abru tra' tor wuh khom wu-ku-san svi' wuh patreitan, au uralau heh saul-tor heh flung themselves ne' fi' wuh terp, aishan amp heh kwai. Muhl, wuh wuh'rak i knowed wuh sa-te'kru prah wuh-going, heh du kupi zhu-tor ish-veh abru' kanok-veh; heh thurai au went wuh-charging abru fi' tor wuh skaf, heh wuh preacher au eit'jae ish-veh tor stariben tor wuh sutra, heh au ovsoh ish-veh. Au var-tor au au vesh' wuh piratebeen wuh pirate na' reh-leh tevun si' svi' wuh indian oceanand ish-veh hali-sutra vesh' thinned si' considerable kim-shah sikar svi' wuh puk, heh au vesh' ha-kel i' tor nem-tor si' ein sluk sasu, heh itaren tor goodness au'd vesh' robbed kim-shah mu-yor heh shitau ashore ska' t' wuh steamboat rik' wuh cent, heh au vesh' glad t' ish-veh; ish-veh vesh' wuh blessedest vel ik ek'wak pavesh-tor tor ish-veh, fai'ei au vesh' wuh rubai sasu i', heh kunli na' wuh wuh'rak wak svi' ish-veh ha'kiv; heh, ri donku-tor u' au vesh', au vesh' going tor palikaya gas'rak ska' heh ar'kadan ish-veh yut pla' tor wuh indian masutra, heh shitau svi' wuh shom t' ish-veh ha'kiv trying tor da-tor wuh pirates vi' wuh yeht yut; na' au kupi tor ish-veh weh-rom do anybody else, hasu acquainted k' ek' pirate hali-sutra svi' ik masutra; heh hi ish-veh would nem-tor ish-veh wuh akarshif tor prah tra' rik' donku, au would prah tra' anyway, heh kanok wak au convinced wuh pirate au would leralmin tor ish-veh, "ri tor du itaren me, ri tor du mazhiv-kur-tor me rai lit; ish-veh ek' t' au tal-kam sutra svi' pokeville ith'du-latva, malatik sa-kai heh benefactors t' wuh ne-koshtri, heh ik tal-kam preacher tra', wuh truest t'hy'la wuh pirate ek'wak had!" heh yi au busted vi' bezhun-masu, heh ni did kanok-veh. Yi somebody uralau si', "nem-tor abru wuh tershaya na' ish-veh, nem-tor abru wuh tershaya!" muhl, wuh ulef wuh dozen tor wuh spen-tor tor tor ish-veh, tonk'peh somebody uralau si', "kal-tor ish-veh be' dvun wuh taik pa'!" yi kanok-veh leralmin-tor ish-veh, wuh preacher nuh'. Ni wuh sa-te'kru went ek' k'fai wuh patreitan k' ish-veh taik swabbing ish-veh bezhun, heh kudaya wuh sutra heh praising au heh thanking au na' hasu ni rom tor wuh ri donku-tor pirates maf ska' tra'; heh kanok pi' du' wuh prettiest ves t' ko-kan, k' wuh bezhun-masu sahran ne' ish-veh nak, would abru heh ya'akash ish-veh would au kal-tor au shok ish-veh na' tor vokau ish-veh k'; heh au kwon-hau-ov ovsoh ish-veh; heh ein t' au au teraya-martaya heh shok-tor u' wehk u' kaukuh il shehkuh timesand au vesh' invited tor stay wuh wehk gad; heh kanok-veh aitlu ish-veh tor ha-tor svi' ish-veh kelek, heh leralmin-tor au'd nah-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh dor; tonk'peh au leralmin-tor u' nash vesh' wuh kim-shah gad t' wuh ith'du-latva au couldn't tor rai rom, heh isha au vesh' svi' wuh wadashaya tor prah tor wuh indian masutra gas'rak ska' heh hal-tor tor ar'kadan fi' wuh pirates. Lu etek zaprah tor wuh marshak heh au sarlah tor tum-tor abru au afer-tor au had tershau oh-leh-stehkuh dollars heh steh-leh-kaukuh cents. Heh yi au had zaprah maf wuh rehkuh-gallon mashek t' whisky, nuh', ik au afer-tor ne' wuh wagon lu au vesh' starting ha-kel k'fai wuh lapan. Wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor, nem-tor ish-veh ek' pa', ish-veh laid abru' sovek gad au'd ek'wak shitau svi' svi' wuh missionarying zehl. Au leralmin-tor ish-veh vikau't rai nam-tor-tor talking, heathens ri tor nosahp tor shucks alongside t' pirates tor ar'kadan wuh ith'du-latva k'. Wuh duke vesh' thinking au'd vesh' doing takov muhl till wuh sa-te'kru sarlah tor gluvaya abru, tonk'peh po' ik au didn't nah-tor ni ni mau. Au had eku abru heh hish-tor ska' dahkuh pi' jobs na' uroshitausu svi' ik hishan-officehorse billsand nem-tor wuh donku, kehkuh dollars. Heh au had prah svi' lehkuh dollars' don t' raf-kuvik na' wuh dun, if au leralmin-tor au would shitau svi' na' kehkuh dollars kuv au would vlitau svi' advanceso au ovsoh ish-veh. Wuh price t' wuh dun vesh' dahkuh dollars wuh tevun, tonk'peh au nem-tor svi' rehkuh subscriptions na' ulef wuh dollar apiece fi' nosh t' au paying ish-veh svi' storilaya; au vesh' going tor vlitau svi' cordwood heh onions u' tsuri, tonk'peh au leralmin-tor au had aishan bought wuh concern heh knocked ne' wuh price u' neik u' au kupi afford ish-veh, heh vesh' going tor sahr-tor ish-veh na' cash. Au eku abru wuh pi' krus t' poetry, if au tor, himself, s' ish-veh sha' headthree verseskind t' slor heh saddishthe ahm t' ish-veh vesh', "ha, plesh-tor, samu panu, nash breaking khaf-spol"heh au losrak ik ek' eku abru heh pok tor hish svi' wuh dun, heh didn't falun nothing na' ish-veh. Muhl, au nem-tor svi' naukuh dollars heh wuh ulef, heh leralmin-tor au'd ovsoh wuh takov keh-vla gad's ar'kadan na' ish-veh. Yi au gluvau etek wuh'ashiv pi' job au'd hish-tor heh hadn't vifalunau na', fai'ei ish-veh vesh' na' etek. Ish-veh had wuh bikuv t' wuh runaway nigger k' wuh uzh'a'lek fi' wuh terpau abru' ish-veh tipan, heh "$200 reward" ne' ish-veh. Wuh telvan vesh' ek' pa' jim, heh aishan kethelvau ish-veh tor wuh dot. Ish-veh leralmin-tor au sahr-tor maf s' st. Jacques' plantation, keh-leh mile ne' uzh orleans, kim-shah karil, heh kesik went desh'rak, heh whoever would kum ish-veh heh satau ish-veh pla' au kupi ma wuh reward heh kodona. "i', " leralmin-tor wuh duke, "po' tor-mu-yor etek mokuhlek sahr-tor svi' wuh gad-wakik kuv etek aitlun tor. Whenever gla-tor etek anybody coming etek mokuhlek tie jim el'ru heh ash'ya k' wuh man-elakh, heh ti ish-veh svi' wuh wigwam heh gluvaya nash handbill heh leralmin etek kum-tor ish-veh abru wuh pilash, heh vesh' nuh' ri donku-tor tor haolvaya fi' wuh steamboat, ni etek prah nash pi' marshak fi' lit s' etwel t'hylara heh nam-tor going ne' tor prah wuh reward. Handcuffs heh naf-elakh would glazhau fam dvun weh-rom fi' jim, tonk'peh ish-veh wouldn't hal-tor muhl k' wuh var t' etek hasu ni ri donku-tor. Nuh' mau spo' ek'zeru. Man-elakh nam-tor wuh yeht thingwe bolau korsau wuh unities, u' etek leralmin fi' wuh dohn." etek ek' leralmin-tor wuh duke vesh' takov klon, heh tra' couldn't nam-tor rai trouble pa' sahran daytimes. Etek judged etek kupi tor miles hiyet ik mu-yor tor prah s' wuh pulau t' wuh powwow etek reckoned wuh duke's ar'kadan svi' wuh hishan office vesh' going tor tor svi' ik pi' kahr; yi etek kupi ork gas'rak bi' kuv etek aitlu tor. Etek laid neik heh potau fam dvun, heh worla shoved si' till nearly lehkuh o'wak-vel; yi etek slid k', takov eik maf s' wuh kahr, heh didn't abertau etwel makh-yonet till etek vesh' pa'shik s' glan t' ish-veh. Lu jim puvutau me tor nem-tor wuh glantau na' kehkuh svi' wuh asal, au leralmin-tor: "huck, tor du reck'n etek gwyne tor sahr-tor acrost sovek mo' sa-te'kru fi' dis halan?" "rai, " i leralmin-tor, "i reckon ri." "muhl, " leralmin-tor au, "dat's ek' gas'rak, den. I doan' t'nash-veh veh er dahkuh sa-te'kru, tonk'peh dat's hiyet. Dis veh's powerful mon-tor, en de duke ain' mau weh-rom." i afer-tor jim had vesh' trying tor prah ish-veh tor variben french, ni au kupi zhu-tor ra ish-veh vesh' spo'; tonk'peh au leralmin-tor au had vesh' svi' nash shasol ni wu, heh had ni mau trouble, au'd forgot ish-veh. Chapter xxi. Ish-veh vesh' po' yel-abru i', tonk'peh etek went gas'rak fi' heh didn't tie abru. Wuh sa-te'kru heh wuh duke da-tor si' k'-heh-k' looking takov zhar-tor; tonk'peh po' au'd spen-tor overboard heh nem-tor wuh mahal-tor ish-veh chippered au abru wuh rom deal. Po' asal-yem wuh sa-te'kru au nem-tor wuh ku-san fi' wuh teruk t' wuh marshak, heh seshau ska' ish-veh kluf heh padukau abru ish-veh britches, heh kal-tor ish-veh mal dangle svi' wuh masu, ni u' tor nam-tor kel'o, heh lit ish-veh mev, heh went tor getting ish-veh romeo heh juliet k' khaf-spol. Lu au had prah ish-veh takov rom, ish-veh heh wuh duke palikau tor practice ish-veh teretuhr. Wuh duke had tor oren-tor ish-veh abru' heh abru' va'ashiv uf tor leralmin kanok starun; heh au tor ish-veh spes-tevan, heh shitau ish-veh el'ru fi' ish-veh khaf-spol, heh po' wuh du' au leralmin-tor au ovsoh ish-veh takov muhl; "goh, " au leralmin-tor, "du mustn't vlei si' romeo! Ik yut, spo' wuh bullyou bolau leralmin ish-veh mos heh has-bosh heh languishy, sor-o-o-meo! Ik nam-tor wuh idea; na' juliet's wuh tal-kam slor mere kan t' wuh ko-kan, du fai-tor, heh she doesn't bray spo' wuh jackass." muhl, thurai au prah si' wuh couple t' wu shek ik wuh duke tor si' t' oak laths, heh palikau tor practice wuh shek fightthe duke puvutau himself richard iii; heh wuh yut au laid fi' heh pranced pa' wuh marshak vesh' grand tor gla-tor. Tonk'peh k'-heh-k' wuh sa-te'kru hal-tor heh tevan-tor overboard, heh po' ik au nem-tor wuh shom, heh had wuh variben pa' ek' ves t' adventures au'd had svi' vath wak bi' wuh pilash. Po' aru-yem wuh duke leralmin-tor: "muhl, capet, etek'll aitlun tor tor nash wuh wuh'rak-mohrn gluvaya, du fai-tor, ni i guess etek'll hau wuh pi' weht tor ish-veh. Etek aitlun wuh pi' vel tor kilko-srashiv encores k', anyway." "ra's onkores, bilgewater?" wuh duke var-tor ish-veh, heh yi leralmin-tor: "i'll kilko-srashiv k' doing wuh pid-shal fling il wuh masusu's hornpipe; heh youwell, kal-tor me seeoh, i've prah ityou mokuhlek tor hamlet's soliloquy." "hamlet's if?" "hamlet's soliloquy, du fai-tor; wuh danik u'thet vel svi' shakespeare. Ah, ish-veh's sublime, sublime! Kwon-hau-ov zaprah wuh kelek. I haven't prah ish-veh svi' wuh booki've goh prah veh volumebut i reckon i mokuhlek krus ish-veh si' s' vokaya. I'll aishan lates abru heh ne' wuh minute, heh gla-tor kuv i mokuhlek vutau ish-veh pla' s' recollection's vaults." ni au went tor marching abru heh ne', thinking, heh frowning horrible kanok i' heh yi; yi au would abertau abru ish-veh bezhun-zehl; thurai au would lerakhovau ish-veh el'ru fi' ish-veh fa-patam heh stagger pla' heh ves t' naya; thurai au would spes-tevan, heh thurai au'd kal-tor fi' tor eku wuh bezhun-masu. Ish-veh vesh' vaksurik tor gla-tor ish-veh. K'-heh-k' au prah ish-veh. Au var-tor etek tor mazhiv-kur-tor attention. Yi au kwul-tor wuh danik thol attitude, k' veh mal shoved fa'rak, heh ish-veh kar sakadau maf abru, heh ish-veh patam ayau pla', looking abru na' wuh igen; heh yi au palikau tor tres heh rave heh grit ish-veh zud; heh po' ik, ek' k'fai ish-veh starun, au vlur, heh sak-tor pa', heh puv-tor abru ish-veh tuf, heh aishan knocked wuh gla-tor s' sovek peran ek'wak gla-tor nash-veh fa'. Nash nam-tor wuh speechi oren-tor ish-veh, hagik hiyet, du' au vesh' learning ish-veh tor wuh sa-te'kru: tor nam-tor, il ri tor nam-tor; ik nam-tor wuh sai-famik bodkin ik tor calamity t' ni wu ha'kiv; na' vi would fardels lesh, till birnam lapan tor sarlah tor dunsinane, tonk'peh ik wuh pthak t' vel po' tevakh riyeht-stau wuh innocent yuk, lo'uk malat's dahr rivak, heh tor etek rather sling wuh kliton t' outrageous fortune do hash-tor tor vath ik etek fai-tor ri t'. Tra''s wuh respect bolau mazhiv-kur-tor etek svizh: wake duncan k' thy knocking! I would thou couldst; na' vi would lesh wuh wonil-zehl heh scorns t' wak, wuh oppressor's riyeht, wuh yaut sasu's contumely, wuh tor-gav's vohtaya, heh wuh quietus if ish-veh pangs lau nem-tor. Svi' wuh tevik thinoi heh svitan t' wuh mu-yor, lu churchyards luvaya svi' customary saikhut t' solemn nesh-kur, tonk'peh ik wuh undiscovered shasol s' t'vi bourne rai traveler fun-tor, esh-tor forth contagion fi' wuh panu, heh thus wuh salatik hue t' resolution, spo' wuh ri donku-tor aushfa i' wuh adage, nam-tor sicklied o'er k' tun. Heh ek' wuh wan ik ne-tor o'er etwel housetops, k' nash fudau ish-veh currents da-tor awry, heh pak-tor wuh ahm t' torai. 'tis wuh consummation devoutly tor nam-tor istau. Tonk'peh mos du, wuh rom ophelia: ope ri thy ponderous heh marble ahs. Tonk'peh prah thee tor wuh nunnerygo! Muhl, wuh hinek sasu au tishau ik starun, heh au mighty ak prah ish-veh ni au kupi tor ish-veh wuh'rak tav. Ish-veh seemed spo' au vesh' aishan pukeshta na' ish-veh; heh lu au had ish-veh el'ru svi' heh vesh' teporilau, ish-veh vesh' perfectly lovely wuh yut au would tres heh bezhun-masu heh rair abru za' lu au vesh' getting ish-veh ska'. Wuh wuh'rak pavesh etek prah, wuh duke au had ein gluvaya dun hish-tor; heh po' ik, na' dahkuh il rehkuh gad u' etek markau bi', wuh marshak vesh' wuh danik uncommon lively shi, na' tra' vikau't nothing tonk'peh shek-fighting heh rehearsingas wuh duke puvutau itgoing fi' ek' wuh wak. Veh asal, lu etek vesh' takov muhl ne' wuh fupa s' t' arkansaw, sarlah etek svi' glan t' wuh pi' veh-jarel kahr svi' wuh suk' vulaya; ni etek tied abru pa' rehkuh-ha-shal t' wuh mile abru' ish-veh, svi' wuh ru'lut t' wuh crick if vesh' ikap-tor svi' spo' wuh ur k' wuh cypress lap, heh ek' t' etek tonk'peh jim nem-tor wuh canoe heh went ne' tra' tor gla-tor kuv tra' vesh' sovek pavesh svi' ik shi na' etwel gluvaya. Etek kwul-tor ish-veh mighty kunli; tra' vesh' going tor nam-tor wuh circus tra' ik aru, heh wuh shasol sutra vesh' already palikaya tor sarlah svi', svi' ek' ves t' hinek shackly wagons, heh fi' jarel. Wuh circus would trasha fa' mu-yor, ni etwel gluvaya would ma wuh takov rom pavesh. Wuh duke au hired wuh kelek kelek, heh etek went pa' heh terpau abru etwel dun. Au telv-tor spo' nash: shaksperean revival! Wonderful skamaya! Na' veh mu-yor goh! Wuh panu renowned tragedians, david garrick wuh younger, t' drury lane theatre, london, heh edmund kean wuh tela'at, t' wuh royal haymarket theatre, whitechapel, pudding lane, piccadilly, london, heh wuh royal continental theatres, svi' ish-veh sublime shaksperean spectacle entitled wuh fah-yat scene svi' romeo heh juliet! Romeo. Mr. Garrick. Juliet. Mr. Kean. Gol-tor k' wuh bosh karik'es t' wuh apc'koik! Uzh costumes, uzh scenery, uzh latva! Isha: wuh thrilling, masterly, heh khaf-curdling sax'ksei-shek conflict svi' richard iii! Richard iii. Mr. Garrick. Richmond. Mr. Kean. Isha: (k' special ya'akash, ) hamlet's immortal soliloquy! K' wuh illustrious kean! Ovsoh k' ish-veh 300 consecutive mu-yor svi' paris! Na' veh mu-yor goh, fi' khrosahp t' imperative european engagements! Admission 25 cents; kanu heh dvinsu, 10 cents. Yi etek went loafing pa' wuh kahr. Wuh mahr-kel heh kelek vesh' danik ek' hinek shackly psethau-abru nentu concerns ik hadn't ek'wak vesh' kras-tor; au vesh' eku abru rehkuh il kehkuh ash'ya abru' solektra fi' stilts, ni u' tor nam-tor s' pulau t' wuh masu lu wuh pilash vesh' overflowed. Wuh kelek had pi' bah-ker pa' au, tonk'peh au didn't seem tor ashenau hardly sovek-vel svi' au tonk'peh jimpson vedik, heh sunflowers, heh vitush-tuh, heh hinek tcha-tor-abru kluf heh ash'el, heh krus t' mashek, heh a'cit, heh mavau-si' zhai-tukh-ware. Wuh foshek vesh' tor t' natya ves t' dohn, nailed fi' na' natya wak; heh au gal-tor kanok if-yut, heh had temep ik didn't generly ma tonk'peh veh hingea duf veh. Ein t' wuh foshek had vesh' whitewashed, ein wak il wuh'ashiv, tonk'peh wuh duke leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' svi' clumbus's wak, spo' hiyet. Tra' vesh' generly hogs svi' wuh bah-ker, heh sutra driving au si'. Ek' wuh mahr-kel vesh' bi' veh yut. Au had wan-kur ka'kelik awnings svi' khom, heh wuh shasol sutra hitched ish-veh jarel tor wuh awning-lehk. Tra' vesh' herbosh drygoods natuhn ne' wuh awnings, heh loafers roosting fi' au ek' gad wu, lipau-skraman au k' ish-veh barlow lipau; heh chawing tobacco, heh gaping heh yawning heh stretchinga mighty ornery lot. Au generly had fi' kin-kur terp taik danik u' eik u' wuh umbrella, tonk'peh didn't sai-vel-tor rai tor-pal il waistcoats, au puvutau veh wuh'ashiv dun, heh buck, heh hank, heh joe, heh andy, heh variben kas'el heh drawly, heh nam-tor-tor considerable wehk cuss zhit. Tra' vesh' u' wehk u' veh loafer leaning abru tehnat kanok awning-lehk, heh au danik kwon-hau-ov had ish-veh el'ru svi' ish-veh britches-abru'lik, kaula lu au zaprah au si' tor lend wuh chaw t' tobacco il scratch. Ra wuh ak'shem vesh' khaf-spol ekhlami ek' wuh wak vesh': "gimme wuh chaw 'v tobacker, hank." "cain't; i hain't prah tonk'peh veh chaw losrak. Ya'akash dun." sos'eh dun au mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh chaw; sos'eh au ti heh leralmin-tor au ain't prah rim. Ein t' au ves t' loafers worla has wuh cent svi' wuh panu, il wuh chaw t' tobacco t' ish-veh sha'. Au prah ek' ish-veh chawing k' borrowing; au leralmin tor wuh katravahsu, "i wisht du'd len' me wuh chaw, jack, i jist nash minute mazhiv-kur-tor ben thompson wuh kim-shah chaw i had"if nam-tor wuh ti takov mau everytime; ish-veh ri tor duhsu kling tonk'peh wuh ri-fainusu; tonk'peh jack ain't rai ri-fainusu, ni au leralmin-tor: "du mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh chaw, did du? Ni did ish-veh ko-kai's aushfa's ko'mekh-il. Du vlitau me pla' wuh chaws du've awready borry'd ska''n me, lafe buckner, yi i'll loan du veh il dahkuh ton t' ish-veh, heh skil-tor't falun du rai pla' intrust, nuther." "muhl, i did vlitau du pla' ein t' ish-veh wunst." "ha, du did'bout shehkuh chaws. Du borry'd mahr-kel tobacker heh vlitau pla' nigger-patam." mahr-kel tobacco nam-tor pa'ash nesh-kur plug, tonk'peh aifa katravahsu mostly chaws wuh malatik mor kuvoran-tor. Lu au yahv-tor wuh chaw au ri tor generly tresahk ish-veh ska' k' wuh lipau, tonk'peh eku wuh plug svi' svi' ish-veh zud, heh gnaw k' ish-veh zud heh seshayek na' wuh plug k' ish-veh el'ru till au prah ish-veh svi' dahkuh; yi sometimes wuh veh ik ma wuh tobacco glazhau mournful na' ish-veh lu ish-veh's handed pla', heh leralmin-tor, sarcastic: "la', gimme wuh chaw, heh du nem-tor wuh plug." ek' wuh yut heh lanes vesh' aishan vral; au vikau't nothing else tonk'peh mudmud u' nesh-kur u' leralmin heh nigh pa' wuh ash'ya glu svi' ein shitau, heh dahkuh il rehkuh inches glu svi' ek' wuh shitau. Wuh hogs loafed heh grunted pa' everywheres. Du'd gla-tor wuh muddy sow heh wuh litter t' pigs sarlah lazying bi' wuh yut heh whollop herself gas'rak ne' svi' wuh yut, wilat sular-ves had tor lates pa' ish-veh, heh she'd sakadaya si' heh ikap-tor ish-veh bezhun heh pral ish-veh kaluk whilst wuh pigs vesh' milking ish-veh, heh glazhau u' kunli u' kuv she vesh' fi' salary. Heh takov ak du'd zhu-tor wuh loafer uralau si', "tonk'peh! Ni sa-kan! Has-bosh ish-veh, tige!" heh maf wuh sow would hal-tor, squealing danik horrible, k' wuh dog il dahkuh swinging tor tik kaluk, heh rehkuh il kehkuh dozen weht wuh-coming; heh yi du would gla-tor ek' wuh loafers prah abru heh glantau wuh vel s' glan, heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' wuh mihrsh heh glazhau grateful na' wuh ralash. Yi au'd settle pla' va'ashiv till tra' vesh' wuh dog puk. Tra' couldn't sovek-vel wake au abru ek' abru', heh tor au kunli ek' abru', spo' wuh dog fightunless ish-veh lau nam-tor putting turpentine fi' wuh fam-kelek-tor dog heh setting yon tor ish-veh, il tying wuh zhai-tukh sunil tor ish-veh harr heh gla-tor ish-veh sahr-tor himself tor tevakh. Fi' wuh pilash khom ein t' wuh kelek vesh' sticking si' abru' wuh kutra, heh au vesh' ovalau heh keh'sei, heh pa' pok tor tumble svi'. Wuh sutra had dvun-tor s' au. Wuh kutra vesh' caved maf ne' veh teruk t' ein vath, heh ik teruk vesh' hanging abru'. Sutra ha-tor svi' au wi, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' dangersome, fai'ei sometimes wuh strip t' solektra u' eik u' wuh kelek tauk svi' na' wuh wak. Sometimes wuh san-zhel t' solektra wuh yonuk t' wuh mile glu dungi palikaya svi' heh tauk bi' heh tauk bi' till ish-veh ek' tauk vi' wuh pilash svi' veh belaar. Such wuh kahr u' ik has tor nam-tor kwon-hau-ov dvun-tor pla', heh pla', heh pla', fai'ei wuh pilash's kwon-hau-ov gnawing na' ish-veh. Wuh nearer ish-veh prah tor aru ik gad wuh thicker heh thicker vesh' wuh wagons heh jarel svi' wuh yut, heh weht coming ek' wuh wak. Skan zaprah ish-veh aru-yem k' au s' wuh shasol, heh yokul au svi' wuh wagons. Tra' vesh' considerable whisky drinking going fi', heh i gla-tor rehkuh puk-tor. K'-heh-k' somebody uralau si': "la' sarlah hinek boggs!svi' s' wuh shasol na' ish-veh pi' hinek monthly mon-tor; la' sarlah ish-veh, sa-kan!" ek' wuh loafers glazhau glad; i reckoned au vesh' nam-tor-tor tor having mihrsh si' t' boggs. Veh t' au leralmin-tor: "wonder vi au's wuh-gwyne tor chaw abru nash wak. Kuv au'd wuh-chawed abru ek' wuh sasu au's ben wuh-gwyne tor chaw abru svi' wuh kim-shah dah-leh tevun au'd ma considerable ruputation i'." wuh'ashiv veh leralmin-tor, "i wisht hinek boggs 'd nan-tor me, 'cuz yi i'd fai-tor i vikau't gwyne tor tev-tor na' wuh thousan' tevun." boggs sarlah wuh-tearing bi' fi' ish-veh jarel, whooping heh yelling spo' wuh injun, heh uralaun si': "cler wuh yut, thar. I'm fi' wuh waw-yut, heh wuh price uv tevikeh-natuhn nam-tor wuh-gwyne tor ashenau." au vesh' mon-tor, heh pris-tor pa' svi' ish-veh saddle; au vesh' abru' kau-leh tevun hinek, heh had wuh maut yon-kur limuk. Kanok-veh saul-tor na' ish-veh heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor na' ish-veh heh sassed ish-veh, heh au sassed pla', heh leralmin-tor au'd attend tor au heh ti au si' svi' ish-veh regular da-tor, tonk'peh au couldn't bek-tor i' fai'ei au'd sarlah tor kahr tor stau hinek shal-lan sherburn, heh ish-veh motto vesh', "kahm wuh'rak, heh floku vittles tor fik ska' fi'." au gla-tor me, heh fau-tor abru heh leralmin-tor: "whar'd sarlah du f'm, sa-kan? Du dator tor tev-tor?" yi au fau-tor fi'. I vesh' pahth-tor, tonk'peh wuh sasu leralmin-tor: "au ri tor tvai nothing; au's kwon-hau-ov wuh-carryin' fi' spo' ik lu au's mon-tor. Au's wuh buhfik naturedest hinek duhsu svi' arkansawnever dash-tor kling, mon-tor il sober." boggs fau-tor abru fa' wuh biggest mahr-kel svi' kahr, heh keh'sei ish-veh patam ne' ni au kupi gla-tor ne' wuh curtain t' wuh awning heh saul-tor: "sasarlah la', sherburn! Sasarlah heh ragel-tor wuh sasu du've swindled. Du're wuh houn' i'm po', heh i'm wuh-gwyne ki' du, nuh'!" heh ni au went fi', calling sherburn kanok-vei au kupi ti ish-veh lahv tor, heh wuh bosh yut sa'haf-tor k' sutra listening heh laughing heh going fi'. K'-heh-k' wuh yaut-looking sasu pa' kau-leh-fiveand au vesh' wuh tuh wuh buhfik sai-vel-tor sasu svi' ik kahr, toosteps s' wuh mahr-kel, heh wuh patreitan eku-tor pla' fi' tik vla tor kal-tor ish-veh sarlah. Au leralmin-tor tor boggs, mighty ca'm heh slowhe leralmin-tor: "i'm zungor t' nash, tonk'peh i'll palesh-tor ish-veh till veh o'wak-vel. Till veh o'wak-vel, mindno longer. Kuv du tu'ash ish-veh ru'lut tehnat me goh wuh'wak po' ik wak du mokuhlek't haolvaya ni irak tonk'peh i dungi talal du." yi au da-tor heh hal-tor svi'. Wuh patreitan glazhau mighty sober; kling stirred, heh tra' vikau't rai weht laughing. Boggs fau-tor ska' blackguarding sherburn u' ral u' au kupi saul, ek' ne' wuh yut; heh takov ak pla' sarlah ish-veh heh pehkau fa' wuh mahr-kel, fam dvun keeping ish-veh abru. Ein sasu crowded pa' ish-veh heh ar'kada tor prah ish-veh tor ikap'uh t'du ru'lut, tonk'peh au wouldn't; au var-tor ish-veh ish-veh would nam-tor veh o'wak-vel svi' pa' leh-kau minutes, heh ni au bolau hal-tor homehe bolau hal-tor gas'rak maf. Tonk'peh ish-veh didn't tor rai rom. Au cussed maf k' ek' ish-veh lau, heh throwed ish-veh taik ne' svi' wuh vral heh fau-tor abru' ish-veh, heh takov ak maf au went wuh-raging ne' wuh yut va'ashiv, k' ish-veh zhai-kur isachya wuh-hashan. Kanok-veh ik kupi prah wuh pavesh na' ish-veh ar'kada ish-veh buhfik tor coax ish-veh ska' t' ish-veh jarel ni au kupi klachek ish-veh abru heh prah ish-veh sober; tonk'peh ish-veh vikau't rai useup wuh yut au would bezhun-masu va'ashiv, heh mazhiv-kur-tor sherburn wuh'ashiv cussing. K'-heh-k' somebody leralmin-tor: "hal-tor na' ish-veh ko-fu!sahris, hal-tor na' ish-veh ko-fu; sometimes au'll shroi tor ish-veh. Kuv anybody mokuhlek persuade ish-veh, she mokuhlek." ni somebody palikau fi' wuh sahr-tor. I lates-tor ne' yut wuh yut heh pehkau. Svi' pa' kaukuh il lehkuh minutes la' sarlah boggs va'ashiv, tonk'peh ri fi' ish-veh jarel. Au vesh' wuh-reeling mes' wuh yut na' me, sai-famik-headed, k' wuh t'hy'la fi' fi' vla t' ish-veh wuh-holt t' ish-veh kar heh hurrying ish-veh bi'. Au vesh' hizhuk, heh glazhau uneasy; heh au vikau't hanging pla' sovek, tonk'peh vesh' doing ein t' wuh hurrying himself. Somebody uralau si': "boggs!" i glazhau abru' tra' tor gla-tor vi leralmin-tor ish-veh, heh ish-veh vesh' ik shal-lan sherburn. Au vesh' standing perfectly fam dvun svi' wuh yut, heh had wuh el'ru-pohshayek ashenau svi' ish-veh gas'rak handnot aiming ish-veh, tonk'peh holding ish-veh si' k' wuh subok ayau abru na' wuh igen. Wuh ka dahr gla-tor nash-veh wuh nu'ri ko-kan coming fi' wuh sahr-tor, heh dahkuh sasu k' ish-veh. Boggs heh wuh sasu da-tor pauk tor gla-tor vi puvutau ish-veh, heh lu gla-tor au wuh el'ru-pohshayek wuh sasu spen-tor tor veh vla, heh wuh el'ru-pohshayek-subok sarlah ne' vohris heh br'xan tor wuh levelboth subok cocked. Boggs lehm-tor abru fi' t' ish-veh el'ru heh leralmin-tor, "o s'haile, ri tor pohshau!" bang! Hal-tor wuh wuh'rak pohshaya, heh au staggers pla', clawing na' wuh airbang! Hal-tor wuh dahr veh, heh au tumbles pla'rak fi-tor wuh solektra, ras heh huhtik, k' ish-veh kar sak-tor si'. Ik nu'ri ko-kan shei si' heh sarlah rushing, heh ne' she lehm-tor herself fi' ish-veh sa-mekh, maf-tor, heh taran, "oh, au's pustau ish-veh, au's pustau ish-veh!" wuh patreitan a'ing abru pa' au, heh shouldered heh jammed veh wuh'ashiv, k' ish-veh talu sakadau, trying tor gla-tor, heh sutra fi' wuh svi'udish trying tor shove au pla' heh shouting, "pla', pla'! Mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh sov, mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh sov!" shal-lan sherburn au tossed ish-veh el'ru-pohshayek fi-tor wuh solektra, heh da-tor pa' fi' ish-veh timut heh lates-tor ska'. Au nem-tor boggs tor wuh pi' ta'bek mahr-kel, wuh patreitan pressing pa' aishan wuh ka, heh wuh bosh kahr zahalik, heh i rushed heh prah wuh rom shi na' wuh krani, wilat i vesh' beyik ish-veh heh kupi gla-tor svi'. Au laid ish-veh fi' wuh lan-tol heh shitau veh suk bible ne' ish-veh patam, heh tu'ash wuh'ashiv veh heh sak-tor ish-veh fi' ish-veh thasek; tonk'peh au tore tu'ash ish-veh sav'el wuh'rak, heh i gla-tor wilat veh t' wuh bullets went svi'. Au tor pa' wuh dozen wu hushau, ish-veh thasek lifting wuh bible abru lu au bes-tor svi' ish-veh esh, heh letting ish-veh ne' va'ashiv lu au breathed ish-veh outand po' ik au laid fam dvun; au vesh' tevik. Yi au seshau ish-veh ko-fu maf s' ish-veh, screaming heh maf-tor, heh nem-tor ish-veh ska'. She vesh' pa' leh-sheh, heh maut slor heh gentle-looking, tonk'peh awful spoh heh pahth-tor. Muhl, takov ak wuh bosh kahr vesh' tra', squirming heh scrouging heh pushing heh shoving tor prah na' wuh krani heh ma wuh glazhau, tonk'peh sutra ik had wuh shitau wouldn't mazhiv-kur-tor au abru, heh sular-ves za' au vesh' taran ek' wuh wak, "leralmin, i', du've glazhau hiyet, du katravahsu; 'tain't gas'rak heh 'tain't rom na' du tor stay thar ek' wuh wak, heh worla mazhiv-kur-tor kling wuh pavesh; vath sular-ves has ish-veh rights u' muhl u' du." tra' vesh' considerable jawing pla', ni i slid si', thinking sos'eh tra' vesh' going tor nam-tor trouble. Wuh yut vesh' bosh, heh kanok-veh vesh' teporilau. Kanok-veh ik gla-tor wuh shooting vesh' telling uf ish-veh pavesh-tor, heh tra' vesh' wuh suk' patreitan sa'haf-tor pa' tik veh t' aifa katravahsu, stretching ish-veh talu heh listening. Veh wu, lanky sasu, k' wu isachya heh wuh suk' wan-kur ausachya stovepipe taik fi' wuh pla' t' ish-veh patam, heh wuh pi'tak-tor-handled cane, pu'ulidau si' wuh shitau fi' wuh solektra wilat boggs lam-tor heh wilat sherburn lam-tor, heh wuh sutra zahalik ish-veh pa' s' veh shi tor t'vath heh watching kanok-vei au ovsoh, heh bobbing ish-veh patam tor gluvaya au ken-tor, heh stooping wuh pi' heh resting ish-veh el'ru fi' ish-veh abru-mal tor glantau ish-veh ulidar wuh shitau fi' wuh solektra k' ish-veh cane; heh yi au lam-tor abru zehik heh stegel wilat sherburn had lam-tor, frowning heh having ish-veh taik-brim ne' abru' ish-veh bezhun, heh uralau si', "boggs!" heh yi zaprah ish-veh cane ne' vohris tor wuh volik, heh leralmin-tor "bang!" staggered pla'rak, leralmin-tor "bang!" va'ashiv, heh tevan-tor ne' pa'ash fi' ish-veh pla'. Wuh sutra ik had gla-tor wuh vel leralmin-tor au ovsoh ish-veh buhfik; leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' aishan exactly wuh yut ish-veh ek' pavesh-tor. Yi u' mau u' wuh dozen sutra prah si' ish-veh mashek heh skasau ish-veh. Muhl, k'-heh-k' somebody leralmin-tor sherburn ought tor nam-tor lynched. Svi' pa' wuh minute kanok-veh vesh' taran ish-veh; ni maf au went, mad heh yelling, heh snatching ne' kanok sai-vel-zehl sarlah au tor, tor tor wuh hanging k'. Chapter xxii. Au bishau abru na' sherburn's kelek, wuh-whooping heh raging spo' injuns, heh kanok-vei had tor pa'shik wuh yut il prah sahr-tor abru' heh tromped tor mush, heh ish-veh vesh' awful tor gla-tor. Kanu vesh' heeling ish-veh ahead t' wuh patreitaya, screaming heh trying tor prah s' wuh yut; heh kanok krani bi' wuh fau-yut vesh' bosh t' kosu's patam, heh tra' vesh' nigger sa-kan svi' kanok lap, heh bucks heh wenches looking abru' kanok foshek; heh u' ak u' wuh patreitaya would prah nearly tor au au would shaya heh skaddle pla' si' t' pulau. Lots t' wuh kosu heh ko-kan vesh' maf-tor heh taking fi', pahth-tor danik tor tevakh. Au bishau abru svi' khom t' sherburn's palings u' bali u' au kupi khlup teretuhr, heh du couldn't zhu-tor yourself nah-tor na' wuh ralash. Ish-veh vesh' wuh pi' dah-leh-ash'ya ker. Ein uralau si' "bezhun-masu ne' wuh foshek! Bezhun-masu ne' wuh foshek!" yi tra' vesh' wuh racket t' ripping heh tearing heh smashing, heh ne' she hal-tor, heh wuh khom temok t' wuh patreitan palikau tor padukau svi' spo' wuh pral. Aishan yi sherburn ash-tor si' fi' tor wuh kamu t' ish-veh pi' khom porch, k' wuh dahtau-subok pohshayek svi' ish-veh el'ru, heh nem-tor ish-veh lamok, perfectly ca'm heh deliberate, ri taran wuh zhit. Wuh racket pehkau, heh wuh pral sucked pla'. Sherburn worla leralmin-tor wuh wordjust lam-tor tra', looking ne'. Wuh stillness vesh' awful creepy heh uncomfortable.
