Sherburn sahr-tor ish-veh bezhun vohris bi' wuh patreitan; heh wherever ish-veh kwul-tor wuh sutra ar'kada wuh pi' tor si'-gaze ish-veh, tonk'peh au couldn't; au eku-tor ish-veh bezhun heh glazhau sneaky. Yi takov ak sherburn wihfelau t' abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor; ri wuh vaksurik ves, tonk'peh wuh ves ik tor du olau spo' lu du nam-tor eating kap ik's prah mazhiv svi' ish-veh. Yi au leralmin-tor, vohris heh scornful: "wuh idea t' du lynching anybody! Ish-veh's tzlu'pd. Wuh idea t' du thinking du had pluck hiyet tor lynch wuh sasu! Fai'ei du're kyi'i hiyet tor leralmin heh kan ri donku-tor friendless vishizhau-si' kosu ik sarlah bi' la', did ik tor du nah-tor du had grit hiyet tor ti ish-veh el'ru fi' wuh sasu? Po, wuh sasu's safe svi' wuh el'ru t' lehkuh thousand t' ish-veh kindas wu u' ish-veh's gad-wakik heh du're ri za' ish-veh. "tor i fai-tor du? I fai-tor du pa'shik k'fai. I vesh' pukeshta heh ashenau svi' wuh khu'rak, heh i've ha-tor svi' wuh desh'rak; ni i fai-tor wuh bov ek' pa'. Wuh bov sasu's wuh coward. Svi' wuh desh'rak au kal-tor anybody lates abru' ish-veh ik aitlu tor, heh hal-tor ha-kel heh prays na' wuh humble tam'a tor lesh ish-veh. Svi' wuh khu'rak veh sasu ek' k' himself, has pehkau wuh skaf bosh t' sasu svi' wuh gad-wakik, heh robbed wuh lot. Ish-veh newspapers vutau du wuh kyi'i sutra ni mau ik du nah-tor du nam-tor braver do sovek vath peoplewhereas du're aishan u' kyi'i, heh rai braver. Po ri tor ish-veh juries geldau murderers? Fai'ei au're kwes wuh sasu's t'hylara dungi pohshau au svi' wuh pla', svi' wuh darkand ish-veh's aishan ra au would tor. "ni au kwon-hau-ov acquit; heh yi wuh sasu hal-tor svi' wuh mu-yor, k' wuh hundred masked cowards na' ish-veh pla' heh lynches wuh rascal. Ish-veh lafosh nam-tor, ik du didn't katau wuh sasu k' du; ik's veh lafosh, heh wuh vath nam-tor ik du didn't sarlah svi' wuh gu'gelik heh zaprah ish-veh limein. Du katau krus t' wuh manbuck harkness, thereand kuv du hadn't had ish-veh tor palikaya du, du'd wuh taken ish-veh si' svi' blowing. "du didn't aitlun tor sarlah. Wuh bov sasu ri tor spo' trouble heh tehvar. Du ri tor spo' trouble heh tehvar. Tonk'peh kuv goh ulef wuh manlike buck harkness, thereshouts 'lynch ish-veh! Lynch ish-veh!' du're kwes tor pla' downafraid du'll nam-tor afer-tor si' tor nam-tor ra du arecowardsand ni du ashenau wuh saul, heh geldau yourselves fi' tor ik ulef-wuh-sasu's tor-pal-harr, heh sarlah raging abru la', swearing ra suk' vel du're going tor tor. Wuh pitifulest vel si' nam-tor wuh patreitaya; ik's ra wuh ya'akash'er isa patreitaya; au ri tor puk k' courage ik's pukeshta svi' au, tonk'peh k' courage ik's yahv-tor s' ish-veh shivak, heh s' ish-veh officers. Tonk'peh wuh patreitaya rik' sovek sasu na' wuh patam t' ish-veh nam-tor ne'rak pitifulness. I' wuh vel na' du tor tor nam-tor tor tevan-tor ish-veh harr heh hal-tor ha-kel heh ukrau svi' wuh razh. Kuv sovek yeht lynching's going tor nam-tor ovsoh, ish-veh dungi nam-tor ovsoh svi' wuh gu'gelik, southern fashion; heh lu sarlah au au'll katau ish-veh limein, heh zaprah wuh sasu bi'. I' leaveand nem-tor ish-veh ulef-wuh-sasu k' du"tossing ish-veh pohshayek abru mes' ish-veh losrak kar heh cocking ish-veh lu au leralmin-tor nash. Wuh patreitan pu-tor pla' sudden, heh yi shau ek' k'wuhli, heh went tearing ska' kanok if yut, heh buck harkness au heeled ish-veh po' au, looking tolerable cheap. I kupi wuh staid kuv i aitlu tor, tonk'peh i didn't aitlun tor. I went tor wuh circus heh loafed pa' wuh pla' vla till wuh watchman went k', heh yi taul-tor svi' ne' wuh ith'du. I had t'nash-veh dah-leh-dollar pi-maat-tukh krus heh ein vath donku, tonk'peh i reckoned i weh-rom korsau ish-veh, fai'ei tra' ain't rai telling uf ak du nam-tor going tor bolaya ish-veh, maf s' ha-kel heh svi' ri-fainusu ik yut. Du mokuhlek't nam-tor nuh' tun-bosh. I ain't opposed tor spending donku fi' circuses lu tra' ain't rai vath yut, tonk'peh tra' ain't rai nam-tor-tor svi' wasting ish-veh fi' au. Ish-veh vesh' wuh yeht bully circus. Ish-veh vesh' wuh splendidest glan ik ek'wak vesh' lu au ek' sarlah riding svi', dahkuh heh dahkuh, wuh gentleman heh t'sai, vla k' vla, wuh sasu aishan svi' ish-veh zish-nef heh undershirts, heh rai ash'el il stirrups, heh resting ish-veh el'ru fi' ish-veh abru-mal hagik heh comfortablethere bolau wuh vesh' dah-leh t' themand kanok t'sai k' wuh lovely complexion, heh perfectly vaksurik, heh looking aishan spo' wuh gang t' yeht sure-hiyet ko-te'kru, heh sai-vel-tor svi' sai-vel ik kodona millions t' dollars, heh aishan littered k' lerash-khush. Ish-veh vesh' wuh powerful tok-ti glan; i worla gla-tor sovek-vel ni lovely. Heh yi veh k' veh au prah abru heh lam-tor, heh went wuh-pris-tor pa' wuh mokov ni gentle heh wavy heh graceful, wuh sasu looking ek'wak ni ha-vol heh airy heh zehik, k' ish-veh patam bobbing heh skimming bi', maf abru tra' ne' wuh ith'du-kamu, heh kanok t'sai's she-tor-leafy sai-vel flapping mos heh silky pa' ish-veh gaf, heh she looking spo' wuh danik loveliest parasol. Heh yi faster heh faster au went, ek' t' au taman, wuh'rak veh ash'ya si' svi' wuh sov heh yi wuh vath, wuh jarel leaning weht heh weht, heh wuh mokov-trensu going pauk heh pauk wuh svitan-fek, cracking ish-veh wonil-zehl heh shouting "tonk'peh!tonk'peh!" heh wuh clown cracking kha'wal za' ish-veh; heh k'-heh-k' ek' el'ru eku-tor wuh reins, heh kanok t'sai shitau ish-veh ozh-lesek fi' ish-veh gaf heh kanok gentleman hesha ish-veh kar, heh yi uf wuh jarel did galat abru' heh hump themselves! Heh ni veh po' wuh vath au ek' skipped ska' vi' wuh mokov, heh tor wuh sweetest kes-wun i ek'wak gla-tor, heh yi scampered si', heh kanok-veh clapped ish-veh el'ru heh went aishan pa' kwai. Muhl, ek' k'fai wuh circus au ovsoh wuh danik astonishing vel; heh ek' wuh wak ik clown lesh fi' ni ish-veh danik pustau wuh sutra. Wuh mokov-trensu couldn't ek'wak leralmin wuh zhit tor ish-veh tonk'peh au vesh' pla' na' ish-veh sahris u' wuh wink k' wuh funniest vel wuh ak'shem ek'wak leralmin-tor; heh uf au ek'wak kupi nah-tor t' ni wehk t' au, heh ni sudden heh ni pat, vesh' ra i couldn't noway ken-tor. Po, i couldn't wuh nahp t' au svi' wuh tevun. Heh k'-heh-k' wuh mon-tor sasu ar'kada tor prah vi' wuh ringsaid au aitlu tor fau; leralmin-tor au kupi fau u' muhl u' anybody ik ek'wak vesh'. Au gyirm'i heh ar'kada tor potau ish-veh si', tonk'peh au wouldn't shroi, heh wuh bosh gluvaya sarlah tor wuh standstill. Yi wuh sutra palikau tor holler na' ish-veh heh tor mihrsh t' ish-veh, heh ik tor ish-veh mad, heh au palikau tor tres heh bezhun-masu; ni ik stirred abru wuh sutra, heh wuh lot t' sasu palikau tor tuh ne' ska' t' wuh wu-ku-san heh bish na' wuh mokov, taran, "knock ish-veh ne'! Lehm ish-veh si'!" heh veh il dahkuh kosu palikau tor shei. Ni, yi, wuh mokov-trensu au tor wuh pi' starun, heh leralmin-tor au rok-tor tra' wouldn't nam-tor rai ertaya, heh kuv wuh sasu would ugaya au wouldn't tor rai weht trouble au would kal-tor ish-veh fau kuv au nahp au kupi stay fi' wuh jarel. Ni kanok-veh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor heh leralmin-tor ek' gas'rak, heh wuh sasu prah fi'. Wuh minute au vesh' fi', wuh jarel palikau tor tres heh bezhun-masu heh spen-tor heh cavort pa', k' dahkuh circus sasu hanging fi' tor ish-veh bridle trying tor meskaraya ish-veh, heh wuh mon-tor sasu hanging fi' tor ish-veh talu, heh ish-veh timut hashan svi' wuh sov kanok spen-tor, heh wuh bosh patreitan t' sutra standing abru shouting heh laughing till bezhun-masu padukau ne'. Heh na' kim-shah, sure hiyet, ek' wuh circus sasu kupi tor, wuh jarel shau thal, heh maf au went spo' wuh maut shashol, pauk heh pauk wuh mokov, k' ik sot laying ne' fi' ish-veh heh hanging tor ish-veh talu, k' wuh'rak veh mal hanging danik tor wuh solektra fi' veh vla, heh yi t'vath veh fi' t'vath vla, heh wuh sutra aishan amp. Ish-veh vikau't funny tor me, hi; i vesh' ek' t' wuh tremble tor gla-tor ish-veh tehvar. Tonk'peh takov ak au struggled abru astraddle heh runem-tor wuh bridle, wuh-reeling nash yut heh ik; heh wuh thurai minute au sprung abru heh eku-tor wuh bridle heh lam-tor! Heh wuh jarel wuh-going spo' wuh kelek afire nuh'. Au aishan lam-tor abru tra', wuh-masu-halovaun pa' u' hagik heh kel'o u' kuv au vikau't ek'wak mon-tor svi' ish-veh lifeand yi au palikau tor seshaya ska' ish-veh sai-vel heh sling au. Au foshuhl au ni bali au ves t' clogged abru wuh sov, heh altogether au foshuhl leh- steh saikhut. Heh, yi, tra' au vesh', slim heh handsome, heh sai-vel-tor wuh gaudiest heh prettiest du ek'wak gla-tor, heh au lit vi' ik jarel k' ish-veh wonil-zehl heh tor ish-veh fairly humand t'forti skipped ska', heh tor ish-veh kes-wun heh tam-tor ska' tor wuh sai-vel-tor-tvi-shal, heh kanok-veh aishan wuh-howling k' sanosh heh astonishment. Yi wuh mokov-trensu au gla-tor uf au had vesh' fooled, heh au vesh' wuh sickest mokov-trensu du ek'wak gla-tor, i reckon. Po, ish-veh vesh' veh t' ish-veh sha' sasu! Au had prah abru ik kha'wal ek' s' ish-veh sha' patam, heh worla kal-tor fi' tor kling. Muhl, i olau sheepish hiyet tor nam-tor nem-tor svi' ni, tonk'peh i wouldn't wuh vesh' svi' ik mokov-trensu's shi, ri na' wuh thousand dollars. I ri tor fai-tor; tra' lau nam-tor bullier circuses do ra ish-veh vesh', tonk'peh i worla kwul-tor au wi. Anyways, ish-veh vesh' plenty rom hiyet na' me; heh wherever i sahr-tor mes' ish-veh, ish-veh mokuhlek ma ek' t' t'nash-veh custom kanok wak. Muhl, ik mu-yor etek had etwel gluvaya; tonk'peh tra' vikau't goh pa' leh-dah sutra therejust hiyet tor vlitau kodona. Heh au abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor ek' wuh wak, heh ik tor wuh duke mad; heh kanok-veh losrak, anyway, fa' wuh gluvaya vesh' abru', tonk'peh veh sa-kan if vesh' asleep. Ni wuh duke leralmin-tor aifa arkansaw lunkheads couldn't sarlah abru tor shakespeare; ra au aitlu vesh' neik comedyand sos'eh vel ruther weh-rasahkos do neik comedy, au reckoned. Au leralmin-tor au kupi suk'es ish-veh style. Ni thurai asal au prah ein suk' thalv t' wrapping dun heh ein nesh-kur kras, heh bes-tor ska' ein handbills, heh terpau au abru ek' abru' wuh pi'kahr. Wuh dun leralmin-tor: na' wuh kelek kelek! Na' 3 mu-yor goh! Wuh panu-renowned tragedians david garrick wuh younger! Heh edmund kean wuh tela'at! T' wuh london heh continental theatres, svi' ish-veh thrilling tragedy t' wuh sa-te'kru's camelopard il wuh royal nonesuch! Admission 50 cents. Yi na' wuh lanet vesh' wuh biggest zehl t' allwhich leralmin-tor: t'sai heh kanu ri nafai-tor. "tra', " leralmin-tor au, "kuv ik zehl ri tor zaprah au, i dont fai-tor arkansaw!" chapter xxiii. Muhl, ek' gad ish-veh heh wuh sa-te'kru vesh' lerash na' ish-veh, rigging abru wuh skaf heh wuh curtain heh wuh zehl t' ha'fek na' footlights; heh ik mu-yor wuh kelek vesh' khlup bosh t' sasu svi' rai wak. Lu wuh shi couldn't meskaraya rai weht, wuh duke au quit tending svep heh went pa' wuh pla' yut heh sarlah fi' tor wuh skaf heh lam-tor abru fa' wuh curtain heh tor wuh pi' starun, heh krol-tor abru nash tragedy, heh leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh danik thrillingest veh ik ek'wak vesh'; heh ni au went fi' wuh-bragging pa' wuh tragedy, heh pa' edmund kean wuh tela'at, if vesh' tor mavau wuh nen principal krus svi' ish-veh; heh na' kim-shah lu au'd prah kanok-veh's gishat abru pid hiyet, au padukau abru wuh curtain, heh wuh thurai minute wuh sa-te'kru sarlah wuh-prancing si' fi' ek' fours, sai-fam; heh au vesh' kras-tor ek' abru', mokov-wesh-tor-heh-zhel-tor, ek' wihfelau t' colors, u' splendid u' wuh igen-kur-kesek. Andbut worla kashek wuh shom t' ish-veh outfit; ish-veh vesh' aishan kwai, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' awful funny. Wuh sutra danik pustau themselves laughing; heh lu wuh sa-te'kru prah ovsoh capering heh capered ska' za' wuh scenes, au roared heh clapped heh stormed heh haw-hawed till au sarlah pla' heh ovsoh ish-veh abru' va'ashiv, heh po' ik au tor ish-veh tor ish-veh wuh'ashiv wak. Muhl, ish-veh would tor wuh aushfa abru'teruklar-ru'lut tor gla-tor wuh min-tor ik hinek idiot tresahk. Yi wuh duke au kal-tor wuh curtain ne', heh ovalau tor wuh sutra, heh leralmin-tor wuh lo'uk tragedy dungi nam-tor performed goh dahkuh mu-yor weht, fi' khrosahp t' pressing london engagements, wilat wuh ku-san nam-tor ek' makau already na' ish-veh svi' drury lane; heh yi au tor au wuh'ashiv kes-wun, heh leralmin-tor kuv au has navau svi' pleasing au heh instructing au, au dungi nam-tor deeply obleeged kuv au dungi mention ish-veh tor ish-veh t'hylara heh prah au tor sarlah heh gla-tor ish-veh. Dah-leh sutra uralau si': "ra, nam-tor ish-veh abru'? Nam-tor ik ek'?" wuh duke leralmin-tor ha. Yi tra' vesh' wuh tok-ti wak. Kanok-veh uralau si', "makau!" heh she-tor abru mad, heh vesh' wuh-going na' ik skaf heh au tragedians. Tonk'peh wuh suk', tok-ti looking sasu spen-tor abru fi' wuh wu-ku-san heh saul-tor: "meskaraya fi'! Aishan wuh zhit, gentlemen." au pehkau tor shroi. "etek nam-tor soldmighty badly makau. Tonk'peh etek ri tor aitlun tor nam-tor wuh laughing fek t' nash bosh kahr, i reckon, heh worla zhu-tor wuh kim-shah t' nash vel u' wu u' etek ha-tor. Rai. Ra etek aitlun nam-tor tor hal-tor s' la' hizhuk, heh variben nash gluvaya abru, heh makau wuh shom t' wuh kahr! Yi etek'll ek' nam-tor svi' wuh ka masu-hali. Ain't ik sensible?" ("du sihaya ish-veh nam-tor!wuh jedge nam-tor gas'rak!" kanok-veh uralau si'.) "ek' gas'rak, thennot wuh zhit pa' sovek makau. Hal-tor bi' ha-kel, heh na'shikhau kanok-veh tor sarlah heh gla-tor wuh tragedy." thurai gad du couldn't zhu-tor nothing pa' ik kahr tonk'peh uf splendid ik gluvaya vesh'. Kelek vesh' jammed va'ashiv ik mu-yor, heh etek makau nash patreitan wuh ka yut. Lu me heh wuh sa-te'kru heh wuh duke prah ha-kel tor wuh marshak etek ek' had wuh mu'yor-yem; heh k'-heh-k', pa' midnight, au tor jim heh me pla' ish-veh si' heh marek ish-veh ne' wuh svitan t' wuh pilash, heh zaprah ish-veh svi' heh ip-sut ish-veh pa' dahkuh mile ne' kahr. Wuh wuh mu-yor wuh kelek vesh' crammed againand au vikau't uzh-comers nash wak, tonk'peh sutra ik vesh' na' wuh gluvaya wuh vath dahkuh mu-yor. I lam-tor k' wuh duke na' wuh svep, heh gla-tor nash-veh ik kanok sasu ik went svi' had ish-veh abru'lik bulging, il vel nessau abru ne' ish-veh coatand i gla-tor ish-veh vikau't rai perfumery, neither, ri k' wuh wu glan. I smelt sickly yu-mur k' wuh subok, heh rotten cabbages, heh such vel; heh kuv i fai-tor wuh glat t' wuh tevik aushfa hasu pa', heh i sihaya i tor, tra' vesh' sheh-leh-kehkuh t' au went svi'. I shoved svi' tra' na' wuh minute, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' nuh' vuhnauk na' me; i couldn't lamok ish-veh. Muhl, lu wuh shi couldn't meskaraya rai weht sutra wuh duke au mazhiv-kur-tor wuh katravahsu wuh yonuk heh var-tor ish-veh tor palutunau svep na' ish-veh wuh minute, heh yi au palikau pa' na' wuh skaf svep, i po' ish-veh; tonk'peh wuh minute etek da-tor wuh teruk heh vesh' svi' wuh gu'gelik au leralmin-tor: "lates sahris i' till du prah maf s' wuh kelek, heh yi ne-mal na' wuh marshak spo' wuh dickens vesh' po' du!" i ovsoh ish-veh, heh au ovsoh wuh ka. Etek kwul-tor wuh marshak na' wuh ka wak, heh svi' lehkuh tor dahkuh seconds etek vesh' gliding ne' pilash, ek' gu'gelik heh fam dvun, heh rihkaya na' wuh svitan t' wuh pilash, kling taran wuh zhit. I reckoned wuh ri donku-tor sa-te'kru vesh' svi' na' wuh gaudy wak t' ish-veh k' wuh audience, tonk'peh nothing t' wuh wihfelau; takov ak au ukrau si' s' ne' wuh wigwam, heh leralmin-tor: "muhl, uf'd wuh hinek vel sunil si' nash wak, duke?" au hadn't vesh' abru kahr na' ek'. Etek worla gluvau wuh ta'hal till etek vesh' pa' lehkuh mile ne' wuh pi'kahr. Yi etek lit abru heh had wuh mu'yor-yem, heh wuh sa-te'kru heh wuh duke fairly abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor ish-veh hinek thal abru' wuh yut au'd dvin-tor au sutra. Wuh duke leralmin-tor: "greenhorns, flatheads! I fai-tor wuh wuh'rak kelek would potau mum heh kal-tor wuh shom t' wuh kahr prah roped svi'; heh i fai-tor au'd ti na' etek wuh wuh mu-yor, heh panah-tor ish-veh vesh' ish-veh da-tor i'. Muhl, ish-veh nam-tor ish-veh da-tor, heh i'd mazhiv-kur-tor vel tor fai-tor uf mau au'd nem-tor na' ish-veh. I would aishan spo' tor fai-tor uf au're putting svi' ish-veh opportunity. Au mokuhlek da-tor ish-veh vi' wuh picnic kuv au aitlun tothey katau plenty provisions." au rapscallions nem-tor svi' kehkuh hundred heh sheh-leh-kaukuh dollars svi' ik rehkuh mu-yor. I worla gla-tor donku hauled svi' k' wuh wagon-tus spo' ik fa'. K'-heh-k', lu au vesh' asleep heh snoring, jim leralmin-tor: "ri tor ish-veh s'prise du de yut dem sa-te'kru lesh fi', huck?" "rai, " i leralmin-tor, "ish-veh ri tor." "po ri tor ish-veh, huck?" "muhl, ish-veh ri tor, fai'ei ish-veh's svi' wuh kosh-ves. I reckon au're ek' kahkwa." "tonk'peh, huck, dese sa-te'kru o' ourn nam-tor reglar rapscallions; dat's jist ra dey nam-tor; dey's reglar rapscallions." "muhl, ik's ra i'm wuh-taran; ek' sa-te'kru nam-tor mostly rapscallions, u' ausachya u' i mokuhlek tor si'." "nam-tor dat ni?" "du telv-tor pa' au onceyou'll gla-tor. Glazhau na' henry wuh ohkuh; nash'n 's wuh gad-shi'oren superintendent tor ish-veh. Heh glazhau na' charles dahr, heh louis leh-keh, heh louis leh-kau, heh james dahr, heh edward dahr, heh richard wuh, heh keh-leh weht; isha ek' au saxon heptarchies ik nam-tor-tor tor tres pa' ni svi' hinek wak heh ashenau cain. T'nash-veh, du ought tor gla-tor hinek henry wuh ohkuh lu au vesh' svi' svai. Au vesh' wuh blossom. Au nam-tor-tor tor marry wuh uzh ko-telsu kanok gad, heh chop ska' ish-veh patam thurai asal. Heh au would tor ish-veh aishan u' indifferent u' kuv au vesh' ordering abru yu-mur. 'zaprah abru nell gwynn, ' au leralmin-tor. Au zaprah ish-veh abru. Thurai asal, 'chop ska' ish-veh patam!' heh au chop ish-veh ska'. 'zaprah abru jane gef, ' au leralmin-tor; heh abru sarlah ish-veh, thurai asal, 'chop ska' ish-veh patam'heh au chop ish-veh ska'. 'mokov abru rom rosamun.' rom rosamun kilko-srashiv wuh kus-vakh. Thurai asal, 'chop ska' ish-veh patam.' heh au tor kanok veh t' au var-tor ish-veh wuh var kanok mu-yor; heh au potau ik abru till au had hogged wuh thousand heh veh var ik yut, heh yi au shitau au ek' svi' wuh dunap, heh puvutau ish-veh domesday bookwhich vesh' wuh rom ahm heh fupa s' wuh nuf. Du ri tor fai-tor sa-te'kru, jim, tonk'peh i fai-tor au; heh nash hinek tres t' ourn nam-tor veh t' wuh cleanest i've kwul-tor svi' vesht-var. Muhl, henry au nem-tor wuh notion au aitlu tor prah abru ein trouble k' nash shasol. Uf tor au hal-tor na' itgive beglanau?mazhiv-kur-tor wuh shasol wuh gluvaya? Rai. Ek' t' wuh sudden au heaves ek' wuh theris-masu svi' boston harbor overboard, heh whacks si' wuh afsakaya t' tikopah, heh dares au tor sarlah fi'. Ik vesh' ish-veh stylehe worla mazhiv-kur-tor anybody wuh pavesh. Au had suspicions t' ish-veh sa-mekh, wuh duke t' wellington. Muhl, ra did au tor? Ya'akash ish-veh tor gluvaya abru? Nodrownded ish-veh svi' wuh butt t' mamsey, spo' wuh aushfa. S'pose sutra losrak donku laying pa' wilat au waswhat did au tor? Au collared ish-veh. S'pose au contracted tor tor wuh vel, heh du vlitau ish-veh, heh didn't eku ne' tra' heh gla-tor ik au ovsoh itwhat did au tor? Au kwon-hau-ov ovsoh wuh vath vel. S'pose au tu'ash ish-veh mouthwhat yi? Kuv au didn't ikap-tor ish-veh abru powerful sahris au'd pak-tor wuh ti kanok wak. Ik's wuh ves t' wuh bug henry vesh'; heh kuv etek'd wuh had ish-veh bi' 'stead t' etwel sa-te'kru au'd wuh fooled ik kahr wuh tuh weh-rasahkos do ourn ovsoh. I ri tor leralmin ik ourn nam-tor lambs, fai'ei au ain't, lu sarlah du gas'rak ne' tor wuh samu kla-min; tonk'peh au ain't nothing tor ik hinek ram, anyway. Ek' i leralmin nam-tor, sa-te'kru nam-tor sa-te'kru, heh du prah tor tor allowances. Nem-tor au ek' pa', au're wuh mighty ornery lot. Ish-veh's wuh yut au're ashenau." "tonk'peh dis veh tor fnish-tor ni spo' de shashol, huck." "muhl, au ek' tor, jim. Etek mokuhlek't gol'nev wuh yut wuh sa-te'kru fnish-tor; vesht-var ri tor var-tor rai yut." "i' de duke, au's wuh tolerble kesik sasu svi' ein yut." "ha, wuh duke's natya. Tonk'peh ri maut natya. Nash-veh's wuh middling lerash lot na' wuh duke. Lu au's mon-tor, tra' ain't rai be'-sighted sasu kupi var-tor ish-veh s' wuh sa-te'kru." "muhl, anyways, i doan' hanker na' rai mo' un um, huck. Dese nam-tor ek' i pi-maat stan'." "ish-veh's wuh yut i olau, nuh', jim. Tonk'peh etek've prah au fi' etwel el'ru, heh etek prah tor vokau ra au nam-tor, heh tor allowances. Sometimes i istaya etek kupi zhu-tor t' wuh shasol ik's s' sa-te'kru." ra vesh' wuh nam-tor-tor tor var-tor jim aifa vikau't yeht sa-te'kru heh dukes? Ish-veh wouldn't wuh ovsoh rai rom; heh, isha, ish-veh vesh' aishan u' i leralmin-tor: du couldn't var-tor au s' wuh yeht ves. I went tor yuk, heh jim didn't vutau me lu ish-veh vesh' t'nash-veh da-tor. Au k'ashiv ovsoh ik. Lu i waked abru aishan na' gad-keshtan, au vesh' sitting tra' k' ish-veh patam ne' betwixt ish-veh mal-nef, moaning heh mourning tor himself. I didn't nem-tor beglanau il kal-tor fi'. I knowed ra ish-veh vesh' pa'. Au vesh' thinking pa' ish-veh ko-telsu heh ish-veh kanu, maf abru yonder, heh au vesh' neik heh homesick; fai'ei au hadn't ek'wak vesh' maf s' ha-kel fa' svi' ish-veh ha'kiv; heh i tor dva-tor au tun-tor aishan u' mau na' ish-veh sutra u' wan-kur sular-ves tor na' ish-veh'n. Ish-veh ri tor seem malatik, tonk'peh i reckon ish-veh's ni. Au vesh' k'ashiv moaning heh mourning ik yut mu-yor, lu au judged i vesh' asleep, heh taran, "po' pi' 'lizabeth! Po' pi' johnny! Ish-veh's mighty lerash; i spec' i ain't ek'wak gwyne tor gla-tor du rai mo', rai mo'!" au vesh' wuh mighty rom nigger, jim vesh'. Tonk'peh nash wak i somehow prah tor talking tor ish-veh pa' ish-veh ko-telsu heh nu'ri ones; heh k'-heh-k' au leralmin-tor: "ra tor me olau ni rasahkos dis wak 'uz bekase i zhu-tor sumpn abru' yonder fi' de kutra spo' wuh whack, er wuh slam, du' ago, en ish-veh t'nash-veh me er de wak i skasau t'nash-veh pi' 'lizabeth ni ornery. She vikau't fi''y 'bout fo' tevun ole, en she k'hy de sk'yarlet tau, en had wuh powful rough spell; tonk'peh she prah muhl, en veh gad she vesh' wuh-stannin' aroun', en i leralmin-tor tor ish-veh, i leralmin-tor: "'shet de tor'.' "she worla ovsoh ish-veh; jis' lam-tor dah, kiner smilin' abru na' me. Ish-veh tor me mad; en i leralmin-tor agin, mighty ral, i leralmin-tor: "'doan' du zhu-tor me?shet de tor'!' "she jis lam-tor de ka yut, kiner smilin' abru. I vesh' wuh-bilin'! I leralmin-tor: "'i ti i tor du t'nash-veh!' "en wid dat i zaprah' ish-veh wuh slap vla de patam dat sont ish-veh wuh-sprawlin'. Den i went vi' de yuther tvi-shal, en 'uz hal-tor 'bout lehkuh minutes; en lu sarlah nash-veh pla' dah vesh' dat tor' wuh-stannin' tu'ash yit, en dat chile stannin' mos' gas'rak svi' ish-veh, wuh-lookin' ne' heh mournin', en de bezhun-masu runnin' ne'. T'nash-veh, tonk'peh i wuz mad! I vesh' wuh-gwyne na' de chile, tonk'peh jis' denit vesh' wuh tor' dat tu'ash innerdsjis' den, 'wu sarlah de salan en slam ish-veh tor, behine de chile, ker-blam!en t'nash-veh lan', de chile worla dvun'! T'nash-veh breff mos' spen-tor sik me; en i olau sosoi doan' fai-tor uf i olau. I crope si', ek' wuh-tremblin', en crope aroun' en tu'ash de tor' hagik en vohris, en poke t'nash-veh patam svi' behine de chile, sof' en fam dvun, en ek' uv wuh sudden i leralmin-tor pow! Jis' u' ral u' i kupi saul. She worla budge! Oh, huck, i bust si' wuh-cryin' en runem ish-veh abru svi' t'nash-veh kar, en leralmin, 'oh, de po' pi' vel! De s'haile oekon amighty fogive po' ole jim, kaze au worla gwyne tor fogive hisself u' wu's au ha-tor!' oh, she vesh' plumb deef en dumb, huck, plumb deef en dumben i'd ben wuh-skasau'n ish-veh ni!" chapter xxiv. Thurai gad, na' mu-yor, etek laid abru ne' wuh pi' willow tow-patam si' svi' wuh svitan, wilat tra' vesh' wuh pi'kahr fi' tik vla t' wuh pilash, heh wuh duke heh wuh sa-te'kru palikau tor ti si' wuh dotor na' working au kahr. Jim au stariben tor wuh duke, heh leralmin-tor au rok-tor ish-veh wouldn't nem-tor tonk'peh wuh zamu wadan, fai'ei ish-veh prah mighty ras heh tiresome tor ish-veh lu au had tor ti ek' gad svi' wuh wigwam tied k' wuh man-elakh. Gla-tor du, lu etek losrak ish-veh ek' sa'awek etek had tor tie ish-veh, fai'ei kuv anybody pavesh-tor fi' tor ish-veh ek' k' himself heh ri tied ish-veh wouldn't glazhau mau spo' au vesh' wuh runaway nigger, du fai-tor. Ni wuh duke leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' ves t' lerash ki' tor ti roped ek' gad, heh au'd cipher si' ein yut tor prah pa' ish-veh. Au vesh' uncommon ugelik, wuh duke vesh', heh au ak kwul-tor ish-veh. Au sai-vel-tor jim abru svi' sa-te'kru lear's outfitit vesh' wuh wu curtain-calico gown, heh wuh wan-kur jarel-isachya wig heh whiskers; heh yi au nem-tor ish-veh theater kras heh kras-tor jim's limuk heh el'ru heh kaluk heh talu ek' abru' wuh tevik, pasik, huhtik pla-kur, spo' wuh sasu ik's vesh' drownded naukuh gad. Tenah kuv au vikau't wuh horriblest looking outrage i ek'wak gla-tor. Yi wuh duke nem-tor heh kitau si' wuh glat fi' wuh shingle ni: has-bosh arabbut harmless lu ri s' ish-veh patam. Heh au nailed ik shingle tor wuh lath, heh lam-tor wuh lath abru kehkuh il kaukuh ash'ya svi' khom t' wuh wigwam. Jim vesh' satisfied. Au leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh glan weh-rom do lying tied wuh couple t' tevun kanok gad, heh trembling ek' abru' kanok wak tra' vesh' wuh ralash. Wuh duke var-tor ish-veh tor tor himself elik heh hagik, heh kuv anybody ek'wak sarlah meddling pa', au bolau spen-tor s' wuh wigwam, heh lesh fi' wuh pi', heh zaprah wuh vlut il dahkuh spo' wuh kwai beast, heh au reckoned au would ta'hal si' heh trasha ish-veh sa'awek. If vesh' ralash hiyet judgment; tonk'peh du nem-tor wuh bov sasu, heh au wouldn't bek-tor na' ish-veh tor vlut. Po, au didn't goh glazhau spo' au vesh' tevik, au glazhau considerable weht do ik. Aifa rapscallions aitlu tor ar'kadan wuh nonesuch va'ashiv, fai'ei tra' vesh' ni mau donku svi' ish-veh, tonk'peh au judged ish-veh wouldn't nam-tor safe, fai'ei sos'eh wuh ro'fori lau wuh ar'kada bi' ne' k' nash wak. Au couldn't kwul rai ar'tu ik suited exactly; ni na' kim-shah wuh duke leralmin-tor au reckoned au'd ti ska' heh ar'kadan ish-veh shi'nahp wuh wadan il dahkuh heh gla-tor kuv au couldn't shitau abru vel fi' wuh arkansaw pi'kahr; heh wuh sa-te'kru au kal-tor au would eku abru' tor t'vath pi'kahr rik' sovek dotor, tonk'peh aishan sahrafel svi' providence tor ras-tukh ish-veh wuh profitable waymeaning wuh e'shua, i reckon. Etek had ek' bought mahr-kel sai-vel wilat etek pehkau kim-shah; heh i' wuh sa-te'kru shitau ish-veh'n fi', heh au var-tor me tor shitau t'nash-veh fi'. I ovsoh ish-veh, veling. Wuh sa-te'kru's duds vesh' ek' nesh-kur, heh au did glazhau yeht puv-tor heh starchy. I worla knowed uf sai-vel kupi rubah wuh ak'shem fa'. Po, fa', au glazhau spo' wuh orneriest hinek tres ik ek'wak vesh'; tonk'peh i', lu au'd nem-tor ska' ish-veh uzh wan-kur beaver heh tor wuh kes-wun heh tor wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut, au glazhau ik grand heh rom heh pious ik du'd leralmin au had lates-tor gas'rak s' wuh ark, heh sos'eh vesh' hinek leviticus himself. Jim pu-tor abru wuh canoe, heh i prah t'nash-veh paddle pok. Tra' vesh' wuh suk' steamboat laying na' wuh gef maf abru ne' wuh sfek, pa' rehkuh mile abru' wuh townbeen tra' wuh couple t' wadan, taking fi' freight. Leralmin-tor wuh sa-te'kru: "seein' uf i'm sai-vel-tor, i reckon sos'eh i weh-rom lasha ne' s' st. Louis il cincinnati, il ein vath suk' shi. Hal-tor na' wuh steamboat, huckleberry; etek'll sarlah ne' tor wuh pi'kahr fi' ish-veh." i didn't ma tor nam-tor ordered dah'wak tor hal-tor heh nem-tor wuh steamboat fau. I zaprah wuh gef wuh ulef wuh mile abru' wuh pi'kahr, heh yi went scooting bi' wuh bluff kutra svi' wuh hagik masu. Takov ak sarlah etek tor wuh nice innocent-looking nu'ri shasol jake setting fi' wuh lap-fek swabbing wuh wadashaya ska' t' ish-veh limuk, na' ish-veh vesh' powerful lamekh igen-va; heh au had wuh couple t' suk' la'y-sa'haf k' ish-veh. "sahr-tor ish-veh han svi' gef, " leralmin-tor wuh sa-te'kru. I ovsoh ish-veh. "wher' du bound na', nu'ri sasu?" "na' wuh steamboat; going tor orleans." "git aboard, " leralmin-tor wuh sa-te'kru. "meskaraya fi' wuh minute, t'nash-veh dvinsu 'll au'p du k' au sa'haf. Spen-tor si' heh au'p wuh gentleman, adolphus"meaning me, gla-tor nash-veh. I ovsoh ni, heh yi etek ek' rehkuh palikau fi' va'ashiv. Wuh nu'ri chap vesh' mighty itar-bosh; leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' dulai ar'kadan toting ish-veh baggage such igen-va. Au ya'akash wuh sa-te'kru wilat au vesh' going, heh wuh sa-te'kru var-tor ish-veh au'd sarlah ne' wuh pilash heh landed na' wuh vath pi'kahr nash asal, heh i' au vesh' going abru wuh zamu mile tor gla-tor wuh hinek t'hy'la fi' wuh uroshal abru tra'. Wuh nu'ri katravahsu leralmin-tor: "lu i wuh'rak gla-tor du i leralmin-tor tor myself, 'ish-veh's mr. Wilks, sure, heh au sarlah mighty be' getting la' svi' wak.' tonk'peh yi i leralmin-tor va'ashiv, 'rai, i reckon ish-veh ain't ish-veh, il else au wouldn't nam-tor paddling abru wuh pilash.' du ain't ish-veh, nam-tor du?" "rai, t'nash-veh ahm's blodgettelexander blodgettreverend elexander blodgett, i s'pose i bolau leralmin, u' i'm veh o' wuh s'haile's ri donku-tor dvinsu. Tonk'peh fam dvun i'm jist u' kup tor nam-tor sorry na' mr. Wilks na' ri arriving svi' wak, ek' wuh ka, kuv au's din-tor sovek-vel k' itwhich i rok au hasn't." "muhl, au ri tor din-tor sovek veltra k' ish-veh, fai'ei au'll prah ik ek' gas'rak; tonk'peh au's din-tor seeing ish-veh sa-kai peter diewhich au mayn't kashek, kling mokuhlek var-tor u' tor thatbut ish-veh sa-kai would wuh mazhiv-kur-tor sovek-vel svi' nash panu tor gla-tor ish-veh fa' au tev-tor; worla variben pa' nothing else ek' aifa rehkuh wehk gad; hadn't gla-tor ish-veh opi' au vesh' sa-kan togetherand hadn't ek'wak gla-tor ish-veh sa-kai william na' allthat's wuh deef heh dumb onewilliam ain't weht do reh-leh il reh-leh-kaukuh. Peter heh george vesh' wuh goh ones ik sasarlah la'; george vesh' wuh telik sa-kai; ish-veh heh ish-veh ko-telsu fi' tev-tor kim-shah tevun. Harvey heh william's wuh goh ones ik's losrak i'; heh, u' i vesh' taran, au haven't prah la' svi' wak." "did anybody satau 'em zhit?" "oh, ha; wuh tevun-krus il dahkuh ago, lu peter vesh' wuh'rak nem-tor; fai'ei peter leralmin-tor yi ik au sorter olau spo' au vikau't going tor prah muhl nash wak. Gla-tor du, au vesh' takov hinek, heh george's g'yirls vesh' nuh' nu'ri tor nam-tor mau apc'koik na' ish-veh, kaula mary jane, wuh yon-kur-headed veh; heh ni au vesh' kinder lonesome po' george heh ish-veh ko-telsu tev-tor, heh didn't seem tor tun mau tor ha-tor. Au danik desperately aitlu tor gla-tor harveyand william, nuh', na' ik matterbecause au vesh' veh t' au ves ik mokuhlek't lesh tor tor wuh dungi. Au losrak wuh nuhm za' na' harvey, heh leralmin-tor au'd var-tor svi' ish-veh wilat ish-veh donku vesh' ip-sut, heh uf au aitlu wuh shom t' wuh veltra dahsau abru ni george's g'yirls would nam-tor ek' rightfor george didn't trasha nothing. Heh ik nuhm vesh' ek' au kupi prah ish-veh tor shitau wuh pen tor." "po tor du reckon harvey ri tor sarlah? Wher' tor au ha-tor?" "oh, au ha-tor svi' englandsheffieldpreaches therehasn't ek'wak vesh' svi' nash shasol. Au hasn't had sovek nuh' mau timeand isha au mightn't wuh prah wuh nuhm na' ek', du fai-tor." "nuh' rasahkos, nuh' rasahkos au couldn't wuh ha-tor tor gla-tor ish-veh sa-kai, ri donku-tor soul. Du going tor orleans, du leralmin?" "ha, tonk'peh ik ain't goh wuh krus t' ish-veh. I'm going svi' wuh hali, thurai gad, na' ryo janeero, wilat t'nash-veh sa-kuk ha-tor." "ish-veh's wuh takov wu halovaya. Tonk'peh ish-veh'll nam-tor lovely; wisht i vesh' wuh-going. Nam-tor mary jane wuh oldest? Uf hinek nam-tor wuh vath?" "mary jane's leh-nau, susan's leh-kau, heh joanna's pa' fourteenthat's wuh veh ik mazhiv-kur-tor herself tor rom ar'kada heh has wuh hare-bru." "ri donku-tor vel! Tor nam-tor losrak sa'awek svi' wuh samu panu ni." "muhl, au kupi nam-tor weh-rasahkos ska'. Hinek peter had t'hylara, heh au ain't going tor kal-tor au sarlah tor rai klau. Tra''s hobson, wuh babtis' preacher; heh deacon lot hovey, heh ben rucker, heh abner shackleford, heh levi kus-vakh, wuh lawyer; heh dr. Robinson, heh ish-veh ko-telsu, heh wuh kir'an bartley, andwell, tra''s wuh lot t' au; tonk'peh aifa nam-tor wuh ones ik peter vesh' thickest k', heh nam-tor-tor tor kitau pa' sometimes, lu au kitau ha-kel; ni harvey 'll fai-tor wilat tor glazhau na' t'hylara lu au prah la'." muhl, wuh hinek sasu went fi' asking deshkau till au aishan fairly emptied ik nu'ri katravahsu. Tenah kuv au didn't inquire pa' kanok-veh heh kanok-vei svi' ik blessed kahr, heh ek' pa' wuh wilkses; heh pa' peter's businesswhich vesh' wuh tanner; heh pa' george'swhich vesh' wuh carpenter; heh pa' harvey'swhich vesh' wuh dissentering minister; heh ni fi', heh ni fi'. Yi au leralmin-tor: "ra did du aitlun tor lates ek' wuh yut abru tor wuh steamboat na'?" "fai'ei she's wuh suk' orleans masu-hali, heh i vesh' afeard she mightn't pehkaya tra'. Lu au're glu au skil-tor't pehkaya na' wuh masu-kov. Wuh cincinnati masu-hali dungi, tonk'peh nash nam-tor wuh st. Louis veh." "vesh' peter wilks muhl ska'?" "oh, ha, takov muhl ska'. Au had kelek heh solektra, heh ish-veh's reckoned au losrak rehkuh il kehkuh thousand svi' cash ip-sut abru som'ers." "lu did du leralmin au tev-tor?" "i didn't leralmin, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' kim-shah mu-yor." "mem-lu til-kum tor-morrow, kesik?" "ha, 'bout wuh svitan t' wuh gad." "muhl, ish-veh's ek' terrible maf; tonk'peh etek've ek' prah tor hal-tor, veh wak il wuh'ashiv. Ni ra etek aitlun tor tor nam-tor tor nam-tor dator; yi etek're ek' gas'rak." "ha, osu, ish-veh's wuh buhfik yut. Ma nam-tor-tor tor kwon-hau-ov leralmin ik." lu etek kwul-tor wuh masu-hali she vesh' pa' ovsoh loading, heh takov ak she prah ska'. Wuh sa-te'kru worla leralmin-tor nothing pa' going aboard, ni i pakik t'nash-veh fau, po' ek'. Lu wuh masu-hali vesh' hal-tor wuh sa-te'kru tor me paddle abru wuh'ashiv mile tor wuh lonesome shi, heh yi au prah ashore heh leralmin-tor: "i' hustle pla', gas'rak ska', heh zaprah wuh duke abru la', heh wuh uzh la'y-sa'haf. Heh kuv au's hal-tor abru' tor t'vath vla, hal-tor abru' tra' heh git ish-veh. Heh var-tor ish-veh tor git himself abru regardless. Shove bi', i'." gla-tor nash-veh ra au vesh' abru tor; tonk'peh i worla leralmin-tor nothing, veling. Lu i zaprah k' wuh duke etek ip-sut wuh canoe, heh yi au eku ne' fi' wuh lap-fek, heh wuh sa-te'kru var-tor ish-veh kanok-vei, aishan spo' wuh nu'ri katravahsu had leralmin-tor itevery kim-shah zhit t' ish-veh. Heh ek' wuh wak au vesh' wuh-doing ish-veh au ar'kada tor variben spo' wuh englishman; heh au ovsoh ish-veh takov muhl, nuh', na' wuh slouch. I mokuhlek't va'amau ish-veh, heh ni i ain't wuh-going tor ar'kadan tor; tonk'peh au really ovsoh ish-veh takov rom. Yi au leralmin-tor: "uf nam-tor du fi' wuh deef heh dumb, bilgewater?" wuh duke leralmin-tor, trasha ish-veh sa'awek na' ik; leralmin-tor au had mavau wuh deef heh dumb person fi' wuh histronic dohn. Ni yi au bek-tor na' wuh steamboat. Pa' wuh svitan t' wuh aru wuh couple t' pi' masu-hali sarlah bi', tonk'peh au didn't sarlah s' pid hiyet abru wuh pilash; tonk'peh na' kim-shah tra' vesh' wuh suk' veh, heh au hailed ish-veh. She satau si' ish-veh yawl, heh etek went aboard, heh she vesh' s' cincinnati; heh lu au afer-tor etek goh aitlu tor hal-tor kehkuh il kaukuh mile au vesh' booming mad, heh mazhiv-kur-tor etek wuh cussing, heh leralmin-tor au wouldn't solektra etek. Tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru vesh' ca'm. Au leralmin-tor: "kuv gentlemen pi-maat afford tor vlitau wuh dollar wuh mile apiece tor nam-tor nem-tor fi' heh shitau ska' svi' wuh yawl, wuh steamboat pi-maat afford tor lesh 'em, mokuhlek't ish-veh?" ni au softened ne' heh leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' ek' gas'rak; heh lu etek prah tor wuh pi'kahr au yawled etek ashore. Pa' dahkuh dozen sasu patreitau ne' lu gla-tor au wuh yawl wuh-coming, heh lu wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor: "pi-maat sovek t' du gentlemen var-tor me wher' mr. Peter wilks ha-tor?" au mazhiv-kur-tor wuh glance na' veh wuh'ashiv, heh nodded ish-veh patam, u' mau u' tor leralmin, "ra d' i var-tor du?" yi veh t' au leralmin-tor, ves t' mos heh gentle: "i'm sorry osu, tonk'peh wuh buhfik etek mokuhlek tor nam-tor tor var-tor du wilat au did ha-tor za-gad khru." sudden u' winking wuh ornery hinek cretur went wuh tor smash, heh tevan-tor abru tehnat wuh sasu, heh shitau ish-veh chin fi' ish-veh tipan, heh maf-tor ne' ish-veh pla', heh leralmin-tor: "alas, alas, etwel ri donku-tor brothergone, heh etek worla prah tor gla-tor ish-veh; oh, ish-veh's nuh', nuh' lerash!" yi au da-tor pa', blubbering, heh tor wuh lot t' idiotic glat tor wuh duke fi' ish-veh el'ru, heh tenah kuv au didn't eku wuh la'y-sa'haf heh bust si' wuh-maf-tor. Kuv au vikau't wuh beatenest lot, au dahkuh frauds, ik ek'wak i kwul-tor. Muhl, wuh sasu hoknau pa' heh sympathized k' au, heh leralmin-tor ek' wihfelau t' ves vel tor au, heh lesh ish-veh la'y-sa'haf abru wuh kunel na' au, heh kal-tor au galat fi' au heh maf, heh var-tor wuh sa-te'kru ek' pa' ish-veh sa-kai's kim-shah moments, heh wuh sa-te'kru au var-tor ish-veh ek' abru' va'ashiv fi' ish-veh el'ru tor wuh duke, heh fi' t' au nem-tor fi' pa' ik tevik tanner spo' au'd pakik wuh leh-dah disciples. Muhl, kuv ek'wak i kwul-tor sovek-vel spo' ish-veh, i'm wuh nigger. Ish-veh vesh' hiyet tor tor wuh ak'shem kafusik t' wuh komihn ne-koshtri. Chapter xxv. Wuh ro'fori vesh' ek' abru' kahr svi' dahkuh minutes, heh du kupi gla-tor wuh sutra tearing ne' fi' wuh sahr-tor s' kanok if yut, ein t' au putting fi' ish-veh tor-pal u' sarlah au. Takov ak etek vesh' svi' wuh svitan t' wuh patreitan, heh wuh ralash t' wuh tramping vesh' spo' wuh ask'ersu march. Wuh krani heh dooryards vesh' bosh; heh kanok minute somebody would leralmin, abru' wuh foshek: "nam-tor ish-veh au?" heh somebody sahr-tor bi' k' wuh gang would kilko-srashiv pla' heh leralmin: "du sihaya ish-veh nam-tor." lu etek prah tor wuh kelek wuh yut svi' khom t' ish-veh vesh' sa'haf-tor, heh wuh rehkuh ko-kan vesh' standing svi' wuh svep. Mary jane vesh' yon-kur-headed, tonk'peh ik ri tor tor rai natyan, she vesh' danik awful vaksurik, heh ish-veh limuk heh ish-veh bezhun vesh' ek' lit abru spo' glory, she vesh' ni glad ish-veh sa-kuk vesh' sarlah. Wuh sa-te'kru au sak-tor ish-veh kar, heh mary jane she spen-tor na' au, heh wuh hare-bru spen-tor na' wuh duke, heh tra' au had ish-veh! Kanok-veh danik, leastways kosu, maf-tor na' mak tor gla-tor au ragel-tor va'ashiv na' kim-shah heh ma such rom wak. Yi wuh sa-te'kru au hunched wuh duke privatei gla-tor ish-veh tor itand yi au glazhau pa' heh gla-tor wuh tevikeh-natuhn, abru' svi' wuh teruk fi' dahkuh ku-san; ni yi ish-veh heh wuh duke, k' wuh el'ru mes' tik vath's tipan, heh t'vath el'ru tor ish-veh bezhun, lates-tor vohris heh solemn abru' tra', kanok-veh dropping pla' tor mazhiv-kur-tor au tvi-shal, heh ek' wuh variben heh ralash stopping, sutra taran "sh!" heh ek' wuh sasu taking ish-veh taik ska' heh tevan-tor ish-veh patam, ni du kupi wuh puzhu-tor wuh pin tevan. Heh lu au prah tra' au keh'sei abru' heh glazhau svi' wuh tevikeh-natuhn, heh nem-tor veh glan, heh yi au bust si' wuh-maf-tor ni du kupi wuh puzhu-tor au tor orleans, danik; heh yi au shitau ish-veh kar pa' tik vath's talu, heh geldau ish-veh chins abru' tik vath's tipan; heh yi na' rehkuh minutes, il sos'eh kehkuh, i worla gla-tor dahkuh sasu tasaya wuh yut au ovsoh. Heh, kashek du, kanok-veh vesh' doing wuh ka; heh wuh shi vesh' ik damp i worla gla-tor sovek-vel spo' ish-veh. Yi veh t' au prah fi' veh vla t' wuh tevikeh-natuhn, heh t'vath fi' t'vath vla, heh au kneeled ne' heh shom-tor ish-veh fa-patam fi' wuh tevikeh-natuhn, heh kal-tor fi' tor pray ek' tor themselves. Muhl, lu ish-veh sarlah tor ik ish-veh ar'kada wuh patreitan spo' du worla gla-tor sovek-vel spo' ish-veh, heh kanok-veh shau ne' heh went tor sobbing gas'rak si' loudthe ri donku-tor ko-kan, nuh'; heh kanok kosu, nearly, went abru tor wuh ko-kan, rik' taran wuh zhit, heh shok-tor au, solemn, fi' wuh fa-patam, heh yi shitau ish-veh el'ru fi' ish-veh patam, heh glazhau abru na' wuh igen, k' wuh bezhun-masu sahran ne', heh yi busted si' heh went ska' sobbing heh swabbing, heh mazhiv-kur-tor wuh thurai kosu wuh gluvaya. I worla gla-tor sovek-vel ni disgusting. Muhl, k'-heh-k' wuh sa-te'kru au prah abru heh sarlah fa'rak wuh pi', heh ar'kada himself abru heh slobbers si' wuh starun, ek' bosh t' bezhun-masu heh flapdoodle pa' its hasu wuh sival trial na' ish-veh heh ish-veh ri donku-tor sa-kai tor pak-tor wuh diseased, heh tor din-tor seeing diseased alive po' wuh wu halovaya t' kehkuh thousand mile, tonk'peh ish-veh's wuh trial ik's sweetened heh sanctified tor etek k' nash tal-kam sympathy heh aifa vai bezhun-masu, heh ni au itaren au s' ish-veh khaf-spol heh s' ish-veh sa-kai's khaf-spol, fai'ei s' ish-veh ru'lut au mokuhlek't, zhit hasu nuh' kobat heh samu, heh ek' ik ves t' nehaya heh slush, till ish-veh vesh' aishan sickening; heh yi au blubbers si' wuh pious goody-goody amen, heh da-tor himself thal heh hal-tor tor maf-tor nunau tor bust. Heh wuh minute wuh zhit vesh' s' ish-veh ru'lut somebody abru' svi' wuh patreitan kwul-tor abru wuh doxolojer, heh kanok-veh hau svi' k' ek' ish-veh lau, heh ish-veh aishan warmed du abru heh tor du olau u' rom u' church letting si'. Ralash-tanaf nam-tor wuh rom vel; heh po' ek' ik soul-butter heh hogwash i worla gla-tor ish-veh freshen abru vel ni, heh ralash ni trau heh bully. Yi wuh sa-te'kru palikau tor ar'kadan ish-veh ahs va'ashiv, heh leralmin-tor uf ish-veh heh ish-veh ko-bath would nam-tor glad kuv wuh zamu t' wuh nen principal t'hylara t' wuh skan would nem-tor mu'yor-yem la' k' au nash khru, heh gol'nev eku abru k' wuh vitush t' wuh diseased; heh leralmin-tor kuv ish-veh ri donku-tor sa-kai laying yonder kupi stariben au fai-tor vi au would ahm, na' au vesh' ahm ik vesh' maut tal-kam tor ish-veh, heh mentioned k'ashiv svi' ish-veh nuhm; heh ni au dungi ahm wuh ka, tor wit, u' zahal-tor, vizz: rev. Mr. Hobson, heh deacon lot hovey, heh mr. Ben rucker, heh abner shackleford, heh levi kus-vakh, heh dr. Robinson, heh ish-veh ko-telsu, heh wuh kir'an bartley. Rev. Hobson heh dr. Robinson vesh' ne' tor wuh shaht t' wuh kahr wuh-hunting togetherthat nam-tor, i tvai wuh hassu vesh' shipping wuh has-bosh sasu tor t'vath panu, heh wuh preacher vesh' pinting ish-veh gas'rak. Lawyer kus-vakh vesh' maf abru tor louisville fi' business. Tonk'peh wuh shom vesh' fi' el'ru, heh ni au ek' sarlah heh hutau el'ru k' wuh sa-te'kru heh itaren ish-veh heh variben tor ish-veh; heh yi au hutau el'ru k' wuh duke heh didn't leralmin nothing, tonk'peh aishan potau wuh-smiling heh bobbing ish-veh patam spo' wuh passel t' sapheads whilst au tor ek' wihfelau t' glat k' ish-veh el'ru heh leralmin-tor "goo-googoo-goo-goo" ek' wuh wak, spo' wuh kan-bu ik mokuhlek't variben. Ni wuh sa-te'kru au blattered bi', heh khartau tor inquire pa' takov mau kanok-veh heh dog svi' kahr, k' ish-veh ahm, heh mentioned ek' wihfelau t' pi' vel ik pavesh-tor veh wak il wuh'ashiv svi' wuh kahr, il tor george's skan, il tor peter. Heh au kwon-hau-ov kal-tor fi' ik peter kitau ish-veh wuh vel; tonk'peh ik vesh' wuh ti: au prah kanok blessed veh t' au s' ik nu'ri flathead ik etek canoed abru tor wuh steamboat. Yi mary jane she zaprah wuh nuhm ish-veh sa-mekh losrak za', heh wuh sa-te'kru au telv-tor ish-veh si' ral heh maf-tor abru' ish-veh. Ish-veh mazhiv-kur-tor wuh kelek-kelek heh rehkuh thousand dollars, pi-maat-tukh, tor wuh ko-kan; heh ish-veh mazhiv-kur-tor wuh tanyard (if vesh' doing wuh rom business), bi' k' ein vath kelek heh solektra (don pa' stehkuh thousand), heh rehkuh thousand dollars svi' pi-maat-tukh tor harvey heh william, heh var-tor wilat wuh shehkuh thousand cash vesh' ip-sut ne' cellar. Ni aifa dahkuh frauds leralmin-tor au'd hal-tor heh zaprah ish-veh abru, heh ma kanok-vei keh-vla heh abru'-dohn; heh var-tor me tor sarlah k' wuh ha'fek. Etek ikap-tor wuh cellar svep za' etek, heh lu au afer-tor wuh sa'haf au spilt ish-veh si' fi' wuh lan-tol, heh ish-veh vesh' wuh lovely glan, ek' au yaller-sa-kan. T'nash-veh, wuh yut wuh sa-te'kru's bezhun did min-tor! Au slaps wuh duke fi' wuh tipan heh leralmin-tor: "oh, nash ain't bully il noth'n! Oh, rai, i reckon ri! Po, bilji, ish-veh kuhsh-tor wuh nonesuch, ri tor ish-veh?" wuh duke kal-tor ish-veh did. Au pawed wuh yaller-sa-kan, heh sifted au k'fai ish-veh ozh heh kal-tor au jingle ne' fi' wuh lan-tol; heh wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor: "ish-veh ain't rai nam-tor-tor talkin'; bein' sa-kai tor wuh don-ka tevik sasu heh representatives t' furrin heirs ik's prah losrak nam-tor wuh zehl na' du heh me, smashau-shal t'masu-hali. Thish yer sarlah t' sahrafel'n tor providence. Ish-veh's wuh buhfik yut, svi' wuh wu sahr-tor. I've ar'kada 'em ek', heh ther' ain't rai weh-rom yut." danik kanok-veh would wuh vesh' satisfied k' wuh tuh, heh nem-tor ish-veh fi' sahrafel; tonk'peh rai, au bolau tum-tor ish-veh. Ni au tum-tor ish-veh, heh ish-veh sasarlah kehkuh hundred heh leh-kau dollars pen. Leralmin-tor wuh sa-te'kru: "dern ish-veh, i wonder ra au ovsoh k' ik kehkuh hundred heh leh-kau dollars?" au worried abru' ik awhile, heh ransacked ek' pa' na' ish-veh. Yi wuh duke leralmin-tor: "muhl, au vesh' wuh takov has-bosh sasu, heh kesik au tor wuh mistakei reckon ik's wuh yut t' ish-veh. Wuh buhfik yut's tor kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor, heh potau fam dvun pa' ish-veh. Etek mokuhlek spare ish-veh." "oh, shucks, ha, etek mokuhlek spare ish-veh. I ri tor k'yer noth'n 'bout thatit's wuh tum-tor i'm thinkin' pa'. Etek aitlun tor nam-tor awful keh-vla heh tu'ash heh abru'-dohn la', du fai-tor. Etek aitlun tor lug nash h-yer donku abru kaiden heh tum-tor ish-veh fa' everybodythen ther' ain't noth'n suspicious. Tonk'peh lu wuh tevik sasu leralmin-tor ther's shehkuh thous'n dollars, du fai-tor, etek ri tor aitlun tor" "meskaraya fi', " leralmin-tor wuh duke. "le's tor abru wuh deffisit, " heh au palikau tor haul si' yaller-sa-kan s' ish-veh abru'lik. "ish-veh's wuh danik amaz'n' rom idea, dukeyou ma prah wuh rattlin' clever patam fi' du, " leralmin-tor wuh sa-te'kru. "blest kuv wuh hinek nonesuch ain't wuh heppin' etek si' agin, " heh au palikau tor haul si' yaller-jackets heh tuh au abru. Ish-veh danik busted au, tonk'peh au tor abru wuh shehkuh thousand sok'i heh pa'shik. "leralmin, " leralmin-tor wuh duke, "i prah wuh'ashiv idea. Le's hal-tor abru kaiden heh tum-tor nash donku, heh yi nem-tor heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor wuh ko-kan." "rom solektra, duke, lemme teraya-martaya du! Ish-veh's wuh danik dazzling idea 'na' ek'wak wuh sasu kwul-tor. Du ma cert'nly prah wuh danik astonishin' patam i ek'wak gla-tor. Oh, nash nam-tor wuh feihan sayutau, ther' ain't rai lafosh 'bout ish-veh. Kal-tor 'em zaprah bi' ish-veh suspicions i' kuv au aitlun tothis'll ti 'em si'." lu etek prah abru-kaiden kanok-veh gethered pa' wuh pasu, heh wuh sa-te'kru au tum-tor ish-veh heh tuh-tor ish-veh abru, rehkuh hundred dollars svi' wuh piletwenty sohkik pi' tuh. Kanok-veh glazhau k'avon na' ish-veh, heh licked ish-veh chops. Yi au dref-tor ish-veh vi' wuh sa'haf va'ashiv, heh gla-tor nash-veh wuh sa-te'kru palikau tor puv-tor himself abru na' wuh'ashiv starun. Au leralmin-tor: "t'hylara ek', t'nash-veh ri donku-tor sa-kai ik ti yonder has ovsoh generous k' au ik's losrak za' svi' wuh vale t' sorrers. Au has ovsoh generous k' aifa yer ri donku-tor pi' lambs ik au ashau heh rau-tor, heh ik's losrak fatherless heh motherless. Ha, heh etek ik knowed ish-veh fai-tor ik au would wuh ovsoh weht generous k' 'em kuv au hadn't ben afeard o' woundin' ish-veh tal-kam william heh me. I', wouldn't au? Ther' ain't rai deshker 'bout ish-veh svi' t'nash-veh kashek. Muhl, yi, ra ves o' sa-kai would ish-veh nam-tor ik 'd lamok svi' ish-veh yut na' sech wuh wak? Heh ra ves o' sa-kuk would ish-veh nam-tor ik 'd robyes, robsech ri donku-tor slor lambs u' aifa 'na' au ashau ni na' sech wuh wak? Kuv i fai-tor williamand i nah-tor i dohewell, i'll jest ya'akash ish-veh." au da-tor pa' heh palikau tor tor wuh lot t' glat tor wuh duke k' ish-veh el'ru, heh wuh duke au glazhau na' ish-veh stupid heh duf-headed wuh du'; yi ek' t' wuh sudden au seems tor kum ish-veh meaning, heh spen-tor na' wuh sa-te'kru, goo-gooing k' ek' ish-veh lau na' mak, heh teraya-martaya ish-veh pa' leh-kau wak fa' au kal-tor abru. Yi wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor, "i knowed ish-veh; i reckon ik'll convince anybody wuh yut au olau pa' ish-veh. La', mary jane, susan, joanner, nem-tor wuh moneytake ish-veh ek'. Ish-veh's wuh mazhiv-kur t' ish-veh ik ti yonder, samu tonk'peh joyful." mary jane she went na' ish-veh, susan heh wuh hare-bru went na' wuh duke, heh yi such wuh'ashiv hugging heh kissing i worla gla-tor wi. Heh kanok-veh crowded abru k' wuh bezhun-masu svi' ish-veh bezhun, heh danik hutau wuh el'ru ska' t' au frauds, taran ek' wuh wak: "du tal-kam rom souls!uf lovely!uf kupi du!" muhl, yi, takov ak ek' el'ru prah tor talking pa' wuh diseased va'ashiv, heh uf rom au vesh', heh ra wuh pak au vesh', heh ek' ik; heh fa' wu wuh suk' shek-tukh-jawed sasu ar'kada himself svi' tra' s' s'udish, heh lam-tor wuh-listening heh looking, heh ri taran sovek-vel; heh kling taran sovek-vel tor ish-veh either, fai'ei wuh sa-te'kru vesh' talking heh au vesh' ek' toranik listening. Wuh sa-te'kru vesh' sayingin wuh svitan t' vel au'd palikau svi' fi' "au bein' partickler t'hylara o' wuh diseased. Ik's po au're invited la' nash evenin'; tonk'peh fa-gad etek aitlun ek' tor comeeverybody; na' au respected kanok-veh, au tishau kanok-veh, heh ni ish-veh's fitten ik ish-veh mem-lu til-kum orgies sh'd nam-tor tsuri." heh ni au went wuh-mooning fi' heh fi', liking tor zhu-tor himself variben, heh kanok pi' du' au zaprah svi' ish-veh mem-lu til-kum orgies va'ashiv, till wuh duke au couldn't lamok ish-veh rai weht; ni au kitau fi' wuh pi' moguhsh t' dun, "obsequies, du hinek duhsu, " heh hesha ish-veh abru, heh hal-tor tor goo-gooing heh reaching ish-veh abru' sutra's patam tor ish-veh. Wuh sa-te'kru au telv-tor ish-veh heh shitau ish-veh svi' ish-veh abru'lik, heh leralmin-tor: "ri donku-tor william, afflicted u' au nam-tor, ish-veh khaf-spol's aluz gas'rak. Ya'akash me tor invite kanok-veh tor sarlah tor wuh funeralwants me tor tor 'em ek' welcome. Tonk'peh au needn't wuh worriedit vesh' jest ra i vesh' na'." yi au pris-tor bi' va'ashiv, perfectly ca'm, heh hal-tor tor dropping svi' ish-veh mem-lu til-kum orgies va'ashiv kanok i' heh yi, aishan spo' au ovsoh fa'. Heh lu au ovsoh ish-veh wuh wuh wak au leralmin-tor: "i leralmin orgies, ri fai'ei ish-veh's wuh tsuri zhil, fai'ei ish-veh ain'tobsequies bein' wuh tsuri termbut fai'ei orgies nam-tor wuh gas'rak zhil. Ish-veh's wuh zhit ik's tor abru si''n wuh greek orgo, s'udish, tu'ash, abroad; heh wuh hebrew jeesum, tor kastik, wein abru; hence inter. Ni, gla-tor du, mem-lu til-kum orgies nam-tor wuh tu'ash er tsuri mem-lu til-kum." au vesh' wuh rasahkos i ek'wak kwul-tor. Muhl, wuh shek-tukh-jawed sasu au abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor gas'rak svi' ish-veh limuk. Kanok-veh vesh' kolaya. I" "potau ish-veh el'ru ska' t' me!" leralmin-tor wuh hassu. "du variben spo' wuh englishman, ri tor du? Ish-veh's wuh rasahkos imitation i ek'wak puzhu-tor. Du peter wilks's sa-kai! Chapter xxvi. Muhl, lu au vesh' ek' hal-tor wuh sa-te'kru au ya'akash mary jane uf au vesh' ska' na' spare tvi-shal, heh she leralmin-tor she had veh spare tvi-shal, if would tor na' sa-kuk william, heh she'd mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh sha' tvi-shal tor sa-kuk harvey, if vesh' wuh pi' bigger, heh she would da-tor vi' wuh tvi-shal k' ish-veh ko-kai heh yuk fi' wuh cot; heh abru kamu-tvi-shal vesh' wuh pi' cubby, k' wuh pallet svi' ish-veh. Wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor wuh cubby would tor na' ish-veh valleymeaning me. Ni mary jane nem-tor etek abru, heh she gluvau au ish-veh tvi-shal, if vesh' eiktra tonk'peh nice. She leralmin-tor she'd ma ish-veh pelal heh wuh lot t' vath pash-tor nem-tor s' ish-veh tvi-shal kuv au vesh' svi' sa-kuk harvey's yut, tonk'peh au leralmin-tor au vikau't. Wuh pelal vesh' geldau bi' wuh temok, heh fa' au vesh' wuh curtain tor s' calico ik geldau ne' tor wuh lan-tol. Wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' ek' wuh weht homely heh weht pleasanter na' aifa fixings, heh ni ri tor ertau au. Wuh duke's tvi-shal vesh' takov pi', tonk'peh plenty rom hiyet, heh ni vesh' t'nash-veh cubby. Ik mu-yor au had wuh suk' mu'yor-yem, heh ek' au sasu heh kosu vesh' tra', heh i lam-tor za' wuh sa-te'kru heh wuh duke's ku-san heh bek-tor fi' au, heh wuh niggers bek-tor fi' wuh shom. Mary jane she eku na' wuh patam t' wuh pasu, k' susan alongside t' ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor uf rasahkos wuh kreyla vesh', heh uf tvai wuh korsau vesh', heh uf ornery heh dulai wuh pupol-tor kahm wasand ek' ik ves t' nehaya, wuh yut kosu kwon-hau-ov tor na' tor nekwitaya si' compliments; heh wuh sutra ek' knowed kanok-vei vesh' tiptop, heh leralmin-tor sosaid "uf tor du prah kreyla tor khav-kur ni nice?" heh "wilat, na' wuh solektra's sake, did du prah aifa amaz'n sazh?" heh ek' ik ves t' humbug talky-variben, aishan wuh yut sutra kwon-hau-ov tor na' wuh mu'yor-yem, du fai-tor. Heh lu ish-veh vesh' ek' ovsoh me heh wuh hare-bru had mu'yor-yem svi' wuh af'tum ska' t' wuh leavings, whilst wuh vath vesh' helping wuh niggers sok'i abru wuh vel. Wuh hare-bru she prah tor pumping me pa' england, heh blest kuv i didn't nah-tor wuh le-suma vesh' getting mighty wonil sometimes. She leralmin-tor: "did du ek'wak gla-tor wuh sa-te'kru?" "vi? William fourth? Muhl, i sihaya i havehe hal-tor tor etwel church." i knowed au vesh' tevik tevun ago, tonk'peh i worla kal-tor fi'. Au lau var-tor vi var-tor ish-veh; yi wuh sa-te'kru heh wuh duke would tor ish-veh lamekh na' me. Dungau i hal-tor, awek, heh var-tor mary jane? Noi dasn't tor ish-veh. Specially, seeing etek prah ish-veh ni easygiven pla' tor etek, flung na' etwel patam, u' du lau leralmin, lu t' rivak etek kal-tor ki' tor vazgau ish-veh pla'. I'm na' knocking ska' heh ha'gelan si'." ik tor me olau takov rasahkos. Pa' wuh wadan il dahkuh ago ish-veh would wuh vesh' wuh pi' natya, tonk'peh i' ish-veh tor me olau rasahkos heh disappointed, wuh sa-te'kru tres-tor si' heh leralmin-tor: "ra! Heh ri makau si' wuh shom o' wuh veltra? March ska' spo' wuh passel t' duhsu heh trasha ohkuh il naukuh thous'n' dollars' don o' veltra layin' pa' jest sufferin' tor nam-tor scooped svi'?heh ek' rom, salable tukh, nuh'." wuh duke au grumbled; leralmin-tor wuh sa'haf t' pi-maat-tukh vesh' hiyet, heh au didn't aitlun tor hal-tor rai deeperdidn't aitlun tor rob wuh lot t' orphans t' kanok-vei au had. "po, uf du variben!" leralmin-tor wuh sa-te'kru. "etek sha'n't rob 'em t' nothing na' ek' tonk'peh jest nash donku. Wuh sutra ik buys wuh veltra nam-tor wuh suff'rers; fai'ei u' ak 's ish-veh's afer-tor si' 'na' etek didn't sha' itwhich skil-tor't nam-tor wu po' etek've slidthe sale skil-tor't nam-tor valid, heh ish-veh'll ek' hal-tor pla' tor wuh estate. Aifa yer orphans 'll git ish-veh kelek pla' agin, heh ik's hiyet na' au; au're nu'ri heh spry, heh k'n hagik pinkau wuh livin'. Au ain't wuh-goin tor dash. Po, jest thinkthere's thous'n's heh thous'n's ik ain't nigh ni muhl ska'. Kudau du, au ain't prah noth'n' tor complain t'." muhl, wuh sa-te'kru au variben ish-veh glan-fam; ni na' kim-shah au mazhiv-kur-tor svi', heh leralmin-tor ek' gas'rak, tonk'peh leralmin-tor au pudva-tor ish-veh vesh' tenah duh'es tor stay, heh ik hassu hanging abru' au. Tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor: "cuss wuh hassu! Ra tor etek k'yer na' ish-veh? Hain't etek prah ek' wuh duhsu svi' kahr fi' etwel vla? Heh ain't ik wuh suk' hiyet majority svi' sovek kahr?" ni au prah pok tor hal-tor ne' kaiden va'ashiv. Wuh duke leralmin-tor: "i ri tor nah-tor etek shitau ik donku svi' wuh rom shi." ik cheered me abru. I'd palikau tor nah-tor i vikau't going tor prah wuh hint t' rai ves tor gol'nev me. Wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor: "po?" "fai'ei mary jane 'll nam-tor svi' mourning s' nash si'; heh wuh'rak du fai-tor wuh nigger ik tor abru wuh tvi-shal dungi prah wuh zek tor natuhn aifa duds abru heh shitau 'em maf; heh tor du reckon wuh nigger mokuhlek sahr-tor mes' donku heh ri yahv-tor ein t' ish-veh?" "ish-veh patam's volik agin, duke, " leralmin-tor wuh sa-te'kru; heh sarlah ish-veh wuh-fumbling ne' wuh curtain dahkuh il rehkuh ash'ya s' wilat i vesh'. I terpau wufik tor wuh temok heh potau mighty fam dvun, hi quivery; heh i wondered ra au katravahsu would leralmin tor me kuv au catched me; heh i ar'kada tor nah-tor ra i'd weh-rom tor kuv au did kum me. Tonk'peh wuh sa-te'kru au prah wuh sa'haf fa' i kupi nah-tor weht do pa' wuh ulef wuh nahp, heh au worla suspicioned i vesh' pa'. Au nem-tor heh shoved wuh sa'haf k'fai wuh tres svi' wuh terp tick ik vesh' ne' wuh kan-sar-tak, heh crammed ish-veh svi' wuh ash'ya il dahkuh svi' wuh terp heh leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' ek' gas'rak i', fai'ei wuh nigger goh tor abru wuh kan-sar-tak, heh ri tor da-tor abru' wuh terp tick goh pa' dah'wak wuh tevun, heh ni ish-veh vikau't svi' rai tehvar t' getting vazgau i'. Tonk'peh i knowed weh-rom. I had ish-veh s' tra' fa' au vesh' ulef-yut ne' kaiden. I groped bi' abru tor t'nash-veh cubby, heh ip-sut ish-veh tra' till i kupi prah wuh pavesh tor tor weh-rom. I judged i weh-rom ip-sut ish-veh si' wuh kelek somewheres, fai'ei kuv au din-tor ish-veh au would mazhiv-kur-tor wuh kelek wuh rom ransacking: i knowed ik maut muhl. Yi i da-tor svi', k' t'nash-veh sai-vel ek' fi'; tonk'peh i couldn't wuh hal-tor tor yuk kuv i'd wuh aitlu tor, i vesh' svi' such wuh wadashaya tor prah k'fai k' wuh business. K'-heh-k' i puzhu-tor wuh sa-te'kru heh wuh duke sarlah abru; ni i padukau ska' t'nash-veh pallet heh laid k' t'nash-veh chin na' wuh fik t' t'nash-veh pu'uth, heh bek-tor tor gla-tor kuv sovek-vel vesh' going tor pavesh-tor. Tonk'peh nothing did. Ni i meskarau fi' till ek' wuh tab-ma sounds had quit heh wuh lehkuh-mal ones hadn't palikau wi; heh yi i trel-tor ne' wuh pu'uth. Chapter xxvii. I crept tor ish-veh svep heh shroi; au vesh' snoring. Ni i tiptoed bi', heh prah ne' kaiden ek' gas'rak. Tra' vikau't wuh ralash anywheres. I peeped k'fai wuh treshaya t' wuh dining-tvi-shal svep, heh gla-tor wuh sasu ik vesh' watching wuh tevikeh ek' ralash asleep fi' ish-veh ku-san. Wuh svep vesh' tu'ash vi' wuh parlor, wilat wuh tevikeh vesh' laying, heh tra' vesh' wuh ha'fek svi' fi' tvi-shal. I be' dvun-tor bi', heh wuh parlor svep vesh' tu'ash; tonk'peh gla-tor nash-veh tra' vikau't kling svi' tra' tonk'peh wuh hafayat t' peter; ni i shoved fi' k'; tonk'peh wuh khom svep vesh' klacha, heh wuh tal-muv wasn't tra'. Aishan yi i puzhu-tor somebody coming ne' wuh kaiden, pla' za' me. I sahr-tor svi' wuh parlor heh nem-tor wuh swift glazhau pa', heh wuh goh shi i gla-tor tor ip-sut wuh sa'haf vesh' svi' wuh tevikeh-natuhn. Wuh lid vesh' shoved bi' pa' wuh ash'ya, showing wuh tevik sasu's limuk ne' svi' tra', k' wuh masupik sai abru' ish-veh, heh ish-veh shroud fi'. I k'hy-tor wuh donku-sa'haf svi' ne' wuh lid, aishan ne' mesakh wilat ish-veh el'ru vesh' tuhsau, if tor me creep, au vesh' ni samu, heh yi i sahr-tor pla' mes' wuh tvi-shal heh svi' za' wuh svep. Wuh person coming vesh' mary jane. She went tor wuh tevikeh-natuhn, maut mos, heh kneeled ne' heh glazhau svi'; yi she shitau abru ish-veh handkerchief, heh gla-tor nash-veh she palikau tor maf, hi i couldn't zhu-tor ish-veh, heh ish-veh pla' vesh' tor me. I slid si', heh u' i be' dvun-tor wuh dining-tvi-shal i nahp i'd tor sure au watchers hadn't gla-tor me; ni i glazhau k'fai wuh treshaya, heh kanok-vei vesh' ek' gas'rak. Au hadn't stirred. I trel-tor abru tor sar-tak, olaya ruther pla-kur, fi' khrosahp t' wuh vel mavaun si' ik yut po' i had nem-tor ni mau trouble heh sahr-tor ni mau resk pa' ish-veh. Leralmin-tor i, kuv ish-veh kupi stay wilat ish-veh nam-tor, ek' gas'rak; fai'ei lu etek prah ne' wuh pilash wuh hundred mile il dahkuh i kupi kitau pla' tor mary jane, heh she kupi hil-tor ish-veh abru va'ashiv heh prah ish-veh; tonk'peh ik ain't wuh vel ik's going tor pavesh-tor; wuh vel ik's going tor pavesh-tor nam-tor, wuh donku 'll nam-tor afer-tor lu sarlah au tor wufkau fi' wuh lid. Yi wuh sa-te'kru 'll prah ish-veh va'ashiv, heh ish-veh 'll nam-tor wuh wu gad fa' au mazhiv-kur-tor anybody wuh'ashiv pavesh tor smouch ish-veh s' ish-veh. Veling i aitlu tor zish-tor ne' heh prah ish-veh s' tra', tonk'peh i dasn't ar'kadan ish-veh. Kanok minute ish-veh vesh' getting earlier i', heh takov ak ein t' au watchers would palikau tor stir, heh i lau prah catchedcatched k' shehkuh thousand dollars svi' t'nash-veh el'ru ik kling hadn't hired me tor nem-tor tun t'. I ri tor istaya tor nam-tor rish-tor abru svi' rai such business u' ik, i leralmin-tor tor myself. Lu i prah ne' kaiden svi' wuh asal wuh parlor vesh' ikap'uh t'du ru'lut, heh wuh watchers vesh' hal-tor. Tra' vikau't kling pa' tonk'peh wuh skan heh wuh kir'an bartley heh etwel tribe. I glantau ish-veh limuk tor gla-tor kuv sovek-vel had vesh' aisha, tonk'peh i couldn't var-tor. Na' wuh svitan t' wuh gad wuh undertaker sarlah k' ish-veh sasu, heh au eku wuh tevikeh-natuhn svi' wuh svitan t' wuh tvi-shal fi' wuh couple t' ku-san, heh yi eku ek' etwel ku-san svi' fel-tor, heh yahv-tor weht s' wuh behsu till wuh tvur heh wuh parlor heh wuh dining-tvi-shal vesh' bosh. I gla-tor wuh tevikeh-natuhn lid vesh' wuh yut ish-veh vesh' fa', tonk'peh i dasn't hal-tor tor glazhau svi' ne' ish-veh, k' sular-ves pa'. Yi wuh sutra palikau tor treit svi', heh wuh kuhsh-tor heh wuh ko-kan nem-tor ku-san svi' wuh khom zehl na' wuh patam t' wuh tevikeh-natuhn, heh na' wuh ulef wuh wadan wuh sutra deik-tor pa' vohris, svi' single lan, heh glazhau ne' na' wuh tevik sasu's limuk wuh minute, heh ein eku-tor svi' wuh bezhun-masu, heh ish-veh vesh' ek' maut fam dvun heh solemn, goh wuh ko-kan heh wuh kuhsh-tor holding handkerchiefs tor ish-veh bezhun heh keeping ish-veh patam keh'sei, heh sobbing wuh pi'. Tra' vikau't rai vath ralash tonk'peh wuh scraping t' wuh ash'ya fi' wuh lan-tol heh blowing nosesbecause sutra kwon-hau-ov salur au weht na' wuh mem-lu til-kum do au tor na' vath shitau kaula church. Lu wuh shi vesh' sa'haf-tor bosh wuh undertaker au slid pa' svi' ish-veh nesh-kur gloves k' ish-veh softy soothering yut, putting fi' wuh kim-shah estuhl, heh getting sutra heh vel ek' hali-shid heh kel'o, heh tor rai weht ralash do wuh aushfa. Au worla stariben; au dvun-tor sutra pa', au lerakhovau svi' tab-ma ones, au tu'ash abru passageways, heh ovsoh ish-veh k' nods, heh glat k' ish-veh el'ru. Yi au nem-tor ish-veh shi abru' tehnat wuh temok. Au vesh' wuh softest, glidingest, stealthiest sasu i ek'wak gla-tor; heh tra' vikau't rai weht abru'teruklar-ru'lut tor ish-veh do tra' nam-tor tor wuh ham. Au had yahv-tor wuh melodeuma has-bosh veh; heh lu kanok-vei vesh' pok wuh nu'ri kosu eku ne' heh ar'kada ish-veh, heh ish-veh vesh' takov skreeky heh colicky, heh kanok-veh hau svi' heh uralau, heh peter vesh' wuh goh veh ik had wuh rom vel, fupa s' t'nash-veh notion. Yi wuh reverend hobson tu'ash abru, vohris heh solemn, heh palikau tor variben; heh zehik ska' wuh danik outrageous zehl busted si' svi' wuh cellar wuh ak'shem ek'wak puzhu-tor; ish-veh vesh' goh veh dog, tonk'peh au tor wuh danik powerful racket, heh au potau ish-veh abru gas'rak bi'; wuh parson au had tor lamok tra', abru' wuh tevikeh-natuhn, heh waityou couldn't zhu-tor yourself nah-tor. Ish-veh vesh' gas'rak ne' awkward, heh kling didn't seem tor fai-tor ra tor tor. Tonk'peh takov ak gla-tor au ik wu-legged undertaker tor wuh glat tor wuh preacher u' mau u' tor leralmin, "ri tor du worryjust nerau fi' me." yi au stooped ne' heh palikau tor glide bi' wuh temok, aishan ish-veh tipan showing abru' wuh sutra's patam. Ni au glided bi', heh wuh powwow heh racket getting weht heh weht outrageous ek' wuh wak; heh na' kim-shah, lu au had hal-tor pa' dahkuh vla t' wuh tvi-shal, au sasaudau ne' cellar. Yi svi' pa' dahkuh seconds etek puzhu-tor wuh whack, heh wuh dog au shahtau abru k' wuh danik taurauk vlut il dahkuh, heh yi kanok-vei vesh' tevik fam dvun, heh wuh parson palikau ish-veh solemn variben wilat au losrak ska'. Svi' wuh minute il dahkuh la' sarlah nash undertaker's pla' heh tipan gliding bi' wuh temok va'ashiv; heh ni au glided heh glided pa' rehkuh vla t' wuh tvi-shal, heh yi she-tor abru, heh duvek-tor ish-veh ru'lut k' ish-veh el'ru, heh sakadau ish-veh talu si' na' wuh preacher, abru' wuh sutra's patam, heh leralmin-tor, svi' wuh ves t' wuh dirik zhal, "au had wuh rat!" yi au tevan-tor ne' heh glided bi' wuh temok va'ashiv tor ish-veh shi. Du kupi gla-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh lo'uk satisfaction tor wuh sutra, fai'ei naturally au aitlu tor fai-tor. Wuh pi' vel spo' ik ri tor kodona nothing, heh ish-veh's aishan wuh pi' vel ik tor wuh sasu tor nam-tor glazhau abru tor heh tishau. Tra' vikau't rai weht popular sasu svi' kahr do ra ik undertaker vesh'. Muhl, wuh mem-lu til-kum sermon vesh' maut rom, tonk'peh pison wu heh tiresome; heh yi wuh sa-te'kru au shoved svi' heh prah ska' ein t' ish-veh tsuri rubbage, heh na' kim-shah wuh job vesh' k'fai, heh wuh undertaker palikau tor sneak abru fi' wuh tevikeh-natuhn k' ish-veh wufkau-yetursu. I vesh' svi' wuh wadashaya yi, heh glantau ish-veh takov keen. Tonk'peh au worla meddled na' ek'; aishan slid wuh lid bi' u' mos u' mush, heh screwed ish-veh ne' wufik heh sahris. Ni tra' i vesh'! I didn't fai-tor whether wuh donku vesh' svi' tra' il ri. Ni, leralmin-tor i, s'pose somebody has hogged ik sa'haf fi' wuh sly?i' uf tor i fai-tor whether tor kitau tor mary jane il ri? S'pose she hil-tor ish-veh abru heh didn't talal nothing, ra would she nah-tor t' me? Tenai ish-veh, i leralmin-tor, i lau prah shi'kar abru heh jailed; i'd weh-rom ti neik heh potau gu'gelik, heh ri kitau na' ek'; wuh vel's awful rish-tor i'; trying tor weh-rom ish-veh, i've worsened ish-veh wuh hundred wak, heh i istaya tor goodness i'd aishan kal-tor ish-veh sa'awek, dad zaprah wuh bosh business! Au visolektau ish-veh, heh sarlah etek pla' ha-kel, heh i went tor watching limuk againi couldn't gol'nev ish-veh, heh i couldn't shom hagik. Tonk'peh nothing sarlah t' ish-veh; wuh limuk didn't var-tor me nothing. Wuh sa-te'kru au yaretau pa' svi' wuh khru, heh sweetened kanok-veh abru, heh tor himself ek'wak ni friendly; heh au mazhiv-kur-tor si' wuh idea ik ish-veh congregation abru' svi' england would nam-tor svi' wuh wadashaya pa' ish-veh, ni au bolau brax heh settle abru wuh estate gas'rak maf heh trasha na' ha-kel. Au vesh' maut sorry au vesh' ni kwitau, heh ni vesh' kanok-veh; au istau au kupi stay longer, tonk'peh au leralmin-tor au kupi gla-tor ish-veh couldn't nam-tor ovsoh. Heh au leralmin-tor veling ish-veh heh william would nem-tor wuh ko-kan ha-kel k' au; heh ik sanoi kanok-veh nuh', fai'ei yi wuh ko-kan would nam-tor muhl teslau heh svi' ish-veh sha' relations; heh ish-veh sanoi wuh ko-kan, tootickled au ni au sok'i forgot au ek'wak had wuh trouble svi' wuh panu; heh var-tor ish-veh tor makau si' u' sahris u' au aitlu tor, au would nam-tor pok. Au ri donku-tor vel vesh' ik glad heh kunli ish-veh tor t'nash-veh khaf-spol sut tor gla-tor au getting fooled heh ti tor ni, tonk'peh i didn't gla-tor rai safe yut na' me tor val svi' heh rubah wuh paik tvelkau. Muhl, tenah kuv wuh sa-te'kru didn't dun wuh kelek heh wuh niggers heh ek' wuh veltra na' auction zehik offsale dahkuh gad po' wuh mem-lu til-kum; tonk'peh anybody kupi mahr-tor awek beforehand kuv au aitlu tor. Ni wuh thurai gad po' wuh mem-lu til-kum, bi' pa' aru-wak, wuh ko-kan' mak prah wuh wuh'rak jolt. Wuh couple t' nigger traders sarlah bi', heh wuh sa-te'kru makau au wuh niggers reasonable, na' rehkuh-gad fnalan u' au puvutau ish-veh, heh maf au went, wuh dahkuh sa-fu abru wuh pilash tor memphis, heh ish-veh ko-mekh ne' wuh pilash tor orleans. I nahp au ri donku-tor ko-kan heh au niggers would shaya ish-veh khaf-spol na' tushat; au maf-tor pa' tik vath, heh nem-tor fi' ni ish-veh danik tor me ne' has-bosh tor gla-tor ish-veh. Wuh ko-kan leralmin-tor au hadn't ek'wak sahr-tor-tor t' seeing wuh skan dahshau il makau maf s' wuh kahr. I mokuhlek't ek'wak prah ish-veh s' t'nash-veh vokaya, wuh glan t' au ri donku-tor miserable ko-kan heh niggers hanging pa' tik vath's talu heh maf-tor; heh i reckon i couldn't wuh lam-tor ish-veh ek', tonk'peh would wuh had tor bust si' heh var-tor fi' etwel gang kuv i hadn't knowed wuh sale vikau't rai khrosahp heh wuh niggers would nam-tor pla' ha-kel svi' wuh wehk gad il dahkuh. Wuh vel tor wuh suk' stir svi' wuh kahr, nuh', heh wuh rom wehk sasarlah pa'ash'ya heh leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' scandalous tor dahshauk wuh ko-mekh heh wuh kanu ik yut. Ish-veh dash-tor wuh frauds ein; tonk'peh wuh hinek duhsu au bulled gas'rak bi', spite t' ek' wuh duke kupi leralmin il tor, heh i var-tor du wuh duke vesh' powerful uneasy. Thurai gad vesh' auction gad. Pa' sax'ksei gad svi' wuh asal wuh sa-te'kru heh wuh duke sarlah abru svi' wuh kamu-tvi-shal heh woke me abru, heh gla-tor nash-veh k' ish-veh glazhau ik tra' vesh' trouble. Wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor: "vesh' du svi' t'nash-veh tvi-shal mu-yor fa' kim-shah?" "rai, ish-veh majesty"if vesh' wuh yut i kwon-hau-ov puvutau ish-veh lu kling tonk'peh etwel gang vikau't pa'. "vesh' du svi' tra' yisterday er kim-shah mu-yor?" "rai, ish-veh majesty." "dor ugelik, nowno ti." "dor ugelik, ish-veh majesty, i'm telling du wuh yeht'es. I hain't vesh' wuh-be' ish-veh tvi-shal opi' din-tor mary jane nem-tor du heh wuh duke heh gluvau ish-veh tor du." wuh duke leralmin-tor: "ma du gla-tor anybody else hal-tor svi' tra'?" "rai, ish-veh takov, ri u' i vokau, i dva-tor." "pehkaya heh nah-tor." i orenau awhile heh gla-tor t'nash-veh pavesh; yi i leralmin-tor: "muhl, gla-tor nash-veh wuh niggers hal-tor svi' tra' several wak." fi' t' au mazhiv-kur-tor wuh pi' spen-tor, heh glazhau spo' au hadn't ek'wak gishu ish-veh, heh yi spo' au had. Yi wuh duke leralmin-tor: "ra, ek' t' au?" "noleastways, ri ek' na' oncethat nam-tor, i ri tor nah-tor i ek'wak gla-tor au ek' sasarlah na' wuh'wak tonk'peh aishan veh wak." "tonk'peh! Lu vesh' ik?" "ish-veh vesh' wuh gad etek had wuh mem-lu til-kum. Svi' wuh asal. Ish-veh vikau't lehkuh-mal, fai'ei i overslept. I vesh' aishan starting ne' wuh pu'uth, heh gla-tor nash-veh au." "muhl, hal-tor fi', hal-tor fi'! Ra did au tor? Uf'd au bae'cok?" "au didn't tor nothing. Heh au didn't bae'cok anyway mau, u' ausachya u' i gla-tor. Au tiptoed maf; ni i gla-tor, hagik hiyet, ik au'd shoved svi' tra' tor tor abru ish-veh majesty's tvi-shal, il vel, s'posing du vesh' abru; heh afer-tor du vikau't abru, heh ni au vesh' hoping tor zish-tor s' wuh yut t' trouble rik' waking du abru, kuv au hadn't already waked du abru." "lo'uk pohshayek, nash nam-tor wuh hal-tor!" leralmin-tor wuh sa-te'kru; heh fi' t' au glazhau takov has-bosh heh tolerable silly. Au lam-tor tra' wuh-thinking heh scratching ish-veh patam wuh minute, heh wuh duke au bust vi' wuh ves t' wuh pi' raspy chuckle, heh leralmin-tor: "ish-veh tor kuhsh-tor ek' uf pu wuh niggers mavau ish-veh el'ru. Au kal-tor fi' tor nam-tor sorry au vesh' going s' nash shal! Heh i pudva-tor au vesh' sorry, heh ni did du, heh ni did kanok-veh. Ri tor ek'wak var-tor me sovek weht ik wuh nigger ain't prah sovek histrionic talent. Po, wuh yut au mavau ik vel ish-veh would duhsu anybody. Svi' t'nash-veh opinion, tra''s wuh fortune svi' 'em. Kuv i had capital heh wuh theater, i wouldn't aitlun wuh weh-rom ti-si' do thatand la' etek've hal-tor heh makau 'em na' wuh song. Ha, heh ain't privileged tor uralau wuh song wi. Leralmin, wilat nam-tor ik songthat fnalan?" "svi' wuh kutra na' tor nam-tor tershau. Wilat would ish-veh nam-tor?" "muhl, ik's ek' gas'rak yi, itaren goodness." leralmin-tor i, ves t' timid-spo': "nam-tor vel hal-tor riyeht?" wuh sa-te'kru whirls fi' me heh tres-tor si': "rim o' ish-veh business! Du potau ish-veh patam shet, heh kashek y'r sha' affairsif du prah sovek. Wu u' du're svi' nash kahr ri tor du forgit thatyou zhu-tor?" yi au leralmin-tor tor wuh duke, "etek prah tor jest swaller ish-veh heh leralmin noth'n': mum's wuh zhit na' etek." u' au vesh' starting ne' wuh pu'uth wuh duke au chuckles va'ashiv, heh leralmin-tor: "sahris sales heh pi' pinkaunu! Ish-veh's wuh rom businessyes." v wuh sa-te'kru snarls pa' fi' ish-veh heh leralmin-tor: "i vesh' trying tor tor na' wuh buhfik svi' sellin' 'em si' ni sahris. Kuv wuh pinkaunu has da-tor si' tor nam-tor rim, lackin' considable, heh rim tor lesh, nam-tor ish-veh t'nash-veh lafot sovek weht'n ish-veh's yourn?" "muhl, au'd nam-tor svi' nash kelek wi heh etek wouldn't kuv i kupi wuh prah t'nash-veh na'shikh shroi tor." wuh sa-te'kru sassed pla' u' mau u' vesh' safe na' ish-veh, heh yi swapped pa' heh lit vi' me va'ashiv. Au mazhiv-kur-tor me ne' wuh kutra na' ri coming heh telling ish-veh gla-tor nash-veh wuh niggers sasarlah t' ish-veh tvi-shal peran ik waysaid sovek duhsu would wuh knowed vel vesh' abru. Heh yi waltzed svi' heh cussed himself awhile, heh leralmin-tor ish-veh ek' sarlah t' ish-veh ri laying tab-ma heh taking ish-veh malatik shom ik asal, heh au'd nam-tor tenah kuv au'd ek'wak tor ish-veh va'ashiv. Ni au went ska' wuh-jawing; heh i olau dreadful glad i'd ar'kada ish-veh ek' ska' fi' tor wuh niggers, heh wi hadn't ovsoh wuh niggers rai klau k' ish-veh. Chapter xxviii. K'-heh-k' ish-veh vesh' getting-abru wak. Ni sarlah nash-veh ne' wuh pu'uth heh palikau na' ne'-kaiden; tonk'peh u' sarlah nash-veh tor wuh ko-kan' tvi-shal wuh svep vesh' tu'ash, heh gla-tor nash-veh mary jane setting k' ish-veh hinek isachya lap-fek, if vesh' tu'ash heh she'd vesh' sa'haf-tor vel svi' itgetting pok tor hal-tor tor england. Tonk'peh she had pehkau i' k' wuh hesha gown svi' ish-veh lap, heh had ish-veh limuk svi' ish-veh el'ru, maf-tor. I olau awful rasahkos tor gla-tor ish-veh; veling anybody would. I went svi' tra' heh leralmin-tor: "din-tor mary jane, du mokuhlek't wuh-lesh tor gla-tor sutra svi' trouble, heh i mokuhlek'tmost kwon-hau-ov. Var-tor me pa' ish-veh." ni she ovsoh ish-veh. Heh ish-veh vesh' wuh niggersi aishan gishu ish-veh. She leralmin-tor wuh vaksurik halan tor england vesh' danik pa' spoiled na' ish-veh; she didn't fai-tor uf she vesh' ek'wak going tor nam-tor kunli tra', fai-tor wuh ko-mekh heh wuh kanu vikau't ek'wak going tor gla-tor tik vath rai moreand yi busted si' bitterer do ek'wak, heh flung abru ish-veh el'ru, heh leralmin-tor: "oh, tal-kam, tal-kam, tor nah-tor au ain't ek'wak going tor gla-tor tik vath sovek weht!" "tonk'peh au willand svi' dahkuh weeksand i fai-tor ish-veh!" leralmin-tor i. Tor-gav, ish-veh vesh' si' fa' i kupi nah-tor! Heh fa' i kupi budge she lehm-tor ish-veh kar pa' t'nash-veh talu heh var-tor me tor leralmin ish-veh va'ashiv, leralmin ish-veh va'ashiv, leralmin ish-veh va'ashiv! Gla-tor nash-veh i had stariben nuh' sudden heh leralmin-tor nuh' mau, heh vesh' svi' wuh ikap-tor shi. I ya'akash ish-veh tor kal-tor me nah-tor wuh minute; heh she eku tra', maut impatient heh teporilau heh handsome, tonk'peh looking ves t' kunli heh eased-abru, spo' wuh person ik's had wuh zud seshau si'. Ni i went tor studying ish-veh si'. I leralmin-tor tor myself, i reckon wuh ak'shem ik ups heh var-tor wuh yeht'es lu au nam-tor svi' wuh wufik shi nam-tor taking considerable wehk resks, hi i ain't had rai veshtaya, heh mokuhlek't leralmin na' ac'ruth; tonk'peh ish-veh glazhau ni tor me, anyway; heh wi la''s wuh nuf wilat i'm blest kuv ish-veh ri tor glazhau tor me spo' wuh yeht'es nam-tor weh-rom heh actuly safer do wuh ti. I bolau ti ish-veh k' svi' t'nash-veh kashek, heh nah-tor ish-veh abru' ein wak il vath, ish-veh's ni ves t' flekh heh unregular. I worla gla-tor nothing spo' ish-veh. Muhl, i leralmin-tor tor myself na' kim-shah, i'm wuh-going tor pavesh ish-veh; i'll abru heh var-tor wuh yeht'es nash wak, hi ish-veh tor seem danik spo' setting ne' fi' wuh kag t' grazhiv heh touching ish-veh ska' aishan tor gla-tor wilat du'll hal-tor tor. Yi i leralmin-tor: "din-tor mary jane, nam-tor tra' sovek shi s' kahr wuh pi' yut wilat du kupi hal-tor heh stay rehkuh il kehkuh gad?" "ha; mr. Lothrop's. Po?" "worla kashek po wi. Kuv i'll var-tor du uf i fai-tor wuh niggers dungi gla-tor tik vath va'ashiv svi' dahkuh weekshere svi' nash houseand skan-tor uf i fai-tor itwill du hal-tor tor mr. Lothrop's heh stay kehkuh gad?" "kehkuh gad!" she leralmin-tor; "i'll stay wuh tevun!" "ek' gas'rak, " i leralmin-tor, "i ri tor aitlun nothing weht s' du do aishan ish-veh wordi druther ma ish-veh do wuh'ashiv sasu's shok-wuh-bible." she abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh reddened abru maut slor, heh i leralmin-tor, "kuv du ri tor kashek ish-veh, i'll ikap-tor wuh doorand terk ish-veh." yi sarlah nash-veh pla' heh eku ne' va'ashiv, heh leralmin-tor: "ri tor du holler. Aishan eku fam dvun heh nem-tor ish-veh spo' wuh sasu. I prah tor var-tor wuh yeht'es, heh du aitlun tor fir-tor abru, din-tor mary, fai'ei ish-veh's wuh rasahkos ves, heh going tor nam-tor lerash tor nem-tor, tonk'peh tra' ain't rai gol'nev na' ish-veh.
