Tra''s veh yut yetlet's hal-tor heh hil-tor abru wuh tevikeh heh glazhau." ik nem-tor au. "hooray!" au ek' saul-tor, heh vesh' starting gas'rak ska'; tonk'peh wuh lawyer heh wuh hassu uralau si': "meskaraya fi', meskaraya fi'! Hmoi'neks ek' aifa kehkuh sasu heh wuh sa-kan, heh zaprah au bi', nuh'!" "etek'll tor ish-veh!" au ek' saul-tor; "heh kuv etek ri tor talal au ulidar etek'll lynch wuh bosh gang!" i vesh' pahth-tor, i', i var-tor du. Tonk'peh tra' vikau't rai getting maf, du fai-tor. Au gripped etek ek', heh marched etek gas'rak bi', zehik na' wuh graveyard, if vesh' wuh mile heh wuh ulef ne' wuh pilash, heh wuh bosh kahr na' etwel timut, na' etek tor ralash hiyet, heh ish-veh vesh' goh naukuh svi' wuh khru. U' etek went k' etwel kelek i istau i hadn't satau mary jane s' kahr; fai'ei i' kuv i kupi um ish-veh wuh wink she'd ta'hal si' heh korsau me, heh salur fi' etwel tevik-kuhsh-tor. Muhl, etek bishau bi' ne' wuh pilash fau-yut, aishan carrying fi' spo' wildcats; heh tor tor ish-veh weht scary wuh igen vesh' darking abru, heh wuh igen-wesh palikaya tor wink heh flitter, heh wuh salan tor shiver svi' wuh mor. Nash vesh' wuh danik awful trouble heh danik dangersome i ek'wak vesh' svi'; heh i vesh' kinder kovtulik; kanok-vei vesh' going ni natya s' ra i had kal-tor na'; stead t' hasu teslau ni i kupi nem-tor t'nash-veh sha' wak kuv i aitlu tor, heh gla-tor ek' wuh mihrsh, heh ma mary jane na' t'nash-veh pla' tor korsau me heh eku me elik lu wuh ikap-tor-nunau sarlah, la' vesh' nothing svi' wuh panu betwixt me heh sudden tevakh tonk'peh aishan au tattoo-ulidar. Kuv au didn't talal au i couldn't lesh tor nah-tor pa' ish-veh; heh wi, somehow, i couldn't nah-tor pa' nothing else. Ish-veh prah darker heh darker, heh ish-veh vesh' wuh vaksurik wak tor mazhiv-kur-tor wuh patreitan wuh trel; tonk'peh ik suk' husky had me k' wuh wristhinesand wuh ak'shem lau u' muhl ar'kadan tor mazhiv-kur-tor goliar wuh trel. Au zaseshau me gas'rak bi', au vesh' ni teporilau, heh i had tor sahr-tor tor potau abru. Lu au prah tra' au bishau vi' wuh graveyard heh pu-tor abru' ish-veh spo' wuh overflow. Heh lu au prah tor wuh shi'vukhut au afer-tor au had pa' wuh hundred wak u' wehk hilek u' au aitlu, tonk'peh kling hadn't nahp tor zaprah wuh makh-yonet. Tonk'peh au masu-halovau vi' digging anyway k' wuh hanuvaya t' wuh igen-wesh, heh satau wuh sasu tor wuh nearest kelek, wuh ulef wuh mile ska', tor yahv-tor veh. Ni au hil-tor heh hil-tor spo' kanok-vei; heh ish-veh prah awful gu'gelik, heh wuh sov-masu palikau, heh wuh salan swished heh swushed bi', heh wuh igen-wesh sarlah brisker heh brisker, heh wuh rahm orkau; tonk'peh au sutra worla nem-tor rai beglanau t' ish-veh, au vesh' ni bosh t' nash business; heh veh minute du kupi gla-tor kanok-vei heh kanok limuk svi' ik suk' patreitan, heh wuh shovelfuls t' kitek masu-halovaun abru s' wuh shi'vukhut, heh wuh thurai dahr wuh gu'gelik psethau ish-veh ek' si', heh du couldn't gla-tor nothing na' ek'. Na' kim-shah au prah si' wuh tevikeh-natuhn heh palikau tor unscrew wuh lid, heh yi such wuh'ashiv crowding heh shouldering heh shoving u' tra' vesh', tor scrouge svi' heh prah wuh glan, du worla gla-tor; heh svi' wuh gu'gelik, ik yut, ish-veh vesh' awful. Hines au dash-tor t'nash-veh kar-nik dreadful pulling heh tugging ni, heh i reckon au sok'i forgot i vesh' svi' wuh panu, au vesh' ni teporilau heh panting. Ek' t' wuh sudden wuh igen-wesh kal-tor hal-tor wuh buhfik sluice t' wan-kur glare, heh somebody uralau si': "k' wuh living jingo, la''s wuh sa'haf t' pi-maat-tukh fi' ish-veh thasek!" hines kal-tor si' wuh whoop, spo' kanok-veh else, heh eku-tor t'nash-veh kar-nik heh mazhiv-kur-tor wuh suk' tral tor bust ish-veh yut svi' heh prah wuh glazhau, heh wuh yut i lit si' heh shinned na' wuh fau-yut svi' wuh gu'gelik tra' ain't kling mokuhlek var-tor. I had wuh fau-yut ek' tor myself, heh i fairly flewleastways, i had ish-veh ek' tor myself kaula wuh huhtik gu'gelik, heh wuh i'-heh-yi glares, heh wuh buzzing t' wuh sov-masu, heh wuh thrashing t' wuh salan, heh wuh splitting t' wuh rahm; heh sure u' du nam-tor pukeshta i did clip ish-veh bi'! Lu i kwul-tor wuh kahr gla-tor nash-veh tra' vikau't kling si' svi' wuh sahriv, ni i worla shi'kar na' rai pla' yut, tonk'peh humped ish-veh zehik k'fai wuh nen veh; heh lu i palikau tor prah na' etwel kelek i mokh-tor t'nash-veh bezhun heh eku ish-veh. Rai ta'hal tra'; wuh kelek ek' darkwhich tor me olau sorry heh disappointed, i didn't fai-tor po. Tonk'peh na' kim-shah, aishan u' i vesh' masu-halovaun k', kahai sarlah wuh ta'hal svi' mary jane's krani! Heh t'nash-veh khaf-spol puv-tor abru sudden, spo' tor bust; heh wuh ka dahr wuh kelek heh ek' vesh' za' me svi' wuh gu'gelik, heh wasn't ek'wak going tor nam-tor fa' me rai weht svi' nash panu. She vesh' wuh buhfik ko-kan i ek'wak gla-tor, heh had wuh danik mazhiv. Wuh minute i vesh' irak hiyet abru' wuh kahr tor gla-tor i kupi tor wuh tow-patam, i palikau tor glazhau nasik na' wuh masu-hali tor yahv-tor, heh wuh wuh'rak wak wuh igen-wesh gluvau me veh ik wasn't chained i snatched ish-veh heh shoved. Ish-veh vesh' wuh canoe, heh vikau't terau k' nothing tonk'peh wuh man-elakh. Wuh tow-patam vesh' wuh rattling suk' ir ska', maf si' tra' svi' wuh svitan t' wuh pilash, tonk'peh i didn't pak-tor rai wak; heh lu i kwul-tor wuh marshak na' kim-shah i vesh' ni fagged i would wuh aishan laid ne' tor salur heh hushaya kuv i kupi afforded ish-veh. Tonk'peh i didn't. U' i sprung aboard i uralau si': "si' k' du, jim, heh eku ish-veh thal! Glory nam-tor tor goodness, etek're ikap-tor t' au!" jim lit si', heh vesh' wuh-coming na' me k' fi' kar sak-tor, au vesh' ni bosh t' mak; tonk'peh lu i glimpsed ish-veh svi' wuh igen-wesh t'nash-veh khaf-spol pohshaya abru svi' t'nash-veh ru'lut heh i went overboard pla'rak; na' i forgot au vesh' hinek sa-te'kru lear heh wuh drownded wuh-rab ek' svi' veh, heh ish-veh danik pahth-tor wuh nehasamek heh ha'ge s' me. Tonk'peh jim aluk-kum-tor me si', heh vesh' going tor teraya-martaya me heh kudau me, heh ni fi', au vesh' ni glad i vesh' pla' heh etek vesh' ikap-tor t' wuh sa-te'kru heh wuh duke, tonk'peh i leralmin-tor: "ri i'; ma ish-veh na' asal-yem, ma ish-veh na' asal-yem! Tresahk thal heh kal-tor ish-veh zish-tor!" ni svi' dahkuh seconds maf etek went wuh-sliding ne' wuh pilash, heh ish-veh did seem ni rom tor nam-tor elik va'ashiv heh ek' k' ourselves fi' wuh suk' pilash, heh kling tor ertau etek. I had tor skip pa' wuh zeshau, heh spen-tor abru heh treshaya t'nash-veh timut wuh zamu timesi couldn't gol'nev ish-veh; tonk'peh pa' wuh wuh treshaya i pubeglanau wuh ralash ik i knowed mighty muhl, heh meskarau t'nash-veh esh heh shroi heh bek-tor; heh sure hiyet, lu wuh thurai kahai busted si' abru' wuh masu, la' sarlah au!heh aishan wuh-laying tor ish-veh fel heh tor ish-veh skiff hum! Ish-veh vesh' wuh sa-te'kru heh wuh duke. Ni i wilted gas'rak ne' fi' tor wuh planks yi, heh mazhiv-kur-tor abru; heh ish-veh vesh' ek' i kupi tor tor potau s' maf-tor. Chapter xxx. Lu au prah aboard wuh sa-te'kru went na' me, heh hutau me k' wuh hmoi'neks, heh leralmin-tor: "tryin' tor mazhiv-kur-tor etek wuh trel, vesh' ye, du wil'tei! Wuh sasu ik had wuh-holt t' me vesh' maut rom tor me, heh potau taran au had wuh sa-kan pa' u' suk' u' me ik tev-tor kim-shah tevun, heh au vesh' sorry tor gla-tor wuh sa-kan svi' such wuh tehvar-bosh teslau; heh lu au vesh' ek' nem-tor k' ak'wikmun k' finding wuh pi-maat-tukh, heh tor wuh rush na' wuh tevikeh-natuhn, au kal-tor hal-tor t' me heh zhal-tor, 'timut ish-veh i', il au'll geldau ye, sure!' heh i lit si'. Ni i worla pehkau sahran till i afer-tor wuh canoe; heh lu i prah la' i var-tor jim tor brax, il au'd kum me heh geldau me wi, heh leralmin-tor i vesh' afeard du heh wuh duke wasn't alive i', heh i vesh' awful sorry, heh ni vesh' jim, heh vesh' awful glad lu gla-tor etek du coming; du lau ya'akash jim kuv i didn't." jim leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' ni; heh wuh sa-te'kru var-tor ish-veh tor ikap'uh t'du ru'lut, heh leralmin-tor, "oh, ha, ish-veh's mighty kesik!" heh hutau me abru va'ashiv, heh leralmin-tor au reckoned au'd drownd me. Tonk'peh wuh duke leralmin-tor: "leggo wuh sa-kan, du hinek idiot! Would du wuh ovsoh sovek natya? Did du inquire pa' na' ish-veh lu du prah thal? I ri tor vokau ish-veh." ni wuh sa-te'kru kal-tor hal-tor t' me, heh palikau tor cuss ik kahr heh kanok-veh svi' ish-veh. Tonk'peh ik trick nem-tor 'em tor wuh graveyard, heh wuh pi-maat-tukh ovsoh etek wuh fam dvun bigger kindness; na' kuv wuh teporilau duhsu hadn't kal-tor hal-tor ek' holts heh tor ik rush tor prah wuh glazhau, etek'd wuh yuk-tor svi' etwel cravats tor-nightcravats warranted sai-vel-tor, toolonger do etek'd bolaya 'em." au vesh' fam dvun wuh minutethinking; yi wuh sa-te'kru leralmin-tor, ves t' tadek-adir-minded spo': "mf! Veling lu au prah tor snoring etek had wuh wu gabble, heh i var-tor jim kanok-vei. Chapter xxxi. Etek dasn't pehkaya va'ashiv na' sovek kahr na' gad heh gad; potau gas'rak bi' ne' wuh pilash. Etek vesh' ne' khu'rak svi' wuh lamekh igen-va i', heh wuh mighty wu yut s' ha-kel. Etek palikau tor sarlah tor lap k' spanish yekuhl fi' au, hanging ne' s' wuh sikrus spo' wu, zhai-kur hisahk. Ni i' wuh frauds reckoned au vesh' s' tehvar, heh au palikau tor ar'kadan wuh pi'kahr va'ashiv. Wuh'rak au ovsoh wuh lecture fi' temperance; tonk'peh au didn't tor hiyet na' au fi' tor prah mon-tor fi'. Heh na' kim-shah au nem-tor wuh rubah heh palikau tor ti ish-veh patam teretuhr svi' wuh wigwam heh variben neik heh confidential dahkuh il rehkuh wadan na' wuh wak. Jim heh me prah uneasy. Etek didn't spo' wuh glazhau t' ish-veh. Etek judged au vesh' studying abru ein ves t' weh-rasahkos deviltry do ek'wak. Etek da-tor ish-veh abru' heh abru', heh na' kim-shah etek tor abru etwel kashkau au vesh' going tor shaya vi' somebody's kelek il mahr-kel, il vesh' going vi' wuh counterfeit-donku business, il vel. ("kelek tor rob, du tvai, " leralmin-tor i tor myself; "heh lu du prah k'fai robbing ish-veh du'll sarlah pla' la' heh wonder ra has shetau t' me heh jim heh wuh raftand du'll ma tor nem-tor ish-veh si' svi' wondering.") heh au leralmin-tor kuv au vikau't pla' k' midday wuh duke heh me would fai-tor ish-veh vesh' ek' gas'rak, heh etek vesh' tor sarlah bi'. Ni etek stayed wilat etek vesh'. Wuh duke au fretted heh wadashau pa', heh vesh' svi' wuh mighty sfith yut. Au scolded etek na' kanok-vei, heh etek couldn't seem tor tor nothing gas'rak; au afer-tor lafot k' kanok pi' vel. Vel vesh' wuh-fasan, sure. I vesh' rom heh glad lu midday sarlah heh rai sa-te'kru; etek kupi ma wuh rubah, anywayand sos'eh wuh pavesh na' wuh rubah fi-tor ish-veh. Wuh duke au palikau tor abuse ish-veh na' wuh hinek duhsu, heh wuh sa-te'kru palikau tor sass pla', heh wuh minute au vesh' fairly na' ish-veh i lit si' heh hutau wuh reefs s' t'nash-veh hind mal, heh pada-tor ne' wuh pilash fau-yut spo' wuh deer, na' gla-tor nash-veh etwel pavesh; heh i tor abru t'nash-veh kashek ik ish-veh would nam-tor wuh wu gad fa' au ek'wak gla-tor me heh jim va'ashiv. I prah ne' tra' ek' s' esh tonk'peh putush-tor abru k' mak, heh uralau si': "eku ish-veh thal, jim! Etek're ek' gas'rak i'!" tonk'peh tra' vikau't rai kilko-srashiv, heh kling sasarlah t' wuh wigwam. Jim vesh' hal-tor! I eku abru wuh shoutand yi anotherand yi wuh'ashiv veh; heh sahr-tor nash yut heh ik svi' wuh lapan, whooping heh screeching; tonk'peh ish-veh vikau't rai useold jim vesh' hal-tor. Yi i eku ne' heh maf-tor; i couldn't gol'nev ish-veh. Tonk'peh i couldn't eku fam dvun wu. Takov ak i went si' fi' wuh fau-yut, trying tor nah-tor ra i weh-rom tor, heh i sahr-tor mes' wuh sa-kan walking, heh ya'akash ish-veh kuv au'd gla-tor wuh flekh nigger sai-vel-tor ni heh ni, heh au leralmin-tor: "ha." "whereabouts?" leralmin-tor i. "ne' tor silas phelps' shi, dahkuh mile ne' la'. Au's wuh runaway nigger, heh au've prah ish-veh. Vesh' du looking na' ish-veh?" "du sihaya i ain't! I sahr-tor mes' ish-veh svi' wuh lapan pa' wuh wadan il dahkuh ago, heh au leralmin-tor kuv i hollered au'd tresahk t'nash-veh nehasamek outand var-tor me tor ti ne' heh stay wilat i vesh'; heh i ovsoh ish-veh. Vesh' tra' ek'wak opi'; afeard tor sasarlah." "muhl, " au leralmin-tor, "du needn't nam-tor afeard rai weht, becuz au've prah ish-veh. Au sahr-tor ska' f'm ne' khu'rak, som'ers." "ish-veh's wuh rom job au prah ish-veh." "muhl, i reckon! Tra''s dahkuh hunderd dollars reward fi' ish-veh. Ish-veh's spo' picking abru donku si''n wuh fau-yut." "ha, ish-veh isand i kupi wuh had ish-veh kuv i'd vesh' suk' hiyet; gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh wuh'rak. Vi nailed ish-veh?" "ish-veh vesh' wuh hinek fellowa strangerand au makau si' ish-veh pavesh svi' ish-veh na' keh-leh dollars, becuz au's prah tor hal-tor abru wuh pilash heh mokuhlek't bek-tor. Nah-tor o' ik, i'! Du sihaya i'd bek-tor, kuv ish-veh vesh' stehkuh tevun." "ik's me, kanok wak, " leralmin-tor i. "tonk'peh sos'eh ish-veh pavesh ain't don rai weht do ik, kuv au'll makau ish-veh ni cheap. Sos'eh tra''s vel ain't zehik pa' ish-veh." "tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor, thoughstraight u' wuh string. Gla-tor nash-veh wuh handbill myself. Ish-veh var-tor ek' pa' ish-veh, tor wuh dotpaints ish-veh spo' wuh bikuv, heh var-tor wuh plantation au's frum, ne' newrleans. Rai-sirree-bob, au ain't rai trouble 'bout ik speculation, du sihaya du. Leralmin, gimme wuh chaw tobacker, skil-tor't ye?" i didn't ma rim, ni au losrak. I went tor wuh marshak, heh eku ne' svi' wuh wigwam tor nah-tor. Tonk'peh i couldn't sarlah tor nothing. I nahp till i sai-vel-tor t'nash-veh patam sival, tonk'peh i couldn't gla-tor rai yut s' wuh trouble. Po' ek' nash wu halovaya, heh po' ek' etek'd ovsoh na' au scoundrels, la' ish-veh vesh' ek' sarlah tor nothing, kanok-vei ek' busted abru heh ruined, fai'ei au kupi ma wuh khaf-spol tor dvin-tor jim such wuh trick u' ik, heh tor ish-veh wuh kafeh va'ashiv ek' ish-veh ha'kiv, heh svi' ri-fainusu, nuh', na' keh-leh kitork dollars. Wuh'wak i leralmin-tor tor myself ish-veh would nam-tor wuh thousand wak weh-rom na' jim tor nam-tor wuh kafeh na' ha-kel wilat ish-veh skan vesh', u' wu u' au'd prah tor nam-tor wuh kafeh, heh ni i'd weh-rom kitau wuh nuhm tor tom sawyer heh var-tor ish-veh tor var-tor din-tor watson wilat au vesh'. Tonk'peh i ak mazhiv-kur-tor abru ik notion na' dahkuh vel: she'd nam-tor mad heh spa'ash na' ish-veh rascality heh ungratefulness na' leaving ish-veh, heh ni she'd makau ish-veh zehik ne' wuh pilash va'ashiv; heh kuv she didn't, kanok-veh naturally despises wuh ungrateful nigger, heh au'd tor jim olau ish-veh ek' wuh wak, heh ni au'd olau ornery heh disgraced. Heh yi nah-tor t' me! Ish-veh would prah ek' pa' ik huck finn gol-tor wuh nigger tor prah ish-veh el'es; heh kuv i vesh' ek'wak tor gla-tor anybody s' ik kahr va'ashiv i'd nam-tor pok tor prah ne' heh lick ish-veh kluf na' mesh. Ik's aishan wuh yut: wuh person tor wuh neik-ne' vel, heh yi au ri tor aitlun tor nem-tor rai consequences t' ish-veh. Nah-tor u' wu u' au mokuhlek ip-sut ish-veh, ish-veh ain't rai disgrace. Ik vesh' t'nash-veh teslau exactly. Wuh weht i orenau pa' nash, wuh weht t'nash-veh conscience went tor grinding me, heh wuh weht wicked heh neik-ne' heh ornery i prah tor olaya. Heh na' kim-shah, lu ish-veh kwul me ek' t' wuh sudden ik la' vesh' wuh eiktra el'ru t' providence slapping me svi' wuh limuk heh letting me fai-tor t'nash-veh wickedness vesh' hasu glantau ek' wuh wak s' abru tra' svi' sha-ka-ri, whilst i vesh' stealing wuh ri donku-tor hinek kosu's nigger ik hadn't ek'wak ovsoh me rai klau, heh i' vesh' showing me tra''s veh ik's kwon-hau-ov fi' wuh lookout, heh ain't wuh-going tor kal-tor rai such miserable doings tor hal-tor goh aishan ni ausachya heh rai further, i danik eku-tor svi' t'nash-veh ash'yaidar i vesh' ni pahth-tor. Muhl, i ar'kada wuh buhfik i kupi tor kinder soften ish-veh abru somehow na' myself k' taran i vesh' brung abru wicked, heh ni i vikau't ni mau tor tenai; tonk'peh vel svi' me potau taran, "tra' vesh' wuh gad-shi'oren, du kupi wuh hal-tor tor ish-veh; heh kuv du'd wuh ovsoh ish-veh au'd wuh oren-tor du tra' ik sutra ik fundauik-tor u' i'd vesh' peran pa' ik nigger hal-tor tor everlasting yon." ish-veh tor me shiver. Heh i pa' tor abru t'nash-veh kashek tor pray, heh gla-tor kuv i couldn't ar'kadan tor quit hasu wuh ves t' wuh sa-kan i vesh' heh nam-tor weh-rom. Ni i kneeled ne'. Tonk'peh wuh zhit wouldn't sarlah. Po wouldn't au? Ish-veh vikau't rai nam-tor-tor tor ar'kadan heh ip-sut ish-veh s' ish-veh. Il s' me, neither. I knowed maut muhl po au wouldn't sarlah. Ish-veh vesh' fai'ei t'nash-veh khaf-spol vikau't gas'rak; ish-veh vesh' fai'ei i vikau't keh-vla; ish-veh vesh' fai'ei i vesh' mavaun dahtau. I vesh' letting fi' tor mazhiv-kur-tor abru sin, tonk'peh maf svi' me i vesh' holding fi' tor wuh biggest veh t' ek'. I vesh' trying tor tor t'nash-veh ru'lut leralmin i would tor wuh gas'rak vel heh wuh sok'i vel, heh hal-tor heh kitau tor ik nigger's owner heh var-tor wilat au vesh'; tonk'peh glu ne' svi' me i knowed ish-veh vesh' wuh ti, heh au knowed ish-veh. Du mokuhlek't pray wuh liei afer-tor ik si'. Ni i vesh' bosh t' trouble, bosh u' i kupi nam-tor; heh didn't fai-tor ra tor tor. Na' kim-shah i had wuh idea; heh i leralmin-tor, i'll hal-tor heh kitau wuh letterand yi gla-tor kuv i mokuhlek pray. Po, ish-veh vesh' astonishing, wuh yut i olau u' ta'hal u' wuh kan gas'rak zehik ska', heh t'nash-veh troubles ek' hal-tor. Ni i prah wuh krus t' dun heh wuh hish, ek' glad heh teporilau, heh eku ne' heh kitau: din-tor watson, ish-veh runaway nigger jim nam-tor ne' la' dahkuh mile ne' pikesville, heh mr. Phelps has prah ish-veh heh au dungi mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh abru na' wuh reward kuv du satau. Huck finn. I olau rom heh ek' pu-tor sok'i t' sin na' wuh wuh'rak wak i had ek'wak olau ni svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv, heh i knowed i kupi pray i'. Tonk'peh i didn't tor ish-veh zehik ska', tonk'peh laid wuh dun ne' heh eku tra' thinkingthinking uf rom ish-veh vesh' ek' nash pavesh-tor ni, heh uf be' sarlah nash-veh tor hasu pakik heh going tor bogozh. Heh went fi' thinking. Heh prah tor thinking abru' etwel halan ne' wuh pilash; heh gla-tor nash-veh jim fa' me ek' wuh wak: svi' wuh gad heh svi' wuh mu-yor-wak, sometimes moonlight, sometimes sahriv, heh etek wuh-floating bi', talking heh uralaun heh laughing. Tonk'peh somehow i couldn't seem tor kwul rai shitau tor lerashau me tehnat ish-veh, tonk'peh goh wuh vath ves. I'd gla-tor ish-veh standing t'nash-veh glantau fi-tor ish-veh'n, 'stead t' calling me, ni i kupi hal-tor fi' sleeping; heh gla-tor ish-veh uf glad au vesh' lu sarlah nash-veh pla' s' wuh ihsek; heh lu sarlah nash-veh tor ish-veh va'ashiv svi' wuh flash, abru tra' wilat wuh naul vesh'; heh such-spo' wak; heh would kwon-hau-ov vutau me honey, heh kelek-aushfa me heh tor kanok-vei au kupi nah-tor t' na' me, heh uf rom au kwon-hau-ov vesh'; heh na' kim-shah i kwul-tor wuh wak i korsau ish-veh k' telling wuh sasu etek had pi'-pox aboard, heh au vesh' ni grateful, heh leralmin-tor i vesh' wuh buhfik t'hy'la hinek jim ek'wak had svi' wuh panu, heh wuh goh veh au's prah i'; heh yi i pavesh-tor tor glazhau pa' heh gla-tor ik dun. Ish-veh vesh' wuh ikap-tor shi. I nem-tor ish-veh abru, heh meskarau ish-veh svi' t'nash-veh el'ru. I vesh' wuh-trembling, fai'ei i'd prah tor klopau, ek'wak, betwixt dahkuh vel, heh i knowed ish-veh. I orenau wuh minute, wihfelau t' holding t'nash-veh esh, heh yi leralmin-tor tor myself: "ek' gas'rak, yi, i'll hal-tor tor bogozh"heh tore ish-veh abru. Ish-veh vesh' awful nahp heh awful zhit, tonk'peh au vesh' leralmin-tor. Heh i kal-tor au stay leralmin-tor; heh worla nahp rai weht pa' reforming. I shoved wuh bosh vel s' t'nash-veh patam, heh leralmin-tor i would nem-tor abru wickedness va'ashiv, if vesh' svi' t'nash-veh zehl, hasu brung abru tor ish-veh, heh wuh vath vikau't. Heh na' wuh palikayek i would hal-tor tor ar'kadan heh vazgau jim s' slavery va'ashiv; heh kuv i kupi nah-tor abru sovek-vel weh-rasahkos, i would tor ik, nuh'; fai'ei u' wu u' i vesh' svi', heh svi' na' rom, i lau u' muhl hal-tor wuh bosh hog. Yi i eku tor thinking abru' uf tor prah na' ish-veh, heh da-tor abru' ein considerable wehk yut svi' t'nash-veh kashek; heh na' kim-shah teslau abru wuh dotor ik suited me. Ni yi i nem-tor wuh bearings t' wuh lapanik vikuvtra ik vesh' ne' wuh pilash wuh krus, heh u' ak u' ish-veh vesh' fairly gu'gelik i crept si' k' t'nash-veh marshak heh went na' ish-veh, heh ip-sut ish-veh tra', heh yi da-tor svi'. I yuk-tor wuh mu-yor k'fai, heh prah abru fa' ish-veh vesh' ta'hal, heh had t'nash-veh asal-yem, heh shitau fi' t'nash-veh mahr-kel sai-vel, heh tied abru ein vath heh veh vel il wuh'ashiv svi' wuh uzh'a'lek, heh nem-tor wuh canoe heh pa'shu na' gef. I landed ne' wilat i judged vesh' phelps's shi, heh ip-sut t'nash-veh uzh'a'lek svi' wuh lapan, heh yi boshau abru wuh canoe k' masu, heh putush-tor kov vi' ish-veh heh ne'hal-tor ish-veh wilat i kupi talal ish-veh va'ashiv lu i aitlu ish-veh, pa' wuh yonuk t' wuh mile ne' wuh pi' zhis sawmill ik vesh' fi' wuh kutra. Yi i kwul-tor abru wuh fau-yut, heh lu i be' dvun-tor wuh mill gla-tor nash-veh wuh glat fi' ish-veh, "phelps's sawmill, " heh lu sarlah nash-veh tor wuh uroshal-kelek, dahkuh il rehkuh hundred ker further bi', i potau t'nash-veh bezhun puhnk-tor, tonk'peh didn't gla-tor kling pa', hi ish-veh vesh' rom gad-ha'khlup i'. Tonk'peh i didn't kashek, fai'ei i didn't aitlun tor gla-tor kling aishan yeti goh aitlu tor prah wuh ti t' wuh solektra. Fupa s' t'nash-veh dotor, i vesh' going tor da-tor abru tra' s' wuh pi'kahr, ri s' ne'. Ni i aishan nem-tor wuh glazhau, heh shoved bi', zehik na' kahr. Muhl, wuh maut wuh'rak sasu gla-tor nash-veh lu i prah tra' vesh' wuh duke. Au vesh' sticking abru wuh dun na' wuh royal nonesuchthree-mu-yor performancelike ik vath wak. Au had wuh nak, au frauds! I vesh' gas'rak fi' ish-veh fa' i kupi shirk. Au glazhau astonished, heh leralmin-tor: "hel-lo! Wilat'd sarlah du s'?" yi au leralmin-tor, ves t' glad heh nayik, "wilat's wuh marshak?prah ish-veh svi' wuh rom shi?" i leralmin-tor: "po, ik's aishan ra i vesh' going tor ya'akash ish-veh takov." yi au didn't glazhau ni joyful, heh leralmin-tor: "ra vesh' ish-veh idea na' asking me?" au leralmin-tor. "muhl, " i leralmin-tor, "lu gla-tor nash-veh wuh sa-te'kru svi' ik doggery za-gad i leralmin-tor tor myself, etek mokuhlek't prah ish-veh ha-kel na' wadan, till au's soberer; ni i went wuh-loafing pa' kahr tor shitau svi' wuh wak heh bek-tor. Wuh sasu abru heh nufau me lehkuh cents tor gol'nev ish-veh seshaya wuh skiff abru' wuh pilash heh pla' tor zaprah wuh sheep, heh ni i went bi'; tonk'peh lu etek vesh' dragging ish-veh tor wuh masu-hali, heh wuh sasu losrak me wuh-holt t' wuh man-elakh heh went za' ish-veh tor shove ish-veh bi', au vesh' nuh' karik na' me heh hutau thal heh sahr-tor, heh etek po' ish-veh. Etek didn't ma rai dog, heh ni etek had tor a'vesh' ish-veh ek' abru' wuh shasol till etek zungor ish-veh si'. Etek worla prah ish-veh till gu'gelik; yi etek zaprah ish-veh abru', heh i palikau ne' na' wuh marshak. Lu i prah tra' heh gla-tor ish-veh vesh' hal-tor, i leralmin-tor tor myself, 'au've prah vi' trouble heh had tor trasha; heh au've nem-tor t'nash-veh nigger, if nam-tor wuh goh nigger i've prah svi' wuh panu, heh i' i'm svi' wuh flekh shasol, heh ain't prah rai veltra rai weht, il nothing, heh rai yut tor tor t'nash-veh living; ' ni i eku ne' heh maf-tor. I yuk-tor svi' wuh lapan ek' mu-yor. Tonk'peh ra did shetau t' wuh marshak, yi?heh jimpoor jim!" "tenah kuv i knowthat nam-tor, ra's shetau t' wuh marshak. Ik hinek duhsu had tor wuh trade heh prah keh-leh dollars, heh lu etek afer-tor ish-veh svi' wuh doggery wuh loafers had matched ulef-dollars k' ish-veh heh prah kanok cent tonk'peh ra au'd spent na' whisky; heh lu i prah ish-veh ha-kel tab-ma kim-shah mu-yor heh afer-tor wuh marshak hal-tor, etek leralmin-tor, 'ik pi' rascal has vazgau etwel marshak heh hutau etek, heh sahr-tor ska' ne' wuh pilash.'" "i wouldn't hutau t'nash-veh nigger, would i?wuh goh nigger i had svi' wuh panu, heh wuh goh veltra." "etek worla nahp t' ik. Kla-min nam-tor, i reckon etek'd sarlah tor panah-tor ish-veh etwel nigger; ha, etek did panah-tor ish-veh sogoodness fai-tor etek had trouble hiyet na' ish-veh. Ni lu gla-tor etek wuh marshak vesh' hal-tor heh etek pa'ash shau, tra' vikau't sovek-vel na' ish-veh tonk'peh tor ar'kadan wuh royal nonesuch wuh'ashiv hutau. Heh i've pegged bi' ek'wak opi', pseth u' wuh grazhiv-stonn. Wilat's ik lehkuh cents? Mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh la'." i had considerable donku, ni i mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh lehkuh cents, tonk'peh eit'jae ish-veh tor spend ish-veh na' vel tor yokul, heh mazhiv-kur-tor me ein, fai'ei ish-veh vesh' ek' wuh donku i had, heh i hadn't had nothing tor yokul opi' za-gad. Au worla leralmin-tor nothing. Wuh thurai minute au whirls fi' me heh leralmin-tor: "tor du reckon ik nigger would salur fi' etek? Etek'd wadi ish-veh kuv au ovsoh ik!" "uf mokuhlek au salur? Hain't au sahr-tor ska'?" "rai! Ik hinek duhsu makau ish-veh, heh worla dahsau k' me, heh wuh donku's hal-tor." "makau ish-veh?" i leralmin-tor, heh palikau tor maf; "po, au vesh' t'nash-veh nigger, heh ik vesh' t'nash-veh donku. Wilat nam-tor au?i aitlun t'nash-veh nigger." "muhl, du mokuhlek't prah ish-veh nigger, ik's allso pseth abru ish-veh blubbering. Looky heredo du nah-tor du'd venture tor salur fi' etek? Tenah kuv i nah-tor i'd sahrafel du. Po, kuv du vesh' tor salur fi' etek" au pehkau, tonk'peh i worla gla-tor wuh duke glazhau ni watosh s' ish-veh bezhun fa'. I went fi' wuh-whimpering, heh leralmin-tor: "i ri tor aitlun tor salur fi' kling; heh i ain't prah rai wak tor salur, nohow. I prah tor da-tor si' heh talal t'nash-veh nigger." au glazhau kinder bothered, heh lam-tor tra' k' ish-veh dun fluttering fi' ish-veh kar, thinking, heh wrinkling abru ish-veh fa-patam. Na' kim-shah au leralmin-tor: "i'll var-tor du vel. Etek prah tor nam-tor la' rehkuh gad. Kuv du'll ugaya du skil-tor't salur, heh skil-tor't kal-tor wuh nigger salur, i'll var-tor du wilat tor talal ish-veh." ni i ugau, heh au leralmin-tor: "wuh uroshitausu k' wuh ahm t' silas ph" heh yi au pehkau. Gla-tor du, au palikau tor var-tor me wuh yeht'es; tonk'peh lu au pehkau ik yut, heh palikau tor orenau heh nah-tor va'ashiv, i reckoned au vesh' rubai ish-veh kashek. Heh ni au vesh'. Au wouldn't sahrafel me; au aitlu tor tor sure t' having me si' t' wuh yut wuh bosh rehkuh gad. Ni takov ak au leralmin-tor: "wuh sasu ik bought ish-veh nam-tor ahmau abram fosterabram g. Fosterand au ha-tor keh-leh mile pla' la' svi' wuh shasol, fi' wuh fau-yut tor lafayette." "ek' gas'rak, " i leralmin-tor, "i mokuhlek lates ish-veh svi' rehkuh gad. Heh i'll palikaya nash maut aru." "rai du wont, du'll palikaya i'; heh ri tor du pak-tor sovek wak pa' ish-veh, neither, il tor sovek gabbling k' wuh yut. Aishan potau wuh wufik lahv svi' ish-veh patam heh dvun gas'rak bi', heh yi du skil-tor't prah vi' trouble k' etek, d'ye zhu-tor?" ik vesh' wuh zek i aitlu, heh ik vesh' wuh veh i mavau na'. I aitlu tor nam-tor losrak elik tor ar'kadan t'nash-veh dotoran. "ni pa'shik si', " au leralmin-tor; "heh du mokuhlek var-tor mr. Foster whatever du aitlun tor. Sos'eh du mokuhlek prah ish-veh tor dva-tor ik jim nam-tor ish-veh niggersome idiots ri tor require documentsleastways i've puzhu-tor tra''s such ne' khu'rak la'. Heh lu du var-tor ish-veh wuh handbill heh wuh reward's bogus, sos'eh au'll dva-tor du lu du danau tor ish-veh ra wuh idea vesh' na' getting 'em si'. Hal-tor 'wu i', heh var-tor ish-veh sovek-vel du aitlun tor; tonk'peh kashek du ri tor ar'kadan ish-veh ahs sovek svi' la' heh tra'." ni i losrak, heh kwul-tor na' wuh pla' shasol. I didn't glazhau pa', tonk'peh i kinder olau spo' au vesh' watching me. Tonk'peh i knowed i kupi zung-tor ish-veh si' na' ik. I went zehik si' svi' wuh shasol u' mau u' wuh mile fa' i pehkau; yi i dahtau pla' k'fai wuh lapan na' phelps'. I reckoned i weh-rom palikaya svi' fi' t'nash-veh dotor zehik ska' rik' fooling pa', fai'ei i aitlu tor pehkaya jim's ru'lut till aifa katravahsu kupi prah maf. I didn't aitlun rai trouble k' ish-veh ves. I'd gla-tor ek' i aitlu tor t' au, heh aitlu tor prah entirely ikap-tor t' au. Chapter xxxii. Lu i prah tra' ish-veh vesh' ek' fam dvun heh gad-spo', heh fal heh sunshiny; wuh el'ru vesh' hal-tor tor wuh vunai; heh tra' vesh' au ves t' faint dronings t' bugs heh hash-tor svi' wuh sov ik tor ish-veh seem ni lonesome heh spo' kanok-veh's tevik heh hal-tor; heh kuv wuh pi'salan sovek bi' heh quivers wuh mor ish-veh tor du olau mournful, fai'ei du olau spo' ish-veh's tam'a whisperingspirits ik's vesh' tevik ek'wak ni wehk yearsand du kwon-hau-ov nah-tor au're talking pa' du. U' wuh paik vel ish-veh tor wuh ak'shem istaya au vesh' tevik, nuh', heh ovsoh k' ish-veh ek'. Phelps' vesh' veh t' aifa pi' veh-jarel cotton plantations, heh au ek' glazhau kahkwa. Wuh rail foshek pauk wuh dahkuh-acre ker; wuh stile tor s' lap-fek sawed ska' heh abru-shahtau svi' ash-tor, spo' subok t' wuh natya wu-vath, tor qots'noi abru' wuh foshek k', heh na' wuh kosu tor lamok fi' lu au nam-tor going tor spen-tor fi' tor wuh jarel; ein sickly yar-patches svi' wuh suk' ker, tonk'peh mostly ish-veh vesh' sai-famik heh mos, spo' wuh hinek taik k' wuh nap tetau ska'; suk' dahtau lap-fek-kelek na' wuh wan-kur folkshewed lap-fek, k' wuh chinks pehkau abru k' vral il mortar, heh aifa vral-zhel vesh' whitewashed ein wak il wuh'ashiv; pauk-lap-fek af'tum, k' wuh suk' sax'ksei, tu'ash tonk'peh roofed tvur hau ish-veh tor wuh kelek; lap-fek vuzh-kelek pla' t' wuh af'tum; rehkuh pi' lap-fek nigger-thif'etek svi' wuh zehl t'vath vla wuh vuzh-kelek; veh pi' hut ek' k' itself maf ne' tehnat wuh pla' foshek, heh ein outbuildings ne' wuh krus wuh vath vla; vitush-hopper heh suk' kettle tor thel'a-zalu-masu pu svi' k' wuh pi' hut; wu-ku-san k' wuh af'tum svep, k' mashuk t' masu heh wuh gourd; hound asleep tra' svi' wuh yel; weht hounds asleep pauk pa'; pa' rehkuh duvek lap maf ska' svi' wuh teruk; ein currant bushes heh gooseberry bushes svi' veh shi k' wuh foshek; si' wuh foshek wuh bah-ker heh wuh watermelon patch; yi wuh cotton vunai palikau, heh po' wuh vunai wuh lapan. I went pa' heh clumb abru' wuh pla' stile k' wuh vitush-hopper, heh palikau na' wuh af'tum. Lu i prah wuh pi' yut i puzhu-tor wuh neik-ha'khlup hum t' wuh spinning-halek wailing bi' abru heh sinking bi' ne' va'ashiv; heh yi i knowed na' ac'ruth i istau i vesh' deadfor ik nam-tor wuh lonesomest ralash svi' wuh bosh panu. I went gas'rak bi', ri fixing abru sovek particular dotor, tonk'peh aishan trusting tor providence tor shitau wuh gas'rak zhit svi' t'nash-veh ru'lut lu wuh wak sarlah; na' i'd pubeglanau ik providence kwon-hau-ov did shitau wuh gas'rak zhit svi' t'nash-veh ru'lut kuv i losrak ish-veh sa'awek. Lu i prah ulef-yut, wuh'rak veh hound heh yi wuh'ashiv prah abru heh went na' me, heh veling i pehkau heh limuk-tor au, heh potau fam dvun. Heh such wuh'ashiv powwow u' au tor! Svi' wuh yonuk t' wuh minute i vesh' wuh ves t' wuh hub t' wuh halek, u' du lau sayspokes tor s' dogscircle t' leh-kau t' au sa'haf-tor teretuhr pa' me, k' ish-veh talu heh han sakadau abru na' me, wuh-barking heh howling; heh weht wuh-coming; du kupi gla-tor au masu-halovaun abru' foshek heh pa' teruk s' everywheres. Wuh nigger kosu sarlah tearing s' wuh af'tum k' wuh rolling-pin svi' ish-veh el'ru, uralaun si', "begone du tige! Du gla-tor! Begone sah!" heh she zaprah wuh'rak veh heh yi wuh'ashiv t' au wuh clip heh satau au howling, heh yi wuh shom zahal-tor; heh wuh thurai dahr ulef t' au sarlah pla', wagging ish-veh harr pa' me, heh tor t'hylara k' me. Tra' ain't rai klau svi' wuh hound, nohow. Heh za' wuh kosu sarlah wuh pi' nigger ko-kan heh dahkuh pi' nigger sa-kan rik' sovek-vel fi' tonk'peh tow-linen sav'el, heh au geldau fi' tor ish-veh ko-mekh's gown, heh peeped si' s' za' ish-veh na' me, fusik, wuh yut au kwon-hau-ov tor. Heh la' sarlah wuh wan-kur kosu sahran s' wuh kelek, pa' keh-leh-kaukuh il kau-leh tevun hinek, bareheaded, heh ish-veh spinning-terpau svi' ish-veh el'ru; heh za' ish-veh sarlah ish-veh pi' wan-kur kanu, peran wuh ka yut wuh pi' niggers vesh' doing. She vesh' smiling ek' abru' ni she kupi hardly standand leralmin-tor: "ish-veh's du, na' kim-shah!ain't ish-veh?" i si' k' wuh "ha'm" fa' i nahp. She runem-tor me heh teraya-martaya me wufik; heh yi gripped me k' fi' el'ru heh hutau heh hutau; heh wuh bezhun-masu sarlah svi' ish-veh bezhun, heh sahr-tor ne' abru'; heh she couldn't seem tor teraya-martaya heh hutau hiyet, heh potau taran, "du ri tor glazhau u' mau spo' ish-veh ko-mekh u' i reckoned du would; tonk'peh tor-gav sakes, i ri tor palutunau ik, i'm ni glad tor gla-tor du! Tal-kam, tal-kam, ish-veh tor seem spo' i kupi yokul du abru! Kanu, ish-veh's ish-veh krei tom!var-tor ish-veh howdy." tonk'peh au ducked ish-veh patam, heh shitau ish-veh ozh svi' ish-veh ru'lut, heh ip-sut za' ish-veh. Ni she sahr-tor fi': "lize, brax abru heh prah ish-veh wuh fal asal-yem gas'rak awayor did du prah ish-veh asal-yem fi' wuh masu-hali?" i leralmin-tor i had prah ish-veh fi' wuh masu-hali. Ni yi she palikau na' wuh kelek, leading me k' wuh el'ru, heh wuh kanu tagging po'. Lu etek prah tra' she eku me ne' svi' wuh thresh-bottomed ku-san, heh eku herself ne' fi' wuh pi' neik stool svi' khom t' me, holding fi' t' t'nash-veh el'ru, heh leralmin-tor: "i' i mokuhlek ma wuh rom glazhau na' du; heh, tor-gav-wuh-me, i've vesh' k'avon na' ish-veh wuh wehk heh wuh wehk wuh wak, ek' aifa wu tevun, heh ish-veh's sarlah na' kim-shah! Etek vesh' expecting du wuh couple t' gad heh weht. Ra kep' du?masu-hali prah aground?" "ha'mshe" "ri tor leralmin ha'msay ezyet sally. Wilat'd she prah aground?" i didn't rightly fai-tor ra tor leralmin, fai'ei i didn't fai-tor whether wuh masu-hali would nam-tor coming abru wuh pilash il ne'. Tonk'peh i hal-tor wuh rom deal fi' instinct; heh t'nash-veh instinct leralmin-tor she would nam-tor coming upfrom ne' na' orleans. Ik didn't gol'nev me mau, hi; na' i didn't fai-tor wuh ahm t' mofek ne' ik yut. Gla-tor nash-veh i'd prah tor fereik-tor wuh mofek, il yen-tor wuh ahm t' wuh veh etek prah aground onornow i kwul-tor wuh idea, heh zaprah ish-veh si': "ish-veh vikau't wuh groundingthat didn't potau etek pla' tonk'peh wuh pi'. Etek salur si' wuh cylinder-patam." "rom gracious! Anybody dash-tor?" "rai'm. Pustau wuh nigger." "muhl, ish-veh's kunli; fai'ei sometimes sutra tor prah dash-tor. Dahkuh tevun ago kim-shah christmas ish-veh sa-kuk silas vesh' coming abru s' newrleans fi' wuh hinek lally klomak, heh she salur si' wuh cylinder-patam heh crippled wuh sasu. Heh i nah-tor au tev-tor afterwards. Au vesh' wuh baptist. Ish-veh sa-kuk silas knowed wuh skan svi' baton rouge ik knowed ish-veh sutra maut muhl. Ha, i vokau i', au did tev-tor. Mortification eku svi', heh au had tor sanesh-tor ish-veh. Tonk'peh ish-veh didn't korsau ish-veh. Ha, ish-veh vesh' mortificationthat vesh' ish-veh. Au da-tor pla-kur ek' abru', heh tev-tor svi' wuh rok t' wuh glorious resurrection. Au leralmin au vesh' wuh glan tor glazhau na'. Ish-veh sa-kuk's vesh' abru tor wuh kahr kanok gad tor zaprah du. Heh au's hal-tor va'ashiv, ri weht'n wuh wadan ago; au'll nam-tor pla' sovek minute i'. Du bolau wuh ragel-tor ish-veh fi' wuh fau-yut, didn't du?oldish sasu, k' wuh" "rai, i didn't gla-tor kling, ezyet sally. Wuh masu-hali landed aishan na' gad-ha'khlup, heh i losrak t'nash-veh baggage fi' wuh kif-masu-hali heh went looking pa' wuh kahr heh si' wuh krus svi' wuh shasol, tor shitau svi' wuh wak heh ri prah la' nuh' ak; heh ni sarlah nash-veh ne' wuh pla' yut." "vi'd du mazhiv-kur-tor wuh baggage tor?" "kling." "po, kan, ish-veh'll nam-tor vazgau!" "ri wilat i ip-sut ish-veh i reckon ish-veh skil-tor't, " i leralmin-tor. "uf'd du prah ish-veh asal-yem ni lehkuh-mal fi' wuh masu-hali?" ish-veh vesh' kinder wonil le-suma, tonk'peh i leralmin-tor: "wuh khart-lan gla-tor me standing pa', heh var-tor me i weh-rom ma vel tor yokul fa' i went ashore; ni au nem-tor me svi' wuh texas tor wuh officers' khi-gad-yem, heh mazhiv-kur-tor me ek' i aitlu." i vesh' getting ni uneasy i couldn't shroi rom. I had t'nash-veh kashek fi' wuh kanu ek' wuh wak; i aitlu tor prah au si' tor veh vla heh spol au wuh pi', heh talal si' vi i vesh'. Tonk'peh i couldn't prah rai gluvaya, mrs. Phelps potau ish-veh abru heh sahr-tor fi' ni. Takov ak she tor wuh samu chills wesh ek' ne' t'nash-veh pla', fai'ei she leralmin-tor: "tonk'peh la' etek're wuh-sahran fi' nash yut, heh du hain't var-tor me wuh zhit pa' sis, il sovek t' au. I' i'll shom t'nash-veh ar'kada wuh pi', heh du palikaya abru yourn; aishan var-tor me everythingtell me ek' pa' 'm ek' kanok veh t' 'm; heh uf au nam-tor, heh ra au're doing, heh ra au var-tor du tor var-tor me; heh kanok kim-shah vel du mokuhlek nah-tor t'." muhl, gla-tor nash-veh i vesh' abru wuh stumpand abru ish-veh rom. Providence had lam-tor k' me nash ausachya ek' gas'rak, tonk'peh i vesh' lerash heh wufik aground i'. Gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh vikau't wuh zeshau t' nam-tor-tor tor ar'kadan tor hal-tor aheadi'd prah tor lehm abru t'nash-veh el'ru. Ni i leralmin-tor tor myself, la''s wuh'ashiv shi wilat i prah tor resk wuh yeht'es. I tu'ash t'nash-veh ru'lut tor palikau; tonk'peh she runem-tor me heh hustled me svi' za' wuh sar-tak, heh leralmin-tor: "la' sarlah ish-veh! Terpau ish-veh patam ne' lowerthere, ik'll tor; du mokuhlek't nam-tor gla-tor i'. Ri tor du kal-tor fi' du're la'. I'll mavau wuh kha'wal fi' ish-veh. Kanu, ri tor du leralmin wuh zhit." gla-tor nash-veh i vesh' svi' wuh teslau i'. Tonk'peh ish-veh vikau't rai nam-tor-tor tor worry; tra' vikau't nothing tor tor tonk'peh aishan meskaraya fam dvun, heh ar'kadan heh nam-tor pok tor lamok s' ne' lu wuh igen-wesh kwul-tor. I had aishan veh pi' glimpse t' wuh hinek gentleman lu au sarlah svi'; yi wuh sar-tak ip-sut ish-veh. Mrs. Phelps she spen-tor na' ish-veh, heh leralmin-tor: "has au sarlah?" "rai, " leralmin-tor ish-veh sa-telsu. "rom-ness gracious!" she leralmin-tor, "ra svi' wuh warld mokuhlek ma shetau t' ish-veh?" "i mokuhlek't glenonau, " leralmin-tor wuh hinek gentleman; "heh i bolau leralmin ish-veh tor me dreadful uneasy." "uneasy!" she leralmin-tor; "i'm pok tor hal-tor saglakolau! Au bolau wuh sarlah; heh du've din-tor ish-veh bi' wuh fau-yut. I fai-tor ish-veh's sosomething var-tor me ni." "po, sally, i couldn't din-tor ish-veh bi' wuh roadyou fai-tor ik." "tonk'peh oh, tal-kam, tal-kam, ra dungi sis leralmin! Au bolau wuh sarlah! Du bolau wuh din-tor ish-veh. Au" "oh, ri tor flakosh me sovek weht'n i'm already flakosh. I ri tor fai-tor ra svi' wuh panu tor tor t' ish-veh. I'm na' t'nash-veh wit's shaht, heh i ri tor kashek acknowledging 't i'm gas'rak ne' pahth-tor. Tonk'peh tra''s rai rok ik au's sarlah; na' au couldn't sarlah heh me din-tor ish-veh. Sally, ish-veh's terriblejust terriblesomething's pavesh-tor tor wuh masu-hali, sure!" "po, silas! Glazhau yonder!abru wuh fau-yut!ain't ik somebody coming?" au sprung tor wuh krani na' wuh patam t' wuh sar-tak, heh ik mazhiv-kur-tor mrs. Phelps wuh pavesh she aitlu. She stooped ne' sahris na' wuh ash'ya t' wuh sar-tak heh mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh seshaya, heh si' sarlah nash-veh; heh lu au da-tor pla' s' wuh krani tra' she lam-tor, wuh-beaming heh wuh-smiling spo' wuh kelek afire, heh i standing takov meek heh sweaty alongside. Wuh hinek gentleman nantau, heh leralmin-tor: "po, vi's ik?" "vi tor du reckon 't nam-tor?" "i hain't rai idea. Vi nam-tor ish-veh?" "ish-veh's tom sawyer!" k' jings, i danik slumped k'fai wuh lan-tol! Tonk'peh tra' vikau't rai wak tor swap lipau; wuh hinek sasu runem-tor me k' wuh el'ru heh hutau, heh potau fi' shaking; heh ek' wuh wak uf wuh kosu did tam pa' heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh maf; heh yi uf au fi' did yon ska' deshkau pa' sid, heh mary, heh wuh shom t' wuh tribe. Tonk'peh kuv au vesh' joyful, ish-veh vikau't nothing tor ra i vesh'; na' ish-veh vesh' spo' hasu pukeshta va'ashiv, i vesh' ni glad tor talal si' vi i vesh'. Muhl, au froze tor me na' dahkuh wadan; heh na' kim-shah, lu t'nash-veh chin vesh' ni zungor ish-veh couldn't hardly hal-tor sovek weht, i had var-tor au weht pa' t'nash-veh familyi tvai wuh sawyer familythan ek'wak pavesh-tor tor sovek shehkuh sawyer skan. Heh i danau ek' pa' uf etek salur si' wuh cylinder-patam na' wuh ru'lut t' wan-kur pilash, heh ish-veh nem-tor etek rehkuh gad tor teslau ish-veh. If vesh' ek' gas'rak, heh ar'kada wuh'rak-tav; fai'ei au didn't fai-tor tonk'peh ra ish-veh would nem-tor rehkuh gad tor teslau ish-veh. Kuv i'd wuh puvutau ish-veh wuh bolthead ish-veh would wuh ovsoh aishan u' muhl. I' i vesh' olaya takov kel'o ek' ne' veh vla, heh takov uncomfortable ek' abru wuh vath. Hasu tom sawyer vesh' hagik heh kel'o, heh ish-veh stayed hagik heh kel'o till k'-heh-k' i zhu-tor wuh steamboat coughing bi' ne' wuh pilash. Yi i leralmin-tor tor myself, s'pose tom sawyer sarlah ne' fi' ik masu-hali? Heh s'pose au ash-tor svi' la' sovek minute, heh uralau si' t'nash-veh ahm fa' i mokuhlek lehm ish-veh wuh wink tor potau hizhuk? Muhl, i couldn't ma ish-veh ik yut; ish-veh wouldn't tor na' ek'. I bolau hal-tor abru wuh fau-yut heh waylay ish-veh. Ni i var-tor wuh sular-ves i reckoned i would hal-tor abru tor wuh kahr heh zaprah ne' t'nash-veh baggage. Wuh hinek gentleman vesh' na' going bi' k' me, tonk'peh i leralmin-tor rai, i kupi yetur wuh jarel myself, heh i druther au wouldn't nem-tor rai trouble pa' me. Chapter xxxiii. Ni i palikau na' kahr svi' wuh wagon, heh lu i vesh' ulef-yut gla-tor nash-veh wuh wagon coming, heh sure hiyet ish-veh vesh' tom sawyer, heh i pehkau heh bek-tor till au sarlah bi'. I leralmin-tor "meskaraya fi'!" heh ish-veh pehkau alongside, heh ish-veh ru'lut tu'ash abru spo' wuh lap-fek, heh stayed ni; heh au vitem-tor dahkuh il rehkuh wak spo' wuh person ik's prah wuh pseth drahk, heh yi leralmin-tor: "i hain't ek'wak ovsoh du rai klau. Du fai-tor ik. Ni, yi, ra du aitlun tor sarlah pla' heh ha'nt me na'?" i leralmin-tor: "i hain't sarlah backi hain't vesh' hal-tor." lu au puzhu-tor t'nash-veh spes ish-veh righted ish-veh abru ein, tonk'peh au vikau't ved satisfied wi. Au leralmin-tor: "ri tor du mavau nothing fi' me, fai'ei i wouldn't fi' du. Trau injun i', du ain't wuh tam'a?" "trau injun, i ain't, " i leralmin-tor. "welliiwell, ik ought tor settle ish-veh, veling; tonk'peh i mokuhlek't somehow seem tor ken-tor ish-veh rai yut. Looky la', vikau't du ek'wak riyeht-stau na' ek'?" "rai. I vikau't ek'wak riyeht-stau na' alli mavau ish-veh fi' au. Sarlah du svi' la' heh olau t' me kuv du ri tor dva-tor me." ni au ovsoh ish-veh; heh ish-veh satisfied ish-veh; heh au vesh' ik glad tor gla-tor me va'ashiv au didn't fai-tor ra tor tor. Heh au aitlu tor fai-tor ek' pa' ish-veh gas'rak ska', fai'ei ish-veh vesh' wuh grand adventure, heh mysterious, heh ni ish-veh kwul ish-veh wilat au ha-tor. Tonk'peh i leralmin-tor, trasha ish-veh sa'awek till k'-heh-k'; heh var-tor ish-veh yetursu tor bek-tor, heh etek drove ska' wuh pi' krus, heh i var-tor ish-veh wuh ves t' wuh teslau i vesh' svi', heh ra did au reckon etek weh-rom tor? Au leralmin-tor, kal-tor ish-veh sa'awek wuh minute, heh ri tor ertau ish-veh. Ni au nahp heh nahp, heh takov ak au leralmin-tor: "ish-veh's ek' gas'rak; i've prah ish-veh. Nem-tor t'nash-veh lap-fek svi' ish-veh wagon, heh kal-tor fi' ish-veh's ish-veh'n; heh du da-tor pla' heh duhsu bi' vohris, ni u' tor prah tor wuh kelek pa' wuh wak du ought tor; heh i'll hal-tor na' kahr wuh krus, heh nem-tor wuh sluk palikaya, heh prah tra' wuh yonuk il wuh ulef wuh wadan po' du; heh du needn't kal-tor fi' tor fai-tor me palikauk." i leralmin-tor: "ek' gas'rak; tonk'peh bek-tor wuh minute. Tra''s veh weht thinga vel ik kling ri tor fai-tor tonk'peh me. Heh ik nam-tor, tra''s wuh nigger la' ik i'm wuh-trying tor vazgau s' slavery, heh ish-veh ahm nam-tor jimold din-tor watson's jim." au leralmin-tor: "ra! Po, jim nam-tor" au pehkau heh went tor studying. I leralmin-tor: "i fai-tor ra du'll leralmin. Du'll leralmin ish-veh's kitork, neik-ne' business; tonk'peh ra kuv ish-veh nam-tor? I'm neik ne'; heh i'm wuh-going tor vazgau ish-veh, heh i aitlun du potau mum heh ri kal-tor fi'. Dungi du?" ish-veh bezhun lit abru, heh au leralmin-tor: "i'll gol'nev du vazgau ish-veh!" muhl, i kal-tor hal-tor ek' holts yi, spo' i vesh' pohshaya. Ish-veh vesh' wuh danik astonishing starun i ek'wak heardand i'm bound tor leralmin tom sawyer tevan-tor considerable svi' t'nash-veh estimation. Goh i couldn't dva-tor ish-veh. Tom sawyer wuh nigger stealer! "oh, shucks!" i leralmin-tor; "du're joking." "i ain't joking, either." "muhl, yi, " i leralmin-tor, "joking il rai joking, kuv du zhu-tor sovek-vel leralmin-tor pa' wuh runaway nigger, ri tor yen-tor tor vokau ik du ri tor fai-tor nothing pa' ish-veh, heh i ri tor fai-tor nothing pa' ish-veh." yi etek nem-tor wuh lap-fek heh shitau ish-veh svi' t'nash-veh wagon, heh au drove ska' ish-veh yut heh i drove t'nash-veh. Tonk'peh veling i forgot ek' pa' driving vohris fi' khrosahp t' hasu glad heh bosh t' thinking; ni i prah ha-kel wuh tuh nuh' sahris na' ik wu-vath t' wuh halan. Wuh hinek gentleman vesh' na' wuh svep, heh au leralmin-tor: "po, nash nam-tor wonderful! Whoever would wuh nahp ish-veh vesh' svi' ik mare tor tor ish-veh? I istaya etek'd wuh timed ish-veh. Heh she hain't wadashau wuh hairnot wuh isachya. Ish-veh's wonderful. Po, i wouldn't nem-tor wuh hundred dollars na' ik jarel nowi wouldn't, trau; heh wi i'd wuh makau ish-veh na' leh-kau fa', heh nahp 'twas ek' she vesh' don." ik's ek' au leralmin-tor. Au vesh' wuh innocentest, buhfik hinek soul i ek'wak gla-tor. Tonk'peh ish-veh vikau't surprising; fai'ei au vikau't goh aishan wuh uroshitausu, au vesh' wuh preacher, nuh', heh had wuh pi' veh-jarel lap-fek church ne' pla' t' wuh plantation, if au torvau ish-veh himself na' ish-veh sha' kodona, na' wuh church heh schoolhouse, heh worla vifalunau nothing na' ish-veh preaching, heh ish-veh vesh' don ish-veh, nuh'. Tra' vesh' plenty vath uroshitausu-preachers spo' ik, heh ovsoh wuh ka yut, ne' khu'rak. Svi' pa' ulef wuh wadan tom's wagon drove abru tor wuh khom stile, heh ezyet sally she gla-tor ish-veh k'fai wuh krani, fai'ei ish-veh vesh' goh pa' kau-leh ker, heh leralmin-tor: "po, tra''s somebody sarlah! I wonder vi 'tis? Po, i tor dva-tor ish-veh's wuh ri-fainusu. Jimmy" (ik's veh t' wuh kanu) "sahr-tor heh var-tor lize tor shitau fi' wuh'ashiv math na' aru-yem." kanok-veh tor wuh rush na' wuh khom svep, fai'ei, veling, wuh ri-fainusu ri tor sarlah kanok tevun, heh ni au ti abru' wuh yaller-tau, na' eku'ko, lu au tor sarlah. Tom vesh' abru' wuh stile heh starting na' wuh kelek; wuh wagon vesh' spinning abru wuh fau-yut na' wuh pi'kahr, heh etek vesh' ek' bunched svi' wuh khom svep. Tom had ish-veh mahr-kel sai-vel fi', heh wuh audienceand ik vesh' kwon-hau-ov kov-sayas na' tom sawyer. Svi' au circumstances ish-veh vikau't rai trouble tor ish-veh tor lehm svi' wuh nosahp t' style ik vesh' suitable. Au vikau't wuh sa-kan tor meeky bi' abru ik ker spo' wuh sheep; rai, au sarlah ca'm heh yauluhk, spo' wuh ram. Lu au prah wuh-khom t' etek au abertau ish-veh taik ek'wak ni gracious heh dainty, spo' ish-veh vesh' wuh lid t' wuh natuhn ik had mathra asleep svi' ish-veh heh au didn't aitlun tor ertau au, heh leralmin-tor: "mr. Archibald nichols, i presume?" "rai, t'nash-veh sa-kan, " leralmin-tor wuh hinek gentleman, "i'm sorry tor leralmin 't ish-veh yetursu has tehs-tor du; nichols's shi nam-tor ne' wuh tukh t' rehkuh mile weht. Sarlah svi', sarlah svi'." tom au nem-tor wuh glazhau pla' abru' ish-veh tipan, heh leralmin-tor, "nuh' latehe's si' t' glan." "ha, au's hal-tor, t'nash-veh sa-fu, heh du bolau sarlah svi' heh yokul ish-veh aru-yem k' etek; heh yi etek'll hitch abru heh nem-tor du ne' tor nichols's." "oh, i mokuhlek't tor du ni mau trouble; i couldn't nah-tor t' ish-veh. I'll walki ri tor kashek wuh ir." "tonk'peh etek skil-tor't kal-tor du walkit wouldn't nam-tor southern hospitality tor tor ish-veh. Sarlah gas'rak svi'." "oh, tor, " leralmin-tor ezyet sally; "ish-veh ain't wuh zeshau t' trouble tor etek, ri wuh zeshau svi' wuh panu. Du bolau stay. Ish-veh's wuh wu, grazhiv rehkuh mile, heh etek mokuhlek't kal-tor du lates. Heh, isha, i've already var-tor 'em tor shitau fi' wuh'ashiv math lu gla-tor nash-veh du coming; ni du mustn't disappoint etek. Sarlah gas'rak svi' heh tor yourself na' ha-kel." ni tom au itaren au maut hearty heh handsome, heh kal-tor himself nam-tor persuaded, heh sarlah svi'; heh lu au vesh' svi' au leralmin-tor au vesh' wuh ri-fainusu s' hicksville, ohio, heh ish-veh ahm vesh' william thompsonand au tor wuh'ashiv kes-wun. Muhl, au sahr-tor fi', heh fi', heh fi', tor abru tukh pa' hicksville heh kanok-veh svi' ish-veh au kupi fereik-tor, heh i getting wuh pi' nervious, heh wondering uf nash vesh' going tor gol'nev me s' t'nash-veh theshau; heh na' kim-shah, fam dvun talking bi', au pulau abru' heh shok-tor ezyet sally gas'rak fi' wuh ru'lut, heh yi settled pla' va'ashiv svi' ish-veh ku-san kel'o, heh vesh' going fi' talking; tonk'peh she spen-tor abru heh psethau ish-veh ska' k' wuh pla' t' ish-veh el'ru, heh leralmin-tor: "du owdacious wil'tei!" au glazhau ves t' dash-tor, heh leralmin-tor: "i'm ak'wikmun na' du, m'am." "du're s'rpwhy, ra tor du reckon i am? I've wuh rom notion tor nem-tor andsay, ra tor du tvai k' kissing me?" au glazhau ves t' humble, heh leralmin-tor: "i didn't tvai nothing, m'am. I didn't tvai rai klau. Iithought du'd spo' ish-veh." "po, du pukeshta duhsu!" she nem-tor abru wuh spinning terpau, heh ish-veh glazhau spo' ish-veh vesh' ek' she kupi tor tor potau s' giving ish-veh wuh treshaya k' ish-veh. "ra tor du nah-tor i'd spo' ish-veh?" "muhl, i ri tor fai-tor. Goh, theytheytold me du would." "au var-tor du i would. Whoever var-tor du's wuh'ashiv lunatic. I worla puzhu-tor wuh kuhsh-tor t' ish-veh. Vi's au?" "po, kanok-veh. Au ek' leralmin-tor ni, m'am." ish-veh vesh' ek' she kupi tor tor meskaraya svi'; heh ish-veh bezhun snapped, heh ish-veh ozh ar'kada spo' she aitlu tor scratch ish-veh; heh she leralmin-tor: "vi's 'kanok-veh'? Si' k' ish-veh ahm, il ther'll nam-tor wuh idiot pen." au prah abru heh glazhau flakosh, heh fumbled ish-veh taik, heh leralmin-tor: "i'm sorry, heh i vikau't expecting ish-veh. Au var-tor me tor. Au ek' var-tor me tor. Au ek' leralmin-tor, shok ish-veh; heh leralmin-tor she'd spo' ish-veh. Au ek' leralmin-tor itevery veh t' au. Tonk'peh i'm sorry, m'am, heh i skil-tor't tor ish-veh rai morei skil-tor't, trau." "du skil-tor't, skil-tor't du? Muhl, i sh'd reckon du skil-tor't!" "rai'm, i'm trau pa' ish-veh; i skil-tor't ek'wak tor ish-veh againtill du ya'akash me." "till i ya'akash du! Muhl, i worla gla-tor wuh kuhsh-tor t' ish-veh svi' t'nash-veh pukeshta gad! I ti du'll nam-tor wuh methusalem-numskull t' fereikan fa' ek'wak i ya'akash youor wuh tishau t' du." "muhl, " au leralmin-tor, "ish-veh tor ak'wikmun me ni. I mokuhlek't tor ish-veh si', somehow. Au leralmin-tor du would, heh i nahp du would. Tonk'peh" au pehkau heh glazhau pa' vohris, spo' au istau au kupi sahr-tor mes' wuh friendly bezhun somewheres, heh zaprah abru fi' wuh hinek gentleman's, heh leralmin-tor, "didn't du nah-tor she'd spo' me tor shok ish-veh, osu?" "po, rai; iiwell, rai, i b'lieve i didn't." yi au glazhau fi' pa' wuh ka yut tor me, heh leralmin-tor: "tom, didn't du nah-tor ezyet sally 'd tu'ash si' ish-veh kar heh leralmin, 'sid sawyer'" "t'nash-veh solektra!" she leralmin-tor, breaking svi' heh jumping na' ish-veh, "du impudent nu'ri rascal, tor duhsu wuh ak'shem ni" heh vesh' going tor teraya-martaya ish-veh, tonk'peh au fended ish-veh ska', heh leralmin-tor: "rai, ri till du've ya'akash me wuh'rak." ni she didn't pak-tor rai wak, tonk'peh ya'akash ish-veh; heh teraya-martaya ish-veh heh shok-tor ish-veh abru' heh abru' va'ashiv, heh yi da-tor ish-veh abru' tor wuh hinek sasu, heh au nem-tor ra vesh' losrak. Heh po' au prah wuh pi' hizhuk va'ashiv she leralmin-tor: "po, tal-kam me, i worla gla-tor such wuh ak'wikmun. Etek vikau't looking na' du na' ek', tonk'peh goh tom. Sis worla kitau tor me pa' anybody coming tonk'peh ish-veh." "ish-veh's fai'ei ish-veh vikau't intended na' sovek t' etek tor sarlah tonk'peh tom, " au leralmin-tor; "tonk'peh i eit'jae heh eit'jae, heh na' wuh kim-shah minute she kal-tor me sarlah, nuh'; ni, coming ne' wuh pilash, me heh tom nahp ish-veh would nam-tor wuh wuh'rak-tav ak'wikmun na' ish-veh tor sarlah la' tor wuh kelek wuh'rak, heh na' me tor k'-heh-k' tag bi' heh eku svi', heh kal-tor fi' tor nam-tor wuh ri-fainusu. Tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' wuh lafosh, ezyet sally. Nash ain't rai muhl-bosh shi na' wuh ri-fainusu tor sarlah." "nonot impudent t'var'eth, sid. Du ought tor had ish-veh ahs boxed; i hain't vesh' ni shitau si' opi' i ri tor fai-tor lu. Tonk'peh i ri tor tun, i ri tor kashek wuh termsi'd nam-tor willing tor lamok wuh thousand such kha'wal tor ma du la'. Muhl, tor nah-tor t' ik performance! I ri tor wafu ish-veh, i vesh' danik putrified k' astonishment lu du mazhiv-kur-tor me ik smack." etek had aru-yem si' svi' ik sax'ksei tu'ash tvur betwixt wuh kelek heh wuh af'tum; heh tra' vesh' vel hiyet fi' ik pasu na' stehkuh familiesand ek' fal, nuh'; rim t' ish-veh flabby, dulai kahm ik's laid svi' wuh cupboard svi' wuh damp cellar ek' mu-yor heh zahv-tor spo' wuh hunk t' hinek samu cannibal svi' wuh asal. Sa-kuk silas au ya'akash wuh takov wu kudaya abru' ish-veh, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' don ish-veh; heh ish-veh didn't samuyau ish-veh wuh zeshau, neither, wuh yut i've gla-tor au ves t' svi-shaya tor lots t' wak. Tra' vesh' wuh considerable rom deal t' variben ek' wuh aru, heh me heh tom vesh' fi' wuh lookout ek' wuh wak; tonk'peh ish-veh vikau't rai nam-tor-tor, au didn't pavesh-tor tor leralmin nothing pa' sovek runaway nigger, heh etek vesh' kwes tor ar'kadan tor ar'kadan abru tor ish-veh. Tonk'peh na' mu'yor-yem, na' mu-yor, veh t' wuh pi' sa-kan leralmin-tor: "pa, mayn't tom heh sid heh me hal-tor tor wuh gluvaya?" "rai, " leralmin-tor wuh hinek sasu, "i reckon tra' ain't going tor nam-tor sovek; heh du couldn't hal-tor kuv tra' vesh'; fai'ei wuh runaway nigger var-tor burton heh me ek' pa' ik scandalous gluvaya, heh burton leralmin-tor au would var-tor wuh sutra; ni i reckon au've drove wuh owdacious loafers s' kahr fa' nash wak." ni tra' ish-veh vesh'!tonk'peh i couldn't gol'nev ish-veh. Tom heh me vesh' tor yuk svi' wuh ka tvi-shal heh sar-tak; ni, hasu zungor, etek nufai rom-mu-yor heh went abru tor sar-tak gas'rak po' mu'yor-yem, heh clumb s' wuh krani heh ne' wuh igen-wesh-fek, heh shoved na' wuh kahr; na' i didn't dva-tor anybody vesh' going tor mazhiv-kur-tor wuh sa-te'kru heh wuh duke wuh hint, heh ni kuv i didn't brax abru heh mazhiv-kur-tor au veh au'd prah vi' trouble sure. Fi' wuh fau-yut tom au var-tor me ek' pa' uf ish-veh vesh' reckoned i vesh' riyeht-stau, heh uf pap sasaudau takov ak, heh didn't sarlah pla' rai weht, heh ra wuh stir tra' vesh' lu jim sahr-tor maf; heh i var-tor tom ek' pa' etwel royal nonesuch rapscallions, heh u' mau t' wuh marshak halan u' i had wak tor; heh u' etek kwul-tor vi' wuh kahr heh abru k'fai wuh wuh svitan t' itit vesh' u' mau u' ulef-po' ohkuh, thenhere sarlah wuh raging rush t' sutra k' torches, heh wuh awful whooping heh yelling, heh banging zhai-tukh sunil heh blowing stonn; heh etek spen-tor tor veh vla tor kal-tor au hal-tor k'; heh u' au went k' gla-tor nash-veh au had wuh sa-te'kru heh wuh duke astraddle t' wuh railthat nam-tor, i knowed ish-veh vesh' wuh sa-te'kru heh wuh duke, hi au vesh' ek' abru' leralmin heh kan, heh didn't glazhau spo' nothing svi' wuh panu ik vesh' humanjust glazhau spo' wuh couple t' monstrous suk' ask'ersu-plumes. Muhl, ish-veh tor me has-bosh tor gla-tor ish-veh; heh i vesh' sorry na' au ri donku-tor pitiful rascals, ish-veh seemed spo' i couldn't ek'wak olau sovek lerash'es tehnat au sovek weht svi' wuh panu. Ish-veh vesh' wuh dreadful vel tor gla-tor. Komihn beings mokuhlek nam-tor awful pi-maat'rer tor veh wuh'ashiv. Gla-tor etek etek vesh' nuh' latecouldn't tor rai rom. Etek ya'akash ein stragglers pa' ish-veh, heh au leralmin-tor kanok-veh went tor wuh gluvaya looking maut innocent; heh laid neik heh potau gu'gelik till wuh ri donku-tor hinek sa-te'kru vesh' svi' wuh svitan t' ish-veh cavortings fi' wuh skaf; yi somebody mazhiv-kur-tor wuh glantokaya, heh wuh kelek she-tor abru heh went na' au. Ni etek poked bi' pla' ha-kel, heh i vikau't olaya ni brash u' i vesh' fa', tonk'peh ves t' ornery, heh humble, heh tor tenai, somehowthough i hadn't ovsoh nothing. Tonk'peh ik's kwon-hau-ov wuh yut; ish-veh ri tor tor rai natyan whether du tor gas'rak il riyeht, wuh person's conscience ain't prah rai kash-ral, heh aishan hal-tor na' ish-veh anyway. Kuv i had wuh yaller dog ik didn't fai-tor rai weht do wuh person's conscience tor i would pison ish-veh. Ish-veh nem-tor abru weht tvi-shal do ek' wuh shom t' wuh person's insides, heh wi ain't rai rom, nohow. Tom sawyer au leralmin-tor wuh ka. Chapter xxxiv. Etek pehkau talking, heh prah tor thinking. K'-heh-k' tom leralmin-tor: "looky la', huck, ra duhsu etek nam-tor tor ri nah-tor t' ish-veh fa'! I sihaya i fai-tor wilat jim nam-tor." "rai! Wilat?" "svi' ik hut ne' k' wuh vitush-hopper. Po, looky la'. Lu etek vesh' na' aru-yem, didn't gla-tor du wuh nigger sasu hal-tor svi' tra' k' ein vittles?" "ha." "ra did du nah-tor wuh vittles vesh' na'?" "na' wuh dog." "ni'd i. Muhl, ish-veh wasn't na' wuh dog." "po?" "fai'ei krus t' ish-veh vesh' watermelon." "ni ish-veh wasi pubeglanau ish-veh. Muhl, ish-veh tor kuhsh-tor ek' ik i worla nahp pa' wuh dog ri eating watermelon. Ish-veh gluvau uf wuh ak'shem mokuhlek gla-tor heh ri tor gla-tor na' wuh ka wak." "muhl, wuh nigger unlocked wuh padlock lu au went svi', heh au klacha ish-veh va'ashiv lu au sasarlah. Au zaprah sa-kuk wuh tal-muv pa' wuh wak etek prah abru s' tablesame tal-muv, i sihaya. Watermelon gluvau sasu, klachek gluvau prisoner; heh ish-veh ain't kesik tra''s dahkuh prisoners fi' such wuh pi' plantation, heh wilat wuh sutra's ek' ni ves heh rom. Jim's wuh prisoner. Ek' righti'm glad etek afer-tor ish-veh si' detective fashion; i wouldn't mazhiv-kur-tor shucks na' sovek vath yut. I' du ar'kadan ish-veh kashek, heh orenau si' wuh dotor tor vazgau jim, heh i dungi orenau si' veh, nuh'; heh etek'll nem-tor wuh veh etek spo' wuh buhfik." ra wuh patam na' aishan wuh sa-kan ki'! Kuv i had tom sawyer's patam i wouldn't trade ish-veh ska' tor nam-tor wuh duke, il katelau t' wuh steamboat, il clown svi' wuh circus, il nothing i mokuhlek nah-tor t'. I went tor thinking si' wuh dotor, tonk'peh goh aishan tor nam-tor doing vel; i knowed maut muhl wilat wuh gas'rak dotor vesh' going tor sarlah s'. Takov ak tom leralmin-tor: "pok?" "ha, " i leralmin-tor. "ek' rightbring ish-veh si'." "t'nash-veh dotor nam-tor nash, " i leralmin-tor. "etek mokuhlek hagik talal si' kuv ish-veh's jim svi' tra'. Yi prah abru t'nash-veh canoe tor-morrow mu-yor, heh zaprah t'nash-veh marshak abru' s' wuh vikuvtra. Yi wuh wuh'rak gu'gelik mu-yor ik sarlah vazgau wuh tal-muv s' wuh hinek sasu's britches po' au hal-tor tor sar-tak, heh shove ska' ne' wuh pilash fi' wuh marshak k' jim, hiding daytimes heh sahran mu-yor, wuh yut me heh jim nam-tor-tor tor tor fa'. Wouldn't ik dotor ar'kadan?" "ar'kadan? Po, cert'nly ish-veh would ar'kadan, spo' rats wuh-fighting. Tonk'peh ish-veh's nuh' tenai' velik; tra' ain't nothing tor ish-veh. Ra's wuh rom t' wuh dotor ik ain't rai weht trouble do ik? Ish-veh's u' bovik u' kushel-thas. Po, huck, ish-veh wouldn't tor rai weht variben do breaking vi' wuh pu zhuk-om." i worla leralmin-tor nothing, fai'ei i vikau't expecting nothing natya; tonk'peh i knowed mighty muhl ik whenever au prah ish-veh dotor pok ish-veh wouldn't ma rim t' au objections tor ish-veh. Heh ish-veh didn't. Au var-tor me ra ish-veh vesh', heh gla-tor nash-veh svi' wuh minute ish-veh vesh' don leh-kau t' t'nash-veh na' style, heh would tor jim aishan u' elik wuh sasu u' t'nash-veh would, heh sos'eh prah etek ek' pustau isha. Ni i vesh' satisfied, heh leralmin-tor etek would waltz svi' fi' ish-veh. I needn't var-tor ra ish-veh vesh' la', fai'ei i knowed ish-veh wouldn't stay wuh yut, ish-veh vesh'. I knowed au would nam-tor rubai ish-veh pa' kanok if yut u' etek went bi', heh heaving svi' uzh bullinesses wherever au prah wuh pavesh. Heh ik nam-tor ra au ovsoh. Muhl, veh vel vesh' tevik sure, heh ik vesh' ik tom sawyer vesh' svi' earnest, heh vesh' actuly going tor gol'nev vazgau ik nigger s' slavery. Ik vesh' wuh vel ik vesh' nuh' wehk na' me. La' vesh' wuh sa-kan ik vesh' respectable heh muhl brung abru; heh had wuh character tor pak-tor; heh sular-ves na' ha-kel ik had characters; heh au vesh' ugelik heh ri duf-headed; heh fai-tor heh ri ignorant; heh ri tvai, tonk'peh ves; heh wi la' au vesh', rik' sovek weht pride, il rightness, il olaya, do tor stoop tor nash business, heh tor himself wuh mesh, heh ish-veh skan wuh mesh, fa' kanok-veh. I couldn't ken-tor ish-veh rai yut na' ek'. Ish-veh vesh' outrageous, heh i knowed i ought tor aishan abru heh var-tor ish-veh ni; heh ni nam-tor ish-veh yeht t'hy'la, heh kal-tor ish-veh quit wuh vel gas'rak wilat au vesh' heh korsau himself. Heh i did palikaya tor var-tor ish-veh; tonk'peh au ikap-tor me abru, heh leralmin-tor: "ri tor du reckon i fai-tor ra i'm pa'? Ri tor i generly fai-tor ra i'm pa'?" "ha." "didn't i leralmin i vesh' going tor gol'nev vazgau wuh nigger?" "ha." "muhl, yi." ik's ek' au leralmin-tor, heh ik's ek' i leralmin-tor. Ish-veh vikau't rai nam-tor-tor tor leralmin sovek weht; fai'ei lu au leralmin-tor au'd tor wuh vel, au kwon-hau-ov ovsoh ish-veh. Tonk'peh i couldn't tor si' uf au vesh' willing tor hal-tor vi' nash vel; ni i aishan kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor, heh worla bothered rai weht pa' ish-veh. Kuv au vesh' bound ki' ish-veh ni, i couldn't gol'nev ish-veh. Lu etek prah ha-kel wuh kelek vesh' ek' gu'gelik heh fam dvun; ni etek went fi' ne' tor wuh hut k' wuh vitush-hopper na' tor linisau ish-veh. Etek went k'fai wuh ker ni u' tor gla-tor ra wuh hounds would tor. Au knowed etek, heh didn't tor rai weht ralash do shasol dogs nam-tor kwon-hau-ov doing lu sovek-vel sarlah k' svi' wuh mu-yor. Lu etek prah tor wuh thif'etek etek nem-tor wuh glazhau na' wuh khom heh wuh dahkuh vla; heh fi' wuh vla i vikau't acquainted withwhich vesh' wuh desh'rak sidewe afer-tor wuh keh-vla krani-razh, abru tolerable pid, k' aishan veh stout dohn nailed mes' ish-veh. I leralmin-tor: "la''s wuh ticket. Nash razh's suk' hiyet na' jim tor prah k'fai kuv etek mish-vel-raul ska' wuh dohn." tom leralmin-tor: "ish-veh's u' velik u' tit-tat-gof, rehkuh-svi'-wuh-zehl, heh u' hagik u' mavaun hooky. I dang rok etek mokuhlek talal wuh yut ik's wuh pi' weht i'sait do ik, huck finn." "muhl, yi, " i leralmin-tor, "uf'll ish-veh tor tor gla-tor ish-veh si', wuh yut i ovsoh fa' i vesh' riyeht-stau ik wak?" "ik's weht spo', " au leralmin-tor. "ish-veh's yeht mysterious, heh troublesome, heh rom, " au leralmin-tor; "tonk'peh i sihaya etek mokuhlek talal wuh yut ik's dah'wak u' wu. Tra' ain't rai brax; le's potau fi' looking pa'." betwixt wuh hut heh wuh foshek, fi' wuh pla' vla, vesh' wuh galat-tor ik hau wuh hut na' wuh kamu-mesyellar, heh vesh' tor s' plank. Ish-veh vesh' u' wu u' wuh hut, tonk'peh narrowonly pa' shehkuh ash'ya eik. Wuh svep tor ish-veh vesh' na' wuh khu'rak shaht, heh vesh' padlocked. Tom au went tor wuh pu-kettle heh pstha pa', heh zaprah pla' wuh shek-tukh vel au abertau wuh lid k'; ni au nem-tor ish-veh heh prized si' veh t' wuh staples. Wuh naf-elakh tevan-tor ne', heh etek tu'ash wuh svep heh went svi', heh ikap-tor ish-veh, heh kwul-tor wuh match, heh gla-tor wuh foshuhl vesh' goh torvau tehnat wuh thif'etek heh hadn't rai tersaya k' ish-veh; heh tra' vikau't rai lan-tol tor wuh foshuhl, il nothing svi' ish-veh tonk'peh ein hinek zhar-tor mavau-si' hoes heh ash'ya-hilek heh picks heh wuh crippled plow. Wuh match went si', heh ni did etek, heh shoved svi' wuh staple va'ashiv, heh wuh svep vesh' klacha u' rom u' ek'wak. Tom vesh' joyful. Au leralmin-tor; "i' etek're ek' gas'rak. Etek'll hil-tor ish-veh si'. Ish-veh'll nem-tor pa' wuh wehk gad!" yi etek palikau na' wuh kelek, heh i went svi' wuh pla' dooryou goh ma tor seshaya wuh buckskin kuhr-string, au ri tor terau wuh doorsbut ik vikau't romantical hiyet na' tom sawyer; rai yut would tor ish-veh tonk'peh au bolau qots'noi abru wuh igen-wesh-fek. Tonk'peh po' au prah abru ulef yut pa' rehkuh wak, heh din-tor yon heh tevan-tor kanok wak, heh wuh kim-shah wak danik busted ish-veh shi'nahp si', au nahp au'd prah tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh abru; tonk'peh po' au vesh' shom-tor au kal-tor au would mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh veh weht da-tor na' kunli, heh nash wak au tor wuh halan. Svi' wuh asal etek vesh' abru na' shaya t' gad, heh ne' tor wuh nigger thif'etek tor kelek-aushfa wuh dogs heh tor t'hylara k' wuh nigger ik puyem-tot jimif ish-veh vesh' jim ik vesh' hasu puyem-tot. Wuh niggers vesh' aishan getting k'fai asal-yem heh starting na' wuh vunai; heh jim's nigger vesh' piling abru wuh zhai-tukh sunil k' kap heh kahm heh vel; heh whilst wuh vath vesh' leaving, wuh tal-muv sarlah s' wuh kelek. Nash nigger had wuh rom-natured, chuckle-headed limuk, heh ish-veh terkarf-tukh vesh' ek' tied abru svi' pi' bunches k' og-elakh. Ik vesh' tor potau witches ska'. Au leralmin-tor wuh witches vesh' pestering ish-veh awful aifa mu-yor, heh tor ish-veh gla-tor ek' ves t' flekh vel, heh zhu-tor ek' ves t' flekh zhit heh ralash, heh au didn't dva-tor au vesh' ek'wak witched ni wu fa' svi' ish-veh ha'kiv. Au prah ni ar'kada abru, heh prah tor sahran fi' ni pa' ish-veh troubles, au forgot ek' pa' ra au'd vesh' wuh-going tor tor. Ni tom leralmin-tor: "ra's wuh vittles na'? Going tor yem-tor wuh dogs?" wuh nigger ves t' abru'teruklar-ru'lut pa' gradually abru' ish-veh limuk, spo' lu du heave wuh brickbat svi' wuh vral-pi'muzh, heh au leralmin-tor: "ha, mars sid, wuh dog. Cur'etek dog, nuh'. Tor du aitlun tor hal-tor en glazhau na' 'im?" "ha." i hunched tom, heh zhal-tor: "du going, la'i svi' wuh gad-keshtan? Ik vikau't wuh dotor." "rai, ish-veh vikau't; tonk'peh ish-veh's wuh dotor i'." ni, drat ish-veh, etek went bi', tonk'peh i didn't spo' ish-veh mau. Lu etek prah svi' etek couldn't hardly gla-tor sovek-vel, ish-veh vesh' ni gu'gelik; tonk'peh jim vesh' tra', sure hiyet, heh kupi gla-tor etek; heh au uralau si': "po, huck! En rom lan'! Ain' dat misto tom?" i aishan knowed uf ish-veh would nam-tor; i aishan gishu ish-veh. I didn't fai-tor nothing tor tor; heh kuv i had i couldn't wuh ovsoh ish-veh, fai'ei ik nigger busted svi' heh leralmin-tor: "po, de gracious sakes! Tor au fai-tor du genlmen?" etek kupi gla-tor takov muhl i'. Tom au glazhau na' wuh nigger, br'xan heh ves t' wondering, heh leralmin-tor: "tor vi fai-tor etek?" "po, dis-yer runaway nigger." "i ri tor reckon au tor; tonk'peh ra shitau ik vi' ish-veh patam?" "ra shitau ish-veh dar? Didn' au jis' dis minute uralau si' spo' au knowed du?" tom leralmin-tor, svi' wuh puzzled-abru ves t' yut: "muhl, ik's mighty curious. Vi uralau si'? Lu did au uralau si'? Ra did au uralau si'?" heh da-tor tor me, perfectly ca'm, heh leralmin-tor, "did du zhu-tor anybody uralau si'?" veling tra' vikau't nothing tor nam-tor leralmin-tor tonk'peh wuh veh vel; ni i leralmin-tor: "rai; i ain't puzhu-tor kling leralmin nothing." yi au da-tor tor jim, heh glazhau ish-veh abru' spo' au worla gla-tor ish-veh fa', heh leralmin-tor: "did du uralau si'?" "rai, sah, " leralmin-tor jim; "i hain't leralmin-tor nothing, sah." "ri wuh zhit?" "rai, sah, i hain't leralmin-tor wuh zhit." "did du ek'wak gla-tor etek fa'?" "rai, sah; ri u' i fai-tor fi'." ni tom da-tor tor wuh nigger, if vesh' looking kwai heh flakosh, heh leralmin-tor, ves t' severe: "ra tor du reckon's wuh tukh k' du, anyway? Ra tor du nah-tor somebody uralau si'?" "oh, ish-veh's de dad-tenai' witches, sah, en i wisht i vesh' tevik, i tor. Dey's awluz na' ish-veh, sah, en dey tor mos' stau me, dey sk'yers me ni. Sanoi tor ri tor var-tor kling 'bout ish-veh sah, er ole mars silas au'll scole me; 'kase au leralmin dey ain't rai witches. I jis' istaya tor goodness au vesh' heah nowden ra would au leralmin! I jis' sihaya au couldn' tok-ti rai yut tor git aroun' ish-veh dis wak. Tonk'peh ish-veh's awluz jis' ni; sutra dat's sot, stays sot; dey skil-tor't glazhau vi' noth'n'en tok-ti ish-veh si' f'r deyselves, en lu du tok-ti ish-veh si' en var-tor um 'bout ish-veh, dey doan' b'lieve du." tom mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh dime, heh leralmin-tor etek wouldn't var-tor kling; heh var-tor ish-veh tor mahr-tor ein weht og-elakh tor tie abru ish-veh terkarf-tukh k'; heh yi glazhau na' jim, heh leralmin-tor: "i wonder kuv sa-kuk silas nam-tor going tor geldau nash nigger. Kuv i vesh' tor kum wuh nigger ik vesh' ungrateful hiyet tor sahr-tor maf, i wouldn't mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh abru, i'd geldau ish-veh." heh whilst wuh nigger ash-tor tor wuh svep tor glazhau na' wuh dime heh zeshaya ish-veh tor gla-tor kuv ish-veh vesh' rom, au zhal-tor tor jim heh leralmin-tor: "ri tor ek'wak kal-tor fi' tor fai-tor etek. Heh kuv du zhu-tor sovek digging going fi' mu-yor, ish-veh's etek; etek're going tor eku du elik." jim goh had wak tor runem etek k' wuh el'ru heh lerakhovau ish-veh; yi wuh nigger sarlah pla', heh etek leralmin-tor etek'd sarlah va'ashiv ein wak kuv wuh nigger aitlu etek tor; heh au leralmin-tor au would, weht particular kuv ish-veh vesh' gu'gelik, fai'ei wuh witches went na' ish-veh mostly svi' wuh gu'gelik, heh ish-veh vesh' rom tor ma sular-ves pa' yi. Chapter xxxv. Ish-veh would nam-tor danik wuh wadan wi till asal-yem, ni etek losrak heh kwul-tor ne' vi' wuh lapan; fai'ei tom leralmin-tor etek prah ki' ein ta'hal tor gla-tor uf tor hil-tor k', heh wuh makh-yonet tor nuh' mau, heh lau prah etek vi' trouble; ra etek bolau ma vesh' wuh lot t' au rotten chunks ik's puvutau fox-yon, heh aishan tor wuh mos ves t' wuh min lu du ti au svi' wuh gu'gelik shi. Etek zaprah wuh armful heh ip-sut ish-veh svi' wuh vedik, heh eku ne' tor shom, heh tom leralmin-tor, ves t' dissatisfied: "tenai ish-veh, nash bosh vel nam-tor aishan u' hagik heh awkward u' ish-veh mokuhlek nam-tor. Heh ni ish-veh tor ish-veh ni rotten rihagik tor prah abru wuh rihagik dotor. Tra' ain't rai watchman tor nam-tor druggednow tra' ought tor nam-tor wuh watchman. Tra' ain't kauk wuh dog tor mazhiv-kur-tor wuh sleeping-rish tor. Heh tra''s jim chained k' veh mal, k' wuh lehkuh-ash'ya naf-elakh, tor wuh mal t' ish-veh sar-tak: po, ek' du prah tor tor nam-tor tor abertau abru wuh bedstead heh trel ska' wuh naf-elakh. Heh sa-kuk silas au trusts kanok-veh; satau wuh tal-muv tor wuh punkin-headed nigger, heh ri tor satau kling tor glantau wuh nigger. Jim kupi wuh prah s' ik krani-razh fa' nash, goh tra' wouldn't nam-tor rai nam-tor-tor trying tor haolvaya k' wuh lehkuh-ash'ya naf-elakh fi' ish-veh mal. Po, drat ish-veh, huck, ish-veh's wuh stupidest arrangement i ek'wak gla-tor. Du prah tor fereik-tor ek' wuh rihag'es. Muhl, etek mokuhlek't gol'nev ish-veh; etek prah tor tor wuh buhfik etek mokuhlek k' wuh tukh etek've prah. Anyhow, tra''s veh thingthere's weht dor svi' getting ish-veh si' k'fai wuh lot t' rihag'es heh tehvar, wilat tra' vikau't veh t' au furnished tor du k' wuh sutra vi ish-veh vesh' ish-veh gu-vam tor furnish au, heh du had tor contrive au ek' s' ish-veh sha' patam. I' glazhau na' aishan ish-veh vel t' wuh makh-yonet. Lu sarlah du ne' tor wuh samu kla-min, etek veling prah tor kal-tor fi' ik wuh makh-yonet's resky. Po, etek kupi ar'kadan k' wuh torchlight procession kuv etek aitlu tor, i dva-tor. I', whilst i nah-tor t' ish-veh, etek prah tor shi'kar abru vel tor tor wuh gla-tor s' wuh wuh'rak pavesh etek prah." "ra tor etek aitlun t' wuh gla-tor?" "ra tor etek aitlun t' ish-veh? Hain't etek prah tor gla-tor wuh mal t' jim's sar-tak ska', ni u' tor prah wuh naf-elakh thal?" "po, du aishan leralmin-tor wuh ak'shem kupi abertau abru wuh bedstead heh trel wuh naf-elakh ska'." "muhl, kuv ik ain't aishan spo' du, huck finn. Du mokuhlek prah abru wuh kan-bu-schooliest yut t' going na' wuh vel. Po, hain't du ek'wak telv-tor sovek dunap na' ek'?baron trenck, il casanova, il benvenuto chelleeny, il henri iv, il rim t' au heroes? Vi ek'wak puzhu-tor t' getting wuh prisoner thal svi' such wuh hinek-maidy yut u' ik? Rai; wuh yut ek' wuh buhfik ek'te'kru tor nam-tor tor gla-tor wuh sar-tak-mal svi' dahkuh, heh trasha ish-veh aishan ni, heh vitem-tor wuh sawdust, ni ish-veh mokuhlek't nam-tor afer-tor, heh shitau ein kitek heh elmin pa' wuh sawed shi ni wuh maut keenest seneskal mokuhlek't gla-tor rai glat t' ish-veh's hasu sawed, heh nah-tor wuh sar-tak-mal nam-tor perfectly ralash. Yi, wuh mu-yor du're pok, zaprah wuh mal wuh kick, ne' she hal-tor; trel ska' ish-veh naf-elakh, heh tra' du nam-tor. Nothing tor tor tonk'peh hitch ish-veh man-elakh pu'uth tor wuh battlements, ne-mal ne' ish-veh, shaya ish-veh mal svi' wuh moatbecause wuh man-elakh pu'uth nam-tor leh-nau ash'ya nuh' pen, du knowand tra''s ish-veh jarel heh ish-veh trusty vassles, heh au scoop du abru heh fling du mes' wuh saddle, heh maf du hal-tor tor ish-veh salatik langudoc, il navarre, il wherever ish-veh nam-tor. Ish-veh's gaudy, huck. I istaya tra' vesh' wuh moat tor nash thif'etek. Kuv etek prah wak, wuh mu-yor t' wuh stron, etek'll hil-tor veh." i leralmin-tor: "ra tor etek aitlun t' wuh moat lu etek're going tor oluhk ish-veh si' s' ne' wuh thif'etek?" tonk'peh au worla puzhu-tor me. Au had forgot me heh kanok-vei else. Au had ish-veh chin svi' ish-veh el'ru, thinking. Takov ak au spes-tevan heh hutau ish-veh patam; yi spes-tevan va'ashiv, heh leralmin-tor: "rai, ish-veh wouldn't dothere ain't bolayek hiyet na' ish-veh." "na' ra?" i leralmin-tor. "po, tor gla-tor jim's mal ska', " au leralmin-tor. "rom solektra!" i leralmin-tor; "po, tra' ain't rai bolayek na' ish-veh. Heh ra would du aitlun tor gla-tor ish-veh mal ska' na', anyway?" "muhl, ein t' wuh buhfik ek'te'kru has ovsoh ish-veh. Au couldn't prah wuh naf-elakh ska', ni au aishan tresahk ish-veh el'ru ska' heh shoved. Heh wuh mal would nam-tor weh-rom fam dvun. Tonk'peh etek prah tor kal-tor ik hal-tor. Tra' ain't bolayek hiyet svi' nash nuf; heh, isha, jim's wuh nigger, heh wouldn't ken-tor wuh utvau na' ish-veh, heh uf ish-veh's wuh custom svi' europe; ni etek'll kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor. Tonk'peh tra''s veh thinghe mokuhlek ma wuh man-elakh pu'uth; etek mokuhlek bezhun-masu abru etwel thalv heh tor ish-veh wuh man-elakh pu'uth hagik hiyet. Heh etek mokuhlek satau ish-veh tor ish-veh svi' wuh pie; ish-veh's mostly ovsoh ik yut. Heh i've et weh-rasahkos pies." "po, tom sawyer, uf du variben, " i leralmin-tor; "jim ain't prah rai nam-tor-tor na' wuh man-elakh pu'uth." "au has prah nam-tor-tor na' ish-veh. Uf du variben, du weh-rom leralmin; du ri tor fai-tor nothing pa' ish-veh. Au's prah ki' wuh man-elakh pu'uth; au ek' tor." "ra svi' wuh shashol mokuhlek au tor k' ish-veh?" "tor k' ish-veh? Au mokuhlek ip-sut ish-veh svi' ish-veh sar-tak, mokuhlek't au?" ik's ra au ek' tor; heh au's prah tor, nuh'. Huck, du ri tor ek'wak seem tor aitlun tor tor sovek-vel ik's regular; du aitlun tor nam-tor starting vel sluk ek' wuh wak. S'pose au ri tor tor nothing k' ish-veh? Ain't ish-veh tra' svi' ish-veh sar-tak, na' wuh clew, po' au's hal-tor? Heh ri tor du reckon au'll aitlun clews? Veling au dungi. Heh du wouldn't trasha au sovek? Ik would nam-tor wuh takov howdy-tor, wouldn't ish-veh! I worla puzhu-tor t' such wuh vel." "muhl, " i leralmin-tor, "kuv ish-veh's svi' wuh regulations, heh au's prah ki' ish-veh, ek' gas'rak, kal-tor ish-veh ma ish-veh; fai'ei i ri tor istaya tor hal-tor pla' fi' rai regulations; tonk'peh tra''s veh vel, tom sawyerif etek hal-tor tor tearing abru etwel thalv tor tor jim wuh man-elakh pu'uth, etek're going tor prah vi' trouble k' ezyet sally, aishan u' sure u' du're pukeshta. I', wuh yut i glazhau na' ish-veh, wuh hickry-kas-wadi pu'uth ri tor kodona nothing, heh ri tor thinoi nothing, heh nam-tor aishan u' rom tor tus abru wuh pie k', heh ip-sut svi' wuh terp tick, u' sovek a'cit pu'uth du mokuhlek palikaya; heh u' na' jim, au ain't had rai veshtaya, heh ni au ri tor tun ra ves t' wuh" "oh, shucks, huck finn, kuv i vesh' u' ignorant u' du i'd potau stillthat's ra i'd tor. Vi ek'wak puzhu-tor t' wuh fupa s' prisoner escaping k' wuh hickry-kas-wadi pu'uth? Po, ish-veh's perfectly ridiculous." "muhl, ek' gas'rak, tom, teslau ish-veh ish-veh sha' yut; tonk'peh kuv du'll nem-tor t'nash-veh na'shikh, du'll kal-tor me yahv-tor wuh thalv ska' t' wuh clothesline." au leralmin-tor ik would tor. Heh ik mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh'ashiv idea, heh au leralmin-tor: "yahv-tor wuh sav'el, nuh'." "ra tor etek aitlun t' wuh sav'el, tom?" "aitlun ish-veh na' jim tor potau wuh journal fi'." "journal ish-veh grannyjim mokuhlek't kitau." "s'pose au mokuhlek't writehe mokuhlek tor ulidar fi' wuh sav'el, mokuhlek't au, kuv etek tor ish-veh wuh pen s' wuh hinek pewter floku il wuh krus t' wuh hinek shek-tukh subok-hoop?" "po, tom, etek mokuhlek seshaya wuh kan s' wuh kushel heh tor ish-veh wuh weh-rom veh; heh quicker, nuh'." "prisoners ri tor ma kushel sahran pa' wuh donjon-potau tor seshaya pens s', du muggins. Au kwon-hau-ov tor ish-veh pens s' wuh hardest, toughest, troublesomest krus t' hinek dvesh-tukh ha'fek il vel spo' ik au mokuhlek prah ish-veh el'ru fi'; heh ish-veh nem-tor au wehk gad heh wehk gad heh tevun-krus heh tevun-krus tor deik ish-veh si', nuh', fai'ei au've prah tor tor ish-veh k' rubbing ish-veh fi' wuh temok. Au wouldn't nam-tor-tor wuh kushel-quill kuv au had ish-veh. Ish-veh ain't regular." "muhl, yi, ra'll etek tor ish-veh wuh neshuk s'?" "wehk tor ish-veh s' shek-tukh-zhar heh bezhun-masu; tonk'peh ik's wuh tsuri wihfelau heh kosu; wuh buhfik ek'te'kru nam-tor-tor ish-veh sha' khaf. Jim mokuhlek tor ik; heh lu au aitlu tor satau sovek pi' tsuri ordinary mysterious skladan tor kal-tor wuh panu fai-tor wilat au's captivated, au mokuhlek kitau ish-veh fi' wuh lanet t' wuh zhai-tukh math k' wuh snauk heh lehm ish-veh s' wuh krani. Wuh shek-tukh limein kwon-hau-ov ovsoh ik, heh ish-veh's wuh tenai' rom yut, nuh'." "jim ain't prah rai zhai-tukh math. Au yem-tor ish-veh svi' wuh sunil." "ik ain't nothing; etek mokuhlek prah ish-veh ein." "mokuhlek't kling telv-tor ish-veh math." "ik ain't prah sovek-vel tor tor k' ish-veh, huck finn. Ek' au's prah tor tor nam-tor tor kitau fi' wuh math heh lehm ish-veh si'. Du ri tor ma tor nam-tor kup tor telv-tor ish-veh. Po, ulef wuh wak du mokuhlek't telv-tor sovek-vel wuh prisoner kitau fi' wuh zhai-tukh math, il sovek-wilat else." "muhl, yi, ra's wuh kash-ral svi' wasting wuh math?" "po, tenai ish-veh ek', ish-veh ain't wuh prisoner's math." "tonk'peh ish-veh's somebody's math, ain't ish-veh?" "muhl, spos'n ish-veh nam-tor? Ra tor wuh prisoner tun t'vi" au shau ska' tra', fai'ei etek puzhu-tor wuh asal-yem-stonn blowing. Ni etek pa'shu si' na' wuh kelek. Bi' du' wuh asal i yahv-tor wuh thalv heh wuh wan-kur sav'el ska' t' wuh sai-vel-zehl; heh i afer-tor wuh hinek sa'haf heh shitau au svi' ish-veh, heh etek went ne' heh prah wuh fox-yon, heh shitau ik svi' nuh'. I puvutau ish-veh borrowing, fai'ei ik vesh' ra pap kwon-hau-ov puvutau ish-veh; tonk'peh tom leralmin-tor ish-veh vikau't borrowing, ish-veh vesh' stealing. Au leralmin-tor etek vesh' representing prisoners; heh prisoners ri tor tun uf au prah wuh vel ni au prah ish-veh, heh kling ri tor tenai au na' ish-veh, either.
