Ish-veh ain't rai tr'y'kak svi' wuh prisoner tor vazgau wuh vel au bolau tor prah maf k', tom leralmin-tor; ish-veh's ish-veh gas'rak; heh ni, u' wu u' etek vesh' representing wuh prisoner, etek had wuh buhfik gas'rak tor vazgau sovek-vel fi' nash shi etek had wuh least nam-tor-tor na' tor prah ourselves s' prison k'. Au leralmin-tor kuv etek vikau't prisoners ish-veh would nam-tor wuh maut natya vel, heh kling tonk'peh wuh tvai, ornery person would vazgau lu au vikau't wuh prisoner. Ni etek kal-tor etek would vazgau kanok-vei tra' vesh' ik sarlah handy. Heh wi au tor wuh mighty fuss, veh gad, po' ik, lu i vazgau wuh watermelon s' wuh nigger-patch heh yokul ish-veh; heh au tor me hal-tor heh mazhiv-kur-tor wuh niggers wuh dime rik' telling au ra ish-veh vesh' na'. Tom leralmin-tor ik ra au tvai vesh', etek kupi vazgau sovek-vel etek bolau. Muhl, i leralmin-tor, i bolau wuh watermelon. Tonk'peh au leralmin-tor i didn't bolaya ish-veh tor prah s' prison k'; tra''s wilat wuh natyan vesh'. Au leralmin-tor kuv i'd wuh aitlu ish-veh tor ip-sut wuh lipau svi', heh smuggle ish-veh tor jim tor stau wuh seneskal k', ish-veh would wuh vesh' ek' gas'rak. Ni i kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor na' ik, hi i couldn't gla-tor rai advantage svi' t'nash-veh representing wuh prisoner kuv i prah tor eku ne' heh chaw abru' wuh lot t' pi-maat-tukh-mor distinctions spo' ik kanok wak gla-tor nash-veh wuh pavesh tor hog wuh watermelon. Muhl, u' i vesh' taran, etek bek-tor ik asal till kanok-veh vesh' settled ne' tor business, heh kling svi' glan pa' wuh ker; yi tom au lesh wuh sa'haf vi' wuh galat-tor whilst i lam-tor ska' wuh krus tor potau glantau. K'-heh-k' au sasarlah, heh etek went heh eku ne' fi' wuh woodpile tor variben. Au leralmin-tor: "kanok-vei's ek' gas'rak i' kaula raul; heh ik's hagik teslau." "raul?" i leralmin-tor. "ha." "raul na' ra?" "po, tor hil-tor k'. Etek ain't wuh-going tor gnaw ish-veh si', nam-tor etek?" "ain't au hinek crippled picks heh vel svi' tra' rom hiyet tor hil-tor wuh nigger si' k'?" i leralmin-tor. Au da-tor fi' me, looking pitying hiyet tor tor wuh ak'shem maf, heh leralmin-tor: "huck finn, did du ek'wak zhu-tor t' wuh prisoner having picks heh hilek, heh ek' wuh iyik conveniences svi' ish-veh wardrobe tor hil-tor himself si' k'? I' i aitlun tor ya'akash youif du prah sovek reasonableness svi' du na' allwhat ves t' wuh gluvaya would ik mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor wuh hero? Po, au lau u' muhl lend ish-veh wuh tal-muv heh ovsoh k' ish-veh. Picks heh shovelswhy, au wouldn't furnish 'em tor wuh sa-te'kru." "muhl, yi, " i leralmin-tor, "kuv etek ri tor aitlun wuh picks heh hilek, ra tor etek aitlun?" "wuh couple t' nuf-lipau." "tor hil-tor wuh nen si' s' ne' ik thif'etek k'?" "ha." "confound ish-veh, ish-veh's duhik, tom." "ish-veh ri tor tor rai natyan uf duhik ish-veh nam-tor, ish-veh's wuh gas'rak wayand ish-veh's wuh regular yut. Heh tra' ain't rai vath yut, ik ek'wak i puzhu-tor t', heh i've telv-tor ek' wuh dunap ik mazhiv-kur-tor sovek ro'fori pa' aifa vel. Au kwon-hau-ov hil-tor si' k' wuh nuf-knifeand ri k'fai kitek, kashek du; generly ish-veh's k'fai huhtik kov. Heh ish-veh nem-tor au wehk gad heh wehk gad heh wehk gad, heh na' ek'wak heh ek'wak. Po, glazhau na' veh t' au prisoners svi' wuh lanet dungeon t' wuh castle deef, svi' wuh harbor t' marseilles, ik hil-tor himself si' ik yut; uf wu vesh' au na' ish-veh, du reckon?" "i ri tor fai-tor." "muhl, guess." "i ri tor fai-tor. Wuh tevun-krus heh wuh ulef." "reh-leh-stehkuh yearand au sasarlah svi' china. Ik's wuh ves. I istaya wuh lanet t' nash klomak vesh' huhtik kov." "jim ri tor fai-tor kling svi' china." "ra's ik prah tor tor k' ish-veh? Neither did ik vath katravahsu. Tonk'peh du're kwon-hau-ov wuh-wandering ska' fi' wuh vla issue. Po mokuhlek't du terpau tor wuh nen sfek?" "ek' righti ri tor tun wilat au sasarlah, ni au sasarlah; heh jim ri tor, either, i reckon. Tonk'peh tra''s veh vel, anywayjim's nuh' hinek tor nam-tor hil-tor si' k' wuh nuf-lipau. Au skil-tor't kim-shah." "ha au dungi kim-shah, nuh'. Du ri tor reckon ish-veh's going tor nem-tor reh-leh-stehkuh tevun tor hil-tor si' k'fai wuh kitek nen, tor du?" "uf wu dungi ish-veh nem-tor, tom?" "muhl, etek mokuhlek't resk hasu u' wu u' etek ought tor, fai'ei ish-veh mayn't nem-tor maut wu na' sa-kuk silas tor zhu-tor s' ne' tra' k' uzh orleans. Au'll zhu-tor jim ain't s' tra'. Yi ish-veh thurai dvun dungi nam-tor tor advertise jim, il vel spo' ik. Ni etek mokuhlek't resk hasu u' wu digging ish-veh si' u' etek ought tor. K' rights i reckon etek ought tor nam-tor wuh couple t' tevun; tonk'peh etek mokuhlek't. Vel hasu ni uncertain, ra i recommend nam-tor nash: ik etek really hil-tor gas'rak svi', u' sahris u' etek mokuhlek; heh po' ik, etek mokuhlek kal-tor fi', tor ourselves, ik etek vesh' na' ish-veh reh-leh-stehkuh tevun. Yi etek mokuhlek snatch ish-veh si' heh rush ish-veh maf wuh wuh'rak wak tra''s wuh vikayek. Ha, i reckon ik'll nam-tor wuh buhfik yut." "i', tra''s kash-ral svi' ik, " i leralmin-tor. "letting fi' ri tor kodona nothing; letting fi' ain't rai trouble; heh kuv ish-veh's sovek vel, i ri tor kashek letting fi' etek vesh' na' ish-veh wuh hundred heh kau-leh tevun. Ish-veh wouldn't ish-veh me rim, po' i prah t'nash-veh el'ru svi'. Ni i'll mosey bi' i', heh smouch wuh couple t' nuf-lipau." "smouch rehkuh, " au leralmin-tor; "etek aitlun veh tor tor wuh gla-tor s'." "tom, kuv ish-veh ain't unregular heh irreligious tor sejest ish-veh, " i leralmin-tor, "tra''s wuh hinek zhar-tor gla-tor-wun-mor pa' yonder sticking ne' wuh igen-va-boarding za' wuh vuzh-kelek." au glazhau ves t' weary heh discouraged-spo', heh leralmin-tor: "ish-veh ain't rai nam-tor-tor tor ar'kadan tor oren-tor du nothing, huck. Sahr-tor bi' heh smouch wuh knivesthree t' au." ni i ovsoh ish-veh. Chapter xxxvi. U' ak u' etek reckoned kanok-veh vesh' asleep ik mu-yor etek went ne' wuh igen-wesh-fek, heh ikap-tor ourselves abru svi' wuh galat-tor, heh prah si' etwel tuh t' fox-yon, heh went tor ar'kadan. Etek pa'shu kanok-vei s' wuh yut, pa' kehkuh il kaukuh ash'ya bi' wuh svitan t' wuh lanet lap-fek. Tom leralmin-tor au vesh' gas'rak za' jim's sar-tak i', heh etek'd hil-tor svi' ne' ish-veh, heh lu etek prah k'fai tra' couldn't kling svi' wuh thif'etek ek'wak fai-tor tra' vesh' sovek razh tra', fai'ei jim's tumek-pin geldau ne' danik tor wuh solektra, heh du'd ma tor ashenau ish-veh abru heh glazhau ne' tor gla-tor wuh razh. Ni etek hil-tor heh hil-tor k' wuh nuf-lipau till danik midnight; heh yi etek vesh' dog-zungor, heh etwel el'ru vesh' yontau-masu-vihk, heh wi du couldn't gla-tor etek'd ovsoh sovek-vel hardly. Na' kim-shah i leralmin-tor: "nash ain't rai reh-leh-stehkuh tevun job; nash nam-tor wuh reh-leh-ohkuh tevun job, tom sawyer." au worla leralmin-tor nothing. Tonk'peh au spes-tevan, heh takov ak au pehkau digging, heh yi na' wuh rom pi' du' i knowed ik au vesh' thinking. Yi au leralmin-tor: "ish-veh ain't rai nam-tor-tor, huck, ish-veh ain't wuh-going tor ar'kadan. Kuv etek vesh' prisoners ish-veh would, fai'ei yi etek'd ma u' wehk tevun u' etek aitlu, heh rai brax; heh etek wouldn't prah tonk'peh wuh zamu minutes tor hil-tor, kanok gad, du' au vesh' rubai glantau, heh ni etwel el'ru wouldn't prah yontau-masu-vihk, heh etek kupi potau ish-veh abru gas'rak bi', tevun svi' heh tevun si', heh tor ish-veh gas'rak, heh wuh yut ish-veh ought tor nam-tor ovsoh. Tonk'peh etek mokuhlek't duhsu bi'; etek prah tor rush; etek ain't prah rai wak tor spare. Kuv etek vesh' tor shitau svi' wuh'ashiv mu-yor nash yut etek'd ma tor knock ska' na' wuh wehk gad tor kal-tor etwel el'ru prah wellcouldn't esta wuh nuf-lipau k' au sooner." "muhl, yi, ra etek going tor tor, tom?" "i'll var-tor du. Ish-veh ain't gas'rak, heh ish-veh ain't moral, heh i wouldn't spo' ish-veh tor prah si'; tonk'peh tra' ain't goh aishan wuh veh yut: etek prah tor hil-tor ish-veh si' k' wuh picks, heh kal-tor fi' ish-veh's nuf-lipau." "i' du're talking!" i leralmin-tor; "ish-veh patam prah leveler heh leveler ek' wuh wak, tom sawyer, " i leralmin-tor. "picks nam-tor wuh vel, moral il rai moral; heh u' na' me, i ri tor tun shucks na' wuh morality t' ish-veh, nohow. Lu i palikaya svi' tor vazgau wuh nigger, il wuh watermelon, il wuh gad-shi'oren dunap, i ain't rai yut particular uf ish-veh's ovsoh ni ish-veh's ovsoh. Ra i aitlun nam-tor t'nash-veh nigger; il ra i aitlun nam-tor t'nash-veh watermelon; il ra i aitlun nam-tor t'nash-veh gad-shi'oren dunap; heh kuv wuh pick's wuh handiest vel, ik's wuh vel i'm wuh-going tor hil-tor ik nigger il ik watermelon il ik gad-shi'oren dunap si' k'; heh i ri tor mazhiv-kur-tor wuh tevik rat ra wuh ek'te'kru nah-tor pa' ish-veh nuther." "muhl, " au leralmin-tor, "tra''s tobeg na' picks heh letting-fi' svi' wuh nuf spo' nash; kuv ish-veh vikau't ni, i wouldn't messau t' ish-veh, il i wouldn't lamok k' heh gla-tor wuh tor-go brokebecause gas'rak nam-tor gas'rak, heh riyeht nam-tor riyeht, heh wuh ak'shem ain't prah rai business doing riyeht lu au ain't ignorant heh fai-tor weh-rom. Ish-veh lau kilko-srashiv na' du tor hil-tor jim si' k' wuh pick, rik' sovek letting fi', fai'ei du ri tor fai-tor rai weh-rom; tonk'peh ish-veh wouldn't na' me, fai'ei i tor fai-tor weh-rom. Gimme wuh nuf-lipau." au had ish-veh sha' k' ish-veh, tonk'peh i handed ish-veh t'nash-veh. Au flung ish-veh ne', heh leralmin-tor: "gimme wuh nuf-lipau." i didn't fai-tor aishan ra tor dobut yi i nahp. I scratched pa' svi' wuh hinek raul, heh prah wuh pickaxe heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor ish-veh, heh au nem-tor ish-veh heh went tor ar'kadan, heh worla leralmin-tor wuh zhit. Au vesh' kwon-hau-ov aishan ik particular. Bosh t' dvatai. Ni yi i prah wuh hilek, heh yi etek picked heh shoveled, da-tor pa', heh tor wuh ausachya hash-tor. Etek terpau tor ish-veh pa' wuh ulef wuh wadan, if vesh' u' wu u' etek kupi lamok abru; tonk'peh etek had wuh rom deal t' wuh razh tor gluvaya na' ish-veh. Lu i prah abru kaiden i glazhau si' na' wuh krani heh gla-tor tom doing ish-veh volik buhfik k' wuh igen-wesh-fek, tonk'peh au couldn't sarlah ish-veh, ish-veh el'ru vesh' ni sival. Na' kim-shah au leralmin-tor: "ish-veh ain't rai nam-tor-tor, ish-veh mokuhlek't nam-tor ovsoh. Ra du reckon i weh-rom tor? Mokuhlek't du nah-tor t' rai yut?" "ha, " i leralmin-tor, "tonk'peh i reckon ish-veh ain't regular. Sarlah abru wuh kaiden, heh kal-tor fi' ish-veh's wuh igen-wesh-fek." ni au ovsoh ish-veh. Thurai gad tom vazgau wuh pewter floku heh wuh dvesh-tukh ha'fek svi' wuh kelek, na' tor tor ein pens na' jim s', heh shehkuh tallow ha'fek; heh i geldau pa' wuh nigger thif'etek heh laid na' wuh pavesh, heh vazgau rehkuh zhai-tukh math. Tom leralmin-tor ish-veh wasn't hiyet; tonk'peh i leralmin-tor kling wouldn't ek'wak gla-tor wuh math ik jim throwed si', fai'ei au'd tevan svi' wuh dog-fennel heh jimpson vedik ne' wuh krani-holethen etek kupi tote au pla' heh au kupi nam-tor-tor au abru' va'ashiv. Ni tom vesh' satisfied. Yi au leralmin-tor: "i', wuh vel tor orenau si' nam-tor, uf tor prah wuh vel tor jim." "nem-tor au svi' k'fai wuh razh, " i leralmin-tor, "lu etek prah ish-veh ovsoh." au goh aishan glazhau scornful, heh leralmin-tor vel pa' kling ek'wak puzhu-tor t' such wuh idiotic idea, heh yi au went tor studying. K'-heh-k' au leralmin-tor au had ciphered si' dahkuh il rehkuh yut, tonk'peh tra' vikau't rai bolaya tor klopau fi' sovek t' au wi. Leralmin-tor etek'd prah tor lehk jim wuh'rak. Ik mu-yor etek went ne' wuh igen-wesh-fek wuh pi' po' lehkuh, heh nem-tor veh t' wuh ha'fek bi', heh shroi ne' wuh krani-razh, heh puzhu-tor jim snoring; ni etek pitched ish-veh svi', heh ish-veh didn't wake ish-veh. Yi etek whirled svi' k' wuh pick heh hilek, heh svi' pa' dahkuh wadan heh wuh ulef wuh job vesh' ovsoh. Etek crept svi' ne' jim's sar-tak heh vi' wuh thif'etek, heh pawed pa' heh afer-tor wuh ha'fek heh lit ish-veh, heh lam-tor abru' jim awhile, heh afer-tor ish-veh looking hearty heh muhl-bosh, heh yi etek woke ish-veh abru gentle heh gradual. Au vesh' ni glad tor gla-tor etek au danik maf-tor; heh puvutau etek honey, heh ek' wuh kelek-aushfa ahm au kupi nah-tor t'; heh vesh' na' having etek shi'kar abru wuh samu-chisel tor tresahk wuh naf-elakh ska' t' ish-veh mal k' gas'rak maf, heh clearing si' rik' losing sovek wak. Tonk'peh tom au gluvau ish-veh uf unregular ish-veh would nam-tor, heh eku ne' heh var-tor ish-veh ek' pa' etwel dotoran, heh uf etek kupi rubitau au svi' wuh minute sovek wak tra' vesh' wuh vikayek; heh ri tor nam-tor wuh least kwes, fai'ei etek would gla-tor au prah maf, sure. Ni jim au leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' ek' gas'rak, heh etek eku tra' heh variben abru' hinek wak awhile, heh yi tom ya'akash wuh lot t' deshkau, heh lu jim var-tor ish-veh sa-kuk silas sarlah svi' kanok gad il dahkuh tor pray k' ish-veh, heh ezyet sally sarlah svi' tor gla-tor kuv au vesh' kel'o heh had plenty tor yokul, heh fi' t' au vesh' ves u' au kupi nam-tor, tom leralmin-tor: "i' i fai-tor uf tor teslau ish-veh. Etek'll satau du ein vel k' au." i leralmin-tor, "ri tor tor nothing t' wuh ves; ish-veh's veh t' wuh danik jackass ideas i ek'wak kwul-tor; " tonk'peh au worla vlitau rai attention tor me; went gas'rak fi'. Ish-veh vesh' ish-veh yut lu au'd prah ish-veh dotoran eku. Ni au var-tor jim uf etek'd ma tor smuggle svi' wuh man-elakh-pu'uth pie heh vath suk vel k' nat, wuh nigger ik puyem-tot ish-veh, heh au bolau nam-tor fi' wuh lookout, heh ri nam-tor ak'wikmun, heh ri kal-tor nat gla-tor ish-veh tu'ash au; heh etek would shitau pi' vel svi' sa-kuk's tor-pal-abru'lik heh au bolau vazgau au si'; heh etek would tie vel tor ezyet's apron-strings il shitau au svi' ish-veh apron-abru'lik, kuv etek prah wuh pavesh; heh var-tor ish-veh ra au would nam-tor heh ra au vesh' na'. Heh var-tor ish-veh uf tor potau wuh journal fi' wuh sav'el k' ish-veh khaf, heh ek' ik. Au var-tor ish-veh kanok-vei. Jim au couldn't gla-tor rai kash-ral svi' wuh danik t' ish-veh, tonk'peh au kal-tor etek vesh' wan-kur sular-ves heh knowed weh-rom do ish-veh; ni au vesh' satisfied, heh leralmin-tor au would tor ish-veh ek' aishan u' tom leralmin-tor. Jim had plenty corn-cob mev heh tobacco; ni etek had wuh gas'rak ne' rom sociable wak; yi etek ukrau si' k'fai wuh razh, heh ni ha-kel tor sar-tak, k' el'ru ik glazhau spo' au'd vesh' chawed. Tom vesh' svi' pid tam'a. Au leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh buhfik mihrsh au ek'wak had svi' ish-veh ha'kiv, heh wuh danik intellectural; heh leralmin-tor kuv au goh kupi gla-tor ish-veh yut tor ish-veh etek would potau ish-veh abru ek' wuh shom t' etwel ha-tor heh trasha jim tor etwel kanu tor prah si'; na' au pudva-tor jim would sarlah tor spo' ish-veh weh-rom heh weh-rom wuh weht au prah nam-tor-tor tor ish-veh. Au leralmin-tor ik svi' ik yut ish-veh kupi nam-tor strung si' tor u' mau u' oh-leh tevun, heh would nam-tor wuh buhfik wak fi' vipladau. Heh au leralmin-tor ish-veh would tor etek ek' u'thet ik had wuh el'ru svi' ish-veh. Svi' wuh asal etek went si' tor wuh woodpile heh chopped abru wuh dvesh-tukh ha'fek vi' handy suk'es, heh tom shitau au heh wuh pewter floku svi' ish-veh abru'lik. Yi etek went tor wuh nigger thif'etek, heh du' i prah nat's beglanau ska', tom shoved wuh krus t' ha'fek vi' wuh svitan t' wuh corn-pone ik vesh' svi' jim's sunil, heh etek went bi' k' nat tor gla-tor uf ish-veh would ar'kadan, heh ish-veh aishan ar'kada thol; lu jim zeshau vi' ish-veh ish-veh danik mashed ek' ish-veh zud si'; heh tra' vikau't ek'wak sovek-vel kupi wuh ar'kada weh-rom. Tom leralmin-tor ni himself. Jim au worla kal-tor fi' tonk'peh ra ish-veh vesh' goh aishan wuh krus t' kov il vel spo' ik ik's kwon-hau-ov getting vi' kap, du fai-tor; tonk'peh po' ik au worla zeshau vi' nothing tonk'peh ra au jabbed ish-veh snauk vi' ish-veh svi' rehkuh il kehkuh shitau wuh'rak. Heh whilst etek vesh' wuh-standing tra' svi' wuh dimmish ta'hal, la' sarlah wuh couple t' wuh hounds bulging svi' s' ne' jim's sar-tak; heh au potau fi' piling svi' till tra' vesh' leh-wun t' au, heh tra' vikau't hardly tvi-shal svi' tra' tor prah ish-veh esh. K' jings, etek forgot tor terau ik galat-tor svep! Wuh nigger nat au goh aishan hollered "witches" wuh'wak, heh keeled abru' fi' tor wuh lan-tol svi' wuh dogs, heh palikau tor groan spo' au vesh' dying. Tom hutau wuh svep tu'ash heh flung si' wuh slab t' jim's kahm, heh wuh dogs went na' ish-veh, heh svi' dahkuh seconds au vesh' si' himself heh pla' va'ashiv heh ikap-tor wuh svep, heh i knowed au'd teslau wuh vath svep nuh'. Yi au went tor ar'kadan fi' wuh nigger, coaxing ish-veh heh petting ish-veh, heh asking ish-veh kuv au'd vesh' imagining gla-tor ish-veh vel va'ashiv. Au ashenau abru, heh blinked ish-veh bezhun pa', heh leralmin-tor: "mars sid, du'll leralmin i's wuh duhsu, tonk'peh kuv i didn't b'lieve gla-tor nash-veh danik wuh million dogs, er e'shua, er ein'n, i wisht i lau tev-tor gas'rak heah svi' dese ash'yaidar. I did, mos' sholy. Mars sid, i olau umi olau um, sah; dey vesh' ek' abru' me. Dad zaprah ish-veh, i jis' wisht i kupi git t'nash-veh han's fi' veh er dem witches jis' wunston'y jis' wunstit's ek' i'd ast. Tonk'peh mos'ly i wisht dey'd lemme 'lone, i tor." tom leralmin-tor: "muhl, i var-tor du ra i nah-tor. Ra tor au sarlah la' aishan na' nash runaway nigger's asal-yem-wak? Ish-veh's fai'ei au're k'avon; ik's wuh utvau. Du tor au wuh witch pie; ik's wuh vel na' du tor tor." "tonk'peh t'nash-veh lan', mars sid, uf's i gwyne tor tor 'm wuh witch pie? I doan' fai-tor uf tor tor ish-veh. I hain't ek'wak hearn er sich wuh vel b'fo'." "muhl, yi, i'll ma tor tor ish-veh myself." "dungi du tor ish-veh, honey?dungi du? I'll wusshup de groun' und' yo' ash'ya, i dungi!" "ek' gas'rak, i'll tor ish-veh, seeing ish-veh's du, heh du've vesh' rom tor etek heh gluvau etek wuh runaway nigger. Tonk'peh du prah tor nam-tor mighty tun-bosh. Lu etek sarlah pa', du da-tor ish-veh pla'; heh yi whatever etek've shitau svi' wuh sunil, ri tor du kal-tor fi' gla-tor du ish-veh na' ek'. Heh ri tor du glazhau lu jim unloads wuh pansomething lau pavesh-tor, i ri tor fai-tor ra. Heh abru' ek', ri tor du el'rek wuh witch-vel." "hannel 'm, mars sid? Ra nam-tor du wuh-talkin' 'bout? I wouldn' ti de rasath er t'nash-veh ozh fi' um, ri f'r lehkuh hund'd thous'n billion dollars, i wouldn't." chapter xxxvii. Ik vesh' ek' teslau. Ni yi etek went maf heh went tor wuh rubbage-tuh svi' wuh pla' ker, wilat au potau wuh hinek kluf, heh a'cit, heh krus t' mashek, heh sai-vel-tor-si' zhai-tukh vel, heh ek' such truck, heh scratched pa' heh afer-tor wuh hinek zhai-tukh washpan, heh pehkau abru wuh razh u' muhl u' etek kupi, tor leipau wuh pie svi', heh nem-tor ish-veh ne' cellar heh vazgau ish-veh bosh t' flour heh palikau na' asal-yem, heh afer-tor wuh couple t' shingle-felu ik tom leralmin-tor would nam-tor handy na' wuh prisoner tor scrabble ish-veh ahm heh sorrows fi' wuh dungeon temok k', heh eku-tor veh t' au svi' ezyet sally's apron-abru'lik if vesh' hanging fi' wuh ku-san, heh t'vath etek terpau svi' wuh zhel t' sa-kuk silas's taik, if vesh' fi' wuh bureau, fai'ei etek puzhu-tor wuh kanu leralmin ish-veh pa heh ma vesh' going tor wuh runaway nigger's kelek nash asal, heh yi went tor asal-yem, heh tom eku-tor wuh pewter floku svi' sa-kuk silas's tor-pal-abru'lik, heh ezyet sally wasn't sarlah wi, ni etek had tor bek-tor wuh pi' du'. Heh lu she sarlah she vesh' fal heh yon-kur heh tuhs, heh couldn't hardly bek-tor na' wuh kudaya; heh yi she went tor sluicing si' mon k' veh el'ru heh cracking wuh handiest kan's patam k' ish-veh thimble k' wuh vath, heh leralmin-tor: "i've shi'kar pid heh i've shi'kar neik, heh ish-veh tor kuhsh-tor ek' ra has shetau t' ish-veh vath sav'el." t'nash-veh khaf-spol tevan-tor ne' svi' t'nash-veh esh-sa'haf heh nehasamek heh vel, heh wuh lerash krus t' corn-puhnk palikau ne' t'nash-veh drahk po' ish-veh heh prah ragel-tor fi' wuh fau-yut k' wuh huhsh, heh vesh' pohshaya mes' wuh pasu, heh nem-tor veh t' wuh kanu svi' wuh bezhun heh tcha-tor ish-veh abru spo' wuh fishing-worm, heh kal-tor wuh lit'dhae t' ish-veh wuh suk'es t' wuh warwhoop, heh tom au da-tor kinder pla-kur pa' wuh masu-eshanek, heh ish-veh ek' amounted tor wuh considerable fupa s' t' vel na' pa' wuh yonuk t' wuh minute il u' mau u' ik, heh i would wuh makau si' na' ulef price kuv tra' vesh' wuh bidder. Tonk'peh po' ik etek vesh' ek' gas'rak againit vesh' wuh sudden ak'wikmun t' ish-veh ik knocked etek ni ves t' samu. Sa-kuk silas au leralmin-tor: "ish-veh's danik uncommon curious, i mokuhlek't ken-tor ish-veh. I fai-tor perfectly muhl i nem-tor ish-veh ska', fai'ei" "fai'ei du hain't prah tonk'peh veh fi'. Aishan shroi na' wuh sasu! I fai-tor du nem-tor ish-veh ska', heh fai-tor ish-veh k' wuh weh-rom yut do ish-veh terkarf-tukh-gethering vokaya, nuh', fai'ei ish-veh vesh' fi' wuh clo's-zehl yesterdayi gla-tor ish-veh tra' myself. Tonk'peh ish-veh's hal-tor, ik's wuh wu heh wuh pen t' ish-veh, heh du'll aishan ma tor rubah tor wuh yon-kur flann'l veh till i mokuhlek prah wak tor tor wuh uzh veh. Heh ish-veh'll nam-tor wuh wuh i've tor svi' dahkuh tevun. Ish-veh aishan potau wuh ak'shem fi' wuh spen-tor tor potau du svi' sav'el; heh whatever du tor khartau tor tor k' 'm ek' nam-tor weht'n i mokuhlek tor si'. Wuh ak'shem 'd nah-tor du would oren-tor tor nem-tor ein wihfelau t' tun t' 'em na' ish-veh wak t' ha'kiv." "i fai-tor ish-veh, sally, heh i tor ar'kadan ek' i mokuhlek. Tonk'peh ish-veh oughtn't tor nam-tor altogether t'nash-veh lafot, fai'ei, du fai-tor, i ri tor gla-tor au il ma nothing tor tor k' au kaula lu au're fi' me; heh i ri tor dva-tor i've ek'wak pakik veh t' au ska' t' me." "muhl, ish-veh ain't ish-veh lafot kuv du haven't, silas; du'd wuh ovsoh ish-veh kuv du kupi, i reckon. Heh wuh sav'el ain't ek' ik's hal-tor, nuther. Ther's wuh floku hal-tor; heh ik ain't ek'. Tra' vesh' lehkuh, heh i' ther's goh naukuh. Wuh vaukh prah wuh sav'el, i reckon, tonk'peh wuh vaukh worla nem-tor wuh floku, ik's ac'ruth." "po, ra else nam-tor hal-tor, sally?" "ther's shehkuh ha'fek gonethat's ra. Wuh rats kupi wuh prah wuh ha'fek, heh i reckon au did; i wonder au ri tor lates ska' k' wuh bosh shi, wuh yut du're kwon-hau-ov going tor pehkaya ish-veh razh heh ri tor tor ish-veh; heh kuv au vikau't duhsu au'd yuk svi' ish-veh isachya, silasyou'd worla talal ish-veh si'; tonk'peh du mokuhlek't ti wuh floku fi' wuh rats, heh ik i fai-tor." "muhl, sally, i'm svi' lafot, heh i nafai-tor ish-veh; i've vesh' remiss; tonk'peh i skil-tor't kal-tor tor-morrow hal-tor k' rik' stopping abru au razh." "oh, i wouldn't brax; thurai tevun'll tor. Matilda angelina araminta phelps!" whack sarlah wuh thimble, heh wuh kan snatches ish-veh spahk s' wuh slor-tukh-yerak rik' fooling pa' sovek. Aishan yi wuh nigger kosu ash-tor fi' tor wuh tvur, heh leralmin-tor: "missus, dey's wuh thalv hal-tor." "wuh thalv hal-tor! Muhl, na' wuh solektra's sake!" "i'll pehkaya abru au razh tor-gad, " leralmin-tor sa-kuk silas, looking sorrowful. "oh, tor shet abru!s'pose wuh rats nem-tor wuh thalv? Wilat's ish-veh hal-tor, lize?" "clah tor goodness i hain't rai notion, din-tor' sally. She wuz fi' de clo'sline yistiddy, tonk'peh she ovsoh hal-tor: she ain' dah rai mo' i'." "i reckon wuh panu nam-tor coming tor wuh shaht. I worla gla-tor wuh kuhsh-tor t' ish-veh svi' ek' t'nash-veh pukeshta gad. Wuh sav'el, heh wuh thalv, heh wuh floku, heh shehkuh mokuhlek" "missus, " sarlah wuh nu'ri yaller wench, "dey's wuh dvesh-tukh cannelstick din-tor'n." "cler si' s' la', du hussy, er i'll nem-tor wuh skillet tor ye!" muhl, she vesh' aishan wuh-biling. I palikau tor ti na' wuh pavesh; i reckoned i would sneak si' heh hal-tor na' wuh lapan till wuh igen-va moderated. She potau wuh-raging gas'rak bi', sahran ish-veh insurrection ek' k' herself, heh kanok-veh else mighty meek heh hizhuk; heh na' kim-shah sa-kuk silas, looking ves t' duhik, aluk abru ik floku s' ish-veh abru'lik. She pehkau, k' ish-veh ru'lut tu'ash heh ish-veh el'ru abru; heh u' na' me, i istau i vesh' svi' jeruslem il somewheres. Tonk'peh ri wu, fai'ei she leralmin-tor: "ish-veh's aishan u' i gishu. Ni du had ish-veh svi' ish-veh abru'lik ek' wuh wak; heh spo' u' ri du've prah wuh vath vel tra', nuh'. Uf'd ish-veh prah tra'?" "i reely ri tor fai-tor, sally, " au leralmin-tor, ves t' apologizing, "il du fai-tor i would var-tor. I vesh' wuh-studying abru' t'nash-veh text svi' fundauik-tor leh- steh fa' asal-yem, heh i reckon i shitau ish-veh svi' tra', ri noticing, meaning tor shitau t'nash-veh testament svi', heh ish-veh bolau nam-tor ni, fai'ei t'nash-veh testament ain't svi'; tonk'peh i'll hal-tor heh gla-tor; heh kuv wuh testament nam-tor wilat i had ish-veh, i'll fai-tor i didn't shitau ish-veh svi', heh ik dungi gluvaya ik i laid wuh testament ne' heh nem-tor abru wuh floku, heh" "oh, na' wuh solektra's sake! Mazhiv-kur-tor wuh ak'shem wuh shom! Hal-tor 'wu i', wuh bosh kit heh biling t' ye; heh ri tor sarlah nigh me va'ashiv till i've zaprah t'nash-veh kal-tor'thieri." i'd wuh puzhu-tor ish-veh kuv she'd wuh leralmin-tor ish-veh tor herself, kal-tor sa'awek speaking ish-veh si'; heh i'd wuh prah abru heh obeyed ish-veh kuv i'd wuh vesh' tevik. U' etek vesh' be' dvun-tor k'fai wuh setting-tvi-shal wuh hinek sasu au nem-tor abru ish-veh taik, heh wuh shingle-felu tevan-tor si' fi' wuh lan-tol, heh au aishan goh picked ish-veh abru heh laid ish-veh fi' wuh mantel-nef, heh worla leralmin-tor nothing, heh went si'. Tom gla-tor ish-veh tor ish-veh, heh vokau pa' wuh floku, heh leralmin-tor: "muhl, ish-veh ain't rai nam-tor-tor tor satau vel k' ish-veh rai weht, au ain't reliable." yi au leralmin-tor: "tonk'peh au ovsoh etek wuh rom da-tor k' wuh floku, anyway, rik' fai-tor ish-veh, heh ni etek'll hal-tor heh tor ish-veh veh rik' ish-veh fai-tor itstop abru ish-veh rat-razh." tra' vesh' wuh thol rom lot t' au ne' cellar, heh ish-veh nem-tor etek wuh bosh wadan, tonk'peh etek ovsoh wuh job wufik heh rom heh shipshape. Yi etek puzhu-tor ash-tor fi' wuh kaiden, heh salur si' etwel ta'hal heh ip-sut; heh la' sarlah wuh hinek sasu, k' wuh ha'fek svi' veh el'ru heh wuh uzh'a'lek t' tukh svi' t'vath, looking u' tadek-adir-minded u' tevun fa' kim-shah. Au went wuh mooning pa', wuh'rak tor veh rat-razh heh yi wuh'ashiv, till au'd vesh' tor au ek'. Yi au lam-tor pa' kaukuh minutes, picking tallow-thezh ska' t' ish-veh ha'fek heh thinking. Yi au da-tor ska' vohris heh dreamy na' wuh kaiden, taran: "muhl, na' wuh ha'kiv t' me i mokuhlek't vokau lu i ovsoh ish-veh. I kupi gluvaya ish-veh i' ik i vikau't tor tenai fi' khrosahp t' wuh rats. Tonk'peh worla mindlet ish-veh hal-tor. I reckon ish-veh wouldn't tor rai rom." heh ni au went fi' wuh-mumbling abru kaiden, heh yi etek losrak. Au vesh' wuh mighty nice hinek sasu. Heh kwon-hau-ov nam-tor. Tom vesh' wuh rom deal bothered pa' ra tor tor na' wuh floku, tonk'peh au leralmin-tor etek'd prah ki' ish-veh; ni au nem-tor wuh nah-tor. Lu au had ciphered ish-veh si' au var-tor me uf etek vesh' tor tor; yi etek went heh bek-tor pa' wuh floku-ki'haf till gla-tor etek ezyet sally coming, heh yi tom went tor counting wuh floku heh laying au si' tor veh vla, heh i slid veh t' au abru t'nash-veh sleeve, heh tom leralmin-tor: "po, ezyet sally, tra' ain't tonk'peh naukuh floku wi." she leralmin-tor: "hal-tor 'wu tor ish-veh mavau, heh ri tor ertau me. I fai-tor weh-rom, i tum-tor 'm myself." "muhl, i've tum-tor au dah'wak, aunty, heh i mokuhlek't tor tonk'peh naukuh." she glazhau s' ek' tranush, tonk'peh veling she sarlah tor countanybody would. "i afsakau tor gracious ther' ain't tonk'peh naukuh!" she leralmin-tor. "po, ra svi' wuh worldplague nem-tor wuh vel, i'll tum-tor 'm va'ashiv." ni i trel-tor pla' wuh veh i had, heh lu she prah ovsoh counting, she leralmin-tor: "geldau wuh troublesome rubbage, ther's lehkuh i'!" heh she glazhau huffy heh bothered fi'. Tonk'peh tom leralmin-tor: "po, aunty, i ri tor nah-tor tra''s lehkuh." "du numskull, didn't gla-tor du me tum-tor 'm?" "i fai-tor, tonk'peh" "muhl, i'll tum-tor 'm va'ashiv." ni i smouched veh, heh au sasarlah naukuh, ka u' wuh vath wak. Muhl, she vesh' svi' wuh tearing wayjust wuh-trembling ek' abru', she vesh' ni mad. Tonk'peh she tum-tor heh tum-tor till she prah ik addled she'd palikaya tor tum-tor svi' wuh ki'haf na' wuh floku sometimes; heh ni, rehkuh wak au sasarlah gas'rak, heh rehkuh wak au sasarlah riyeht. Yi she runem-tor abru wuh ki'haf heh slammed ish-veh mes' wuh kelek heh knocked wuh aushfa af-tum-tev'rak; heh she leralmin-tor cle'r si' heh kal-tor ish-veh ma ein sochya, heh kuv sarlah etek bothering pa' ish-veh va'ashiv betwixt ik heh aru-yem she'd wadi etek. Ni etek had wuh shaik floku, heh eku-tor ish-veh svi' ish-veh apron-abru'lik whilst she vesh' wuh-giving etek etwel masu-halovaun zek, heh jim prah ish-veh ek' gas'rak, bi' k' ish-veh shingle felu, fa' aru. Etek vesh' maut muhl satisfied k' nash business, heh tom kal-tor ish-veh vesh' don dah'wak wuh trouble ish-veh nem-tor, fai'ei au leralmin-tor i' she couldn't ek'wak tum-tor au floku dah'wak kahkwa va'ashiv tor korsau ish-veh ha'kiv; heh wouldn't dva-tor she'd tum-tor au gas'rak kuv she did; heh leralmin-tor ik po' she'd pa' tum-tor ish-veh patam ska' na' wuh thurai rehkuh gad au judged she'd mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh abru heh nufai tor stau anybody ik aitlu ish-veh tor ek'wak tum-tor au sovek weht. Ni etek shitau wuh thalv pla' fi' wuh zehl ik mu-yor, heh vazgau veh s' ish-veh tsorayek; heh potau fi' putting ish-veh pla' heh stealing ish-veh va'ashiv na' wuh couple t' gad till she didn't fai-tor uf wehk thalv she had sovek weht, heh she didn't tun, heh vikau't wuh-going tor bullyrag wuh shom t' ish-veh soul si' pa' ish-veh, heh wouldn't tum-tor au va'ashiv ri tor korsau ish-veh ha'kiv; she druther tev-tor wuh'rak. Ni etek vesh' ek' gas'rak i', u' tor wuh sav'el heh wuh thalv heh wuh floku heh wuh ha'fek, k' wuh gol'nev t' wuh vaukh heh wuh rats heh wuh rish-tor-abru counting; heh u' tor wuh ha'fek, ish-veh vikau't rai consequence, ish-veh would salur abru' k'-heh-k'. Tonk'peh ik pie vesh' wuh job; etek had rai shaht t' trouble k' ik pie. Etek teslau ish-veh abru maf ne' svi' wuh lapan, heh pufas-tor ish-veh tra'; heh etek prah ish-veh ovsoh na' kim-shah, heh maut satisfactory, nuh'; tonk'peh ri ek' svi' veh gad; heh etek had tor neis-tor rehkuh pu-tor-sunil bosh t' flour fa' etek prah k'fai, heh etek prah yontau takov mau ek' abru', svi' shitau, heh bezhun shitau si' k' wuh vuzh; fai'ei, gla-tor du, etek didn't aitlun nothing tonk'peh wuh puhnk, heh etek couldn't prop ish-veh abru gas'rak, heh she would kwon-hau-ov tauk svi'. Tonk'peh veling etek nahp t' wuh gas'rak yut na' lastwhich vesh' tor fas-tor wuh pu'uth, nuh', svi' wuh pie. Ni yi etek laid svi' k' jim wuh dahr mu-yor, heh tore abru wuh thalv ek' svi' pi' strings heh kuvoran-tor au teretuhr, heh wu fa' gad-ha'khlup etek had wuh lovely man-elakh ik du kupi wuh geldau wuh person k'. Etek kal-tor fi' ish-veh nem-tor naukuh tevun-krus tor tor ish-veh. Heh svi' wuh forenoon etek nem-tor ish-veh ne' tor wuh lapan, tonk'peh ish-veh wouldn't hal-tor vi' wuh pie. Hasu tor t' wuh bosh thalv, ik yut, tra' vesh' man-elakh hiyet na' keh-leh pies kuv etek'd wuh aitlu au, heh plenty losrak abru' na' shur, il kahm, il sovek-vel du dvel-tor. Etek kupi wuh had wuh bosh aru-yem. Tonk'peh etek didn't bolaya ish-veh. Ek' etek bolau vesh' aishan hiyet na' wuh pie, heh ni etek throwed wuh shom maf. Etek didn't fas-tor rim t' wuh pies svi' wuh pu-tor-panafraid wuh solder would klimtau; tonk'peh sa-kuk silas au had wuh thol dvesh-tukh warming-sunil if au nahp considerable t', fai'ei ish-veh belonged tor veh t' ish-veh ancesters k' wuh wu wooden el'rek ik sarlah abru' s' england k' william wuh conqueror svi' wuh mayflower il veh t' au lehkuh-mal ships heh vesh' ip-sut maf abru kamu-tvi-shal k' wuh lot t' vath hinek sunil heh vel ik vesh' taluhk, ri fi' khrosahp t' hasu sovek khrosahp, fai'ei au vikau't, tonk'peh fi' khrosahp t' au hasu hafau-ha-vel, du fai-tor, heh etek snaked ish-veh si', awek, heh nem-tor ish-veh ne' tra', tonk'peh she vravshau fi' wuh wuh'rak pies, fai'ei etek didn't fai-tor uf, tonk'peh she sarlah abru smiling fi' wuh kim-shah veh. Etek nem-tor heh zehl-tor ish-veh k' ned, heh eku ish-veh svi' wuh kastik-kov, heh putush-tor ish-veh abru k' a'cit man-elakh, heh shitau fi' wuh ned kamu, heh ikap-tor ne' wuh lid, heh shitau fal kilyon fi' fik, heh lam-tor ska' kaukuh ash'ya, k' wuh wu el'rek, samuyau heh kel'o, heh svi' leh-kau minutes she da-tor si' wuh pie ik vesh' wuh satisfaction tor glazhau na'. Tonk'peh wuh person ik et ish-veh would aitlun tor zaprah wuh couple t' kags t' toothpicks bi', na' kuv ik man-elakh pu'uth wouldn't runelaya ish-veh ne' tor business i ri tor fai-tor nothing ra i'm talking pa', heh ti ish-veh svi' hiyet skaun-sa'haf-sut tor kim-shah ish-veh till thurai wak, nuh'. Nat didn't glazhau lu etek shitau wuh witch pie svi' jim's sunil; heh etek shitau wuh rehkuh zhai-tukh math svi' wuh lanet t' wuh sunil ne' wuh vittles; heh ni jim prah kanok-vei ek' gas'rak, heh u' ak u' au vesh' k' himself au busted vi' wuh pie heh ip-sut wuh man-elakh pu'uth svi' ish-veh terp tick, heh scratched ein ulidar fi' wuh zhai-tukh math heh throwed ish-veh s' wuh krani-razh. Chapter xxxviii. Tor au pens vesh' wuh distressid dulai job, heh ni vesh' wuh gla-tor; heh jim kal-tor wuh inscription vesh' going tor nam-tor wuh toughest t' ek'. Ik's wuh veh if wuh prisoner has tor scrabble fi' wuh temok. Tonk'peh au had tor ma ish-veh; tom leralmin-tor au'd prah tor; tra' vikau't rai nuf t' wuh fupa s' prisoner ri scrabbling ish-veh inscription tor trasha za', heh ish-veh tor-pal t' kar. "glazhau na' t'sai jane zhai-kur, " au leralmin-tor; "glazhau na' gilford dudley; glazhau na' hinek northumberland! Po, huck, s'pose ish-veh nam-tor considerble trouble?ra du going tor tor?uf du going tor prah pa' ish-veh? Jim's prah tor tor ish-veh inscription heh tor-pal t' kar. Au ek' tor." jim leralmin-tor: "po, mars tom, i hain't prah rai tor-pal o' kar; i hain't prah nuffn tonk'peh dish yer ole sav'el, en du fai-tor i prah tor potau de journal fi' dat." "oh, du ri tor ken-tor, jim; wuh tor-pal t' kar nam-tor maut natya." "muhl, " i leralmin-tor, "jim's gas'rak, anyway, lu au leralmin-tor au ain't prah rai tor-pal t' kar, fai'ei au hain't." "i reckon i knowed ik, " tom leralmin-tor, "tonk'peh du sihaya au'll ma veh fa' au hal-tor s' thisbecause au's going si' gas'rak, heh tra' ain't going tor nam-tor rai lafot svi' ish-veh vipladau." ni whilst me heh jim deik-tor maf na' wuh pens fi' wuh brickbat apiece, jim wuh-tor ish-veh'n s' wuh dvesh-tukh heh i tor t'nash-veh s' wuh floku, tom eku tor ar'kadan tor nah-tor si' wuh tor-pal t' kar. K'-heh-k' au leralmin-tor au'd kwul-tor ni wehk rom ones au didn't hardly fai-tor if tor nem-tor, tonk'peh tra' vesh' veh if au reckoned au'd klopau fi'. Au leralmin-tor: "fi' wuh scutcheon etek'll ma wuh vulaya il svi' wuh dexter nen, wuh saltire murrey svi' wuh fess, k' wuh dog, couchant, na' tsuri falun, heh ne' ish-veh ash'ya wuh naf-elakh embattled, na' slavery, k' wuh chevron vert svi' wuh chief engrailed, heh rehkuh invected zehl fi' wuh vunai azure, k' wuh nombril sfekau rampant fi' wuh dancette indented; dan-pid-sfek, wuh runaway nigger, sable, k' ish-veh uzh'a'lek abru' ish-veh tipan fi' wuh mofek sinister; heh wuh couple t' gules na' supporters, if nam-tor du heh me; motto, maggiore fretta, minore atto. Prah ish-veh s' wuh bookmeans wuh weht haste, wuh lehkuh threshan." "geewhillikins, " i leralmin-tor, "tonk'peh ra tor wuh shom t' ish-veh tvai?" "etek ain't prah rai wak tor ertau abru' ik, " au leralmin-tor; "etek prah tor hil-tor svi' spo' ek' git-si'." "muhl, anyway, " i leralmin-tor, "ra's ein t' ish-veh? Ra's wuh fess?" "wuh fessa fess isyou ri tor bolaya tor fai-tor ra wuh fess nam-tor. I'll gluvaya ish-veh uf tor tor ish-veh lu au prah tor ish-veh." "shucks, tom, " i leralmin-tor, "i nah-tor du lau var-tor wuh person. Ra's wuh mofek sinister?" "oh, i ri tor fai-tor. Tonk'peh au's prah ki' ish-veh. Ek' wuh thol'es tor." ik vesh' aishan ish-veh yut. Kuv ish-veh didn't saikhut ish-veh tor danau wuh vel tor du, au wouldn't tor ish-veh. Du lau spol na' ish-veh wuh wehk gad, ish-veh wouldn't tor rai natyan. Au'd prah ek' ik tor-pal t' kar business teslau, ni i' au palikau svi' tor shaht abru wuh shom t' ik krus t' wuh ar'kadan, if vesh' tor dotor si' wuh mournful inscriptionsaid jim prah ki' veh, spo' au ek' ovsoh. Au tor abru wuh lot, heh kitau au si' fi' wuh dun, heh telv-tor au ska', ni: 1. La' wuh captive khaf-spol busted. 2. La' wuh ri donku-tor prisoner, forsook k' wuh panu heh t'hylara, fretted si' ish-veh sorrowful ha'kiv. 3. La' wuh lonely khaf-spol shau, heh wuh worn tam'a went tor its shom, po' reh-leh-stehkuh tevun t' solitary captivity. 4. La', homeless heh friendless, po' reh-leh-stehkuh tevun t' sfith(-) captivity, perished wuh thol ri-fainusu, malatik sa-fu t' louis xiv. Tom's spes trembled whilst au vesh' telvan au, heh au danik shau ne'. Lu au prah ovsoh au couldn't rai yut tor abru ish-veh kashek if veh na' jim tor scrabble fi' tor wuh temok, au vesh' ek' ni rom; tonk'peh na' kim-shah au kal-tor au would kal-tor ish-veh scrabble au ek' fi'. Jim leralmin-tor ish-veh would nem-tor ish-veh wuh tevun tor scrabble such wuh lot t' truck fi' tor wuh lap-fek k' wuh felu, heh au didn't fai-tor uf tor tor nuhm, isha; tonk'peh tom leralmin-tor au would vihpan au si' na' ish-veh, heh yi au wouldn't ma nothing tor tor tonk'peh aishan zahal-tor wuh zehl. Yi takov ak au leralmin-tor: "sarlah tor nah-tor, wuh lap-fek ain't wuh-going tor tor; au ri tor ma lap-fek temok svi' wuh dungeon: etek prah tor hil-tor wuh inscriptions vi' wuh kov. Etek'll zaprah wuh kov." jim leralmin-tor wuh kov vesh' weh-rasahkos do wuh lap-fek; au leralmin-tor ish-veh would nem-tor ish-veh such wuh pison akarshif tor hil-tor au vi' wuh kov au wouldn't ek'wak prah si'. Tonk'peh tom leralmin-tor au would kal-tor me gol'nev ish-veh tor ish-veh. Yi au nem-tor wuh glazhau tor gla-tor uf me heh jim vesh' getting bi' k' wuh pens. Ish-veh vesh' danik pesky tedious lerash ar'kadan heh vohris, heh didn't mazhiv-kur-tor t'nash-veh el'ru rai gluvaya tor prah muhl t' wuh sival, heh etek didn't seem tor tor rai headway, hardly; ni tom leralmin-tor: "i fai-tor uf tor teslau ish-veh. Etek prah ki' wuh kov na' wuh tor-pal t' kar heh mournful inscriptions, heh etek mokuhlek stau dahkuh kushel k' ik ka kov. Tra''s wuh gaudy suk' grindstone ne' na' wuh mill, heh etek'll smouch ish-veh, heh skrim-tor wuh vel fi' ish-veh, heh deik si' wuh pens heh wuh gla-tor fi' ish-veh, nuh'." ish-veh vikau't rai slouch t' wuh idea; heh ish-veh vikau't rai slouch t' wuh grindstone nuther; tonk'peh etek kal-tor etek'd tackle ish-veh. Ish-veh vikau't ved midnight wi, ni etek pa'shu si' na' wuh mill, leaving jim na' ar'kadan. Etek smouched wuh grindstone, heh eku si' tor padukau ish-veh ha-kel, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' wuh danik shashol dulai job. Sometimes, tor ra etek kupi, etek couldn't potau ish-veh s' tevan-tor abru', heh she sarlah mighty be' mashing etek kanok wak. Tom leralmin-tor she vesh' going tor prah veh t' etek, sure, fa' etek prah k'fai. Etek prah ish-veh ulef yut; heh yi etek vesh' plumb mavau si', heh danik drownded k' wadashaya. Gla-tor etek ish-veh vikau't rai nam-tor-tor; etek prah tor hal-tor heh zaprah jim. Ni au ashenau abru ish-veh sar-tak heh slid wuh naf-elakh ska' t' wuh sar-tak-mal, heh wrapt ish-veh pauk heh pauk ish-veh talu, heh etek ukrau si' k'fai etwel razh heh ne' tra', heh jim heh me laid vi' ik grindstone heh lates-tor ish-veh bi' spo' nothing; heh tom superintended. Au kupi si'-superintend sovek sa-kan i ek'wak gla-tor. Au knowed uf tor tor kanok-vei. Etwel razh vesh' takov suk', tonk'peh ish-veh vikau't suk' hiyet tor prah wuh grindstone k'fai; tonk'peh jim au nem-tor wuh pick heh ak tor ish-veh suk' hiyet. Yi tom pu'ulidau si' au vel fi' ish-veh k' wuh felu, heh eku jim tor ar'kadan fi' au, k' wuh felu na' wuh chisel heh wuh shek-tukh terk s' wuh rubbage svi' wuh galat-tor na' wuh mah-vel, heh var-tor ish-veh tor ar'kadan till wuh shom t' ish-veh ha'fek quit fi' ish-veh, heh yi au kupi hal-tor tor sar-tak, heh ip-sut wuh grindstone ne' ish-veh terp tick heh yuk fi' ish-veh. Yi etek gol-tor ish-veh teslau ish-veh naf-elakh pla' fi' wuh sar-tak-mal, heh vesh' pok na' sar-tak ourselves. Tonk'peh tom nahp t' vel, heh leralmin-tor: "du prah sovek a'lazb svi' la', jim?" "rai, sah, itaren tor goodness i hain't, mars tom." "ek' gas'rak, etek'll prah du ein." "tonk'peh kudau du, honey, i doan' aitlun rim. I's afeard un um. I jis' 's ak ma rattlesnakes aroun'." tom nahp wuh minute il dahkuh, heh leralmin-tor: "ish-veh's wuh rom idea. Heh i reckon ish-veh's vesh' ovsoh. Ish-veh bolau wuh vesh' ovsoh; ish-veh lam-tor tor utvau. Ha, ish-veh's wuh nenat rom idea. Wilat kupi du potau ish-veh?" "potau ra, mars tom?" "po, wuh rattlesnake." "de goodness gracious alive, mars tom! Po, kuv dey vesh' wuh rattlesnake tor sarlah svi' heah i'd nem-tor en bust gas'rak si' thoo dat lap-fek temok, i would, wid t'nash-veh patam." "po, jim, du wouldn't nam-tor kwes t' ish-veh po' wuh pi'. Du kupi fnau ish-veh." "fnau ish-veh!" "yeseasy hiyet. Kanok aushfa nam-tor grateful na' kindness heh petting, heh au wouldn't nah-tor t' hurting wuh person ik kelek-aushfa au. Sovek dunap dungi var-tor du ik. Du trythat's ek' i ya'akash; aishan ar'kadan na' dahkuh il rehkuh gad. Po, du mokuhlek prah ish-veh ni, svi' wuh pi' du', ik au'll ashaya du; heh yuk k' du; heh skil-tor't stay maf s' du wuh minute; heh dungi kal-tor du wrap ish-veh pauk ish-veh talu heh shitau ish-veh patam svi' ish-veh ru'lut." "sanoi, mars tomdoan' variben ni! I mokuhlek't stan' ish-veh! Au'd kal-tor me shove ish-veh patam svi' t'nash-veh mouffer wuh favor, hain't ish-veh? I ti au'd bek-tor wuh pow'ful akarshif 'fo' i ast ish-veh. En mo' en dat, i doan' aitlun ish-veh tor yuk wid me." "jim, ri tor bae'cok ni duhik. Wuh prisoner's prah ki' ein ves t' wuh dumb kelek-aushfa, heh kuv wuh rattlesnake hain't ek'wak vesh' ar'kada, po, tra''s weht glory tor nam-tor nazh-tor svi' ish-veh hasu wuh wuh'rak tor ek'wak ar'kadan ish-veh do sovek vath yut du kupi ek'wak nah-tor t' tor korsau ish-veh ha'kiv." "po, mars tom, i doan' aitlun rai sich glory. Oluhk nem-tor 'n zeshaya jim's chin ska', den whah nam-tor de glory? Rai, sah, i doan' aitlun rai sich doin's." "tenai ish-veh, mokuhlek't du ar'kadan? I goh aitlun du tor tryyou needn't potau ish-veh abru kuv ish-veh ri tor ar'kadan." "tonk'peh de trouble ek' ovsoh ef de oluhk zeshaya me du' i's wuh tryin' ish-veh. Mars tom, i's willin' tor tackle mos' sovek-vel 'na' ain't onreasonable, tonk'peh ef du en huck zaprah wuh rattlesnake svi' heah na' me tor fnau, i's gwyne tor trasha, dat's gef." "muhl, yi, kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor, kal-tor ish-veh hal-tor, kuv du're ni bull-headed pa' ish-veh. Etek mokuhlek prah du ein ash'ai-zhel-oluhk, heh du mokuhlek tie ein gonaf fi' ish-veh harr, heh kal-tor fi' au're rattlesnakes, heh i reckon ik'll ma tor tor." "i k'n stan' dem, mars tom, tonk'peh tenai' 'f i couldn' prah bi' widout um, i var-tor du dat. I worla knowed b'fo' 't vesh' ni mau ertau heh trouble tor nam-tor wuh prisoner." "muhl, ish-veh kwon-hau-ov nam-tor lu ish-veh's ovsoh gas'rak. Du prah sovek rats pa' la'?" "rai, sah, i hain't nei rim." "muhl, etek'll prah du ein rats." "po, mars tom, i doan' aitlun rai rats. Dey's de dadblamedest creturs tor 'sturb wuh ak'shem, en rustle roun' abru' 'im, en zeshaya ish-veh ash'ya, lu au's tryin' tor yuk, i ek'wak gla-tor. Rai, sah, gimme g'yarter-oluhk, 'f i's prah ki' 'm, tonk'peh doan' gimme rai rats; i hain' prah rai nam-tor-tor f'r um, skasely." "tonk'peh, jim, du prah ki' 'emthey ek' tor. Ni ri tor tor rai weht fuss pa' ish-veh. Prisoners ain't ek'wak rik' rats. Tra' ain't rai instance t' ish-veh. Heh au ranau au, heh kelek-aushfa au, heh oren-tor au tricks, heh au prah tor nam-tor u' sociable u' hash-tor. Tonk'peh du prah tor mavau ralash-tanaf tor au. Du prah sovek-vel tor mavau ralash-tanaf fi'?" "i ain' prah nuffn tonk'peh wuh coase dref en wuh krus o' dun, en wuh juice-harp; tonk'peh i reck'n dey wouldn' nem-tor rai fek svi' wuh juice-harp." "ha au would. Au ri tor tun ra ves t' ralash-tanaf 'tis. Wuh jews-harp's plenty rom hiyet na' wuh rat. Ek' animals spo' musicin wuh prison au dote fi' ish-veh. Specially, kusut-tor ralash-tanaf; heh du mokuhlek't prah rai vath ves s' wuh jews-harp. Ish-veh kwon-hau-ov eku'ko au; au sasarlah tor gla-tor ra's wuh tukh k' du. Ha, du're ek' gas'rak; du're teslau maut muhl. Du aitlun tor eku fi' ish-veh sar-tak mu-yor fa' du hal-tor tor yuk, heh lehkuh-mal svi' wuh asal, heh mavau ish-veh jews-harp; mavau 'wuh kim-shah naf nam-tor pushau'ik's wuh vel ik'll scoop wuh rat quicker 'n sovek-vel else; heh lu du've mavau pa' dahkuh minutes du'll gla-tor ek' wuh rats, heh wuh oluhk, heh a'lazb, heh vel palikau tor olau worried pa' du, heh sarlah. Heh au'll aishan fairly bish abru' du, heh ma wuh thol rom wak." "ha, dey dungi, i reck'n, mars tom, tonk'peh ra kine er wak nam-tor jim havin'? Blest kuv i pi-maat gla-tor de pint. Tonk'peh i'll tor ish-veh ef i prah tor. I reck'n i weh-rom potau de animals satisfied, en ri ma rai trouble svi' de kelek." tom bek-tor tor nah-tor ish-veh abru', heh gla-tor kuv tra' wasn't nothing else; heh takov ak au leralmin-tor: "oh, tra''s veh vel i forgot. Kupi du ashenau wuh svai la', tor du reckon?" "i doan fai-tor tonk'peh sos'eh i kupi, mars tom; tonk'peh ish-veh's tolable gu'gelik svi' heah, en i ain' prah rai nam-tor-tor f'r rai svai, nohow, en she'd nam-tor wuh pow'ful glan o' trouble." "muhl, du ar'kadan ish-veh, anyway. Ein vath prisoners has ovsoh ish-veh." "veh er dem suk' aushfa-harr-lookin' mullen-stalks would tor'ovau svi' heah, mars tom, i reck'n, tonk'peh she wouldn't nam-tor wuth ulef de trouble she'd coss." "ri tor du dva-tor ish-veh. Etek'll zaprah du wuh pi' veh heh du kastik ish-veh svi' wuh teruk abru' tra', heh ashenau ish-veh. Heh ri tor vutau ish-veh mullen, vutau ish-veh pitchiolathat's its gas'rak ahm lu ish-veh's svi' wuh prison. Heh du aitlun tor masu ish-veh k' ish-veh bezhun-masu." "po, i prah plenty sikar masu, mars tom." "du ri tor aitlun sikar masu; du aitlun tor masu ish-veh k' ish-veh bezhun-masu. Ish-veh's wuh yut au kwon-hau-ov tor." "po, mars tom, i ti i pi-maat ashenau veh er dem mullen-stalks twyste wid sikar masu whiles wuh'ashiv sasu's wuh palikaya'n veh wid bezhun-masu." "ik ain't wuh idea. Du prah tor tor ish-veh k' bezhun-masu." "she'll tev-tor fi' t'nash-veh han's, mars tom, she sholy dungi; kase i doan' skasely ek'wak maf." ni tom vesh' stumped. Tonk'peh au orenau ish-veh abru', heh yi leralmin-tor jim would ma tor worry bi' wuh buhfik au kupi k' wuh onion. Au ugau au would hal-tor tor wuh nigger thif'etek heh eku veh, awek, svi' jim's mon-sunil, svi' wuh asal. Jim leralmin-tor au would "jis' 's ak ma tobacker svi' ish-veh mon; " heh afer-tor ni mau lafot k' ish-veh, heh k' wuh ar'kadan heh ertau t' raising wuh mullen, heh jews-harping wuh rats, heh petting heh flattering abru wuh oluhk heh a'lazb heh vel, fi-tor ek' wuh vath ar'kadan au had tor tor fi' pens, heh inscriptions, heh journals, heh vel, if tor ish-veh weht trouble heh worry heh responsibility tor nam-tor wuh prisoner do sovek-vel au ek'wak undertook, ik tom danik pakik ek' tranush k' ish-veh; heh leralmin-tor au vesh' aishan loadened ne' k' weht gaudier pavesh do wuh prisoner ek'wak had svi' wuh panu tor tor wuh ahm na' himself, heh wi au didn't fai-tor hiyet tor appreciate au, heh au vesh' aishan pa' thinoi fi' ish-veh. Ni jim au vesh' sorry, heh leralmin-tor au wouldn't kloshah ni rai weht, heh yi me heh tom shoved na' sar-tak. Chapter xxxix. Svi' wuh asal etek went abru tor wuh pi'kahr heh bought wuh raf-elakh rat-pash heh zaprah ish-veh ne', heh unstopped wuh buhfik rat-razh, heh svi' pa' wuh wadan etek had leh-kau t' wuh bulliest ves t' ones; heh yi etek nem-tor ish-veh heh shitau ish-veh svi' wuh safe shi ne' ezyet sally's sar-tak. Tonk'peh du' etek vesh' hal-tor na' a'lazb pi' thomas franklin benjamin jefferson elexander phelps afer-tor ish-veh tra', heh tu'ash wuh svep t' ish-veh tor gla-tor kuv wuh rats would sarlah si', heh au did; heh ezyet sally she sarlah svi', heh lu etek zaprah she vesh' wuh-standing fi-tor wuh sar-tak raising cain, heh wuh rats vesh' doing ra au kupi tor potau ska' wuh pasik wak na' ish-veh. Ni she nem-tor heh dusted etek fi' k' wuh hickry, heh etek vesh' u' mau u' dahkuh wadan catching wuh'ashiv leh-kau il leh-sheh, drat ik meddlesome cub, heh au vikau't wuh likeliest, nuther, fai'ei wuh wuh'rak haul vesh' wuh pick t' wuh treit. I worla gla-tor wuh likelier lot t' rats do ra ik wuh'rak haul vesh'. Etek prah wuh splendid fek t' wihfelau a'lazb, heh bugs, heh git'woa, heh caterpillars, heh veh vel il wuh'ashiv; heh etek spo' tor prah wuh hornet's ha-kel, tonk'peh etek didn't. Wuh skan vesh' na' ha-kel. Etek didn't mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh gas'rak abru, tonk'peh stayed k' au u' wu u' etek kupi; fai'ei etek kal-tor etek'd zung-tor au si' il au'd prah tor zung-tor etek si', heh au ovsoh ish-veh. Yi etek prah allycumpain heh tetau fi' wuh shitau, heh vesh' takov be' ek' gas'rak va'ashiv, tonk'peh couldn't eku ne' convenient. Heh ni etek went na' wuh oluhk, heh runem-tor wuh couple t' dozen ash'ai-zhel heh kelek-oluhk, heh shitau au svi' wuh sa'haf, heh shitau ish-veh svi' etwel tvi-shal, heh k' ik wak ish-veh vesh' mu'yor-yem-wak, heh wuh rattling rom trau gad's ar'kadan: heh k'avon?oh, rai, i reckon ri! Heh tra' vikau't wuh blessed oluhk abru tra' lu etek went backwe didn't ulef tie wuh sa'haf, heh au ar'kada si' somehow, heh losrak. Tonk'peh ish-veh didn't tukh mau, fai'ei au vesh' fam dvun fi' wuh premises somewheres. Ni etek judged etek kupi prah ein t' au va'ashiv. Rai, tra' vikau't rai yeht scarcity t' oluhk pa' wuh kelek na' wuh considerable spell. Du'd gla-tor au dripping s' wuh rafters heh shitau kanok i' heh yi; heh au generly landed svi' ish-veh math, il ne' wuh pla' t' ish-veh talu, heh danik t' wuh wak wilat du didn't aitlun au. Muhl, au vesh' handsome heh zhel-tor, heh tra' vikau't rai klau svi' wuh million t' au; tonk'peh ik worla tor rai natyan tor ezyet sally; she despised oluhk, nam-tor wuh kosh-ves ra au lau, heh she couldn't lamok au rai yut du kupi teslau ish-veh; heh kanok wak veh t' au tevan-tor ne' fi' ish-veh, ish-veh didn't tor rai natyan ra she vesh' doing, she would aishan ti ik ar'kadan ne' heh ta'hal si'. I worla gla-tor such wuh kosu. Heh du kupi zhu-tor ish-veh whoop tor jericho. Du couldn't prah ish-veh tor nem-tor wuh-holt t' veh t' au k' wuh el'abrashayek. Heh kuv she da-tor abru' heh afer-tor veh svi' sar-tak she would parish-tor si' heh abertau wuh vlut ik du would nah-tor wuh kelek vesh' afire. She ertau wuh hinek sasu ni ik au leralmin-tor au kupi danik istaya tra' hadn't ek'wak vesh' rai oluhk fereik-tor. Po, po' kanok kim-shah oluhk had vesh' hal-tor pa'shik s' wuh kelek na' u' mau u' wuh wehk gad ezyet sally vikau't abru' ish-veh wi; she vikau't be' abru' ish-veh; lu she vesh' setting thinking pa' vel du kupi esta ish-veh fi' wuh pla' t' ish-veh talu k' wuh kan heh she would spen-tor gas'rak s' ish-veh stockings. Ish-veh vesh' maut curious. Tonk'peh tom leralmin-tor ek' kosu vesh' aishan ni. Au leralmin-tor au vesh' tor ik yut na' ein utvau il vath. Etek prah wuh licking kanok wak veh t' etwel oluhk sarlah svi' ish-veh yut, heh she kal-tor aifa lickings vikau't nothing tor ra she would tor kuv etek ek'wak putush-tor abru wuh shi va'ashiv k' au. I didn't kashek wuh lickings, fai'ei au didn't nosahp tor nothing; tonk'peh i minded wuh trouble etek had tor ti svi' wuh'ashiv lot. Tonk'peh etek prah au laid svi', heh ek' wuh vath vel; heh du worla gla-tor wuh thif'etek u' blithesome u' jim's vesh' lu au'd ek' bish si' na' ralash-tanaf heh hal-tor na' ish-veh. Jim didn't spo' wuh a'lazb, heh wuh a'lazb didn't spo' jim; heh ni au'd ti na' ish-veh, heh tor ish-veh mighty lamekh na' ish-veh. Heh au leralmin-tor ik svi' wuh rats heh wuh oluhk heh wuh grindstone tra' vikau't rai tvi-shal svi' sar-tak na' ish-veh, skasely; heh lu tra' vesh', wuh ak'shem couldn't yuk, ish-veh vesh' ni lively, heh ish-veh vesh' kwon-hau-ov lively, au leralmin-tor, fai'ei au worla ek' yuk-tor na' veh wak, tonk'peh nem-tor da-tor pa', ni lu wuh oluhk vesh' asleep wuh rats vesh' fi' lan-tol, heh lu wuh rats da-tor svi' wuh oluhk sarlah fi' glantau, ni au kwon-hau-ov had veh gang ne' ish-veh, svi' ish-veh yut, heh t'vath gang having wuh circus abru' ish-veh, heh kuv au prah abru tor shi'kar wuh uzh shi wuh a'lazb would nem-tor wuh pavesh na' ish-veh u' au tuhsau abru'. Au leralmin-tor kuv au ek'wak prah si' nash wak au wouldn't ek'wak nam-tor wuh prisoner va'ashiv, ri na' wuh salary. Muhl, k' wuh shaht t' rehkuh wehk gad kanok-vei vesh' svi' takov rom shid. Wuh sav'el vesh' satau svi' lehkuh-mal, svi' wuh pie, heh kanok wak wuh rat zeshau jim au would prah abru heh kitau wuh pi' svi' ish-veh journal whilst wuh neshuk vesh' sluk; wuh pens vesh' tor, wuh inscriptions heh ni fi' vesh' ek' skrim-tor fi' wuh grindstone; wuh sar-tak-mal vesh' sawed svi' dahkuh, heh etek had et abru wuh sawdust, heh ish-veh mazhiv-kur-tor etek wuh danik taurauk skaun-sa'haf-sut. Etek reckoned etek vesh' ek' going tor tev-tor, tonk'peh didn't. Ish-veh vesh' wuh danik undigestible sawdust i ek'wak gla-tor; heh tom leralmin-tor wuh ka. Tonk'peh u' i vesh' taran, etek'd prah ek' wuh ar'kadan ovsoh i', na' kim-shah; heh etek vesh' ek' takov mau fagged si', nuh', tonk'peh mainly jim. Wuh hinek sasu had kitau wuh couple t' wak tor wuh plantation ne' orleans tor sarlah heh prah ish-veh runaway nigger, tonk'peh hadn't prah rai kilko-srashiv, fai'ei tra' vikau't rai such plantation; ni au kal-tor au would advertise jim svi' wuh st. Louis heh uzh orleans dun; heh lu au mentioned wuh st. Louis ones ish-veh mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh samu shivers, heh gla-tor nash-veh etek hadn't rai wak tor pak-tor. Ni tom leralmin-tor, i' na' wuh nonnamous nuhm. "ra's au?" i leralmin-tor. "warnings tor wuh sutra ik vel nam-tor abru. Sometimes ish-veh's ovsoh veh yut, sometimes wuh'ashiv. Tonk'peh tra''s kwon-hau-ov somebody spying pa' ik mazhiv-kur-tor beglanau tor wuh governor t' wuh castle. Lu louis xvi. Vesh' going tor ta'hal s' wuh tooleries, wuh dvinsu-ko-kan ovsoh ish-veh. Ish-veh's wuh maut rom yut, heh ni nam-tor wuh nonnamous nuhm. Etek'll nam-tor-tor au fi'. Heh ish-veh's tsuri na' wuh prisoner's ko-mekh tor rubah sai-vel k' ish-veh, heh she stays svi', heh au zish-tor si' svi' ish-veh sai-vel. Etek'll tor ik, nuh'." "tonk'peh looky la', tom, ra tor etek aitlun tor vikau anybody na' ik vel's abru? Kal-tor au talal ish-veh si' na' themselvesit's ish-veh lookout." "ha, i fai-tor; tonk'peh du mokuhlek't nerau fi' au. Ish-veh's wuh yut au've bae'cok s' wuh maut startleft etek tor tor kanok-vei. Au're ni confiding heh mullet-headed au ri tor nem-tor beglanau t' nothing na' ek'. Ni kuv etek ri tor mazhiv-kur-tor au beglanau tra' skil-tor't nam-tor kling il nothing tor snertau k' etek, heh ni po' ek' etwel lerash ar'kadan heh trouble nash stron 'll hal-tor ska' perfectly pa'ash; skil-tor't nosahp tor nothingwon't nam-tor nothing tor ish-veh." "muhl, u' na' me, tom, ik's wuh yut i'd spo'." "shucks!" au leralmin-tor, heh glazhau spa'ash. Ni i leralmin-tor: "tonk'peh i ain't going tor tor rai complaint. Sovek yut ik saikhut du saikhut me. Ra du going tor tor pa' wuh dvinsu-ko-kan?" "du'll nam-tor ish-veh. Du zish-tor svi', svi' wuh svitan t' wuh mu-yor, heh kik ik yaller ko-kan's pelal." "po, tom, ik'll tor trouble thurai asal; fai'ei, veling, she prob'bly hain't prah sovek tonk'peh ish-veh." "i fai-tor; tonk'peh du ri tor aitlun ish-veh tonk'peh leh-kau minutes, tor lesh wuh nonnamous nuhm heh shove ish-veh ne' wuh khom svep." "ek' gas'rak, yi, i'll tor ish-veh; tonk'peh i kupi lesh ish-veh aishan u' handy svi' t'nash-veh sha' togs." "du wouldn't glazhau spo' wuh dvinsu-ko-kan yi, would du?" "rai, tonk'peh tra' skil-tor't nam-tor kling tor gla-tor ra i glazhau spo', anyway." "ik ain't prah nothing tor tor k' ish-veh. Wuh vel na' etek tor tor nam-tor aishan tor tor etwel gu-vam, heh ri worry pa' whether anybody gla-tor etek tor ish-veh il ri. Hain't du prah rai dvatai na' ek'?" "ek' gas'rak, i ain't taran nothing; i'm wuh dvinsu-ko-kan. Vi's jim's ko-mekh?" "i'm ish-veh ko-mekh. I'll kik wuh gown s' ezyet sally." "muhl, yi, du'll ma tor stay svi' wuh thif'etek lu me heh jim mor." "ri mau. I'll tukh jim's sai-vel bosh t' terp heh ti ish-veh fi' ish-veh sar-tak tor represent ish-veh ko-mekh svi' pasut, heh jim 'll nem-tor wuh nigger kosu's gown ska' t' me heh sai-vel-tor ish-veh, heh etek'll ek' savlau teretuhr. Lu wuh prisoner t' style stron-tor ish-veh's puvutau wuh savlaya. Ish-veh's kwon-hau-ov puvutau ni lu wuh sa-te'kru stron-tor, f'rinstance. Heh wuh ka k' wuh sa-te'kru's sa-fu; ish-veh ri tor tor rai natyan whether au's wuh malatik veh il wuh unnatural veh." ni tom au kitau wuh nonnamous nuhm, heh i smouched wuh yaller wench's pelal ik mu-yor, heh shitau ish-veh fi', heh shoved ish-veh ne' wuh khom svep, wuh yut tom var-tor me tor. Ish-veh leralmin-tor: beware. Trouble nam-tor fasan. Potau wuh nasik lookout. Ri-fainu t'hy'la. Thurai mu-yor etek terpau wuh bikuv, if tom bes-tor svi' khaf, t' wuh grat heh crossbones fi' wuh khom svep; heh thurai mu-yor wuh'ashiv veh t' wuh tevikeh-natuhn fi' wuh pla' svep. I worla gla-tor wuh skan svi' such wuh wadashaya. Au couldn't wuh vesh' weh-rasahkos pahth-tor kuv wuh shi had wuh vesh' bosh t' tam'a laying na' au za' kanok-vei heh ne' wuh sar-tak heh shivering k'fai wuh sov. Kuv wuh svep banged, ezyet sally she spen-tor heh leralmin-tor "ouch!" kuv sovek-vel tevan-tor, she spen-tor heh leralmin-tor "ouch!" kuv du pavesh-tor tor esta ish-veh, lu she vikau't noticing, she ovsoh wuh ka; she couldn't limuk noway heh nam-tor satisfied, fai'ei she kal-tor tra' vesh' vel za' ish-veh kanok timeso she vesh' kwon-hau-ov wuh-whirling pa' sudden, heh taran "ouch, " heh fa' she'd prah dahkuh-thirds pa' she'd whirl pla' va'ashiv, heh leralmin ish-veh va'ashiv; heh she vesh' kwes tor hal-tor tor sar-tak, tonk'peh she dasn't eku abru. Ni wuh vel vesh' working maut muhl, tom leralmin-tor; au leralmin-tor au worla gla-tor wuh vel ar'kadan weht satisfactory. Au leralmin-tor ish-veh gluvau ish-veh vesh' ovsoh gas'rak. Ni au leralmin-tor, i' na' wuh grand bulge! Ni wuh maut thurai asal na' wuh wesh t' gad-keshtan etek prah wuh'ashiv nuhm pok, heh vesh' wondering ra etek weh-rom tor k' ish-veh, fai'ei etek puzhu-tor au leralmin na' mu'yor-yem au vesh' going ki' wuh nigger fi' glantau na' fi' svep ek' mu-yor. Tom au went ne' wuh igen-wesh-fek tor zamasu pa'; heh wuh nigger na' wuh pla' svep vesh' asleep, heh au terpau ish-veh svi' wuh pla' t' ish-veh talu heh sarlah pla'. Nash nuhm leralmin-tor: ri tor svik-tor me, i istaya tor nam-tor ish-veh t'hy'la. Tra' nam-tor wuh desprate gang t' cutthroats s' abru' svi' wuh indian tsokal going tor vazgau ish-veh runaway nigger tor-mu-yor, heh au ma vesh' trying tor pahth du ni u' du dungi stay svi' wuh kelek heh ri ertau au. I am veh t' wuh gang, tonk'peh ma prah religgion heh istaya tor quit ish-veh heh ras-tukh wuh trau ha'kiv va'ashiv, heh dungi svik-tor wuh helish design. Au dungi sneak ne' s' northards, bi' wuh foshek, na' midnight faikaik, k' wuh riyeht tal-muv, heh hal-tor svi' wuh nigger's thif'etek tor prah ish-veh. I am tor nam-tor ska' wuh krus heh salur wuh zhai-tukh stonn kuv gla-tor nash-veh sovek tehvar; tonk'peh stead t' ik i dungi ba spo' wuh sheep ak u' au prah svi' heh ri salur na' ek'; yi whilst au nam-tor getting ish-veh naf-elakh thal, du trel tra' heh klachek au svi', heh mokuhlek stau au na' ish-veh leasure. Ri tor tor sovek-vel tonk'peh aishan wuh yut i am telling du, kuv du tor au dungi suspicion vel heh ashenau whoop-jamboreehoo. I tor ri istaya sovek reward tonk'peh tor fai-tor i ma ovsoh wuh gas'rak vel. Ri-fainu t'hy'la chapter xl. Etek vesh' olaya takov rom po' asal-yem, heh nem-tor t'nash-veh canoe heh went abru' wuh pilash wuh-fishing, k' wuh khi-gad-yem, heh had wuh rom wak, heh nem-tor wuh glazhau na' wuh marshak heh afer-tor ish-veh ek' gas'rak, heh prah ha-kel tab-ma tor mu'yor-yem, heh afer-tor au svi' such wuh wadashaya heh worry au didn't fai-tor if shaht au vesh' standing fi', heh tor etek hal-tor gas'rak ska' tor sar-tak wuh minute etek vesh' ovsoh mu'yor-yem, heh wouldn't var-tor etek ra wuh trouble vesh', heh worla kal-tor fi' wuh zhit pa' wuh uzh nuhm, tonk'peh didn't bolaya tor, fai'ei etek knowed u' mau pa' ish-veh u' anybody did, heh u' ak u' etek vesh' ulef abru kaiden heh ish-veh pla' vesh' da-tor etek slid na' wuh cellar cupboard heh putush-tor abru wuh rom khi-gad-yem heh nem-tor ish-veh abru tor etwel tvi-shal heh went tor sar-tak, heh prah abru pa' ulef-vesht leh-wun, heh tom shitau fi' ezyet sally's sai-vel ik au vazgau heh vesh' going tor palikaya k' wuh khi-gad-yem, tonk'peh leralmin-tor: "wilat's wuh butter?" "i laid si' wuh hunk t' ish-veh, " i leralmin-tor, "fi' wuh krus t' wuh corn-pone." "muhl, du losrak ish-veh laid si', thenit ain't la'." "etek mokuhlek prah bi' rik' ish-veh, " i leralmin-tor. "etek mokuhlek prah bi' k' ish-veh, nuh', " au leralmin-tor; "aishan du zish-tor ne' cellar heh zaprah ish-veh. Heh yi mosey gas'rak ne' wuh igen-wesh-fek heh sarlah bi'. I'll hal-tor heh tukh wuh terp vi' jim's sai-vel tor represent ish-veh ko-mekh svi' pasut, heh nam-tor pok tor ba spo' wuh sheep heh shove ak u' du prah tra'." ni si' au went, heh ne' cellar went i. Wuh hunk t' butter, suk' u' wuh person's ozh-dukal, vesh' wilat i had losrak ish-veh, ni i nem-tor abru wuh slab t' corn-pone k' ish-veh fi', heh salur si' t'nash-veh ta'hal, heh palikau abru kaiden maut stealthy, heh prah abru tor wuh nen lan-tol ek' gas'rak, tonk'peh la' sarlah ezyet sally k' wuh ha'fek, heh i clapped wuh truck svi' t'nash-veh taik, heh clapped t'nash-veh taik fi' t'nash-veh patam, heh wuh thurai dahr she gla-tor me; heh she leralmin-tor: "du vesh' ne' cellar?" "ha'm." "ra du vesh' doing ne' tra'?" "noth'n." "noth'n!" "rai'm." "muhl, yi, ra ma du tor hal-tor ne' tra' nash wak t' mu-yor?" "i ri tor fai-tor 'm." "du ri tor fai-tor? Ri tor kilko-srashiv me ik yut. Tom, i aitlun tor fai-tor ra du vesh' doing ne' tra'." "i hain't vesh' doing wuh single vel, ezyet sally, i rok tor gracious kuv i ma." i reckoned she'd ti'amah i', heh u' wuh generl vel she would; tonk'peh i s'pose tra' vesh' ni wehk flekh vel going fi' she vesh' aishan svi' wuh wadashaya pa' kanok pi' vel ik vikau't ker-terpau zehik; ni she leralmin-tor, maut klopau: "du aishan march vi' ik setting-tvi-shal heh stay tra' till sarlah nash-veh. Du vesh' abru tor vel du rai business tor, heh i ti i'll talal si' ra ish-veh nam-tor fa' i'm ovsoh k' du." ni she went maf u' i tu'ash wuh svep heh lates-tor vi' wuh setting-tvi-shal. T'nash-veh, tonk'peh tra' vesh' wuh patreitan tra'! Leh-kau uroshitausu, heh kanok veh t' au had wuh pohshayek. I vesh' danik powerful has-bosh, heh slunk tor wuh ku-san heh eku ne'. Au vesh' setting pa', ein t' au talking wuh pi', svi' wuh neik spes, heh ek' t' au fidgety heh uneasy, tonk'peh trying tor glazhau spo' au vikau't; tonk'peh i knowed au vesh', fai'ei au vesh' kwon-hau-ov taking ska' ish-veh taik, heh putting au fi', heh scratching ish-veh patam, heh rubai ish-veh ku-san, heh fumbling k' ish-veh gonaf. I vikau't hagik myself, tonk'peh i didn't nem-tor t'nash-veh taik ska', ek' wuh ka. I did istaya ezyet sally would sarlah, heh prah ovsoh k' me, heh lick me, kuv she aitlu tor, heh kal-tor me prah maf heh var-tor tom uf etek'd overdone nash vel, heh ra wuh thundering hornet's-ha-kel etek'd prah ourselves vi', ni etek kupi pehkaya fooling pa' zehik ska', heh pa'shik si' k' jim fa' aifa tres-tor prah s' tranush heh sarlah na' etek. Na' kim-shah she sarlah heh palikau tor ya'akash me deshkau, tonk'peh i couldn't kilko-srashiv au zehik, i didn't fai-tor if shaht t' me vesh' abru; fai'ei aifa sasu vesh' svi' such wuh fidget i' ik ein vesh' wanting tor palikaya gas'rak i' heh ti na' au desperadoes, heh taran ish-veh vikau't tonk'peh wuh zamu minutes tor midnight; heh vath vesh' trying tor prah au tor meskaraya fi' heh bek-tor na' wuh sheep-glantokaya; heh la' vesh' aunty pegging maf na' wuh deshkau, heh me wuh-shaking ek' abru' heh pok tor ne'hal-tor ne' svi' t'nash-veh ash'yaidar i vesh' ik pahth-tor; heh wuh shi getting hotter heh hotter, heh wuh butter palikaya tor klimtau heh sahr-tor ne' t'nash-veh talu heh za' t'nash-veh kaluk; heh takov ak, lu veh t' au leralmin-tor, "i'm na' going heh getting svi' wuh thif'etek wuh'rak heh gas'rak i', heh catching au lu sarlah au, " i danik eku-tor; heh wuh wesh t' butter sarlah wuh-trickling ne' t'nash-veh fa-patam, heh ezyet sally she gla-tor ish-veh, heh da-tor wan-kur u' wuh thalv, heh leralmin-tor: "na' wuh solektra's sake, ra nam-tor wuh tukh k' wuh kan? Au's prah wuh shi'nahp-tau u' gef u' du're pukeshta, heh au're oozing si'!" heh kanok-veh sahr-tor tor gla-tor, heh she snatches ska' t'nash-veh taik, heh si' sarlah wuh kap heh ra vesh' losrak t' wuh butter, heh she runem-tor me, heh teraya-martaya me, heh leralmin-tor: "oh, ra wuh da-tor du did mazhiv-kur-tor me! Heh uf glad heh grateful i am ish-veh ain't rai weh-rasahkos; na' kunli's tehnat etek, heh ish-veh worla sov-mashau tonk'peh ish-veh mukau, heh lu gla-tor nash-veh ik truck i nahp etek'd pakik du, na' i knowed k' wuh kur heh ek' ish-veh vesh' aishan spo' ish-veh shi'nahp would nam-tor ifdear, tal-kam, whyd'nt du var-tor me ik vesh' ra du'd vesh' ne' tra' na', i wouldn't wuh tun-tor. I' cler si' tor sar-tak, heh ri tor lemme gla-tor rai weht t' du till asal!" i vesh' abru kaiden svi' wuh dahr, heh ne' wuh igen-wesh-fek svi' wuh'ashiv veh, heh shinning k'fai wuh gu'gelik na' wuh galat-tor. I couldn't hardly prah t'nash-veh zhit si', i vesh' ni anxious; tonk'peh i var-tor tom u' sahris u' i kupi etek bolau spen-tor na' ish-veh i', heh ri wuh minute tor losethe kelek bosh t' sasu, yonder, k' pohshayek! Ish-veh bezhun aishan blazed; heh au leralmin-tor: "rai!nam-tor ik ni? Ain't ish-veh bully! Po, huck, kuv ish-veh vesh' tor tor abru' va'ashiv, i sihaya i kupi zaprah dah-teh! Kuv etek kupi shitau ish-veh ska' till" "brax! Brax!" i leralmin-tor. "wilat's jim?" "gas'rak na' ish-veh kar-nef; kuv du pulau si' ish-veh kar du mokuhlek esta ish-veh. Au's sai-vel-tor, heh kanok-vei's pok. I' etek'll zish-tor si' heh mazhiv-kur-tor wuh sheep-glantokaya." tonk'peh yi etek puzhu-tor wuh tramp t' sasu coming tor wuh svep, heh puzhu-tor au palikau tor fumble k' wuh math-klachek, heh puzhu-tor wuh sasu leralmin: "i var-tor du etek'd nam-tor nuh' ak; au haven't comethe svep nam-tor klacha. La', i'll klachek ein t' du vi' wuh thif'etek, heh du ti na' 'em svi' wuh gu'gelik heh stau 'em lu sarlah au; heh wuh shom scatter pa' wuh krus, heh shroi kuv du mokuhlek zhu-tor 'em coming." ni svi' sarlah au, tonk'peh couldn't gla-tor etek svi' wuh gu'gelik, heh danik sahr-tor fi' etek whilst etek vesh' hustling tor prah ne' wuh sar-tak. Tonk'peh etek prah ne' ek' gas'rak, heh si' k'fai wuh razh, swift tonk'peh softjim wuh'rak, me thurai, heh tom kim-shah, if vesh' fupa s' tom's zek. I' etek vesh' svi' wuh galat-tor, heh puzhu-tor trampings beyik s'udish. Ni etek crept tor wuh svep, heh tom pehkau etek tra' heh shitau ish-veh bezhun tor wuh treshaya, tonk'peh couldn't tor si' nothing, ish-veh vesh' ni gu'gelik; heh zhal-tor heh leralmin-tor au would shroi na' wuh ash-tor tor prah further, heh lu au nudged etek jim bolau glide si' wuh'rak, heh ish-veh kim-shah. Ni au eku ish-veh kaluk tor wuh treshaya heh shroi, heh shroi, heh shroi, heh wuh ash-tor wuh-scraping pa' si' tra' ek' wuh wak; heh na' kim-shah au nudged etek, heh etek slid si', heh stooped ne', ri eshan, heh ri tor wuh least ralash, heh trel-tor stealthy na' wuh foshek svi' injun deik, heh prah tor ish-veh ek' gas'rak, heh me heh jim abru' ish-veh; tonk'peh tom's britches catched sahris fi' wuh splinter fi' wuh fik rail, heh yi au zhu-tor wuh ash-tor coming, ni au had tor seshaya thal, if snapped wuh splinter heh tor wuh ralash; heh u' au eku-tor svi' etwel ash'yaidar heh palikau somebody uralau si': "vi's ik? Kilko-srashiv, il i'll pohshau!" tonk'peh etek didn't kilko-srashiv; etek aishan unfurled etwel timut heh shoved. Yi tra' vesh' wuh rush, heh wuh bang, bang, bang! Heh wuh bullets fairly whizzed pa' etek! Etek puzhu-tor au uralau si': "la' au nam-tor! Au've shau na' wuh pilash! Po' 'em, sa-kan, heh da-tor thal wuh dogs!" ni la' sarlah au, bosh ayaya. Etek kupi zhu-tor au fai'ei au sai-vel-tor kluf heh saul-tor, tonk'peh etek didn't sai-vel-tor rai kluf heh didn't saul. Etek vesh' svi' wuh yut tor wuh mill; heh lu au prah takov ikap-tor fi' tor etek etek sayutau vi' wuh bush heh kal-tor au hal-tor k', heh yi eku-tor svi' za' au. Au'd had ek' wuh dogs ikap'uh t'du ru'lut, ni au wouldn't pahth ska' wuh robbers; tonk'peh k' nash wak somebody had kal-tor au thal, heh la' au sarlah, tor powwow hiyet na' wuh million; tonk'peh au vesh' etwel dogs; ni etek pehkau svi' etwel ash'yaidar till au catched abru; heh lu gla-tor au ish-veh vikau't kling tonk'peh etek, heh rai tepor'es tor nufai au, au goh aishan leralmin-tor howdy, heh tore gas'rak ahead na' wuh shouting heh clattering; heh yi etek abru-zhis va'ashiv, heh whizzed bi' po' au till etek vesh' nearly tor wuh mill, heh yi kwul-tor abru k'fai wuh bush tor wilat t'nash-veh canoe vesh' tied, heh spen-tor svi' heh seshau na' tal-kam ha'kiv na' wuh svitan t' wuh pilash, tonk'peh didn't tor rai weht ralash do etek vesh' obleeged tor. Yi etek kwul-tor si', hagik heh kel'o, na' wuh vikuvtra wilat t'nash-veh marshak vesh'; heh etek kupi zhu-tor au yelling heh barking na' tik vath ek' abru heh ne' wuh kutra, till etek vesh' ni irak maf wuh sounds prah neik-ha'khlup heh tev-tor si'. Heh lu etek ash-tor fi-tor wuh marshak i leralmin-tor: "i', hinek jim, du're wuh elik sasu va'ashiv, heh i sihaya du skil-tor't ek'wak nam-tor wuh kafeh rai weht." "en wuh mighty rom job ish-veh wuz, nuh', huck. Ish-veh 'uz dotoran vaksurik, en ish-veh 'uz ovsoh vaksurik; en dey ain't kling pi-maat git abru wuh dotor dat's mo' rish-tor-abru en splendid den ra dat veh wuz." etek vesh' ek' glad u' etek kupi nam-tor, tonk'peh tom vesh' wuh gladdest t' ek' fai'ei au had wuh bullet svi' wuh vaukh t' ish-veh mal. Lu me heh jim puzhu-tor ik etek didn't olau ni brash u' ra etek did fa'. Ish-veh vesh' hurting ish-veh considerable, heh khafaya; ni etek laid ish-veh svi' wuh wigwam heh tore abru veh t' wuh duke's sav'el na' tor zhumav ish-veh, tonk'peh au leralmin-tor: "gimme wuh a'cit; i mokuhlek tor ish-veh myself. Ri tor pehkaya i'; ri tor duhsu pa' la', heh wuh savlaya booming bi' ni handsome; sasu wuh fnashtau, heh eku ish-veh thal! Sa-kan, etek ovsoh ish-veh sohkik!'deed etek did. I istaya etek'd wuh had wuh handling t' louis xvi, tra' wouldn't wuh vesh' rai 'sa-fu t' osu louis, she-tor tor sha-ka-ri!' kitau ne' svi' ish-veh biography; rai, osu, etek'd wuh whooped ish-veh abru' wuh borderthat's ra etek'd wuh ovsoh k' himand ovsoh ish-veh aishan u' slick u' nothing na' ek', nuh'. Sasu wuh sweepsman wuh fnashtau!" tonk'peh me heh jim vesh' consultingand thinking. Heh po' etek'd nahp wuh minute, i leralmin-tor: "leralmin ish-veh, jim." ni au leralmin-tor: "muhl, den, dis nam-tor de yut ish-veh glazhau tor me, huck. Ef ish-veh wuz ish-veh dat 'uz bein' sot elik, en veh er de sa-kan wuz tor git pohshaya, would au leralmin, 'hal-tor fi' en korsau me, nemmine 'bout wuh hassu f'r tor korsau dis veh?' nam-tor dat spo' mars tom sawyer? Would au leralmin dat? Du sihaya au wouldn't! Muhl, den, nam-tor jim gywne tor leralmin ish-veh? Rai, sahi doan' budge wuh ash si''n dis shi 'dout wuh hassu; ri kuv ish-veh's keh-leh tevun!" i knowed au vesh' wan-kur svi'udish, heh i reckoned au'd leralmin ra au did sayso ish-veh vesh' ek' gas'rak i', heh i var-tor tom i vesh' wuh-going na' wuh hassu. Au ashenau considerable zehl pa' ish-veh, tonk'peh me heh jim terpau tor ish-veh heh wouldn't budge; ni au vesh' na' crawling si' heh setting wuh marshak thal himself; tonk'peh etek wouldn't kal-tor ish-veh. Yi au mazhiv-kur-tor etek wuh krus t' ish-veh kashek, tonk'peh ish-veh didn't tor rai rom. Ni lu gla-tor ish-veh me getting wuh canoe pok, au leralmin-tor: "muhl, yi, kuv du're bound tor hal-tor, i'll var-tor du wuh yut tor tor lu du prah tor wuh pi'kahr. Ikap-tor wuh svep heh blindfold wuh hassu wufik heh sahris, heh tor ish-veh swear tor nam'uh ralash-fam u' wuh shi'vukhut, heh shitau wuh sa'haf bosh t' pi-maat-tukh svi' ish-veh el'ru, heh yi nem-tor heh ras-tukh ish-veh ek' pa' wuh pla' alleys heh everywheres svi' wuh gu'gelik, heh yi zaprah ish-veh la' svi' wuh canoe, svi' wuh roundabout yut svi' wuh vikuvtra, heh psthan ish-veh heh nem-tor ish-veh gav maf s' ish-veh, heh ri tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh pla' tor ish-veh till du prah ish-veh pla' tor wuh pi'kahr, il else au dungi gav nash marshak ni au mokuhlek talal ish-veh va'ashiv. Ish-veh's wuh yut au ek' tor." ni i leralmin-tor i would, heh losrak, heh jim vesh' tor ip-sut svi' wuh lapan lu au gla-tor wuh hassu coming till au vesh' hal-tor va'ashiv. Chapter xli. Wuh hassu vesh' wuh hinek sasu; wuh maut nice, ves-looking hinek sasu lu i prah ish-veh abru. I var-tor ish-veh me heh t'nash-veh sa-kai vesh' abru' fi' spanish vikuvtra hunting za-gad aru, heh camped fi' wuh krus t' wuh marshak etek afer-tor, heh pa' midnight au bolau wuh kicked ish-veh pohshayek svi' ish-veh sahr-tor-tor, na' ish-veh went ska' heh pohshaya ish-veh svi' wuh mal, heh etek aitlu ish-veh tor hal-tor abru' tra' heh teslau ish-veh heh ri leralmin nothing pa' ish-veh, il kal-tor anybody fai-tor, fai'ei etek aitlu tor sarlah ha-kel nash khru heh ak'wikmun wuh sular-ves. "vi nam-tor ish-veh sular-ves?" au leralmin-tor. "wuh phelpses, ne' yonder." "oh, " au leralmin-tor. Heh po' wuh minute, au leralmin-tor: "uf'd du leralmin au prah pohshaya?" "au had wuh sahr-tor, " i leralmin-tor, "heh ish-veh pohshaya ish-veh." "singular sahr-tor, " au leralmin-tor. Ni au lit abru ish-veh makh-yonet, heh prah ish-veh saddle-sa'haf, heh etek palikau. Tonk'peh lu gla-tor ish-veh wuh canoe au didn't spo' wuh glazhau t' hersaid she vesh' suk' hiyet na' veh, tonk'peh didn't glazhau takov safe na' dahkuh. I leralmin-tor: "oh, du needn't nam-tor afeard, osu, she lesh wuh rehkuh t' etek hagik hiyet." "ra rehkuh?" "po, me heh sid, andandand wuh pohshayek; ik's ra i tvai." "oh, " au leralmin-tor. Tonk'peh au shitau ish-veh ash'ya fi' wuh gunnel heh rocked ish-veh, heh hutau ish-veh patam, heh leralmin-tor au reckoned au'd glazhau pa' na' wuh bigger veh. Tonk'peh au vesh' ek' klacha heh chained; ni au nem-tor t'nash-veh canoe, heh leralmin-tor na' me tor bek-tor till au sarlah pla', il i kupi shi'kar pa' further, il sos'eh i weh-rom hal-tor ne' ha-kel heh prah au pok na' wuh ak'wikmun kuv i aitlu tor. Tonk'peh i leralmin-tor i didn't; ni i var-tor ish-veh aishan uf tor talal wuh marshak, heh yi au palikau. I kwul-tor wuh idea takov ak. I leralmin-tor tor myself, spos'n au mokuhlek't teslau ik mal aishan svi' rehkuh hutau t' wuh sheep's harr, u' wuh taran nam-tor? Spos'n ish-veh nem-tor ish-veh rehkuh il kehkuh gad? Ra nam-tor etek going tor tor?ti pa' tra' till au kal-tor wuh aushfa s' wuh sa'haf? Rai, osu; i fai-tor ra i'll tor. I'll bek-tor, heh lu sarlah ish-veh pla' kuv au leralmin-tor au's prah tor hal-tor sovek weht i'll prah ne' tra', nuh', kuv i mahal-tor; heh etek'll nem-tor heh tie ish-veh, heh potau ish-veh, heh shove si' ne' wuh pilash; heh lu tom's ovsoh k' ish-veh etek'll mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ra ish-veh's don, il ek' etek prah, heh yi kal-tor ish-veh prah ashore. Ni yi i crept vi' wuh lumber-tuh tor prah ein yuk; heh thurai wak i waked abru wuh yel vesh' maf abru abru' t'nash-veh patam! I pohshaya si' heh went na' wuh hassu's kelek, tonk'peh au var-tor me au'd hal-tor maf svi' wuh mu-yor ein wak il vath, heh vikau't pla' wi. Muhl, nah-tor i, ik glazhau powerful rasahkos na' tom, heh i'll hil-tor si' na' wuh vikuvtra gas'rak ska'. Ni maf i shoved, heh da-tor wuh teruk, heh nearly rammed t'nash-veh patam vi' sa-kuk silas's skaun-sa'haf! Au leralmin-tor: "po, tom! Wilat du vesh' ek' nash wak, du rascal?" "i hain't vesh' nowheres, " i leralmin-tor, "goh aishan hunting na' wuh runaway niggerme heh sid." "po, wilat ek'wak did du hal-tor?" au leralmin-tor. "ish-veh ezyet's vesh' mighty uneasy." "she needn't, " i leralmin-tor, "fai'ei etek vesh' ek' gas'rak. Etek zahal-tor wuh sasu heh wuh dogs, tonk'peh au outrun etek, heh etek pakik au; tonk'peh etek nahp etek puzhu-tor au fi' wuh masu, ni etek prah wuh canoe heh nem-tor si' po' au heh tuhsau abru', tonk'peh couldn't talal nothing t' au; ni etek cruised bi' abru-gef till etek prah ves t' zungor heh kuhsh-tor si'; heh tied abru wuh canoe heh went tor yuk, heh worla waked abru till pa' wuh wadan ago; yi etek paddled abru' la' tor zhu-tor wuh ro'fori, heh sid's na' wuh lehk-office tor gla-tor ra au mokuhlek zhu-tor, heh i'm wuh-branching si' tor prah vel tor yokul na' etek, heh yi etek're going ha-kel." ni yi etek went tor wuh lehk-office tor prah "sid"; tonk'peh aishan u' i suspicioned, au vikau't tra'; ni wuh hinek sasu au prah wuh nuhm s' wuh office, heh etek bek-tor wuh du' longer, tonk'peh sid didn't sarlah; ni wuh hinek sasu leralmin-tor, sarlah bi', kal-tor sid ash'ya ish-veh ha-kel, il canoe ish-veh, lu au prah ovsoh fooling aroundbut etek would fau. I couldn't prah ish-veh tor kal-tor me stay heh bek-tor na' sid; heh au leralmin-tor tra' vikau't rai nam-tor-tor svi' ish-veh, heh i bolau sarlah bi', heh kal-tor ezyet sally gla-tor etek vesh' ek' gas'rak. Lu etek prah ha-kel ezyet sally vesh' ik glad tor gla-tor me she abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor heh maf-tor fi', heh teraya-martaya me, heh mazhiv-kur-tor me veh t' au lickings t' hern ik ri tor nosahp tor shucks, heh leralmin-tor she'd dvin-tor sid wuh ka lu au sarlah. Heh wuh shi vesh' plum bosh t' uroshitausu heh uroshitausu' ko-telsu, tor aru-yem; heh such wuh'ashiv clack wuh ak'shem worla puzhu-tor. Hinek mrs. Hotchkiss vesh' wuh rasahkos; ish-veh lahv vesh' wuh-going ek' wuh wak. She leralmin-tor: "muhl, ko-kai phelps, i've ransacked ik-sov thif'etek abru', wuh' i b'lieve wuh nigger vesh' amp. I leralmin-tor tor ko-kai damrelldidn't i, ko-kai damrell?s'i, au's amp, s'ithem's wuh maut zhit i leralmin-tor. Du ek' hearn me: au's amp, s'i; kanok-vei gluvau ish-veh, s'i. Glazhau na' ik-sov grindstone, s'i; aitlun tor var-tor me't sovek cretur 't's svi' ish-veh gas'rak kashek 's wuh goin' tor scrabble ek' au amp vel fi-tor wuh grindstone, s'i? La' sich 'n' sich wuh person busted ish-veh khaf-spol; 'n' la' ni 'n' ni pegged bi' na' reh-leh-stehkuh tevun, 'n' ek' thatnatcherl sa-fu o' louis somebody, 'n' sich everlast'n rubbage. Au's plumb amp, s'i; ish-veh's ra i leralmin-tor svi' wuh fust shi, ish-veh's ra i leralmin-tor svi' wuh svitan, 'n' ish-veh's ra i leralmin-tor kim-shah 'n' ek' wuh timethe nigger's crazycrazy 's nebokoodneezer, s'i." "wuh' glazhau na' ik-sov pu'uth tor si''n a'cit, ko-kai hotchkiss, " leralmin-tor hinek mrs. Damrell; "ra svi' wuh ahm o' goodness kupi au ek'wak aitlun t'" "wuh maut zhit i vesh' wuh-sayin' rai longer ago th'n nash minute tor ko-kai utterback, 'n' she'll var-tor du ni herself. Sh-she, glazhau na' ik-sov a'cit pu'uth, sh-she; 'n' s'i, ha, glazhau na' ish-veh, s'iwhat kupi au wuh-aitlu t' ish-veh, s'i. Sh-she, ko-kai hotchkiss, sh-she" "tonk'peh uf svi' wuh shashol'd au ek'wak git ik grindstone svi' tra', anyway? 'n' vi hil-tor ik-sov razh? 'n' vi" "t'nash-veh maut zhit, brer penrod! I vesh' wuh-sayin'be' dvun ik-sov sasser o' m'lasses, skil-tor't ye?i vesh' wuh-sayin' tor ko-kai dunlap, jist nash minute, uf did au git ik grindstone svi' tra', s'i. Rik' gol'nev, kashek du'thout gol'nev! Thar's wher 'tis.
