Ri tor var-tor me, s'i; tra' wuz gol'nev, s'i; 'n' ther' wuz wuh plenty gol'nev, nuh', s'i; ther's ben wuh dozen wuh-helpin' ik nigger, 'n' i ti i'd wadi kanok kim-shah nigger fi' nash shi tonk'peh i'd talal si' vi ovsoh ish-veh, s'i; 'n' moreover, s'i" "wuh dozen leralmin-tor du!keh-leh couldn't wuh ovsoh kanok vel ik's vesh' ovsoh. Glazhau na' au nuf-lipau zuneshek heh vel, uf tedious au've vesh' tor; glazhau na' ik sar-tak-mal sawed ska' k' 'm, wuh wehk gad's ar'kadan na' shehkuh sasu; glazhau na' ik nigger tor si''n terp fi' wuh sar-tak; heh glazhau na'" "du lau muhl leralmin ish-veh, brer hightower! Ish-veh's jist u' i vesh' wuh-sayin' tor brer phelps, ish-veh sha' shal. S'e, ra tor du nah-tor t' ish-veh, ko-kai hotchkiss, s'e? Nah-tor o' ra, brer phelps, s'i? Nah-tor o' ik sar-tak-mal sawed ska' ik wuh yut, s'e? Nah-tor t' ish-veh, s'i? I ti ish-veh worla sawed itself ska', s'isomebody sawed ish-veh, s'i; ik's t'nash-veh opinion, nem-tor ish-veh il trasha ish-veh, ish-veh mayn't nam-tor rai 'tum-tor, s'i, tonk'peh sich u' 't nam-tor, ish-veh's t'nash-veh opinion, s'i, 'n' kuv sovek ak'shem k'n palikaya wuh weh-rom veh, s'i, kal-tor ish-veh tor ish-veh, s'i, ik's ek'. I leralmin-tor tor ko-kai dunlap, s'i" "po, dog t'nash-veh aushfa, au bolau wuh ben wuh kelek-bosh o' niggers svi' tra' kanok mu-yor na' kehkuh wehk gad tor wuh ovsoh ek' ik ar'kadan, ko-kai phelps. Glazhau na' ik shirtevery kim-shah inch t' ish-veh kivered abru' k' tsat african writ'n ovsoh k' khaf! Bolau wuh ben wuh marshak uv 'm na' ish-veh gas'rak bi', ek' wuh wak, amost. Po, i'd mazhiv-kur-tor dahkuh dollars ki' ish-veh telv-tor tor me; 'n' u' na' wuh niggers ik kitau ish-veh, i 'neik i'd nem-tor 'n' lash 'm t'll" "sutra tor gol'nev ish-veh, sa-kai marples! Muhl, i reckon du'd nah-tor ni kuv du'd wuh vesh' svi' nash kelek na' wuh du' pla'. Po, au've vazgau kanok-vei au kupi ti ish-veh el'ru onand etek wuh-watching ek' wuh wak, kashek du. Au vazgau ik sav'el gas'rak ska' o' wuh zehl! Heh u' na' ik thalv au tor wuh a'cit pu'uth s', ther' ain't rai telling uf wehk wak au didn't vazgau ik; heh flour, heh ha'fek, heh ha'fek, heh floku, heh wuh hinek warming-sunil, heh danik wuh thousand vel ik i disremember i', heh t'nash-veh uzh calico sai-vel; heh me heh silas heh t'nash-veh sid heh tom fi' wuh ek'kayik glantau gad heh mu-yor, u' i vesh' wuh-telling du, heh ri wuh veh t' etek kupi kum ip-sut il isachya il glan il ralash t' au; heh la' na' wuh kim-shah minute, lo heh behold du, au zish-tor gas'rak svi' ne' etwel han heh duhsu etek, heh ri goh duhsu etek tonk'peh wuh injun tsokal robbers nuh', heh actuly prah maf k' ik nigger safe heh ralash, heh ik k' leh-sheh sasu heh dah-leh-dahkuh dogs gas'rak fi' ish-veh maut timut na' ik maut wak! I var-tor du, ish-veh aishan bangs sovek-vel i ek'wak puzhu-tor t'. Po, sperits couldn't wuh ovsoh weh-rom heh vesh' rai smarter. Heh i reckon au bolau wuh vesh' speritsbecause, du fai-tor etwel dogs, heh ther' ain't rai weh-rom; muhl, au dogs worla kauk prah fi' wuh yut t' 'm wuh'wak! Du danau ik tor me kuv du mokuhlek!sovek t' du!" "muhl, ish-veh tor kuhsh-tor" "tor-gav alive, i worla" "ni gol'nev me, i wouldn't wuh nam-tor" "kelek-pi'tak u' muhl u'" "goodnessgracioussakes, i'd wuh ben afeard tor ha-tor svi' sich wuh" "'fraid tor ha-tor!po, i vesh' ik pahth-tor i dasn't hardly hal-tor tor sar-tak, il prah abru, il ti ne', il eku ne', ko-kai ridgeway. Po, au'd vazgau wuh verywhy, goodness sakes, du mokuhlek guess ra ves t' wuh paikaya i vesh' svi' k' wuh wak midnight sarlah kim-shah mu-yor. I rok tor gracious kuv i vikau't kwes au'd vazgau ein o' wuh skan! I vesh' aishan tor ik be' dvun i didn't ma rai reasoning sutra rai weht. Ish-veh glazhau duhik hiyet i', svi' wuh gad-wakik; tonk'peh i leralmin-tor tor myself, tra''s t'nash-veh dahkuh ri donku-tor sa-kan asleep, 'yut abru kaiden svi' ik lonesome tvi-shal, heh i afsakau tor goodness i vesh' ik uneasy 't i crep' abru tra' heh klacha 'em svi'! I did. Heh anybody would. Fai'ei, du fai-tor, lu du prah pahth-tor ik yut, heh ish-veh potau sahran fi', heh getting weh-rasahkos heh weh-rasahkos ek' wuh wak, heh ish-veh wits prah tor addling, heh du prah tor doing ek' wihfelau o' kwai vel, heh k'-heh-k' du nah-tor tor yourself, spos'n i vesh' wuh sa-kan, heh vesh' maf abru tra', heh wuh svep ain't klacha, heh du" she pehkau, looking ves t' wondering, heh yi she da-tor ish-veh patam pa' vohris, heh lu ish-veh bezhun lit fi' mei prah abru heh nem-tor wuh lates. Leralmin-tor i tor myself, i mokuhlek danau weh-rom uf sarlah etek tor ri nam-tor svi' ik tvi-shal nash asal kuv i hal-tor si' tor veh vla heh orenau abru' ish-veh wuh pi'. Ni i ovsoh ish-veh. Tonk'peh i dasn't hal-tor ausachya, il she'd wuh satau na' me. Heh lu ish-veh vesh' tab-ma svi' wuh gad wuh sutra ek' went, heh yi sarlah nash-veh svi' heh var-tor ish-veh wuh ralash heh shooting waked abru me heh "sid, " heh wuh svep vesh' klacha, heh etek aitlu tor gla-tor wuh mihrsh, ni etek went ne' wuh igen-wesh-fek, heh fi' t' etek prah dash-tor wuh pi', heh etek didn't worla aitlun tor ar'kadan ik rai weht. Heh yi i went fi' heh var-tor ish-veh ek' ra i var-tor sa-kuk silas fa'; heh yi she leralmin-tor she'd forgive etek, heh sos'eh ish-veh vesh' ek' gas'rak hiyet anyway, heh pa' ra wuh ak'shem lau gish t' sa-kan, na' ek' sa-kan vesh' wuh takov harum-scarum lot u' ausachya u' she kupi gla-tor; heh ni, u' wu u' rai klau hadn't sarlah t' ish-veh, she judged she weh-rom shitau svi' ish-veh wak hasu grateful etek vesh' alive heh muhl heh she had etek fam dvun, stead t' fretting abru' ra vesh' vesht heh ovsoh. Ni yi she shok-tor me, heh patted me fi' wuh patam, heh eku-tor vi' wuh ves t' wuh khav-kur orenau; heh takov ak spen-tor abru, heh leralmin-tor: "po, lawsamercy, ish-veh's danik mu-yor, heh sid ri sarlah wi! Ra has shetau t' ik sa-kan?" gla-tor nash-veh t'nash-veh pavesh; ni i skips abru heh leralmin-tor: "i'll sahr-tor gas'rak abru tor kahr heh prah ish-veh, " i leralmin-tor. "rai du skil-tor't, " she leralmin-tor. "du'll stay gas'rak wher' du nam-tor; veh's hiyet tor nam-tor pakik na' wuh wak. Kuv au ain't la' tor mu'yor-yem, ish-veh sa-kuk 'll hal-tor." muhl, au vikau't tra' tor mu'yor-yem; ni gas'rak po' mu'yor-yem sa-kuk went. Au sarlah pla' pa' lehkuh wuh pi' zeshau uneasy; hadn't sahr-tor mes' tom's yut. Ezyet sally vesh' wuh rom deal uneasy; tonk'peh sa-kuk silas au leralmin-tor tra' vikau't rai occasion tor beboys dungi nam-tor sa-kan, au leralmin-tor, heh du'll gla-tor nash-veh da-tor abru svi' wuh asal ek' ralash heh gas'rak. Ni she had tor nam-tor satisfied. Tonk'peh she leralmin-tor she'd eku abru na' ish-veh wuh du' anyway, heh potau wuh ta'hal yontau ni au kupi gla-tor ish-veh. Heh yi lu i went abru tor sar-tak she sarlah abru k' me heh zaprah ish-veh ha'fek, heh k'hy-tor me svi', heh mothered me ni rom i olau tvai, heh spo' i couldn't glazhau ish-veh svi' wuh limuk; heh she eku ne' fi' wuh sar-tak heh variben k' me wuh akarshif, heh leralmin-tor ra wuh splendid sa-kan sid vesh', heh didn't seem tor aitlun tor ek'wak pehkaya talking pa' ish-veh; heh potau asking me kanok i' heh yi kuv i reckoned au kupi wuh prah pakik, il dash-tor, il sos'eh drownded, heh lau nam-tor laying na' nash minute somewheres suffering il tevik, heh she ri k' ish-veh tor gol'nev ish-veh, heh ni wuh bezhun-masu would thezh ne' ralash-fam, heh i would var-tor ish-veh ik sid vesh' ek' gas'rak, heh would nam-tor ha-kel svi' wuh asal, sure; heh she would lerakhovau t'nash-veh el'ru, il sos'eh shok me, heh var-tor me tor leralmin ish-veh va'ashiv, heh potau fi' taran ish-veh, fai'ei ish-veh ovsoh ish-veh rom, heh she vesh' svi' ni mau trouble. Heh lu she vesh' going maf she glazhau ne' svi' t'nash-veh bezhun ni br'xan heh gentle, heh leralmin-tor: "wuh svep ain't going tor nam-tor klacha, tom, heh tra''s wuh krani heh wuh fek; tonk'peh du'll nam-tor rom, skil-tor't du? Heh du skil-tor't hal-tor? Na' t'nash-veh sake." tor-gav fai-tor i aitlu tor hal-tor rasahkos hiyet tor gla-tor pa' tom, heh vesh' ek' intending tor hal-tor; tonk'peh po' ik i wouldn't wuh went, ri na' kingdoms. Tonk'peh she vesh' fi' t'nash-veh kashek heh tom vesh' fi' t'nash-veh kashek, ni i yuk-tor maut restless. Heh dah'wak i went ne' wuh fek maf svi' wuh mu-yor, heh trel-tor pa' khom, heh gla-tor ish-veh setting tra' k' ish-veh ha'fek svi' wuh krani k' ish-veh bezhun na' wuh fau-yut heh wuh bezhun-masu svi' au; heh i istau i kupi tor vel na' ish-veh, tonk'peh i couldn't, goh tor swear ik i wouldn't worla tor nothing tor grieve ish-veh sovek weht. Heh wuh wuh wak i waked abru na' gad-keshtan, heh slid ne', heh she vesh' tra' wi, heh ish-veh ha'fek vesh' danik si', heh ish-veh hinek zhai-kur patam vesh' resting fi' ish-veh el'ru, heh she vesh' asleep. Chapter xlii. Wuh hinek sasu vesh' uptown va'ashiv fa' asal-yem, tonk'peh couldn't prah rai yut t' tom; heh fi' t' au eku na' wuh pasu thinking, heh ri taran nothing, heh looking mournful, heh ish-veh mon getting samu, heh ri eating sovek-vel. Heh k'-heh-k' wuh hinek sasu leralmin-tor: "did i mazhiv-kur-tor du wuh nuhm?" "ra nuhm?" "wuh veh i prah za-gad s' wuh lehk-office." "rai, du didn't mazhiv-kur-tor me rai nuhm." "muhl, i bolau wuh forgot ish-veh." ni au rummaged ish-veh abru'lik, heh yi went ska' somewheres wilat au had laid ish-veh ne', heh zaprah ish-veh, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor ish-veh. She leralmin-tor: "po, ish-veh's s' st. Petersburgit's s' sis." i kal-tor wuh'ashiv lates would tor me rom; tonk'peh i couldn't stir. Tonk'peh fa' she kupi shaya ish-veh tu'ash she eku-tor ish-veh heh runfor she gla-tor vel. Heh ni did i. Ish-veh vesh' tom sawyer fi' wuh yuk-vel; heh ik hinek hassu; heh jim, svi' ish-veh calico sai-vel, k' ish-veh el'ru tied za' ish-veh; heh wuh lot t' sutra. I ip-sut wuh nuhm za' wuh wuh'rak vel ik sarlah handy, heh rushed. She flung herself na' tom, maf-tor, heh leralmin-tor: "oh, au's tevik, au's tevik, i fai-tor au's tevik!" heh tom au da-tor ish-veh patam wuh pi', heh muttered vel il vath, if gluvau au vikau't svi' ish-veh gas'rak kashek; yi she flung abru ish-veh el'ru, heh leralmin-tor: "au's alive, itaren oekon! Heh ik's hiyet!" heh she snatched wuh shok t' ish-veh, heh flew na' wuh kelek tor prah wuh sar-tak pok, heh scattering zek gas'rak heh losrak na' wuh niggers heh kanok-veh else, u' sahris u' ish-veh lahv kupi hal-tor, kanok spen-tor t' wuh yut. I zahal-tor wuh sasu tor gla-tor ra au vesh' going tor tor k' jim; heh wuh hinek hassu heh sa-kuk silas zahal-tor po' tom vi' wuh kelek. Wuh sasu vesh' maut huffy, heh ein t' au aitlu tor geldau jim na' wuh li-fal tor ek' wuh vath niggers pa' tra', ni au wouldn't nam-tor trying tor sahr-tor maf spo' jim ovsoh, heh tor such wuh marshak t' trouble, heh keeping wuh bosh skan pahth-tor danik tor tevakh na' gad heh mu-yor. Tonk'peh wuh vath leralmin-tor, ri tor tor ish-veh, ish-veh wouldn't kilko-srashiv na' ek'; au ain't etwel nigger, heh ish-veh owner would da-tor abru heh tor etek vlitau na' ish-veh, sure. Ni ik cooled au ne' wuh pi', fai'ei wuh sutra ik's kwon-hau-ov wuh danik anxious na' tor geldau wuh nigger ik hain't ovsoh aishan gas'rak nam-tor kwon-hau-ov wuh maut ones ik ain't wuh danik anxious tor vlitau na' ish-veh lu au've prah ish-veh satisfaction s' ish-veh. Au cussed jim considerble, hi, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh cuff il dahkuh vla wuh patam wuh'wak svi' wuh du', tonk'peh jim worla leralmin-tor nothing, heh au worla kal-tor fi' tor fai-tor me, heh au nem-tor ish-veh tor wuh ka thif'etek, heh shitau ish-veh sha' sai-vel fi' ish-veh, heh chained ish-veh va'ashiv, heh ri tor rai sar-tak-mal nash wak, tonk'peh tor wuh suk' staple drove vi' wuh lanet lap-fek, heh chained ish-veh el'ru, nuh', heh fi' mal, heh leralmin-tor au vikau't ki' nothing tonk'peh kap heh masu tor yokul po' nash till ish-veh owner sarlah, il au vesh' makau na' auction fai'ei au didn't sarlah svi' wuh ac'ruth wu-vath t' wak, heh boshau abru etwel razh, heh leralmin-tor wuh couple t' uroshitausu k' pohshayek bolau lamok glantau pa' pa' wuh thif'etek kanok mu-yor, heh wuh bulldog tied tor wuh svep svi' wuh gad-wakik; heh pa' nash wak au vesh' k'fai k' wuh job heh vesh' tapering ska' k' wuh ves t' generl rom-bye cussing, heh yi wuh hinek hassu sarlah heh nem-tor wuh glazhau, heh leralmin-tor: "ri tor nam-tor rai rougher fi' ish-veh do du're obleeged tor, fai'ei au ain't wuh rasahkos nigger. Lu i prah tor wilat i afer-tor wuh sa-kan gla-tor nash-veh i couldn't tresahk wuh bullet si' rik' ein gol'nev, heh au vikau't svi' rai nosh na' me tor trasha tor hal-tor heh prah gol'nev; heh au prah wuh pi' weh-rasahkos heh wuh pi' weh-rasahkos, heh po' wuh akarshif au went s' ish-veh patam, heh wouldn't kal-tor me sarlah wuh-nigh ish-veh sovek weht, heh leralmin-tor kuv i chalked ish-veh marshak au'd stau me, heh rai shaht t' kwai duh'es spo' ik, heh gla-tor nash-veh i couldn't tor sovek-vel na' ek' k' ish-veh; ni i leralmin-tor, i prah ki' gol'nev somehow; heh wuh minute i leralmin-tor ish-veh si' ukrau nash nigger s' somewheres heh leralmin-tor au'll gol'nev, heh au ovsoh ish-veh, nuh', heh ovsoh ish-veh maut muhl. Veling i judged au bolau nam-tor wuh runaway nigger, heh tra' i vesh'! Heh tra' i had tor terpau gas'rak zehik bi' ek' wuh shom t' wuh gad heh ek' mu-yor. Ish-veh vesh' wuh teslau, i var-tor du! I had wuh couple t' hasausu k' wuh chills, heh veling i'd t' tishau tor sahr-tor abru tor kahr heh gla-tor au, tonk'peh i dasn't, fai'ei wuh nigger lau prah maf, heh yi i'd nam-tor tor tenai; heh wi worla wuh skiff sarlah ikap-tor hiyet na' me tor masu-kov. Ni tra' i had tor terpau plumb abi' gad-ha'khlup nash asal; heh i worla gla-tor wuh nigger ik vesh' wuh weh-rom nuss il faithfuller, heh wi au vesh' risking ish-veh el'es tor tor ish-veh, heh vesh' ek' zungor si', nuh', heh gla-tor nash-veh eiktra hiyet au'd vesh' ar'kada nen lerash lately. I tishau wuh nigger na' ik; i var-tor du, gentlemen, wuh nigger spo' ik nam-tor don wuh thousand dollarsand ves skasaya, nuh'. I had kanok-vei i bolau, heh wuh sa-kan vesh' doing u' muhl tra' u' au would wuh ovsoh na' homebetter, sos'eh, fai'ei ish-veh vesh' ni hizhuk; tonk'peh tra' i vesh', k' fi' t' 'm fi' t'nash-veh el'ru, heh tra' i had tor terpau till pa' gad-keshtan nash asal; yi ein sasu svi' wuh skiff sarlah k', heh u' rom kunli would ma ish-veh wuh nigger vesh' setting k' wuh pallet k' ish-veh patam propped fi' ish-veh mal-nef ralash asleep; ni i motioned au svi' hizhuk, heh au trel-tor abru fi' ish-veh heh runem-tor ish-veh heh tied ish-veh fa' au knowed ra au vesh' pa', heh etek worla had rai trouble. Heh wuh sa-kan hasu svi' wuh ves t' wuh flighty yuk, nuh', etek nessau wuh fel heh hitched wuh marshak fi', heh towed ish-veh abru' maut nice heh hizhuk, heh wuh nigger worla tor wuh least zehl il leralmin-tor wuh zhit s' wuh palikaya. Au ain't rai rasahkos nigger, gentlemen; ik's ra i nah-tor pa' ish-veh." somebody leralmin-tor: "muhl, ish-veh sounds maut rom, hassu, i'm obleeged tor leralmin." yi wuh vath softened abru wuh pi', nuh', heh i vesh' mighty itar-bosh tor ik hinek hassu na' doing jim ik rom da-tor; heh i vesh' glad ish-veh vesh' fupa s' t'nash-veh judgment t' ish-veh, nuh'; fai'ei i nahp au had wuh rom khaf-spol svi' ish-veh heh vesh' wuh rom sasu wuh wuh'rak wak gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh. Yi au ek' sep-wafikh ik jim had bae'cok maut muhl, heh vesh' nazh-tor ki' ein beglanau nem-tor t' ish-veh, heh reward. Ni kanok veh t' au ugau, gas'rak si' heh hearty, ik au wouldn't cuss ish-veh rai weht. Yi au sasarlah heh klacha ish-veh abru. I rok-tor au vesh' going tor leralmin au kupi ma veh il dahkuh t' wuh naf-elakh nem-tor ska', fai'ei au vesh' rotten ras, il kupi ma kahm heh yar-kur k' ish-veh kap heh masu; tonk'peh au didn't nah-tor t' ish-veh, heh i reckoned ish-veh vikau't buhfik na' me tor rish svi', tonk'peh i judged i'd prah wuh hassu's yarn tor ezyet sally somehow il vath u' ak u' i'd prah k'fai wuh raf-shayek ik vesh' laying aishan ahead t' meexplanations, i tvai, t' uf i forgot tor mention pa' sid hasu pohshaya lu i vesh' telling uf ish-veh heh me shitau svi' ik dratted mu-yor paddling pa' hunting wuh runaway nigger. Tonk'peh i had plenty wak. Ezyet sally she terpau tor wuh has-bosh-tvi-shal ek' gad heh ek' mu-yor, heh kanok wak gla-tor nash-veh sa-kuk silas mooning pa' i sayutau ish-veh. Thurai asal i puzhu-tor tom vesh' wuh rom deal weh-rom, heh au leralmin-tor ezyet sally vesh' hal-tor tor prah wuh nap. Ni i trel-tor tor wuh has-bosh-tvi-shal, heh kuv i afer-tor ish-veh kum'i i reckoned etek kupi shitau abru wuh yarn na' wuh skan ik would pu-tor. Tonk'peh au vesh' sleeping, heh sleeping maut peaceful, nuh'; heh spoh, ri yon-limuk-tor wuh yut au vesh' lu au sarlah. Ni i eku ne' heh laid na' ish-veh tor wake. Svi' pa' ulef wuh wadan ezyet sally sarlah gliding svi', heh tra' i vesh', abru wuh stump va'ashiv! She motioned me tor nam-tor fam dvun, heh eku ne' k' me, heh palikau tor zhal, heh leralmin-tor etek kupi ek' nam-tor joyful i', fai'ei ek' wuh symptoms vesh' wuh'rak-tav, heh au'd vesh' sleeping spo' ik na' ek'wak ni wu, heh looking weh-rom heh peacefuller ek' wuh wak, heh lehkuh tor veh au'd wake abru svi' ish-veh gas'rak kashek. Ni etek eku tra' watching, heh k'-heh-k' au stirs wuh zeshau, heh tu'ash ish-veh bezhun maut malatik, heh nem-tor wuh glazhau, heh leralmin-tor: "tonk'peh!po, i'm na' ha-kel! Uf's ik? Wilat's wuh marshak?" "ish-veh's ek' gas'rak, " i leralmin-tor. "heh jim?" "wuh ka, " i leralmin-tor, tonk'peh couldn't leralmin ish-veh takov brash. Tonk'peh au worla pubeglanau, tonk'peh leralmin-tor: "rom! Splendid! I' etek're ek' gas'rak heh safe! Did du var-tor aunty?" i vesh' going tor leralmin ha; tonk'peh she chipped svi' heh leralmin-tor: "pa' ra, sid?" "po, pa' wuh yut wuh bosh vel vesh' ovsoh." "ra bosh vel?" "po, wuh bosh vel. Tra' ain't tonk'peh veh; uf etek eku wuh runaway nigger freeme heh tom." "rom solektra! Eku wuh sahr-tor ra nam-tor wuh kan talking pa'! Tal-kam, tal-kam, s' ish-veh patam va'ashiv!" "rai, i ain't s' t'nash-veh patam; i fai-tor ek' ra i'm talking pa'. Etek did eku ish-veh freeme heh tom. Etek laid si' tor tor ish-veh, heh etek ovsoh ish-veh. Heh etek ovsoh ish-veh sohkik, nuh'." au'd prah wuh palikaya, heh she worla rihamau ish-veh abru, aishan eku heh nantau heh nantau, heh kal-tor ish-veh clip bi', heh i gla-tor ish-veh vikau't rai nam-tor-tor na' me tor shitau svi'. "po, aunty, ish-veh kodona etek wuh tepul t' workweeks t' ithours heh wadan, kanok mu-yor, whilst du vesh' ek' asleep. Heh etek had tor vazgau ha'fek, heh wuh thalv, heh wuh sav'el, heh ish-veh sai-vel, heh floku, heh zhai-tukh math, heh nuf-lipau, heh wuh warming-sunil, heh wuh grindstone, heh flour, heh aishan rai shaht t' vel, heh du mokuhlek't nah-tor ra ar'kadan ish-veh vesh' tor tor wuh zuneshek, heh pens, heh inscriptions, heh veh vel il wuh'ashiv, heh du mokuhlek't nah-tor ulef wuh mihrsh ish-veh vesh'. Heh etek had tor tor abru wuh bikuv t' tevikeh-natuhn heh vel, heh nonnamous nuhm s' wuh robbers, heh prah abru heh ne' wuh igen-wesh-fek, heh hil-tor wuh razh vi' wuh thif'etek, heh tor wuh man-elakh pu'uth heh satau ish-veh svi' pufas-tor abru svi' wuh pie, heh satau svi' floku heh vel tor ar'kadan k' svi' ish-veh apron abru'lik" "mercy sakes!" "heh tus abru wuh thif'etek k' rats heh oluhk heh ni fi', na' apc'koik na' jim; heh yi du potau tom la' ni wu k' wuh butter svi' ish-veh taik ik sarlah du be' spiling wuh bosh business, fai'ei wuh sasu sarlah fa' etek vesh' s' wuh thif'etek, heh etek had tor rush, heh au puzhu-tor etek heh kal-tor yetur na' etek, heh i prah t'nash-veh thresh, heh etek sayutau s' wuh yut heh kal-tor au hal-tor k', heh lu wuh dogs sarlah au vikau't interested svi' etek, tonk'peh went na' wuh danik ralash, heh etek prah etwel canoe, heh tor na' wuh marshak, heh vesh' ek' safe, heh jim vesh' wuh elik sasu, heh etek ovsoh ish-veh ek' k' ourselves, heh wasn't ish-veh bully, aunty!" "muhl, i worla puzhu-tor wuh tishau t' ish-veh svi' ek' t'nash-veh pukeshta gad! Ni ish-veh vesh' du, du pi' rapscallions, ik's vesh' tor ek' nash trouble, heh da-tor kanok-veh's wits sok'i svi'udish si' heh pahth-tor etek ek' danik tor tevakh. I've u' rom wuh notion u' ek'wak i had svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv tor nem-tor ish-veh si' o' du nash maut minute. Tor nah-tor, la' i've vesh', mu-yor po' mu-yor, ayou aishan prah muhl wuh'wak, du nu'ri scamp, heh i ti i'll mazhiv-kur wuh hinek harry si' o' fi' o' ye!" tonk'peh tom, au vesh' ni yaut heh joyful, au aishan couldn't meskaraya svi', heh ish-veh lahv aishan went itshe wuh-chipping svi', heh spitting yon ek' bi', heh fi' t' au going ish-veh na' wuh'wak, spo' wuh aushfa convention; heh she leralmin-tor: "muhl, du prah ek' wuh tizh'es du mokuhlek s' ish-veh i', na' kashek i var-tor du kuv i kum du meddling k' ish-veh va'ashiv" "meddling k' vi?" tom leralmin-tor, dropping ish-veh abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh looking ak'wikmun. "k' vi? Po, wuh runaway nigger, veling. Vi'd du reckon?" tom glazhau na' me maut shi'vukhut, heh leralmin-tor: "tom, didn't du aishan var-tor me au vesh' ek' gas'rak? Hasn't au prah maf?" "ish-veh?" leralmin-tor ezyet sally; "wuh runaway nigger? 'deed au hasn't. Au've prah ish-veh pla', safe heh ralash, heh au's svi' ik thif'etek va'ashiv, fi' kap heh masu, heh putush-tor ne' k' naf-elakh, till au's claimed il makau!" tom she-tor keh-vla abru svi' sar-tak, k' ish-veh bezhun fal, heh ish-veh han-sharular sharu heh shutting spo' masu-eshanek, heh uralau si' tor me: "au hain't rai gas'rak tor ikap-tor ish-veh abru! Shove!heh ri tor du pak-tor wuh minute. Da-tor ish-veh thal! Au ain't rai kafeh; au's u' elik u' sovek cretur ik lates-tor nash terra!" "ra tor wuh kan tvai?" "i tvai kanok zhit i leralmin, ezyet sally, heh kuv somebody ri tor hal-tor, i'll hal-tor. I've knowed ish-veh ek' ish-veh ha'kiv, heh ni has tom, tra'. Hinek din-tor watson tev-tor dahkuh tevun-krus ago, heh she vesh' kafusik she ek'wak vesh' going tor makau ish-veh ne' wuh pilash, heh leralmin-tor ni; heh she eku ish-veh elik svi' ish-veh dungi." "yi ra fi' terra did du aitlun tor eku ish-veh elik na', seeing au vesh' already elik?" "muhl, ik nam-tor wuh deshker, i bolau leralmin; heh aishan spo' kosu! Po, i aitlu wuh adventure t' ish-veh; heh i'd wuh masu-tor talu-glu svi' khaf togoodness alive, ezyet polly!" kuv she vikau't standing gas'rak tra', aishan svi'udish wuh svep, looking u' slor heh contented u' wuh ha'su ulef bosh t' pie, i istaya i lau worla! Ezyet sally spen-tor na' ish-veh, heh danik teraya-martaya wuh patam ska' t' ish-veh, heh maf-tor abru' ish-veh, heh i afer-tor wuh rom hiyet shi na' me ne' wuh sar-tak, na' ish-veh vesh' getting takov sultry na' etek, seemed tor me. Heh i peeped si', heh svi' wuh pi' du' tom's ezyet polly hutau herself thal heh lam-tor tra' looking mes' na' tom abru' ish-veh spectacleskind t' grinding ish-veh vi' wuh terra, du fai-tor. Heh yi she leralmin-tor: "ha, du weh-rom da-tor y'r patam awayi would kuv i vesh' du, tom." "oh, deary me!" leralmin-tor ezyet sally; "nam-tor au rubai ni? Po, ik ain't tom, ish-veh's sid; tom'stom'swhy, wilat nam-tor tom? Au vesh' la' wuh minute ago." "du tvai wilat's huck finnthat's ra du tvai! I reckon i hain't ashenau such wuh scamp u' t'nash-veh tom ek' aifa tevun ri tor fai-tor ish-veh lu i gla-tor ish-veh. Ik would nam-tor wuh takov howdy-tor. Sasarlah s' ne' ik sar-tak, huck finn." ni i ovsoh ish-veh. Tonk'peh ri olaya brash. Ezyet sally she vesh' veh t' wuh rish-tor-upest-looking persons i ek'wak seeexcept veh, heh ik vesh' sa-kuk silas, lu au sarlah svi' heh au var-tor ish-veh ek' tor ish-veh. Ish-veh ves t' tor ish-veh mon-tor, u' du lau leralmin, heh au didn't fai-tor nothing na' ek' wuh shom t' wuh gad, heh preached wuh prayer-latva sermon ik mu-yor ik mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh rattling ruputation, fai'ei wuh oldest sasu svi' wuh panu couldn't wuh ken-tor ish-veh. Ni tom's ezyet polly, she var-tor ek' pa' vi i vesh', heh ra; heh i had tor abru heh var-tor uf i vesh' svi' such wuh wufik shi ik lu mrs. Phelps nem-tor me na' tom sawyershe chipped svi' heh leralmin-tor, "oh, hal-tor fi' heh vutau me ezyet sally, i'm nam-tor-tor tor ish-veh i', heh 'tain't rai bolaya tor rubah"ik lu ezyet sally nem-tor me na' tom sawyer i had tor lamok itthere vikau't rai vath yut, heh i knowed au wouldn't kashek, fai'ei ish-veh would nam-tor kov-sayas na' ish-veh, hasu wuh mystery, heh au'd tor wuh adventure s' ish-veh, heh nam-tor perfectly satisfied. Heh ni ish-veh da-tor si', heh au kal-tor fi' tor nam-tor sid, heh tor vel u' mos u' au kupi na' me. Heh ish-veh ezyet polly she leralmin-tor tom vesh' gas'rak pa' hinek din-tor watson setting jim elik svi' ish-veh dungi; heh ni, sure hiyet, tom sawyer had hal-tor heh nem-tor ek' ik trouble heh ertau tor eku wuh elik nigger elik! Heh i couldn't ek'wak ken-tor fa', abi' ik minute heh ik variben, uf au kupi gol'nev wuh ak'shem eku wuh nigger elik k' ish-veh bringing-abru. Muhl, ezyet polly she leralmin-tor ik lu ezyet sally kitau tor ish-veh ik tom heh sid had sarlah ek' gas'rak heh safe, she leralmin-tor tor herself: "glazhau na' ik, i'! I lau ma gishu ish-veh, letting ish-veh hal-tor ska' ik yut rik' anybody tor glantau ish-veh. Ni i' i prah tor hal-tor heh trapse ek' wuh yut ne' wuh pilash, leh-wun hundred mile, heh talal si' ra ik creetur's abru tor nash wak; u' wu u' i couldn't seem tor prah sovek kilko-srashiv s' du pa' ish-veh." "po, i worla puzhu-tor nothing s' du, " leralmin-tor ezyet sally. "muhl, i wonder! Po, i kitau du dah'wak tor ya'akash du ra du kupi tvai k' sid hasu la'." "muhl, i worla prah 'em, sis." ezyet polly she da-tor pa' vohris heh severe, heh leralmin-tor: "du, tom!" "wellwhat?" au leralmin-tor, ves t' pettish. "ri tor du ra me, du impudent thinghand si' au nuhm." "ra nuhm?" "au nuhm. I nam-tor bound, kuv i ma tor nem-tor aholt t' du i'll" "au're svi' wuh lap-fek. Tra', i'. Heh au're aishan wuh ka u' au vesh' lu i prah au s' wuh office. I hain't glazhau vi' au, i hain't estuhl au. Tonk'peh i knowed au'd tor trouble, heh i nahp kuv du vikau't svi' rai brax, i'd" "muhl, du tor bolaya skinning, tra' ain't rai lafosh pa' ish-veh. Heh i kitau wuh'ashiv veh tor var-tor du i vesh' coming; heh i s'pose au" "rai, ish-veh sarlah za-gad; i hain't telv-tor ish-veh wi, tonk'peh ish-veh's ek' gas'rak, i've prah ish-veh." i aitlu tor nufai tor sihaya dahkuh dollars she hadn't, tonk'peh i reckoned sos'eh ish-veh vesh' aishan u' safe tor ri tor. Ni i worla leralmin-tor nothing. Chapter wuh kim-shah wuh wuh'rak wak i catched tom awek i ya'akash ish-veh ra vesh' ish-veh idea, wak t' wuh savlaya?ra ish-veh vesh' au'd dotoran tor tor kuv wuh savlaya ar'kada ek' gas'rak heh au khartau tor eku wuh nigger elik ik vesh' already elik fa'? Heh au leralmin-tor, ra au had dotoran svi' ish-veh patam s' wuh palikaya, kuv etek prah jim si' ek' safe, vesh' na' etek tor sahr-tor ish-veh ne' wuh pilash fi' wuh marshak, heh ma adventures plumb tor wuh ru'lut t' wuh pilash, heh yi var-tor ish-veh pa' ish-veh hasu elik, heh nem-tor ish-veh pla-tor ha-kel fi' wuh steamboat, svi' style, heh vlitau ish-veh na' ish-veh pakik wak, heh kitau zhit ahead heh prah si' ek' wuh niggers pa', heh ma au waltz ish-veh vi' kahr k' wuh torchlight procession heh wuh dvesh-tukh-zhel, heh yi au would nam-tor wuh hero, heh ni would etek. Tonk'peh i reckoned ish-veh vesh' pa' u' muhl wuh yut ish-veh vesh'. Etek had jim s' wuh naf-elakh svi' rai wak, heh lu ezyet polly heh sa-kuk silas heh ezyet sally afer-tor si' uf rom au gol-tor wuh hassu nurse tom, au tor wuh tuh t' fuss abru' ish-veh, heh teslau ish-veh abru nenat, heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ek' au aitlu tor yokul, heh wuh rom wak, heh nothing tor tor. Heh etek had ish-veh abru tor wuh has-bosh-tvi-shal, heh had wuh pid variben; heh tom mazhiv-kur-tor jim keh-leh dollars na' hasu prisoner na' etek ni hasausu, heh doing ish-veh abru ni rom, heh jim vesh' sanoi danik tor tevakh, heh busted si', heh leralmin-tor: "dah, i', huck, ra i var-tor du?ra i var-tor du abru dah fi' jackson islan'? I tole du i prah wuh hairy breas', en ra's de glat un ish-veh; en i tole du i ben don-ka wunst, en gwineter tor nam-tor don-ka agin; en ish-veh's sarlah yeht; en heah she nam-tor! Dah, i'! Doan' variben tor mesigns nam-tor glat, t'nash-veh i var-tor du; en i knowed jis' 's muhl 'na' i 'uz gwineter nam-tor don-ka agin u' i's wuh-stannin' heah dis minute!" heh yi tom au variben bi' heh variben bi', heh leralmin-tor, le's ek' rehkuh zish-tor s' la' veh t' aifa mu-yor heh prah wuh outfit, heh hal-tor na' howling adventures svi' wuh injuns, abru' svi' wuh tsokal, na' wuh couple t' wehk gad il dahkuh; heh i leralmin-tor, ek' gas'rak, ik saikhut me, tonk'peh i ain't prah rai donku na' tor mahr-tor wuh outfit, heh i reckon i couldn't prah rim s' ha-kel, fai'ei ish-veh's kesik pap's vesh' pla' fa' i', heh prah ish-veh ek' maf s' judge thatcher heh mon-tor ish-veh abru. "rai, au hain't, " tom leralmin-tor; "ish-veh's ek' tra' yetsix thousand dollars heh weht; heh ish-veh pap hain't ek'wak vesh' pla' opi'. Hadn't lu sarlah nash-veh maf, anyhow." jim leralmin-tor, ves t' solemn: "au ain't wuh-comin' pla' rai mo', huck." i leralmin-tor: "po, jim?" "nemmine po, huckbut au ain't comin' pla' rai mo." tonk'peh i potau na' ish-veh; ni na' kim-shah au leralmin-tor: "doan' du 'kisau de kelek dat vesh' marek'n ne' de pilash, en dey wuz wuh sasu svi' dah, kivered abru, en i went svi' en unkivered ish-veh heh didn' kal-tor du sarlah svi'? Muhl, den, du pi-maat git yo' donku lu du aitlu ish-veh, kase dat wuz ish-veh." tom's danik muhl i', heh prah ish-veh bullet pa' ish-veh talu fi' wuh glantau-klashausu na' wuh glantau, heh nam-tor kwon-hau-ov seeing ra wak ish-veh nam-tor, heh ni tra' ain't nothing weht tor kitau pa', heh i am rotten glad t' ish-veh, fai'ei kuv i'd wuh knowed ra wuh trouble ish-veh vesh' tor tor wuh dunap i wouldn't wuh tackled ish-veh, heh ain't wuh-going tor rai weht. Tonk'peh i reckon i prah tor ta'hal si' na' wuh tsokal ahead t' wuh shom, fai'ei ezyet sally she's going tor thanai me heh sivilize me, heh i mokuhlek't lamok ish-veh. I vesh' tra' fa'.
